oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya । oṃ śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ oṃ namo nārāyaṇāya oṃ । oṃ namo kṛṣṇāya । oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya ।
namo gaṇapataye । oṃ śrīkṛṣṇaḥ । namas te astu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣa pūrvaja ।। pradhānabuddhyādijagatprapañcasūḥ sa no astu viṣṇur matibhūtimuktidaḥ ।।
guruṃ praṇamya vakṣyāmi purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam ।। dharmaśāstrāditattvajñaṃ vasiṣṭhatanayātmajam ।। svasti śrīgurugaṇeśabhāratīsvarūpiṇe śrīnārāyaṇāya namaḥ । aśeṣavighnendhanajātavedasaṃ namāmi taṃ śuddhadhiyaṃ gaṇādhipam ।।
ṣaḍaṅgavedaiś ca vibhūṣitāṅgaṃ pitāmahaṃ taṃ praṇato asmi nityam ।। itihāsapurāṇānām ādikartre namo namaḥ ।। vakṣo vajraśilāsamūhakaṭhinaṃ vistāri devadviṣo bhinnaṃ yena nakhair mudes tu bhagavān devaḥ sa vaḥ keśavaḥ ।। oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya śrīgaṇeśasarasvatībhyāṃ namaḥ ।
jayati kamalodaravapuḥ kama[la]mukhaḥ kamalagarbhasaṃbhūtaḥ । suranamitacaraṇakamalaḥ kamalāsanasaṃsthito brahmā ।। jayati jalabhāragarbhitanilāmbudanīlavapuḥ । mandaragiriparivartanaviṣamaśilālāñchano vibhuḥ ।।
jayati śaśikhaṇḍamaṇḍitavikaṭajaṭāmukuṭasaṃkaṭalalāṭam । sphuṭadaśanakiraṇavikasitamukhakamalacatuṣṭayaṃ śaṃbhoḥ ।। śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ oṃ namo bhagavate śrīvāsudevāya । oṃ ।
oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya śrīgaṇeśasarasvatībhyāṃ namaḥ । oṃ । prasannavadanaṃ dhyāyet sarvavighnopaśāntaye ।। anekadantaṃ bhaktānām ekadantam upāsmahe ।।
ya brahmācyutaśaṃkaraprabhṛtibhir devaiḥ sadā pūjitā sā māṃ pātu sarasvatī bhagavatī niḥśeṣajāḍyāpahā ।। oṃ । yasmād idaṃ jagad ajāyata yatra tiṣṭhaty ante samastam idaṃ astam upaiti yatra । tasmai namaḥ sadasadādivikalpaśūnya caitanyamātravapuṣe puruṣottamāya ।।
tattvena yaś ca dadhadīśvaratatsvabhāva bhogāpavargatadupāyagatīr udāraḥ । saṃdarśayan niramimīta purāṇaratnaṃ tasmai namo munivarāya parāśarāya ।। purāṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ cakre yas tam vande parāśaram ।। oṃ śrīviṣṇave namaḥ ।
śrīmahāgaṇapataye namaḥ । avighnam astu । tārkṣyādhirūḍhāya sukhapradāya akṣmīvarāhāya namaḥ parasmai ।। hariḥ oṃ viṣṇupurāṇaṃ saṃputaṃ ārambhaṃ śubham astu avighnam astu śrīśriyai nmaḥ [namaḥ] śrīhayagrīvāya nmaḥ [namaḥ] śrīrāmacandrāya parasmai brahmaṇe nmaḥ [namaḥ] hariḥ oṃ avighnam astu । śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ avighnena parisamāptir astu ।
śaktir yasya jagaddhitāya bhagavān vyāso hariḥ putratāṃ yāto yasya parāśaraṃ tam atulam vandāmahe nirmalam ।। maitreyaḥ paripapraccha praṇipatyābhivādya ca ।। dharmaśāstrāṇi sarvāṇi vedāṅgāni yathākramam ।। vakṣyanti sarvaśāstreṣu prāyaśo ye api vidviṣaḥ ।।
babhūva bhūyaś ca yathā mahābhāga bhaviṣyati ।। līnam āsīd yathā yatra layam eṣyati yatra ca ।। samudraparvatānāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ ca yathā bhuvaḥ ।। devādīnāṃ tathā vaṃśān manūn manvantarāṇi ca ।।
kalpāntasya svarūpaṃ ca yugadharmāṃś ca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। vedaśākhāpraṇayanaṃ yathāvad vyāsakartṛkam ।। śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ sarvaṃ tvatto vāsiṣṭhanandana ।। yenāham etaj jānīyāṃ tvatprasādān mahāmune ।।
pituḥ pitā me bhagavān vasiṣṭho yad uvāca ha ।। śrutas tātas tataḥ krodho maitreyāsīn mamātulaḥ ।। bhasmīkṛtāś ca śataśas tasmin satre niśācarāḥ ।। mām uvāca mahābhāgo vasiṣṭho asmatpitāmahaḥ ।।
rākṣasā nāparādhyante pitus te vihitaṃ tathā ।। hanyate tāta kaḥ kena yataḥ svakṛtabhuk pumān ।। yaśasas tapasaś caiva krodho nāśakaraḥ paraḥ ।। varjayanti sadā krodhaṃ tāta mā tadvaśo bhava ।।
satraṃ te viramatv etat kṣamāsārā hi sādhavaḥ ।। upasaṃhṛtavān satraṃ sadyas tadvākyagauravāt ।। saṃprāptaś ca tadā tatra pulastyo brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।। mām uvāca mahābhāgo maitreya pulahāgrajaḥ ।।
tvayā tasmāt samastāni bhavāñ chāstrāṇi vetsyati ।। tvayā tasmān mahābhāga dadāmy anyaṃ mahāvaram ।। devatāpāramārthyaṃ ca yathāvad vetsyate bhavān ।। matprasādād asaṃdigdhā tava vatsa bhaviṣyati ।।
pulastyena yad uktaṃ te sarvam etad bhaviṣyati ।। yad uktaṃ tat smṛtiṃ yātaṃ tvatpraśnād akhilaṃ mama ।। purāṇasaṃhitāṃ samyak tāṃ nibodha yathātatham ।। sthitisaṃyamakartāsau jagato asya jagac ca saḥ ।।
kṛtvā vaiṣṇavam uttamaṃ munivaraṃ maitreyam adhyāpayat tattvārthapratipādanaṃ pravadatāṃ sarvārthadaṃ śṛṇvatām ।। sadaikarūparūpāya viṣṇave sarvajiṣṇave ।। vāsudevāya tārāya sargasthityantakāriṇe ।। avyaktavyaktarūpāya viṣṇave muktihetave ।।
mūlabhūto namas tasmai viṣṇave paramātmane ।। praṇamya sarvabhūtastham acyutaṃ puruṣottamam ।। tam evārthasvarūpeṇa bhrāntidarśanataḥ sthitam ।। praṇamya jagatām īśam ajam akṣayam avyayam ।।
pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavān abjayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। sārasvatāya tenāpi mama sārasvatena ca ।। rūpavarṇādinirdeśaviśeṣaṇavivarjitaḥ ।। varjitaḥ śakyate vaktuṃ yaḥ sadāstīti kevalam ।।
tataḥ sa vāsudeveti vidvadbhiḥ paripaṭhyate ।। ekasvarūpaṃ ca sadā heyābhāvāc ca nirmalam ।। tathā puruṣarūpeṇa kālarūpeṇa ca sthitam ।। vyaktāvyakte tathaivānye rūpe kālas tathāparam ।।
paśyanti sūrayaḥ śuddhaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। rūpāṇi sthitisargāntavyaktisadbhāvahetavaḥ ।। krīḍato bālakasyeva ceṣṭāṃ tasya niśāmaya ।। procyate prakṛtiḥ sūkṣmā nityā sadasadātmikā ।।
śabdasparśavihīnaṃ tad rūpādibhir asaṃhatam ।। tenāgre sarvam evāsīd vyāptaṃ vai pralayād anu ।। paṭhanti caitam evārthaṃ pradhānapratipādakam ।। śrotrādibuddhyānupalabhyam ekaṃ prādhānikaṃ brahma pumāṃs tadāsīt ।।
tasyaiva te anyena dhṛte viyukte rūpāntaraṃ tad dvija kālasaṃjñam ।। tasmāt prākṛtasaṃjño ayam ucyate pratisaṃcaraḥ ।। avyucchinnās tatas tv ete sargasthityantasaṃyamāḥ ।। kālasvarūpaṃ tad viṣṇor maitreya parivartate ।।
kālasvarūparūpaṃ tad viṣṇor maitreya vartate ।। sarvagaḥ sarvabhūteśaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ ।। kṣobhayām āsa saṃprāpte sargakāle vyayāvyayau ।। manaso nopakartṛtvāt tathāsau parameśvaraḥ ।।
sa saṃkocavikāsābhyāṃ pradhānatve api ca sthitaḥ ।। vyaktasvarūpaś ca tathā viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ ।। guṇavyañjanasaṃbhūtiḥ sargakāle dvijottama ।। pradhānatattvena samaṃ tvacā bījam ivāvṛtam ।।
trividho ayam ahaṃkāro mahattattvād ajāyata ।। yathā pradhānena mahān mahatā sa tathāvṛtaḥ ।। sasarja śabdatanmātrād ākāśaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam ।। ākāśas tu vikurvāṇaḥ sparśamātraṃ sasarja ha ।।
ākāśaṃ śabdamātraṃ tu sparśamātraṃ samāvṛṇot ।। jyotir utpadyate vāyos tad rūpaguṇam ucyate ।। jyotiś cāpi vikurvāṇaṃ rasamātraṃ sasarja ha ।। rasamātrāṇi cāmbhāṃsi rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot ।।
saṃghāto jāyate tasmāt tasya gandho guṇo mataḥ ।। tanmātrāṇy aviśeṣāṇi aviśeṣās tato hi te ।। bhūtatanmātrasargo ayam ahaṃkārāt tu tāmasāt ।। ekādaśaṃ manaś cātra devā vaikārikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
śabdādīnām avāptyarthaṃ buddhiyuktāni vai dvija ।। visargaśilpagatyukti karma teṣāṃ ca kathyate ।। śabdādibhir guṇair brahman saṃyuktāny uttarottaraiḥ ।। śāntā ghorāś ca mūḍhāś ca viśeṣās tena te smṛtāḥ ।।
nāśaknuvan prajāḥ sraṣṭum asamāgamya kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। ekasaṃghātalakṣyāś ca saṃprāpyaikyam aśeṣataḥ ।। mahadādyā viśeṣāntā hy aṇḍam utpādayanti te ।। prākṛtaṃ brahmarūpasya viṣṇoḥ sthānam anuttamam ।।
viṣṇur brahmasvarūpeṇa svayam eva vyavasthitaḥ ।। garbhodakaṃ samudrāś ca tasyāsan sumahātmanaḥ ।। tasminn aṇḍe abhavad vipra sadevāsuramānuṣaḥ ।। vṛtaṃ daśaguṇair aṇḍaṃ bhūtādir mahatā tathā ।।
nālikeraphalasyāntar bījaṃ bāhyadalair iva ।। brahmā bhūtvāsya jagato visṛṣṭau saṃpravartate ।। sattvabhṛd bhagavān viṣṇur aprameyaparākramaḥ ।। maitreyākhilabhūtāni bhakṣayaty atibhīṣaṇaḥ ।।
nāgaparyaṅkaśayane śete asau parameśvaraḥ ।। prabuddhaś ca punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ karoti brahmarūpadhṛk ।। sa saṃjñāṃ yāti bhagavān eka eva janārdanaḥ ।। upasaṃharate cānte saṃhartā ca svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।।
sarvendriyāntaḥkaraṇaṃ puruṣākhyaṃ hi yaj jagat ।। sargādikaṃ tato asyaiva bhūtastham upakārakam ।। brahmādyavasthābhir aśeṣamūrtir viṣṇur variṣṭho varado vareṇyaḥ ।। kathaṃ sargādikartṛtvaṃ brahmaṇo abhyupagamyate ।।
bhavanti tapatāṃ śreṣṭha pāvakasya yathoṣṇatā ।। nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। utpannaḥ procyate vidvan nitya evopacārataḥ ।। tat parākhyaṃ tadardhaṃ ca parārdham abhidhīyate ।।
tena tasya nibodha tvaṃ parimāṇopapādanam ।। bhūbhūbhṛtsāgarādīnām aśeṣāṇāṃ ca sattama ।। kāṣṭhātriṃśat kalā triṃśat kalā mauhūrtiko vidhiḥ ।। ahorātrāṇi tāvanti māsaḥ pakṣadvayātmakaḥ ।।
ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ rātrir devānām uttaraṃ dinam ।। caturyugaṃ dvādaśabhis tadvibhāgaṃ nibodha me ।। divyābdānāṃ sahasrāṇi yugeṣv āhuḥ purāvidaḥ ।। saṃdhyāṃśakaś ca tattulyo yugasyānantaro hi saḥ ।।
yugākhyaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ kṛtatretādisaṃjñitaḥ ।। procyate tatsahasraṃ ca brahmaṇo divasaṃ mune ।। bhavanti parimāṇaṃ ca teṣāṃ kālakṛtaṃ śṛṇu ।। ekakāle hi sṛjyante saṃhriyante ca pūrvavat ।।
manvantaraṃ manoḥ kālaḥ surādīnāṃ ca sattama ।। dvāpañcāśat tathānyāni sahasrāṇy adhikāni tu ।। saptaṣaṣṭis tathānyāni niyutāni mahāmune ।। dvicatvāriṃśatā yukta śatenāpy adhikās tathā ।।
divyāhnaḥ pañcasāhasramāsā daśa dināṣṭakam ।। catur yāmā muhūrtau dvāv aṣṭāv api kalās tathā ।। kāṣṭā saptadaśa dvau ca nimeṣau tadanantaram ।। daivasyaikanimeṣasya saptamo bhāga iṣyate ।।
mānuṣābdās tu lakṣyāṇi tathāṣṭādaśa tatparam ।। sahasram aṣṭāviṃśatyā yutāś cābdā catuḥśatī ।। caturviṃśed ahorātre yutā māsāś ca ṣaṭ tathā ।। nāḍyo dvādaśa tāvatyaḥ kalāś ca tadanantaram ।।
pañcaviṃśati kāṣṭāś ca nimeṣā daśasāyikā ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyeyaṃ mānuṣair vatsarair dvija ।। brāhmo naimittiko nāma tasyānte pratisaṃcaraḥ ।। janaṃ prayānti tāpārtā maharlokanivāsinaḥ ।।
bhogiśayyāgataḥ śete trailokyagrāsabṛṃhitaḥ ।। tatpramāṇāṃ hi tāṃ rātriṃ tadante sṛjate punaḥ ।। śataṃ hi tasya varṣāṇāṃ paramāyur mahātmanaḥ ।। tasyānte abhūn mahākalpaḥ pādma ity abhiviśrutaḥ ।।
vārāha iti kalpo ayaṃ prathamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। sasarja sarvabhūtāni tad ācakṣva mahāmune ।। prajāpatipatir devo yathā tan me niśāmaya ।। sattvodriktas tathā brahmā śūnyaṃ lokam avaikṣata ।।
brahmasvarūpī bhagavān anādiḥ sarvasaṃbhavaḥ ।। brahmasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam ।। ayanaṃ tasya tāḥ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। anumānāt taduddhāraṃ kartukāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
matsyakūrmādikāṃ tadvad vārāhaṃ vapur āsthitaḥ ।। sthitaḥ sthirātmā sarvātmā paramātmā prajāpatiḥ ।। praviveśa tadā toyam ātmādhāro dharādharaḥ ।। tuṣṭāva praṇatā bhūtvā bhaktinamrā vasuṃdharā ।।
mām uddharāsmād adya tvaṃ tvatto ahaṃ pūrvam utthitā ।। tathānyāni ca bhūtāni gaganādīny aśeṣataḥ ।। pradhānavyaktabhūtāya kālabhūtāya te namaḥ ।। sargādiṣu prabho brahmaviṣṇurudrātmarūpadhṛk ।।
śeṣe tvam eva govinda cintyamāno manīṣibhiḥ ।। avatāreṣu yad rūpaṃ tad arcanti divaukasaḥ ।। vāsudevam anārādhya ko mokṣaṃ samavāpsyati ।। buddhyā ca yat paricchedyaṃ tad rūpam akhilaṃ tava ।।
mādhavīm iti loko ayam abhidhatte tato hi mām ।। parāparātman viśvātmañ jaya yajñapate anagha ।। tvaṃ vedās tvaṃ tadaṅgāni tvaṃ yajñapuruṣo hare ।। mūrtāmūrtam adṛśyaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ ca puruṣottama ।।
tathaiva māyayā sarvaṃ tvatto aham iva dṛśyate ।। tat sarvaṃ tvaṃ namas tubhyaṃ bhūyo bhūyo namo namaḥ ।। sāmasvaradhvaniḥ śrīmāñ jagarja parighargharam ।। rasātalād utpalapatrasaṃnibhaḥ samutthito nīla ivācalo mahān ।।
sanandanādīn apakalmaṣān munīn cakāra bhūyo api pavitratāspadam ।। śvāsānilārtāḥ paritaḥ prayānti siddhā jane ye niyataṃ vasanti ।। nārāyaṇasyāpi tanur viśanti ।। vidhunvato vedamayaṃ śarīraṃ romāntarasthā munayaḥ stuvanti ।।
sanandanādyā natinamrakandharā dharādharaṃ dhīrataroddhatekṣaṇam ।। prasūtināśasthitihetur īśvaras tvam eva nānyat paramaṃ ca yat padam ।। hutāśajihvo asi tanūruhāṇi darbhāḥ prabho yajñapumāṃs tvam eva ।। sūktāny aśeṣāṇi saṭākalāpo ghrāṇaṃ samastāni havīṃṣi deva ।।
pūrteṣṭadharmaśravaṇo asi deva sanātanātman bhagavan prasīda ।। viśvasya vidmaḥ parameśvaro asi prasīda nātho asi carācarasya ।। vigāhataḥ padmavanaṃ vilagnaṃ sarojinīpatram ivoḍhapaṅkam ।। vyāptaṃ jagad vyāptisamarthadīpte hitāya viśvasya vibho bhava tvam ।।
tavaiṣa mahimā yena vyāptam etac carācaram ।। bhrāntijñānena paśyanti jagadrūpam ayoginaḥ ।। arthasvarūpaṃ paśyanto bhrāmyante mohasaṃplave ।। jñānātmakaṃ prapaśyanti tvadrūpaṃ parameśvara ।।
uddharorvīm ameyātmañ śaṃ no dehy abjalocana ।। samuddhara bhavāyeśa śaṃ no dehy abjalocana ।। bhavatv eṣā namas te astu śaṃ no dehy abjalocana ।। ujjahāra kṣitiṃ kṣipraṃ nyastavāṃś ca mahārṇave ।।
vitatatvāt tu dehasya na mahī yāti saṃplavam ।। yathāvibhāgaṃ bhagavān anādiḥ sarvasaṃbhavaḥ ।। amoghena prabhāvena sasarjāmoghavāñchitaḥ ।। bhūrādyāṃś caturo lokān pūrvavat samakalpayat ।।
cakāra sṛṣṭiṃ bhagavāṃś caturvaktradharo hariḥ ।। pradhānakāraṇībhūtā yato vai sṛjyaśaktayaḥ ।। nīyate tapatāṃ śreṣṭha svaśaktyā vastu vastutām ।। manuṣyatiryagvṛkṣādīn bhūvyomasalilaukasaḥ ।।
sargādau sṛṣṭavān brahmā tan mamācakṣva vistarāt ।। yathā sasarja devo asau devādīn akhilān vibhuḥ ।। abuddhipūrvakaḥ sargaḥ prādurbhūtas tamomayaḥ ।। avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ ।।
bahir antaś cāprakāśaḥ saṃvṛtātmā nagātmakaḥ ।। mukhyā nagā yataś coktā mukhyasargas tatas tv ayam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvāsādhakaṃ sargam amanyad aparaṃ punaḥ ।। yasmāt tiryakpravṛttaḥ sa tiryaksrotas tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
utpathagrāhiṇaś caiva te ajñāne jñānamāninaḥ ।। antaḥprakāśās te sarve āvṛtāś ca parasparam ।। ūrdhvasrotas tṛtīyas tu sāttvikordhvam avartata ।। prakāśā bahir antaś ca ūrdhvasrotodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
tasmin sarge abhavat prītir niṣpanne brahmaṇas tathā ।। asādhakāṃs tu tāñ jñātvā mukhyasargādisaṃbhavān ।। prādurbhūtas tadāvyaktād arvāksrotas tu sādhakaḥ ।। te ca prakāśabahulās tamoudriktā rajo'dhikāḥ ।।
prakāśā bahir antaś ca manuṣyāḥ sādhakās tu te ।। pañcamo anugrahaḥ sargaḥ sa caturdhā vyavasthitaḥ ।। viparyayeṇa cāśaktyā siddhyā tuṣṭyā tathaiva ca ।। nivṛttaṃ vartamānaṃ ca sarve jānanti vai punaḥ ।।
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ sa ucyate ।। te parigrāhiṇaḥ sarge saṃvibhāganatāḥ sadā ।। krodhanāś cāpy aśīlāś ca jñeyā bhūtādikās tu te ।। prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇas tu saḥ ।।
vaikārikas tṛtīyas tu sarga aindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। mukhyasargaś caturthas tu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tatordhvasrotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargas tu sa smṛtaḥ ।। tato arvāksrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ ।।
pañcaite vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtās tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ity ete vai samākhyātā nava sargāḥ prajāpateḥ ।। sṛjato jagadīśasya kim anyac chrotum icchasi ।। vistarāc chrotum icchāmi tvatto munivarottama ।।
khyātyā tayā hy anirmuktāḥ saṃhāre apy upasaṃhṛtāḥ ।। brahmaṇaḥ kurvataḥ sṛṣṭiṃ jajñire mānasās tu tāḥ ।। sisṛkṣur ambhāṃsy etāni svam ātmānam ayūyujat ।। sisṛkṣor jaghanāt pūrvam asurā jajñire tataḥ ।।
sā tu tyaktā tatas tena maitreyābhūd vibhāvarī ।। sattvodriktāḥ samudbhūtā mukhato brahmaṇo dvija ।। tato hi balino rātrāv asurā devatā divā ।। pitṛvan manyamānasya pitaras tasya jajñire ।।
sā cotsṛṣṭābhavat saṃdhyā dinanaktāntarasthitā ।। rajomātrotkaṭā jātā manuṣyā dvijasattama ।। jyotsnā samabhavat sāpi prāksaṃdhyā yābhidhīyate ।। maitreya saṃdhyāsamaye tasmād ete bhavanti vai ।।
brahmaṇas tu śarīrāṇi triguṇopāśrayāṇi tu ।। tataḥ kṣud brahmaṇo jātā jajñe kopas tayā tataḥ ।। virūpāḥ śmaśrulā jātās te abhyadhāvanta taṃ prabhum ।। ūcuḥ khādāma ity anye ye te yakṣās tu jakṣaṇāt ।।
hīnāś ca śiraso bhūyaḥ samārohanta tacchiraḥ ।। varṇena kapiśenogrā bhūtās te piśitāśanāḥ ।। pibanto jajñire vācaṃ gandharvās tena te dvija ।। tataḥ svacchandato anyāni vayāṃsi vayaso asṛjat ।।
sṛṣṭavān udarād gāś ca pārśvābhyāṃ ca prajāpatiḥ ।। uṣṭrān aśvatarāṃś caiva nyaṅkūn anyāś ca jātayaḥ ।। sṛṣṭvā paśvoṣadhīḥ samyag yuyoja sa tadādhvare ।। etān grāmyān paśūn āhur āraṇyāṃś ca nibodha me ।।
audakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamās tu sarīsṛpāḥ ।। agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamān mukhāt ।। bṛhat sāma tathokthaṃ ca dakṣiṇād asṛjan mukhāt ।। vairūpam atirātraṃ ca paścimād asṛjan mukhāt ।।
anuṣṭubhaṃ sa vairājam uttarād asṛjan mukhāt ।। devāsurapitṝn sṛṣṭvā manuṣyāṃś ca prajāpatiḥ ।। yakṣān piśācān gandharvān tathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇān ।। avyayaṃ ca vyayaṃ caiva yad idaṃ sthāṇujaṅgamam ।।
tāny eva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāt tat tasya rocate ।। nānātvaṃ viniyogāṃś ca dhātaivaṃ vyasṛjat svayam ।। vedaśabdebhya evādau devādīnāṃ cakāra saḥ ।।
yathā niyogayogyāni sarveṣām api so akarot ।। dṛśyante tāni tāny eva tathā bhāvā yugādiṣu ।। sisṛkṣāśaktiyukto asau sṛjyaśaktipracoditaḥ ।। brahman vistarato brūhi brahmā tam asṛjad yathā ।।
yac ca teṣāṃ smṛtaṃ karma viprādīnāṃ tad ucyatām ।। ajāyanta dvijaśreṣṭha sattvodriktā mukhāt prajāḥ ।। rajasā tamasā caiva samudriktās tathorutaḥ ।। tamaḥpradhānās tāḥ sarvāś cāturvarṇyam idaṃ tataḥ ।।
pādoruvakṣaḥsthalato mukhataś ca samudgatāḥ ।। cāturvarṇyaṃ mahābhāga yajñasādhanam uttamam ।। āpyāyayante dharmajña yajñāḥ kalyāṇahetavaḥ ।। viśuddhācaraṇopetaiḥ sadbhiḥ sanmārgagāmibhiḥ ।।
yad vābhirucitaṃ sthānaṃ tad yānti manujā dvija ।। samyakchraddhāḥ samācārapravaṇā munisattama ।। śuddhāntaḥkaraṇāḥ śuddhāḥ sarvānuṣṭhānanirmalāḥ ।। śuddhajñānaṃ prapaśyanti viṣṇvākhyaṃ yena tat padam ।।
sa pātayaty aghaṃ ghoram alpam alpālpasāravat ।। prajāsu tāsu maitreya rāgādikam asādhakam ।। rasollāsādayaś cānyāḥ siddhayo aṣṭau bhavanti yāḥ ।। dvandvābhibhavaduḥkhārtās tā bhavanti tataḥ prajāḥ ।।
kṛtrimaṃ ca tathā durgaṃ purakharvaṭakādi yat ।। śītātapādibādhānāṃ praśamāya mahāmate ।। vārtopāyaṃ tataś cakrur hastasiddhiṃ ca karmajām ।। priyaṃgavo hy udārāś ca koradūṣāḥ satīnakāḥ ।।
āḍhakyaś caṇakāś caiva śaṇāḥ saptadaśa smṛtāḥ ।। oṣadhyo yajñiyāś caiva grāmyāraṇyāś caturdaśa ।। priyaṃgusaptamā hy etā aṣṭamās tu kulatthakāḥ ।। tathā veṇuyavāḥ proktās tadvan markaṭakā mune ।।
yajñaniṣpattaye yajñas tathāsāṃ hetur uttamaḥ ।। parāvaravidaḥ prājñās tato yajñān vitanvate ।। upakārakaraṃ puṃsāṃ kriyamāṇāghaśāntidam ।। cetaḥsu vavṛdhe cakrus te na yajñeṣu mānasam ।।
tat sarvaṃ nindamānās te yajñavyāsedhakāriṇaḥ ।। durātmāno durācārā babhūvuḥ kuṭilāśayāḥ ।। maryādāṃ sthāpayām āsa yathāsthānaṃ yathāguṇam ।। lokāṃś ca sarvavarṇānāṃ samyagdharmānupālinām ।।
sthānam aindraṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ saṃgrāmeṣv anivartinām ।। gāndharvaṃ śūdrajātīnāṃ paricaryānuvartinām ।। smṛtaṃ teṣāṃ tu yat sthānaṃ tad eva guruvāsinām ।। prājāpatyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ brāhmaṃ saṃnyāsināṃ smṛtam ।।
yoginām amṛtaṃ sthānaṃ yad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। teṣāṃ tat paramaṃ sthānaṃ yad vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ ।। adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣaracintakāḥ ।। asipatravanaṃ ghoraṃ kālasūtram avīcimat ।।
sthānam etat samākhyātaṃ svadharmatyāginaś ca ye ।। kṣetrajñāḥ samavartanta gātrebhyas tasya dhīmataḥ ।। devādyāḥ sthāvarāntāś ca traiguṇyaviṣaye sthitāḥ ।। evaṃ bhūtāni sṛṣṭāni carāṇi sthāvarāṇi ca ।।
tadānyān mānasān putrān sadṛśān ātmano asṛjat ।। marīciṃ dakṣam atriṃ ca vasiṣṭhaṃ caiva mānasān ।। nava brahmāṇa ity ete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ ।। khyātiṃ bhūtiṃ ca saṃbhūtiṃ kṣamāṃ prītiṃ tathaiva ca ।।
sannatiṃ ca tathaivorjām anasūyāṃ tathaiva ca ।। prasūtiṃ ca tataḥ sṛṣṭvā dadau teṣāṃ mahātmanām ।। patnyo bhavadhvam ity uktvā teṣām eva tu dattavān ।। na te lokeṣv asajjanta nirapekṣāḥ prajāsu te ।।
brahmaṇo abhūn mahān krodhas trailokyadahanakṣamaḥ ।। brahmaṇo abhūt tadā sarvaṃ trailokyam akhilaṃ mune ।। ardhanārīnaravapuḥ pracaṇḍo atiśarīravān ।। vibhajātmānam ity uktvā taṃ brahmāntardadhe tataḥ ।।
bibheda puruṣatvaṃ ca daśadhā caikadhā ca saḥ ।। bibheda bahudhā devaḥ svarūpair asitaiḥ sitaiḥ ।। ātmānam eva kṛtavān prājāpatye manuṃ dvija ।। svāyambhuvo manur devaḥ patnītve jagṛhe vibhuḥ ।।
kanyādvayaṃ ca dharmajña rūpaudāryaguṇānvitam ।। putro yajño mahābhāga dampatyor mithunaṃ tataḥ ।। yāmā iti samākhyātā devāḥ svāyambhuve manau ।। sasarja kanyās tāsāṃ tu samyaṅ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।।
buddhir lajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtis trayodaśī ।। tābhyaḥ śiṣṭā yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ ।। sannatiś cānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā ।। pulastyaḥ pulahaś caiva kratuś carṣivaras tathā ।।
khyātyādyā jagṛhuḥ kanyā munayo munisattama ।। saṃtoṣaṃ ca tathā tuṣṭir lobhaṃ puṣṭir asūyata ।। vyavasāyaṃ prajajñe vai kṣemaṃ śāntir asūyata ।। kāmād ratiḥ sutaṃ harṣaṃ dharmapautram asūyata ।।
kanyā ca nikṛtis tābhyāṃ bhayaṃ narakam eva ca ।। tayor jajñe atha vai māyā mṛtyuṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam ।। mṛtyor vyādhijarāśokatṛṣṇākrodhāś ca jajñire ।। naiṣāṃ bhāryāsti putro vā te sarve hy ūrdhvaretasaḥ ।।
nityapralayahetutvaṃ jagato asya prayānti vai ।। jagaty atra mahābhāga nityaṃ sargasya hetavaḥ ।। sanmārgābhiratāḥ śūrās te nityaṃ sthitikāriṇaḥ ।। nityābhāvaś ca teṣāṃ vai svarūpaṃ mama kathyatām ।।
tais tai rūpair acintyātmā karoty avyāhatān vibhuḥ ।। nityaś ca sarvabhūtānāṃ pralayo ayaṃ caturvidhaḥ ।। prayāti prākṛte caiva brahmāṇḍaṃ prakṛtau layam ।। nityaḥ sadaiva jātānāṃ yo vināśo divāniśam ।।
dainaṃdinī tathā proktā yāntarapralayād anu ।। nityasargo hi sa proktaḥ purāṇārthavicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। saṃsthitaḥ kurute viṣṇur utpattisthitisaṃyamān ।। vaiṣṇavyaḥ parivartante maitreyāharniśaṃ sadā ।।
yo atiyāti sa yāty eva paraṃ nāvartate punaḥ ।। rudrasargaṃ pravakṣyāmi tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।। prādur āsīt prabhor aṅke kumāro nīlalohitaḥ ।। kiṃ rodiṣīti taṃ brahmā rudantaṃ pratyuvāca ha ।।
evam uktaḥ punaḥ so atha saptakṛtvo ruroda vai ।। sthānāni caiṣām aṣṭānāṃ patnīḥ putrāṃś ca vai vibhuḥ ।। bhīmam ugraṃ mahādevam uvāca sa pitāmahaḥ ।। dīkṣito brāhmaṇaḥ soma ity etās tanavaḥ kramāt ।।
svāhā diśas tathā dīkṣā rohiṇī ca yathākramam ।। patnyaḥ smṛtā mahābhāga tadapatyāni me śṛṇu ।। yeṣāṃ sūtiprasūtaiś ca idam āpūritaṃ jagat ।। skandaḥ svargo atha santāno budhaś cānukramāt sutāḥ ।।
dakṣakopāc ca tatyāja sā satī svaṃ kalevaram ।। upayeme duhitaraṃ dakṣasyaiva prajāpateḥ ।। upayeme punaś comām ananyāṃ bhagavān bhavaḥ ।। śriyaṃ ca devadevasya patnī nārāyaṇasya yā ।।
bhṛgoḥ khyātyāṃ samutpannety etad āha kathaṃ bhavān ।। yathā sarvagato viṣṇus tathaiveyaṃ dvijottama ।। bodho viṣṇur iyaṃ buddhir dharmo asau satkriyā tv iyam ।। saṃtoṣo bhagavāṃl lakṣmīs tuṣṭir maitreya śāśvatī ।।
ājyāhutir asau devī puroḍāśo janārdanaḥ ।। citir lakṣmīr harir yūpa idhmā śrīr bhagavān kuśaḥ ।। svāhā lakṣmīr jagannātho vāsudevo hutāśanaḥ ।। maitreya keśavaḥ sūryas tatprabhā kamalālayā ।।
dyauḥ śrīḥ sarvātmako viṣṇur avakāśo ativistaraḥ ।। dhṛtir lakṣmīr jagacceṣṭā vāyuḥ sarvatrago hariḥ ।। lakṣmīsvarūpam indrāṇī devendro madhusūdanaḥ ।। ṛddhiḥ śrīḥ śrīdharo devaḥ svayam eva dhaneśvaraḥ ।।
śrīr devasenā viprendra devasenāpatir hariḥ ।। kāṣṭhā lakṣmīr nimeṣo asau muhūrto asau kalā tu sā ।। latābhūtā jaganmātā śrīr viṣṇur drumasaṃsthitiḥ ।। varaprado varo viṣṇur vadhūḥ padmavanālayā ।।
dhvajaś ca puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ patākā kamalālayā ।। ratirāgau ca dharmajña lakṣmīr govinda eva ca ।। kiṃ vātra bahunoktena saṃkṣepeṇedam ucyate ।। strīnāmni lakṣmīr maitreya nānayor vidyate param ।।
śrīsaṃbaddhaṃ mayāpy etac śrutam āsīn marīcitaḥ ।। sa dadarśa srajaṃ divyām ṛṣir vidyādharīkare ।। atisevyam abhūd brahman tad vanaṃ vanacāriṇām ।। tāṃ yayāce varārohāṃ vidyādharavadhūṃ tataḥ ।।
dadau tasmai viśālākṣī sādaraṃ praṇipatya tam ।। kṛtvā sa vipro maitreya paribabhrāma medinīm ।। trailokyādhipatiṃ devaṃ saha devaiḥ śacīpatim ।। ādāyāmararājāya cikṣeponmattavan muniḥ ।।
nyastā rarāja kailāsaśikhare jāhnavī yathā ।। kareṇāghrāya cikṣepa tāṃ srajaṃ dharaṇītale ।। maitreya devarājānaṃ kruddhaś caitad uvāca ha ।। śriyo dhāma srajaṃ yas tvaṃ maddattāṃ nābhinandasi ।।
harṣotphullakapolena na cāpi śirasā dhṛtā ।। trailokyaśrīr ato mūḍha vināśam upayāsyati ।। ato avamānam asmāsu māninā bhavatā kṛtam ।। tasmāt praṇaṣṭalakṣmīkaṃ trailokyaṃ te bhaviṣyati ।।
taṃ tvaṃ mām atigarveṇa devarājāvamanyase ।। prasādayām āsa muniṃ durvāsasam akalmaṣam ।। pratyuvāca sahasrākṣaṃ durvāsā munisattamaḥ ।। anye te munayaḥ śakra durvāsasam avehi mām ।।
akṣāntisārasarvasvaṃ durvāsasam avehi mām ।। garvaṃ gato asi yenaivaṃ mām apy adyāvamanyase ।। nirīkṣya kas tribhuvane mama yo na gato bhayam ।। viḍambanām imāṃ bhūyaḥ karoṣy anunayātmikām ।।
āruhyairāvataṃ brahman prayayāv amarāvatīm ।। maitreyāsīd apadhvastaṃ saṃkṣīṇauṣadhivīrudham ।। na ca dānādidharmeṣu manaś cakre tadā janaḥ ।। svalpe api hi babhūvus te sābhilāṣā dvijottama ।।
niḥśrīkāṇāṃ kutaḥ sattvaṃ vinā tena guṇāḥ kutaḥ ।। bhavaty apadhvastamatir laṅghitaḥ prathitaḥ pumān ।। devān prati balodyogaṃ cakrur daiteyadānavāḥ ।। śriyā vihīnair niḥsattvair devaiś cakrus tato raṇam ।।
pitāmahaṃ mahābhāgaṃ hutāśanapurogamāḥ ।। parāvareśaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajadhvam asurārdanam ।। prajāpatipatiṃ viṣṇum anantam aparājitam ।। praṇatārtiharaṃ viṣṇuṃ sa vaḥ śreyo vidhāsyati ।।
kṣīrodasyottaraṃ tīraṃ tair eva sahito yayau ।। tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ parāvarapatiṃ harim ।। lokadhāmadharādhāram aprakāśam abhedinam ।। samastānāṃ gariṣṭhaṃ ca bhūrādīnāṃ garīyasām ।।
sarvabhūtaś ca yo devaḥ parāṇām api yaḥ paraḥ ।। yogibhiś cintyate yo asau muktihetor mumukṣubhiḥ ।। sa śuddhaḥ sarvaśuddhebhyaḥ pumān ādyaḥ prasīdatu ।। yasya śaktir na śuddhasya prasīdatu sa no hariḥ ।।
prasīdatu sa no viṣṇur ātmā yaḥ sarvadehinām ।। kāryasyāpi ca yaḥ kāryaṃ prasīdatu sa no hariḥ ।। tatkāryakāryabhūto yas tataś ca praṇato asmi tam ।। tatkāraṇānāṃ hetuṃ taṃ praṇato asmi sureśvaram ।।
kāryakartṛsvarūpaṃ taṃ praṇato asmi paraṃ padam ।। avyaktam avikāraṃ yat tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। tat padaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇoḥ praṇamāmi sadāmalam ।। parabrahmasvarūpasya praṇamāmi tam avyayam ।।
jānanti parameśasya tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। paśyanti praṇave cintyaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। bhavanty abhūtapūrvasya tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। prasīda viṣṇo bhaktānāṃ vraja no dṛṣṭigocaram ।।
praṇamyocuḥ prasīdeti vraja no dṛṣṭigocaram ।। taṃ natāḥ smo jagaddhāma tava sarvagatācyuta ।। ūcur devarṣayaḥ sarve bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ ।। taṃ natāḥ smo jagatsraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭāram aviśeṣaṇam ।।
prasīda praṇatānāṃ tvaṃ sarveṣāṃ dehi darśanam ।। sarvādityaiḥ samaṃ pūṣā pāvako ayaṃ sahāgnibhiḥ ।। sādhyā viśve tathā devā devendraś cāyam īśvaraḥ ।। śaraṇaṃ tvām anuprāptāḥ samastā devatāgaṇāḥ ।।
jagāma darśanaṃ teṣāṃ maitreya parameśvaraḥ ।। apūrvarūpasaṃsthānaṃ tejasāṃ rāśim ūrjitam ।। tuṣṭuvuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ pitāmahapurogamāḥ ।। vasavo marutaḥ sādhyā viśvedevagaṇā bhavān ।।
sa tvam eva jagatsraṣṭā yataḥ sarvagato bhavān ।। vettā vedyaṃ ca sarvātmaṃs tvanmayaṃ cākhilaṃ jagat ।। vayaṃ prasīda sarvātmaṃs tejasāpyāyayasva naḥ ।। yāvan nāyāti śaraṇaṃ tvām aśeṣāghanāśanam ।।
tejasāṃ nātha sarveṣāṃ svaśaktyāpyāyanaṃ kuru ।। prasannadṛṣṭir bhagavān idam āha sa viśvakṛt ।। vadāmy ahaṃ yat kriyatāṃ bhavadbhis tad idaṃ surāḥ ।। mathyatām amṛtaṃ devāḥ sahāye mayy avasthite ।।
sāmānyaphalabhoktāro yūyaṃ vācyā bhaviṣyatha ।। tatpānād balino yūyam amarāś ca bhaviṣyatha ।। na prāpsyanty amṛtaṃ devāḥ kevalaṃ kleśabhāginaḥ ।। saṃdhānam asuraiḥ kṛtvā yatnavanto amṛte abhavan ।।
kṣiptvā kṣīrābdhipayasi śaradabhrāmalatviṣi ।। tato mathitum ārabdhā maitreya tarasāmṛtam ।। kṛṣṇena vāsuker daityāḥ pūrvakāye niveśitāḥ ।। nistejaso asurāḥ sarve babhūvur amitadyute ।।
pucchapradeśe varṣadbhis tadā cāpyāyitāḥ surāḥ ।। mandarādrer adhiṣṭhānaṃ bhramato abhūn mahāmune ।। cakarṣa nāgarājānaṃ daityamadhye apareṇa ca ।। tathāpareṇa maitreya yan na dṛṣṭaṃ surāsuraiḥ ।।
anyena tejasā devān upabṛṃhitavān vibhuḥ ।। havirdhāmābhavat pūrvaṃ surabhiḥ surapūjitā ।। vyākṣiptacetasaś caiva babhūvuḥ stimitekṣaṇāḥ ।। babhūva vāruṇī devī madāghūrṇitalocanā ।।
gandhena pārijāto abhūd devastrīnandanas taruḥ ।। kṣīrodadheḥ samutpanno maitreya paramādbhutaḥ ।। jagṛhuś ca viṣaṃ nāgāḥ kṣīrodābdhisamutthitam ।। bibhratkamaṇḍaluṃ pūrṇam amṛtasya samutthitaḥ ।।
babhūvur muditāḥ sadyo maitreya munibhiḥ saha ।। śrīr devī payasas tasmād utthitā dhṛtapaṅkajā ।। tāṃ tuṣṭuvur mudā yuktāḥ śrīsūktena maharṣayaḥ ।। ghṛtācīpramukhā brahman nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥ ।।
snāpayāṃ cakrire devīṃ sarvalokamaheśvarīm ।। dadau vibhūṣaṇāny aṅge viśvakarmā cakāra ha ।। paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ yayau vakṣaḥsthalaṃ hareḥ ।। lakṣmyā maitreya sahasā parāṃ nirvṛtim āgatāḥ ।।
tyaktā lakṣmyā mahābhāga vipracittipurogamāḥ ।। kamaṇḍaluṃ mahāvīryā yatrāste tad dvijāmṛtam ।। dānavebhyas tad ādāya devebhyaḥ pradadau vibhuḥ ।। udyatāyudhanistriṃśā daityās tāṃś ca samabhyayuḥ ।।
vadhyamānā diśo bheje pātālaṃ ca viveśa vai ।। praṇipatya yathāpūrvam aśāsaṃs tat triviṣṭapam ।। devadeve gate tasmin vāsudeveśvaraṃ harim ।। tuṣṭuvuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣam antardhānagataṃ harim ।।
jyotīṃṣi ca yathāmārgaṃ prayayur munisattama ।। dharme ca sarvabhūtānāṃ tadā matir ajāyata ।। śakraś ca tridaśaśreṣṭhaḥ punaḥ śrīmān ajāyata ।। devarājye sthito devīṃ tuṣṭāvābjakarāṃ tataḥ ।।
durvāsaśāpapātena punar mā bhūd iyaṃ hare ।। tathyeti cābhiprāyeṇas tuṣṭāva śriyamānataḥ ।। śriyam unnidrapadmākṣīṃ viṣṇuvakṣaḥsthalasthitām ।। padmālayāṃ padmakarāṃ padmapatranibhekṣaṇām ।।
vande padmamukhāṃ devīṃ padmanābhapriyām aham ।। saṃdhyā rātriḥ prabhā bhūtir medhā śraddhā sarasvatī ।। ātmavidyā ca devi tvaṃ vimuktiphaladāyinī ।। saumyāsaumyair jagad rūpais tvayaitad devi pūritam ।।
adhyāste devadevasya yogicintyaṃ gadābhṛtaḥ ।। vinaṣṭaprāyam abhavat tvayedānīṃ samedhitam ।। bhavaty etan mahābhāge nityaṃ tvadvīkṣaṇān nṛṇām ।। devi tvaddṛṣṭidṛṣṭānāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ na durlabham ।।
tvayaitad viṣṇunā cāmba jagad vyāptaṃ carācaram ।। mā śarīraṃ kalatraṃ ca tyajethāḥ sarvapāvani ।। tyajethā mama devasya viṣṇor vakṣaḥsthalālaye ।। tyajyante te narāḥ sadyaḥ saṃtyaktā ye tvayāmale ।।
kulaiśvaryaiś ca yujyante puruṣā nirguṇā api ।। sa śūraḥ sa ca vikrānto yas tvayā devi vīkṣitaḥ ।। parāṅmukhī jagaddhātrī yasya tvaṃ viṣṇuvallabhe ।। prasīda devi padmākṣi māsmāṃs tyākṣīḥ kadācana ।।
śṛṇvatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ sarvabhūtasthitā dvija ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣva yas tv iṣṭo varadāhaṃ tavāgatā ।। trailokyaṃ na tvayā tyājyam eṣa me astu varaḥ paraḥ ।। sa tvayā na parityājyo dvitīyo astu varo mama ।।
datto varo mayāyaṃ te stotrārādhanatuṣṭayā ।। māṃ stoṣyati na tasyāhaṃ bhaviṣyāmi parāṅmukhī ।। maitreya śrīr mahābhāgā stotrārādhanatoṣitā ।। devadānavayatnena prasūtāmṛtamanthane ।।
avatāraṃ karoty eṣā tadā śrīs tatsahāyinī ।। yadā tu bhārgavo rāmas tadābhūd dharaṇī tv iyam ।। anyeṣu cāvatāreṣu viṣṇor eṣā sahāyinī ।। viṣṇor dehānurūpāṃ vai karoty eṣātmanas tanum ।।
śriyo na vicyutis tasya gṛhe yāvat kulatrayam ।। alakṣmīḥ kalahādhārā na teṣv āste kadācana ।। kṣīrābdhau śrīr yathā jātā pūrvaṃ bhṛgusutā satī ।। anudinam iha paṭhyate nṛbhir yair vasati na teṣu kadācid apy alakṣmīḥ ।।
bhṛgusargāt prabhṛty eṣa sargo me kathyatāṃ punaḥ ।। tathā dhātṛvidhātārau khyātyāṃ jātau sutau bhṛgoḥ ।। dhātṛvidhātros te bhārye tayor jātau sutāv ubhau ।। tato vedaśirā jajñe prāṇasyāpi sutaṃ śṛṇu ।।
tato vaṃśo mahābhāga vistāraṃ bhārgavo gataḥ ।। virajāḥ parvataś caiva tasya putrau mahātmanaḥ ।। sinīvālī kuhūś caiva rākā cānumatī tathā ।। somaṃ durvāsasaṃ caiva dattātreyaṃ ca yoginam ।।
pūrvajanmani so agastyaḥ smṛtaḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare ।। kṣamā tu suṣuve bhāryā pulahasya prajāpateḥ ।। aṅguṣṭhaparvamātrāṇāṃ jvaladbhāskaratejasām ।। ūrjāyāṃ ca vasiṣṭhasya saptājāyanta vai sutāḥ ।।
sutapāḥ śukra ity ete sarve saptarṣayo amalāḥ ।। tasmāt svāhā sutāṃl lebhe trīn udāraujaso dvija ।। pāvakaṃ pavamānaṃ ca śuciṃ cāpi jalāśinam ।। kathyante vahnayaś caite pitā putratrayaṃ ca yat ।।
evam ekonapañcāśad vahnayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।। agniṣvāttā barhiṣado anagnayaḥ sāgnayaś ca ye ।। te ubhe brahmavādinyau yoginyau cāpy ubhe dvija ।। uttamajñānasaṃpanne sarvaiḥ samuditair guṇaiḥ ।।
śraddhāvān saṃsmarann etām anapatyo na jāyate ।। dvau putrau sumahāvīryau dharmajñau kathitau tava ।। abhīṣṭāyām abhūd brahman pitur atyantavallabhaḥ ।। sa nātiprītimāṃs tasyāṃ tasyāś cābhūd dhruvaḥ sutaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvottamaṃ dhruvaś cakre tam āroḍhuṃ manoratham ।। praṇayenāgataṃ putram utsaṅgārohaṇotsukam ।। svaputraṃ ca tathārūḍhaṃ surucir vākyam abravīt ।। uttamottamam aprāpyam aviveko abhivāñchasi ।।
satyaṃ sutas tvam apy asya kintu na tvaṃ mayā dhṛtaḥ ।। yogyaṃ mamaiva putrasya kim ātmā kliśyate tvayā ।। sunītyām ātmano janma kiṃ tvayā nāvagamyate ।। jagāma kupito mātur nijāyā dvija mandiram ।।
sunītir aṅkam āropya maitreyaitad abhāṣata ।। ko avajānāti pitaraṃ tava yas te aparādhyati ।। suruciḥ prāha bhūpālapratyakṣam atigarvitā ।। śvāsakṣāmekṣaṇā dīnā sunītir vākyam abravīt ।।
na hi puṇyavatāṃ vatsa sapatnair evam ucyate ।। tat ko apahartuṃ śaknoti dātuṃ kaś cākṛtaṃ tvayā ।। tat tvayā nātra kartavyaṃ duḥkhaṃ tadvākyasaṃbhavam ।। yasya puṇyāni tasyaiva matvaitac chāmya putraka ।।
bhāryeti procyate cānyā madvidhā puṇyavarjitā ।। mama putras tathā jātaḥ svalpapuṇyo dhruvo bhavān ।। yasya yāvat sa tenaiva svena tuṣyati buddhimān ।। tat puṇyopacaye yatnaṃ kuru sarvaphalaprade ।।
nimnaṃ yathāpaḥ pravaṇāḥ pātram āyānti saṃpadaḥ ।। naitad durvacasā bhinne hṛdaye mama tiṣṭhati ।। sthānaṃ prāpsyāmy aśeṣāṇāṃ jagatām abhipūjitam ।। prabhāvaṃ paśya me amba tvaṃ dhṛtasyāpi tavodare ।।
sa rājāsanam āpnotu pitrā dattaṃ tathāstu tat ।। icchāmi tad ahaṃ sthānaṃ yan na prāpa pitā mama ।। purāc ca nirgamya tatas tadbāhyopavanaṃ yayau ।। kṛṣṇājinottarīyeṣu viṣṭareṣu samāsthitān ।।
praśrayāvanataḥ samyag abhivādanapūrvakam ।। jātaṃ sunītyāṃ nirvedād yuṣmākaṃ prāptam antikam ।। nirvedakāraṇaṃ kiṃcit tava nādyāpi vidyate ।। na caiveṣṭaviyogādi tava paśyāma bālaka ।।
nirvedaḥ kiṃnimittas te kathyatāṃ yadi vidyate ।। tan niśamya tataḥ procur munayas te parasparam ।। sapatnyā mātur uktasya hṛdayān nāpasarpati ।। kartuṃ vyavasitaṃ tan naḥ kathyatāṃ yadi rocate ।।
tad ucyatāṃ vivakṣus tvam asmābhir upalakṣyase ।। tat sthānam ekam icchāmi bhuktaṃ nānyena yat purā ।। sthānam agryaṃ samastebhyaḥ sthānebhyo munisattamāḥ ।। na hi saṃprāpyate śreṣṭhaṃ tasmād ārādhayācyutam ।।
sa prāpnoty akṣayaṃ sthānam etat satyaṃ mayoditam ।। tam ārādhaya govindaṃ sthānam agryaṃ yadīcchasi ।। tam ārādhya hariṃ yāti muktim apy atidurlabhām ।। tasmiṃs tuṣṭe yad aprāpyaṃ kiṃ tad asti janārdane ।।
prāpa yajñapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ tam ārādhaya suvrata ।। trailokyāntargataṃ sthānaṃ kim u vatsottamottamam ।। kṛṣṇārādhanam evaikaṃ puṃsaḥ sarvaphalapradam ।। sarvair apy evam evoktaṃ tad upāyam abṛhat sate ।।
mayā tatparitoṣāya yaj japtavyaṃ tad ucyatām ।। prasādasumukhās tan me kathayantu maharṣayaḥ ।। kāryam ārādhanaṃ tan no yathāvac chrotum arhasi ।। tasminn eva jagaddhāmni tataḥ kurvīta niścalam ।।
japtavyaṃ yan nibodhaitat tan naḥ pārthivanandana ।। oṃ namo vāsudevāya śuddhajñānasvabhāvine ।। pitāmahas tava purā tasya tuṣṭo janārdanaḥ ।। tathā tvam api govindaṃ toṣayaitat sadā japan ।।
nirjagāma vanāt tasmāt praṇipatya sa tān ṛṣīn ।। madhusaṃjñaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ jagāma yamunātaṭam ।। tato madhuvanaṃ nāmnā khyātam atra mahītale ।। śatrughno madhurāṃ nāma purīṃ yatra cakāra vai ।।
sarvapāpahare tasmiṃs tapas tīrthe cakāra saḥ ।। ātmany aśeṣadeveśaṃ sthitaṃ viṣṇum amanyata ।। sarvabhūtagato vipra sarvabhāvagato abhavat ।। na śaśāka dharā bhāram udvoḍhuṃ bhūtadhāriṇī ।।
dvitīyaṃ ca nanāmārdhaṃ kṣiter dakṣiṇataḥ sthite ।। tadā sā vasudhā vipra cacāla saha parvataiḥ ।। tatkṣobhād amarāḥ kṣobhaṃ paraṃ jagmur mahāmune ।। indreṇa saha saṃmantrya dhyānabhaṅgaṃ pracakramuḥ ।।
samādhibhaṅgam atyantam ārabdhāḥ kartum āturāḥ ।। putreti karuṇāṃ vācam āha māyāmayī tadā ।। nirbandhato mayā labdho bahubhis tvaṃ manorathaiḥ ।। sapatnīvacanād vatsa agates tvaṃ gatir mama ।।
nivartyatāṃ manaḥ kaṣṭān nirbandhāt phalavarjitāt ।। tataḥ samastabhogānāṃ tadante ceṣyate tapaḥ ।। tasmiṃs tvam itthaṃ tapasi kiṃ nāśāyātmano rataḥ ।। anuvartasva mā mohaṃ nivartāsmād adharmataḥ ।।
tyakṣyāmy aham api prāṇāṃs tato vai paśyatas tava ।। samāhitamanā viṣṇau paśyann api na dṛṣṭavān ।। vane abhyudyataśastrāṇi samāyānty apagamyatām ।। abhyudyatograśastrāṇi jvālāmālākulair mukhaiḥ ।।
mumucur dīptaśastrāṇi bhrāmayanto niśācarāḥ ।। trāsāya tasya bālasya yogayuktasya sarvataḥ ।। bhakṣyatāṃ bhakṣyatāṃ cāyam ity ūcus te niśācarāḥ ।। trāsāya rājaputrasya nedus te rajanīcarāḥ ।।
govindāsaktacittasya yayur nendriyagocaram ।। dṛṣṭavān pṛthivīnāthaputro nānyat kathaṃcana ।। saṃkṣobhaṃ paramaṃ jagmus tatparābhavaśaṅkitāḥ ।। śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yātās tapasā tasya tāpitāḥ ।।
dhruvasya tapasā taptās tvāṃ vayaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। tathāyaṃ tapasā deva prayāty ṛddhim aharniśam ।। bhītās tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ yātās tapasas taṃ nivartaya ।। vittapāmbupasomānāṃ sābhilāṣaḥ padeṣu kim ।।
uttānapādatanayaṃ tapasaḥ saṃnivartaya ।। prārthayaty eṣa yaṃ kāmaṃ taṃ karomy akhilaṃ surāḥ ।। nivartayāmy ahaṃ bālaṃ tapasy āsaktamānasam ।। prayayuḥ svāni dhiṣṇyāni śatakratupurogamāḥ ।।
gatvā dhruvam uvācedaṃ caturbhujavapur hariḥ ।। varado aham anuprāpto varaṃ varaya suvrata ।। tuṣṭo ahaṃ bhavatas tena tad vṛṇīṣva varaṃ param ।। unmīlitākṣo dadṛśe dhyānadṛṣṭaṃ hariṃ puraḥ ।।
kirīṭinaṃ samālokya jagāma śirasā mahīm ।। stavāya devadevasya sa cakre mānasaṃ dhruvaḥ ।। ity ākulamatir devaṃ tam eva śaraṇaṃ yayau ।। stotuṃ tad aham icchāmi varam enaṃ prayaccha me ।।
taṃ tvāṃ katham ahaṃ deva stotuṃ śakṣyāmi bālakaḥ ।। stotuṃ pravṛttaṃ tvatpādau tatra prajñāṃ prayaccha me ।। uttānapādatanayaṃ dvijavarya jagatpatiḥ ।। tuṣṭāva praṇato bhūtvā bhūtadhātāram acyutam ।।
bhūtādir ādiprakṛtir yasya rūpaṃ nato asmi tam ।। yasya rūpaṃ namas tasmai puruṣāya guṇātmane ।। buddhyādīnāṃ pradhānasya puruṣasya ca yaḥ paraḥ ।। prapadye śaraṇaṃ śuddhaṃ tvadrūpaṃ parameśvara ।।
tasmai namas te sarvātman yogicintyāvikāravat ।। sarvavyāpī bhuvaḥ sparśād atyatiṣṭhad daśāṅgulam ।। tvatto virāṭ svarāṭ samrāṭ tvattaś cāpy adhipūruṣaḥ ।। tvatto viśvam idaṃ jātaṃ tvatto bhūtabhaviṣyatī ।।
tvatto yajñaḥ sarvahutaḥ pṛṣadājyaṃ paśur dvidhā ।। tvatto yajūṃṣy ajāyanta tvatto aśvāś caikatodataḥ ।। tvanmukhād brāhmaṇā bāhvos tvattaḥ kṣatram ajāyata ।। akṣṇoḥ sūryo anilaḥ prāṇāc candramā manasas tava ।।
diśaḥ śrotrāt kṣitiḥ padbhyāṃ tvattaḥ sarvam abhūd idam ।। saṃyame viśvam akhilaṃ bījabhūte tathā tvayi ।। vistāraṃ ca yathā yāti tvattaḥ sṛṣṭau tathā jagat ।। evaṃ viśvasya nānyas tvaṃ tvatsthāyīśvara dṛśyate ।।
hlādatāpakarī miśrā tvayi no guṇavarjite ।। prabhūtabhūtabhūtāya tubhyaṃ bhūtātmane namaḥ ।। vibhāvyate antaḥkaraṇe puruṣeṣv akṣayo bhavān ।। sarvaṃ tvattas tataś ca tvaṃ namaḥ sarvātmane astu te ।।
kathayāmi tataḥ kiṃ te sarvaṃ vetsi hṛdi sthitam ।। sarvabhūto bhavān vetti sarvasattvamanoratham ।। tapaś ca taptaṃ saphalaṃ yad dṛṣṭo asi jagatpate ।। maddarśanaṃ hi viphalaṃ rājaputra na jāyate ।।
sarvaṃ saṃpadyate puṃsāṃ mayi dṛṣṭipathaṃ gate ।। kim ajñātaṃ tava svāmin manasā yan mayepsitam ।। prārthyate durvinītena hṛdayenātidurlabham ।। tvatprasādaphalaṃ bhuṅkte trailokyaṃ maghavān api ।।
iti garvād avocan māṃ sapatnī mātur uccakaiḥ ।। prārthayāmi prabho sthānaṃ tvatprasādād ato avyayam ।। tvayāhaṃ toṣitaḥ pūrvam anyajanmani bālaka ।। mātāpitroś ca śuśrūṣur nijadharmānupālakaḥ ।।
yauvane akhilabhogāḍhyo darśanīyojjvalākṛtiḥ ।। bhaveyaṃ rājaputro aham iti vāñchā tvayā kṛtā ।। uttānapādasya gṛhe jāto asi dhruva durlabhe ।। anyeṣāṃ tad varaṃ sthānaṃ kule svāyambhuvasya yat ।।
mām ārādhya naro muktim avāpnoty avilambitam ।। bhaviṣyati na saṃdeho matprasādād bhavān dhruva ।। sitārkatanayādīnāṃ sarvarkṣāṇāṃ tathā dhruva ।। sarveṣām upari sthānaṃ tava dattaṃ mayā dhruva ।।
tiṣṭhanti bhavato dattā mayā vai kalpasaṃsthitiḥ ।। vimāne tārakā bhūtvā tāvatkālaṃ nivatsyati ।। kīrtayiṣyanti teṣāṃ ca mahat puṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। tardadhe hariḥ ।।
dhruvo api taṃ namaskṛtya jagāma svapitur gṛham ।। ākarṇyātmajam āyāntaṃ saṃparetaṃ yathāgatam ।। rājānaṃ śraddadhe candra sa candrasya suto mama ।। satyaṃ devarṣiṇā uktam ākarṇya mudito bhavat ।।
vārtā hartur api prītyāṃ hīnaprādrān mahādhanam ।। śaṅkhatūryaninādena brahmaghoṣeṇa bhūyasā ।। niścakrāma purā tūrṇaṃ sadaśvaratham āsthitaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā pavanābhyāse āyāntaṃ tarasā rathāt ।।
avaruhya nṛpaxx dorbhyāṃ x parirebhire ।। athābhinanditaḥ sarvair bandhuvargair dvijottama ।। tenābhivāditāḥ sarve praviveśuḥ saharcix ।। ity uktvā bhagavān īśaḥ tatraivāntaradhīyata ।।
varaṃ prāpya dhruvaṃ sthānam adhyāste sa mahāmatiḥ ।। svayaṃ śuśrūṣaṇād dharmyān mātāpitroś ca vai tathā ।। dvādaśākṣaramāhātmyāt tapasaś ca prabhāvataḥ ।। devāsurāṇām ācāryaḥ ślokam atrośanā jagau ।।
yad enaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā dhruvaṃ saptarṣayaḥ sthitāḥ ।। asyāś ca mahimānaṃ kaḥ śakto varṇayituṃ bhuvi ।। sthānaṃ prāptā paraṃ kṛtvā yā kukṣivivare dhruvam ।। sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate ।।
sarvakalyāṇasaṃyukto dīrghakālaṃ ca jīvati ।। śiṣṭer ādhatta succhāyā pañca putrān akalmaṣān ।। ripor ādhatta bṛhatī cākṣuṣaṃ sarvatejasam ।। prajāpater ātmajāyāṃ vīraṇasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
kanyāyāṃ tapatāṃ śreṣṭha vairājasya prajāpateḥ ।। abhimanyuś ca daśamo naḍvalāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ ।। aṅgaṃ sumanasaṃ khyātiṃ kratum aṅgirasaṃ śibim ।। prajārtham ṛṣayas tasya mamanthur dakṣiṇaṃ karam ।।
vainyo nāma mahīpālo yaḥ pṛthuḥ parikīrtyate ।। yena dugdhā mahī pūrvaṃ prajānāṃ hitakāraṇāt ।। yatra jajñe mahāvīryaḥ sa pṛthur munisattama ।। aṅgasya bhāryā sā dattā tasyāṃ veno vyajāyata ।।
nisargād eva maitreya duṣṭabhāvo vyajāyata ।। ghoṣayām āsa sa tadā pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। bhoktā yajñasya kas tv anyo hy ahaṃ yajñapatiḥ prabhuḥ ।। ūcuḥ sāmakalaṃ samyaṅ maitreya samupasthitāḥ ।।
rājyadehopakārāya prajānāṃ ca hitaṃ param ।। pūjayiṣyāma bhadraṃ te tatrāṃśas te bhaviṣyati ।। asmābhir bhavataḥ kāmān sarvān eva pradāsyati ।। teṣāṃ sarvepsitāvāptiṃ dadāti nṛpa bhūbhṛtām ।।
ko ayaṃ harir iti khyāto yo vai yajñeśvaro mataḥ ।। hutabhug varuṇo dhātā pūṣā bhūmir niśākaraḥ ।। nṛpasyaite śarīrasthāḥ sarvadevamayo nṛpaḥ ।। na dātavyaṃ na hotavyaṃ na yaṣṭavyaṃ ca bho dvijāḥ ।।
mamājñāpālanaṃ dharmo bhavatāṃ ca tathā dvijāḥ ।। haviṣāṃ pariṇāmo ayaṃ yad etad akhilaṃ jagat ।। dharme ca saṃkṣayaṃ yāte kṣīyate cākhilaṃ jagat ।। pāpo dadāti nānujñāṃ tadā proktaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
hanyatāṃ hanyatāṃ pāpa ity ūcus te parasparam ।। vinindaty adhamācāro na sa yogyo bhuvaḥ patiḥ ।। nijaghnur nihataṃ pūrvaṃ bhagavannindanādinā ।। kim etad iti cāsannaṃ papracchus te janaṃ tadā ।।
rāṣṭre tu lokair ārabdhaṃ parasvādānam āturaiḥ ।। sumahān dṛśyate reṇuḥ paravittāpahāriṇām ।। mamanthur ūruṃ putrārtham anapatyasya yatnataḥ ।। dagdhasthūṇāpratīkāśaḥ kharvaṭāsyo atihrasvakaḥ ।।
niṣīdeti tam ūcus te niṣādas tena so abhavat ।। niṣādā muniśārdūla pāpakarmopalakṣaṇāḥ ।। niṣādās te tato jātā venakalmaṣanāśanāḥ ।। tato asya dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ mamanthus te dvijottamāḥ ।।
dīpyamānaḥ svavapuṣā sākṣād agnir iva jvalan ।। śarāś ca divyā nabhasaḥ kavacaṃ ca papāta ha ।। tasmiñ jāte tu bhūtāni saṃprahṛṣṭāni sarvaśaḥ ।। punnāmno narakāt trātaḥ sa tena sumahātmanā ।।
toyāni cābhiṣekārthaṃ sarvāṇy evopatasthire ।। samāgamya tadā vainyam abhyaṣiñcan narādhipam ।। viṣṇor aṃśaṃ pṛthuṃ matvā paritoṣaṃ paraṃ yayau ।। bhavaty avyāhato yasya prabhāvas tridaśair api ।।
so abhiṣikto mahātejā vidhivad dharmakovidaiḥ ।। anurāgāt tatas tasya nāma rājety ajāyata ।। parvatāś ca dadur mārgaṃ dhvajabhaṅgaś ca nābhavat ।। sarvakāmadughā gāvaḥ puṭake puṭake madhu ।।
sūtaḥ sūtyāṃ samutpannaḥ sautye ahani mahāmatiḥ ।। pṛthur evābhavat tasmāt tataḥ pṛthur ajāyata ।। proktau tadā munivarais tāv ubhau sūtamāgadhau ।। karmaitad anurūpaṃ ca pātraṃ stotrasya cāpy ayam ।।
adyajātasya no karma jñāyate asya mahīpateḥ ।। stotraṃ kimāśrayaṃ tv asya kāryam asmābhir ucyatām ।। guṇā bhaviṣyā ye cāsya tair ayaṃ stūyatāṃ nṛpaḥ ।। sadguṇaiḥ ślāghyatām eti stavyāś cābhyāṃ guṇā mama ।।
kariṣyete kariṣyāmi tad evāhaṃ samāhitaḥ ।। tad ahaṃ varjayiṣyāmīty evaṃ cakre matiṃ nṛpaḥ ।। bhaviṣyaiḥ karmabhiḥ samyak susvarau sūtamāgadhau ।। hrīmān maitraḥ kṣamāśīlo vikrānto duṣṭaśāsanaḥ ।।
mānyān mānayitā yajvā brahmaṇyaḥ sādhuvatsalaḥ ।। samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca vyavahārasthitau nṛpaḥ ।। cakāra hṛdi tādṛk ca karmaṇā kṛtavān asau ।। iyāja vividhair yajñair mahadbhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ ।।
tam ūcus tena tāḥ pṛṣṭās tatrāgamanakāraṇam ।। prajāpatiguṇaṃ śūraṃ pṛthuṃ satyaparākramam ।। grastās tataḥ kṣayaṃ yānti prajāḥ sarvāḥ prajeśvara ।। dehi naḥ kṣutparītānāṃ prajānāṃ jīvanauṣadhīḥ ।।
śarāṃś ca divyān kupitaḥ so anvadhāvad vasuṃdharām ।। sā lokān brahmalokādīn saṃtrāsād agaman mahī ।। tatra tatra tu sā vainyaṃ dadṛśe abhyudyatāyudham ।। pravepamānā tadbāṇaparitrāṇaparāyaṇā ।।
yena māṃ hantum atyarthaṃ prakaroṣi nṛpodyamam ।। bahūnāṃ bhavati kṣemaṃ tasya puṇyaprado vadhaḥ ।। ādhāraḥ kaḥ prajānāṃ te nṛpaśreṣṭha bhaviṣyati ।। ātmayogabalenemā dhārayiṣyāmy ahaṃ prajāḥ ।।
pravepitāṅgī paramaṃ sādhvasaṃ samupāgatā ।। tasmād vadāmy upāyaṃ te taṃ kuruṣva yadīcchasi ।। yadīcchasi pradāsyāmi tāḥ kṣīrapariṇāminīḥ ।। taṃ tu vatsaṃ prayaccha tvaṃ kṣareyaṃ yena vatsalā ।।
varauṣadhībījabhūtaṃ vīra sarvatra bhāvaye ।। dhanuṣkoṭyā tadā vainyas tena śailā vivardhitāḥ ।। pravibhāgaḥ purāṇāṃ vā grāmāṇāṃ vā tadābhavat ।। vainyāt prabhṛti maitreya sarvasyaitasya saṃbhavaḥ ।।
tatra tatra prajānāṃ hi nivāsaṃ samarocayat ।। kṛcchreṇa mahatā so api praṇaṣṭāsv oṣadhīṣu vai ।। sasyajātāni sarvāṇi prajānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। tenānnena prajās tāta vartante adyāpi nityaśaḥ ।।
tatas tu pṛthivīsaṃjñām avāpākhiladhāriṇī ।। gandharvair uragair yakṣaiḥ pitṛbhis tarubhis tathā ।। vatsadogdhṛviśeṣāś ca teṣāṃ tadyonayo abhavan ।। sarvasya jagataḥ pṛthvī viṣṇupādatalodbhavā ।।
jajñe mahīpatiḥ pūrvaṃ rājābhūj janarañjanāt ।। na tasya duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcit phaladāyi prajāyate ।। pṛthor janma prabhāvaś ca karoti satataṃ nṛṇām ।। śikhaṇḍinī havirdhānam antardhānād vyajāyata ।।
prācīnabarhiṣaṃ śukraṃ gayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vṛjājinau ।। havirdhānir mahārājo yena saṃvardhitāḥ prajāḥ ।। prācīnabarhir abhavat khyāto bhuvi mahābalaḥ ।। mahatas tapasaḥ pāre savarṇāyāṃ mahīpateḥ ।।
sarve pracetaso nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ ।। daśa varṣasahasrāṇi samudrasalileśayāḥ ।। pracetasaḥ samudrāmbhasy etad ākhyātum arhasi ।। prajāpatiniyuktena bahumānapuraḥsaram ।।
prajāḥ saṃvardhanīyās te mayā coktaṃ tatheti tat ।। kurudhvaṃ mānanīyā ca samyag ājñā prajāpateḥ ।। tathety uktvā ca taṃ bhūyaḥ papracchuḥ pitaraṃ mune ।। bhavema tat samastaṃ naḥ karma vyākhyātum arhasi ।।
sameti nānyathā martyaḥ kim anyat kathayāmi vaḥ ।। ārādhayata govindaṃ yadi siddhim abhīpsatha ।। ārādhanīyo bhagavān anādiḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। tam ārādhyācyutaṃ vṛddhiḥ prajānāṃ vo bhaviṣyati ।।
magnāḥ payodhisalile tapas tepuḥ samāhitāḥ ।। nārāyaṇe muniśreṣṭha sarvalokaparāyaṇe ।। tuṣṭuvur yaḥ stutaḥ kāmān stotur iṣṭān prayacchati ।। cakrus taṃ me muniśreṣṭha supuṇyaṃ vaktum arhasi ।।
tuṣṭuvus tanmayībhūtāḥ samudrasalileśayāḥ ।। tam ādyantam aśeṣasya jagataḥ paramaṃ prabhum ।। jagadbījatayā natvā carurūpavibhāgataḥ ।। śuddharūpapraṇāmeta tuṣṭo viṣṇuḥ pracetasām ।।
yonibhūtam aśeṣasya sthāvarasya carasya ca ।। saṃdhyā ca parameśasya tasmai kālātmane namaḥ ।। jīvabhūtaḥ samastasya tasmai somātmane namaḥ ।। gharmaśītāmbhasāṃ yonis tasmai sūryātmane namaḥ ।।
śabdādisaṃśrayo vyāpī tasmai bhūmyātmane namaḥ ।। tat toyarūpam īśasya namāmo harimedhasaḥ ।। pitṝṇāṃ ca namas tasmai viṣṇave pāvakātmane ।। ākāśayonir bhagavāṃs tasmai vāyvātmane namaḥ ।।
anantamūrtimāñ chuddhas tasmai vyomātmane namaḥ ।। tasmai śabdādirūpāya namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase ।। yas tasmai jñānamūlāya natāḥ sma harimedhase ।। antaḥkaraṇabhūtāya tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ ।।
layasthānaṃ ca yas tasmai namaḥ prakṛtidharmiṇe ।। tam ātmarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ natāḥ sma puruṣottamam ।। natāḥ sma tat paraṃ brahma viṣṇor yat paramaṃ padam ।। asnehacchāyam atanum asaktam asamīraṇam ।।
acakṣuḥśrotram acalam avākpāṇim amānasam ।। abhayaṃ bhrāntirahitam anidram ajarāmaram ।। pūrvāpare na vai yasmiṃs tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। natāḥ sma tat padaṃ viṣṇor jihvādṛggocaraṃ na yat ।।
daśa varṣasahasrāṇi tapaś cerur mahārṇave ।। dadau darśanam unnidranīlotpaladalacchaviḥ ।। praṇipetuḥ śirobhis taṃ bhaktibhārāvanāmitaiḥ ।। prasādasumukho ahaṃ vo varadaḥ samupasthitaḥ ।।
yathā pitrā samādiṣṭaṃ prajānāṃ vṛddhikāraṇam ।। antardhānaṃ jagāmāśu te ca niścakramur jalāt ।। arakṣyamāṇām āvavrur babhūvātha prajākṣayaḥ ।। daśavarṣasahasrāṇi na śekuś ceṣṭituṃ prajāḥ ।।
mukhebhyo vāyum agniṃ ca te asṛjañ jātamanyavaḥ ।। tān agnir adahad ghoras tatrābhūd drumasaṃkṣayaḥ ।। upagamyābravīd etān rājā somaḥ prajāpatīn ।। saṃdhānaṃ vaḥ kariṣyāmi saha kṣitiruhair aham ।।
bhaviṣyaṃ jānatā pūrvaṃ mayā gobhir vivardhitā ।। bhāryā vo astu mahābhāgā dhruvaṃ vaṃśavivardhinī ।। asyām utpatsyate vidvān dakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। agnināgnisamo bhūyaḥ prajāḥ saṃvardhayiṣyati ।।
suramye gomatītīre sa tepe paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। prayuktā kṣobhayām āsa tam ṛṣiṃ sā śucismitā ।। atiṣṭhan mandaradroṇyāṃ viṣayāsaktamānasaḥ ।। prasādasumukho brahmann anujñāṃ dātum arhasi ।।
dināni katicid bhadre sthīyatām ity abhāṣata ।। bubhuje viṣayāṃs tanvī tena sārdhaṃ mahātmanā ।। uktas tayeti sa muniḥ sthīyatām ity abhāṣata ।। yāmīty āha divaṃ brahman praṇayasmitaśobhanam ।।
prāhāsyatāṃ kṣaṇaṃ subhru cirakālaṃ gamiṣyasi ।। śatadvayaṃ kiṃcid ūnaṃ varṣāṇām anvatiṣṭhata ।। proktaḥ proktas tayā tanvyā sthīyatām ity abhāṣata ।। yayau ravaṃ bhayaṃ prema sadbhāvaṃ pūrvanāyake ।।
na muñcaty anyasaktāpi sā jñeyā dakṣiṇā budhaiḥ ।। proktā praṇayabhaṅgārtivedinī na jahau munim ।। navaṃ navam abhūt prema manmathāviṣṭacetasaḥ ।। niṣkrāmantaṃ ca kutreti gamyate prāha sā śubhā ।।
saṃdhyopāstiṃ kariṣyāmi kriyālopo anyathā bhavet ।। kim adya sarvadharmajña parivṛttam ahas tava ।। gatam etan na kurute vismayaṃ kasya kathyatām ।। mayā dṛṣṭā ca tanvaṅgi praviṣṭā ca mamāśramam ।।
kṣaṇe kṣaṇe mayāsūtra praxxddhā nanūttame ।। avahāsaḥ kimartho ayaṃ sadbhāvaḥ kathyatāṃ mama ।। kintv adya tasya kālasya gatāny abdaśatāni te ।। kathyatāṃ bhīru kaḥ kālas tvayā me ramataḥ saha ।।
māsāś ca ṣaṭ tathaivānyat samatītaṃ dinatrayam ।। dinam ekam ahaṃ manye tvayā sārdham ihāsitam ।। viśeṣeṇādya bhavatā pṛṣṭā mārgānuvartinā ।। dhiṅ māṃ dhiṅ mām atīvetthaṃ ninindātmānam ātmanā ।।
hṛto vivekaḥ kenāpi yoṣin mohāya nirmitā ।। matir eṣā hṛtā yena dhik taṃ kāmaṃ mahāgraham ।। kṣuḍtṛxśokamohau ca jarāmṛtyū ṣaḍūrmayaḥ ।। narakagrāmamārgeṇa saṅgenāpahṛtāni me ।।
tām apsarasam āsīnām idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। devarājasya matkṣobhaṃ kurvantyā bhāvaceṣṭitaiḥ ।। satāṃ saptapadaṃ maitram uṣito ahaṃ tvayā saha ।। mamaiva doṣo nitarāṃ yenāham ajitendriyaḥ ।।
tvayā dhik tvāṃ mahāmohamañjūṣāṃ sujugupsitām ।। tāvad galatsvedajalā sā babhūvātivepathuḥ ।। gaccha gaccheti sakrodham uvāca munisattamaḥ ।। ākāśagāminī svedaṃ mamārja tarupallavaiḥ ।।
nirmārjamānā gātrāṇi galatsvedajalāni vai ।। nirjagāma saromāñcasvedarūpī tadaṅgataḥ ।। mayā cāpyāyito gobhiḥ sa tadā vavṛdhe śanaiḥ ।। tāṃ pradāsyanti vo vṛkṣāḥ kopa eṣa praśāmyatām ।।
mamāpatyaṃ tathā vāyoḥ pramlocātanayā ca sā ।। puruṣottamākhyam adrīśaṃ viṣṇor āyatanaṃ yayau ।। ūrdhvabāhur mahāyogī sthitvāsau bhūpanandanāḥ ।। japatā kaṇḍunā devo yenārādhyata keśavaḥ ।।
sa brahmapāraḥ parapārabhūtaḥ paraḥ parāṇām api pārapāraḥ ।। saṃkīrtya tvaṃ triślokyā x prārthanā ca caturthataḥ ।। brahmapārastavenaivaṃ kaṇḍos tuṣṭo acirād dhariḥ ।। kāryeṣu caivaṃ saha karmakartṛ rūpair aśeṣair avatīha sarvam ।।
brahmāvyayaṃ nityam ajaṃ sa viṣṇur apakṣayādyair akhilair asaṅgi ।। tathā rāgādayo doṣāḥ prayāntu praśamaṃ mama ।। avāpa paramāṃ siddhiṃ sa samārādhya keśavam ।। imaṃ stavaṃ yaḥ paṭhati śṛṇuyād vāpi nityaśaḥ ।।
sa kāmadoṣair akhilair muktaḥ prāpnoti vāñchitam ।। yaḥ imaṃ stavaṃ paṭhate śṛṇuyād api nityaśaḥ ।। sa kāmadoṣair akhilair vimukto bhavati dhruvam ।। kāryagauravam etasyāḥ kathane phaladāyi vaḥ ।।
bhūpapatnī mahābhāgā toṣayām āsa bhaktitaḥ ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti śubhāṃ sā ca prāhātmavāñchitam ।। mandabhāgyā samudbhūtā viphalā ca jagatpate ।। tvatprasādāt tathā putraḥ prajāpatisamo astu me ।।
kulaṃ śīlaṃ vayaḥ satyaṃ dākṣiṇyaṃ kṣiprakāritā ।। avisaṃvāditā sattvaṃ vṛddhasevā kṛtajñatā ।। ayonijā ca jāyeyaṃ tvatprasādād adhokṣaja ।। praṇāmanamrām utthāpya varadaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।
prakhyātodārakarmāṇo bhavatyāḥ patayo daśa ।। prajāpatiguṇair yuktaṃ tvam avāpsyasi śobhane ।। trailokyam akhilaṃ sūtis tasya cāpūrayiṣyati ।। manaḥprītikarī nṝṇāṃ matprasādād bhaviṣyasi ।।
sā ceyaṃ māriṣā jātā yuṣmatpatnī nṛpātmajāḥ ।। saṃhṛtya kopaṃ vṛkṣebhyaḥ patnīdharmeṇa māriṣām ।। jajñe dakṣo mahābhāgo yaḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇo abhavat ।। putrān utpādayām āsa prajāsṛṣṭyartham ātmanaḥ ।।
ādeśaṃ brahmaṇaḥ kurvan sṛṣṭyarthaṃ samavasthitaḥ ।। kālasya nayane yuktāḥ saptaviṃśatim indave ।। gandharvāpsarasaś caiva dānavādyāś ca jajñire ।। tapoviśaiṣair iddhānāṃ tadātyantatapasvinām ।।
kathaṃ prācetaso bhūyaḥ sa saṃbhūto mahāmune ।। yad dauhitraś ca somasya punaḥ śvaśuratāṃ gataḥ ।। ṛṣayo atra na muhyanti ye cānye divyacakṣuṣaḥ ।। punaś caiva niruddhyante vidvāṃs tatra na muhyati ।।
tapa eva garīyo abhūt prabhāvaś caiva kāraṇam ।। utpattiṃ vistareṇeha mama brahman prakīrtaya ।। yathā sasarja bhūtāni tathā śṛṇu mahāmate ।। devān ṛṣīn sagandharvān asurān pannagāṃs tathā ।।
tataḥ saṃcintya bahuśaḥ sṛṣṭihetoḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। sutāṃ sutapasā yuktāṃ mahatīṃ lokadhāriṇīm ।। asiknyāṃ janayām āsa sargahetoḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। saṃgamya priyasaṃvādo devarṣir idam abravīt ।।
īdṛśo lakṣyate yatno bhavatāṃ śrūyatām idam ।। antar ūrdhvam adhaś caiva kathaṃ srakṣyatha vai prajāḥ ।। tadā kasmād bhuvo nāntaṃ sarve drakṣyatha bāliśāḥ ।। adyāpi na nivartante samudrebhya ivāpagāḥ ।।
vairiṇyām atha putrāṇāṃ sahasram asṛjat prabhuḥ ।। pūrvoktaṃ vacanaṃ brahman nāradenaiva coditāḥ ।। bhrātṝṇāṃ padavī caiva gantavyā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। jñātvā pramāṇaṃ pṛthvyāś ca prajāḥ srakṣyāmahe tataḥ ।।
adyāpi na nivartante samudrebhya ivāpagāḥ ।। prayāto naśyati tathā tan na kāryaṃ vijānatā ।। krodhaṃ cakre mahābhāgo nāradaṃ sa śaśāpa ca ।। haryaśveṣv atha naṣṭeṣu dakṣaḥ kruddo śapaṃ dvijaḥ ।।
nāradā nāśam eheti garbhavāsaṃ vaseti ca ।। tato dakṣasutāṃ prādāt priyāṃ vai parame dine ।। tasmāt sa nārado jajñe bhūyaḥ śāpabalād ṛṣīn ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ dakṣo asṛjat kanyā vairiṇyām iti naḥ śrutam ।।
saptaviṃśati somāya catasro ariṣṭanemine ।। dve kṛśāśvāya viduṣe tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। dharmapatnyo daśa tv etās tāsv apatyāni me śṛṇu ।। marutvatyā marutvanto vasos tu vasavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
lambāyāś caiva ghoṣo atha nāgavīthī tu jāmijā ।। saṃkalpāyās tu sarvātmā jajñe saṃkalpa eva ca ।। vasavo aṣṭau samākhyātās teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vistaram ।। pratyūṣaś ca prabhāsaś ca vasavo nāmabhiḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
dhruvasya putro bhagavān kālo lokaprakālanaḥ ।। somasya bhagavān varcā varcasvī yena jāyate ।। manoharāyāṃ śiśiraḥ prāṇo atha ravaṇas tathā ।। avijñātagatiś caiva dvau putrāv anilasya tu ।।
tasya śākho viśākhaś ca naigameyaś ca pṛṣṭhajāḥ ।। apatyaṃ kṛttikānāṃ tu kārttikeya iti smṛtaḥ ।। dvau putrau devalasyāpi kṣamāvantau manīṣiṇau ।। prabhāsasya tu bhāryā sā vasūnām aṣṭamasya ha ।।
kartā śilpasahasrāṇāṃ tridaśānāṃ ca vārddhakiḥ ।। manuṣyāś copajīvanti yasya śilpaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। tasya putrāś ca catvāro teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। tvaṣṭuś cāpy ātmajaḥ putro viśvarūpo mahātapāḥ ।।
vṛṣākapiś ca śaṃbhuś ca kapardī raivatas tathā ।। ekādaśaite kathitā rudrās tribhuvaneśvarāḥ ।। śataṃ tv evaṃ samāmnātaṃ rudrāṇām amitaujasām ।। kāśyapasya tu bhāryā yās tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।।
kadrur muniś ca dharmajña tadapatyāni me śṛṇu ।। tuṣitā nāma te anyonyam ūcur vaivasvate antare ।। samavāyīkṛtāḥ sarve samāgamya parasparam ।। manvantare prasūyāmas tan naḥ śreyo bhaved iti ।।
eva svāmin sa pitā caiva mitrāvaruṇa eva ca ।। mārīcāt kaśyapāj jātās te adityā dakṣakanyayā ।। aryamā caiva dhātā ca tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathaiva ca ।। aṃśo bhagaś cātitejā ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।।
vaivasvate antare te vai ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। saptaviṃśati yāḥ proktāḥ somapatnyo atha suvratāḥ ।। b sarvā nakṣatrayoginyas tannāmnaś caiva tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। b dakṣaśāpād yā sapatyāḥ tāsu yakṣagṛhārthite ।।
tāsām apatyāny abhavan dīptāny amitatejasām ।। d ariṣṭanemipatnīnām apatyānīha ṣoḍaśa ।। bahuputrasya viduṣaś catasro vidyutaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। pratyaṅgirasajāḥ śreṣṭhā ṛco brahmarṣisatkṛtāḥ ।।
kṛśāśvasya tu devarṣer devapraharaṇāḥ sutāḥ ।। teṣām apīha satataṃ nirodhotpattir ucyate ।। evaṃ devanikāyās te saṃbhavanti yuge yuge ।। hiraṇyakaśipuś caiva hiraṇyākṣaś ca durjayaḥ ।।
siṃhikā cābhavat kanyā vipracitteḥ parigrahaḥ ।। saṃhlādaś ca mahāvīryā daityavaṃśavivardhanāḥ ।। prahlādaḥ paramāṃ bhaktiṃ ya uvāha janārdane ।। prahlādavan nṛsiṃhaikabhaktibhāvāya dehinām ।।
āvahac chravaṇautsukyaṃ tatprabhāvam asūcayat ।। na dadāha ca yaṃ pūrvaṃ vāsudeve hṛdi sthite ।। cacāla sakalā yasya pāśabaddhasya dhīmataḥ ।। śarīram adrikaṭhinaṃ sarvatrācyutacetasaḥ ।।
nāntāya sarpapatayo babhūvur urutejasaḥ ।। tatyāja nātmanaḥ prāṇān viṣṇusmaraṇadaṃśitaḥ ।। dadhāra daityapatinā kṣiptaṃ svarganivāsinā ।। avāpa saṃkṣayaṃ sadyaś cittasthe madhusūdane ।।
yasya vakṣaḥsthale prāptā daityendrapariṇāmitāḥ ।। babhūva nāntāya purā govindāsaktacetasaḥ ।। yasmin prayuktaṃ cakreṇa kṛṣṇasya vitathīkṛtam ।। jarayām āsa matimān avikāram amatsarī ।।
yathātmani tathānyatra paraṃ maitraguṇānvitaḥ ।। upamānam aśeṣāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ yaḥ sadābhavat ।। kāraṇaṃ cāsya jagato viṣṇur eva sanātanaḥ ।। dadāha nāgnir nāstraiś ca kṣuṇṇas tatyāja jīvitam ।।
bandhabaddho api calati vikṣiptāṅgaiḥ samāhatā ।। tvayaivātīva māhātmyaṃ kathitaṃ yasya dhīmataḥ ।। śrotum icchāmi yasyaitac caritaṃ tv amitaujasaḥ ।। kimarthaṃ cābdhisalile nikṣipto dharmatatparaḥ ।।
kṣiptaḥ kim adriśikharāt kiṃ vā pāvakasaṃcaye ।। saṃśoṣako anilaś cāsya prayuktaḥ kiṃ mahāsuraiḥ ।। śambaraś cāpi māyānāṃ sahasraṃ kiṃ prayuktavān ।। kasmād dattaṃ vināśāya yaj jīrṇaṃ tena dhīmatā ।।
caritaṃ śrotum icchāmi mahāmāhātmyasūcakam ।। ananyamanaso viṣṇau kaḥ samartho nipātane ।। svavaṃśaprabhavair daityaiḥ kartuṃ dveṣo atiduṣkaraḥ ।। daiteyaiḥ prahṛtaṃ kasmāt tan mamākhyātum arhasi ।।
guṇaiḥ samanvite sādhau kiṃ punar yaḥ svapakṣajaḥ ।। daityeśvarasya caritaṃ śrotum icchāmy aśeṣataḥ ।। prahlādasya sadodāracaritasya mahātmanaḥ ।। trailokyaṃ vaśam āninye brahmaṇo varadarpitaḥ ।।
vāyur agnir apāṃ nāthaḥ somaś cāsīn mahāsuraḥ ।। yajñabhāgān aśeṣāṃs tu sa svayaṃ bubhuje asuraḥ ।। vicerur avanau sarve bibhrāṇā mānuṣīṃ tanum ।। udgīyamāno gandharvair bubhuje viṣayān priyān ।।
upāsāṃ cakrire sarve siddhagandharvapannagāḥ ।। daityeśvarasya purataś cakruḥ siddhā mudānvitāḥ ।। papau pānaṃ mudā yuktaḥ prāsāde sumanohare ।। papāṭha bālapāṭhyāni gurugehaṃ gato arbhakaḥ ।।
pānāsaktasya purataḥ pitur daityapates tadā ।। hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prāha prahlādam amitaujasam ।। kālenaitāvatā yat te sadodyuktena śikṣitam ।। samāhitamanā bhūtvā yan me cetasy avasthitam ।।
praṇato asmy antasaṃtānaṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।। vilokya tadguruṃ prāha sphuritādharapallavaḥ ।। asāraṃ grāhito bālo mām avajñāya durmate ।। mamopadeśajanitaṃ nāyaṃ vadati te sutaḥ ।।
mayopadiṣṭaṃ nety eṣa prabravīti gurus tava ।। tam ṛte paramātmānaṃ tāta kaḥ kena śāsyate ।। jagatām īśvarasyeha purataḥ prasabhaṃ mama ।। yato yaś ca svayaṃ viśvaṃ sa viṣṇuḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।
tavāsti martukāmas tvaṃ prabravīṣi punaḥ punaḥ ।। dhātā vidhātā parameśvaraś ca prasīda kopaṃ kuruṣe kimartham ।। yenedṛśāny asādhūni vadaty āviṣṭamānasaḥ ।। sa māṃ tvadādīṃś ca pitaḥ samastān samastaceṣṭāsu yunakti sarvagaḥ ।।
yojito durmatiḥ kena vipakṣavitathastutau ।। jagrāha vidyām aniśaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇodyataḥ ।। samāhūyābravīd gāthā kācit putraka gīyatām ।। kāraṇaṃ sakalasyāsya sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।।
svapakṣahānikartṛtvād yaḥ kulāṅgāratāṃ gataḥ ।। udyatās tasya nāśāya daityāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ।। daiteyās tena satyena mā krāmantv āyudhāni vaḥ ।। nāvāpa vedanām alpām abhūc caiva punar navaḥ ।।
abhayaṃ te prayacchāmi mātimūḍhamatir bhava ।। bhayaṃ bhayānām apahāriṇi sthite manasy anante mama kutra tiṣṭhati । yasmin smṛte janmajarāntakādi bhayāni sarvāṇy apayānti tāta ।। viṣajvālāvilair vaktraiḥ sadyo nayata saṃkṣayam ।।
adaṃśanta samasteṣu gātreṣv ativiṣolbaṇāḥ ।। na vivedātmano gātraṃ tatsmṛtyāhlādasaṃsthitaḥ ।। nāsya tvacaḥ svalpam apīha bhinnaṃ praśādhi daityeśvara karma cānyat ।। tajjā vināśāya bhavanti tasya yathāraṇeḥ prajvalito hutāśaḥ ।।
pātito dharaṇīpṛṣṭhe viṣāṇair apy apīḍyata ।। śīrṇā vakṣaḥsthalaṃ prāpya sa prāha pitaraṃ tataḥ ।। mahāvipatpāpavināśano ayaṃ janārdanānusmaraṇānubhāvaḥ ।। vāyo samedhayāgniṃ tvaṃ dahyatām eṣa pāpakṛt ।।
prajvālya dānavā vahniṃ dadahuḥ svāmicoditāḥ ।। paśyāmi padmāstaraṇāstṛtāni śītāni sarvāṇi diśāṃ mukhāni ।। alaṃ kariṣṇuṃ tv asahiṣṇum itthaṃ sthāṇuṃ sadā staumi sadā sadaiva ।। purohitā mahātmānaḥ sāmnā saṃstūya vāgminaḥ ।।
kopo devanikāyeṣu tatra te saphalo yataḥ ।। tataḥ purohitair ukto hiraṇyakaśipuḥ svakaiḥ ।। yathā vipakṣanāśāya vinītas te bhaviṣyati ।। tato atra kopam atyarthaṃ yoktum arhasi nārbhake ।।
tataḥ kṛtyāṃ vadhāyāsya kariṣyāmo anivartinīm ।। daityair niṣkrāmayām āsa putraṃ pāvakasaṃcayāt ।। adhyāpayām āsa muhur upadeśāntare guroḥ ।। na cānyathaitan mantavyaṃ nātra lobhādikāraṇam ।।
avyāhataiva bhavati tato anudivasaṃ jarā ।। pratyakṣaṃ dṛśyate caitad asmākaṃ bhavatāṃ tathā ।। āgamo ayaṃ tathā tac ca nopādānaṃ vinodbhavaḥ ।। samastāvasthakaṃ tāvad duḥkham evāvagamyatām ।।
manyate bālabuddhitvād duḥkham eva hi tat punaḥ ।। bhrāntijñānavatāṃ puṃsāṃ prahāro api sukhāyate ।। kva cāṅgaśobhāsaurabhyakamanīyādayo guṇāḥ ।। dehe cet prītimān mūḍho bhavitā narake api saḥ ।।
kriyate sukhakartṛtvaṃ tadvilomasya cetaraiḥ ।। tāvanmātraṃ sa evāsya duḥkhaṃ cetasi yacchati ।। tāvanto asya nikhanyante hṛdaye śokaśaṅkavaḥ ।। nāśadāhāpaharaṇaṃ kutas tatraiva tiṣṭhati ।।
yātanāsu yamasyograṃ garbhasaṃkramaṇeṣu ca ।। yadi tat kathyatām evaṃ sarvaṃ duḥkhamayaṃ jagat ।। bhavatāṃ kathyate satyaṃ viṣṇur ekaḥ parāyaṇaḥ ।। jarāyauvanajanmādyā dharmā dehasya nātmanaḥ ।।
yuvāhaṃ vārddhake prāpte kariṣyāmy ātmano hitam ।। kiṃ kariṣyāmi mandātmā samarthena na yat kṛtam ।। śreyaso abhimukhaṃ yāti na kadācit pipāsitaḥ ।। ajñānayanty aśaktyā ca vārddhakaṃ samupasthitam ।।
bālyayauvanavṛddhādyair dehabhāvair asaṃyutaḥ ।। tad asmatprītaye viṣṇuḥ smaryatāṃ bandhamuktidaḥ ।। pāpakṣayaś ca bhavati smaratāṃ tam aharniśam ।। bhavatāṃ jāyatām evaṃ sarvakleśān prahāsyatha ।।
tadā śocyeṣu bhūteṣu dveṣaṃ prājñaḥ karoti kaḥ ।। mudaṃ tathāpi kurvīta hānir dveṣaphalaṃ yataḥ ।। śocyāny aho atimohena vyāptānīti manīṣiṇām ।। kṛtvābhyupagamaṃ tatra saṃkṣepaḥ śrūyatāṃ mama ।।
draṣṭavyam ātmavat tasmād abhedena vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। tathā yatnaṃ kariṣyāmo yathā prāpsyāma nirvṛtim ।। parjanyavaruṇābhyāṃ vā na siddhair na ca rākṣasaiḥ ।। na manuṣyair na paśubhir doṣair naivātmasaṃbhavaiḥ ।।
dveṣerṣyāmatsarādyair vā rāgalobhādibhiḥ kṣayam ।। tām āpnoty amale nyasya keśave hṛdayaṃ naraḥ ।। sarvatra daityāḥ samatām upeta samatvam ārādhanam acyutasya ।। samāśritād brahmataror anantān niḥsaṃśayaṃ prāpsyatha vai mahat phalam ।।
ācacakṣuḥ sa covāca sūdān āhūya satvaraḥ ।। kumārgadeśiko duṣṭo hanyatām avilambitam ।। avijñātam asau pāpo vadhyatāṃ mā vicāryatām ।। viṣadānaṃ yathājñaptaṃ pitrā tasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
abhimantrya sahānnena maitreya bubhuje tadā ।। anantakhyātinirvīryaṃ jarayām āsa durviṣam ।। daityeśvaram upāgamya praṇipatyedam abruvan ।। jīrṇaṃ tac ca sahānnena prahlādena sutena te ।।
kṛtyāṃ tasya vināśāya utpādayata mā ciram ।। sāmapūrvam athocus te prahlādaṃ vinayānvitam ।। daityarājasya tanayo hiraṇyakaśipor bhavān ।। pitā samastalokānāṃ tvaṃ tathaiva bhaviṣyasi ।।
vācyaḥ pitā samastānāṃ gurūṇāṃ paramo guruḥ ।। marīceḥ sakale apy asmin trailokye nānyathā vadet ।। etad apy avagacchāmi satyam atrāpi nānṛtam ।। yad uktaṃ bhrāntis tatrāpi svalpāpi hi na vidyate ।।
tatrāpi nāparādhyāmīty evaṃ manasi me sthitam ।। ko bravīti yathāyuktaṃ kiṃ tu naitad vaco arthavat ।। prahasya ca punaḥ prāha kim anantena sādhv iti ।। śrūyatāṃ yad anantena yadi khedaṃ na yāsyatha ।।
catuṣṭayam idaṃ yasmāt tasmāt kiṃ kim idaṃ vṛthā ।। dharmaḥ prāptas tathaivānyair arthaḥ kāmas tathāparaiḥ ।। avāpur muktim apare puruṣā dhvastabandhanāḥ ।। vimukteś caikato labhyaṃ mūlam ārādhanaṃ hareḥ ।।
tenāpi hi kim ity evam anantena kim ucyate ।। vadantu sādhu vāsādhu viveko asmākam alpakaḥ ।। bahunātra kim uktena sa eva jagataḥ patiḥ ।। sa kartā ca vikartā ca saṃhartā ca hṛdi sthitaḥ ।।
sa bhoktā bhojyam apy evaṃ sa eva jagadīśvaraḥ ।। bhavadbhir etat kṣantavyaṃ bālyād uktaṃ tu yan mayā ।। bhūyo na vakṣyasīty evaṃ naivaṃ jñāto asy abuddhimān ।। tataḥ kṛtyāṃ vināśāya tava sṛkṣyāma durmate ।।
hanti rakṣati caivātmā jagat sarvaṃ carācaram ।। karmaṇā jāyate sarvaṃ karmaiva gatisādhanam ।। tasmāt sarvaprayatnena sādhu karma samācaret ।। kṛtyām utpādayām āsur jvālāmālojjvalānanām ।।
śūlena sā susaṃkruddhā taṃ jaghānātha vakṣasi ।। jagāma khaṇḍitaṃ bhūmau tatrāpi śatadhābhavat ।। bhaṅgo bhavati vajrasya tatra śūlasya kā kathā ।। tān eva sā jaghānāśu kṛtyā nāśaṃ jagāma ca ।।
trāhi kṛṣṇety ananteti vadann abhyavapadyata ।। trāhi viprān imān asmād duḥsahān mantrapāvakāt ।। viṣṇur eva tathā sarve jīvantv ete purohitāḥ ।। cintayāmy aripakṣe api jīvantv ete tathā dvijāḥ ।।
yair diggajair ahaṃ kṣuṇṇo daṣṭaḥ sarpaiś ca yair aham ।। yathā tenādya satyena jīvantv asurayājakāḥ ।। samuttasthur dvijā bhūyas taṃ cocuḥ praśrayānvitam ।। putrapautradhanaiśvaryair yukto vatsa bhavottamaḥ ।।
daityarājāya sakalam ācacakṣur mahāmune ।। āhūya putraṃ papraccha prabhāvasyāsya kāraṇam ।। etan mantrādijanitam utāho sahajaṃ tava ।। praṇipatya pituḥ pādāv idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।।
prabhāva eṣa sāmānyo yasya yasyācyuto hṛdi ।। tasya pāpāgamas tāta hetvabhāvān na vidyate ।। tad bījaṃ janma phalati prabhūtaṃ tasya cāśubham ।। cintayan sarvabhūtastham ātmany api ca keśavam ।।
sarvatra śubhacittasya tasya me jāyate kutaḥ ।। kartavyā paṇḍitair jñātvā sarvabhūtamayaṃ harim ।। krodhāndhakāritamukhaḥ prāha daiteyakiṃkarān ।। giripṛṣṭhe patatv asmiñ śilābhinnāṅgasaṃhatiḥ ।।
papāta so apy adhaḥ kṣipto hṛdayenodvahan harim ।। bhaktiyuktaṃ dadhārainam upagamya ca medinī ।। hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prāha śambaraṃ māyināṃ varam ।। māyāṃ vetti bhavāṃs tasmān māyayainaṃ niṣūdaya ।।
sahasram atra māyānāṃ paśya koṭiśataṃ tathā ।। vināśam icchan durbuddhiḥ sarvatra samadarśini ।। maitreya so api prahlādaḥ sasmāra madhusūdanam ।। ājagāma samājñaptaṃ jvālāmāli sudarśanam ।।
bālasya rakṣatā deham ekaikaśyena sūditam ।। śīghram eṣa mamādeśād durātmā nīyatāṃ kṣayam ।। śīto atirūkṣaḥ śoṣāya taddehasyātiduḥsahaḥ ।। hṛdayena mahātmānaṃ dadhāra dharaṇīdharam ।।
papau janārdanaḥ kruddhaḥ sa yayau pavanaḥ kṣayam ।। jagāma so api bhavanaṃ guror eva mahāmatiḥ ।। grāhayām āsa taṃ bālaṃ rājñām uśanasā kṛtām ।। mene tadainaṃ tatpitre kathayām āsa śikṣitam ।।
prahlādas tattvato vetti bhārgaveṇa yad īritam ।। prahlāda triṣu kāleṣu madhyastheṣu kathaṃ caret ।। cāreṣu pauravargeṣu śaṅkiteṣv itareṣu ca ।। prahlāda kathyatāṃ samyak tathā kaṇṭakaśodhanam ।।
tathā me kathyatāṃ jñātuṃ tavecchāmi manogatam ।। prahlādaḥ prāha daityendraṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ sthitaḥ ।। gṛhītaṃ ca mayā kintu na sad etan mataṃ mama ।। upāyāḥ kathitā hy ete mitrādīnāṃ ca sādhane ।।
sādhyābhāve mahābāho sādhanaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam ।। paramātmani govinde mitrāmitrakathā kutaḥ ।। yatas tato ayaṃ mitraṃ me śatruś ceti pṛthak kutaḥ ।। avidyāntargatair yatnaḥ kartavyas tāta śobhane ।।
bālo agniṃ kiṃ na khadyotam asureśvara manyate ।। āyāsāyāparaṃ karma vidyānyā śilpanaipuṇam ।। niśāmaya mahābhāga praṇipatya bravīmi yat ।। tathāpi bhāvyam evaitad ubhayaṃ prāpyate naraiḥ ।।
tathāpi puṃsāṃ bhāgyāni nodyamā bhūtihetavaḥ ।। bhāgyabhojyāni rājyāni santy anītimatām api ।। yatitavyaṃ samatve ca nirvāṇam api cecchatā ।। rūpam etad anantasya viṣṇor bhinnam iva sthitam ।।
draṣṭavyam ātmavad viṣṇur yato ayaṃ viśvarūpadhṛk ।। prasīdaty acyutas tasmin prasanne kleśasaṃkṣayaḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipuḥ putraṃ padā vakṣasy atāḍayat ।। niṣpiṣya pāṇinā pāṇiṃ hantukāmo jagad yathā ।।
nāgapāśair dṛḍhaṃ baddhvā kṣipyatāṃ mā vilambatha ।। anuyāsyanti mūḍhasya matam asya durātmanaḥ ।। stutiṃ karoti duṣṭānāṃ vadha evopakārakaḥ ।। bhartur ājñāṃ puraskṛtya cikṣipuḥ salilārṇave ।।
udvelo abhūt paraṃ kṣobham upetya ca samantataḥ ।। hiraṇyakaśipur daityān idam āha mahāmune ।। niśchidraiḥ sarvataḥ sarvaiś cīyatām eṣa durmatiḥ ।। kṣayaṃ nīto na vātena na viṣeṇa na kṛtyayā ।।
bālo atiduṣṭacitto ayaṃ nānenārtho asti jīvatā ।। tiṣṭhatv abdasahasrāntaṃ prāṇān hāsyati durmatiḥ ।। ākramya cayanaṃ cakrur yojanāni sahasraśaḥ ।। tuṣṭāvāhnikavelāyām ekāgramatir acyutam ।।
namas te sarvalokātman namas te tigmacakriṇe ।। jagaddhitāya kṛṣṇāya govindāya namo namaḥ ।। rudrarūpāya kalpānte namas tubhyaṃ trimūrtaye ।। piśācā rākṣasāś caiva manuṣyāḥ paśavas tathā ।।
bhūmyāpo agnir nabho vāyuḥ śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rasaḥ ।। eteṣāṃ paramārthaś ca sarvam etat tvam acyuta ।। pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca karma vedoditaṃ bhavān ।। tvam eva viṣṇo sarvāṇi sarvakarmaphalaṃ ca yat ।।
tavaiva vyāptir aiśvaryaguṇasaṃsūcikī prabho ।। havyakavyabhug ekas tvaṃ pitṛdevasvarūpadhṛk ।। rūpāṇi sūkṣmāṇi ca bhūtabhedās teṣv antar ātmākhyam atīva sūkṣmam ।। kim apy acintyaṃ tava rūpam asti tasmai namas te puruṣottamāya ।।
guṇāśrayā namas tasyai śāśvatāyai sureśvara ।। jñānijñānaparicchedyā tāṃ vande ceśvarīṃ parām ।। vyatiriktaṃ na yasyāsti vyatirikto akhilasya yaḥ ।। nāmarūpaṃ na yasyaiko yo astitvenopalabhyate ।।
apaśyantaḥ paraṃ rūpaṃ namas tasmai mahātmane ।। taṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ viṣṇuṃ namasye parameśvaram ।। dhyeyaḥ sa jagatām ādyaḥ sa prasīdatu me avyayaḥ ।। ādhārabhūtaḥ sarvasya sa prasīdatu me hariḥ ।।
yatra sarvaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ yaḥ sarvaṃ sarvataś ca yaḥ ।। mattaḥ sarvam ahaṃ sarvaṃ mayi sarvaṃ sanātane ।। brahmasaṃjño aham evāgre tathānte ca paraḥ pumān ।। tanmayatvam avāpāgryaṃ mene cātmānam acyutam ।।
aham evāvyayo anantaḥ paramātmety acintayat ।। śuddhe antaḥkaraṇe viṣṇus tasthau jñānamayo acyutaḥ ।। calaty uragabandhais tair maitreya truṭitaṃ kṣaṇāt ।। cacāla ca mahī sarvā saśailavanakānanā ।।
prakṣipya tasmāt salilān niścakrāma mahāmatiḥ ।। prahlādo asmīti sasmāra punar ātmānam ātmanā ।। ekāgramatir avyagro yatavākkāyamānasaḥ ।। vyaktāvyakta kalātīta sakaleśa nirañjana ।।
mūrtāmūrta mahāmūrte sūkṣmamūrte sphuṭāsphuṭa ।। sadasadrūpasadbhāva sadasadbhāvabhāvana ।। ekāneka namas tubhyaṃ vāsudevādikāraṇa ।। viśvaṃ yataś caitad aviśvahetor namo astu tasmai puruṣottamāya ।।
āvirbabhūva bhagavān pītāmbaradharo hariḥ ।। namo astu viṣṇavaity etad vyājahārāsakṛd dvija ।। avalokanadānena bhūyo māṃ pāvayāvyaya ।। yathābhilaṣito mattaḥ prahlāda vriyatāṃ varaḥ ।।
teṣu teṣv acyutā bhaktir acyutāstu sadā tvayi ।। tvām anusmarataḥ sā me hṛdayān māpasarpatu ।। varaś ca mattaḥ prahlāda vriyatāṃ yas tavepsitaḥ ।। matpitus tatkṛtaṃ pāpaṃ deva tasya praṇaśyatu ।।
daṃśitaś coragair dattaṃ yad viṣaṃ mama bhojane ।। anyāni cāpy asādhūni yāni pitrā kṛtāni me ।। tvatprasādāt prabho sadyas tena mucyeta me pitā ।। anyaṃ ca te varaṃ dadmi vriyatām asurātmaja ।।
bhavitrī tvatprasādena bhaktir avyabhicāriṇī ।। samastajagatāṃ mūle yasya bhaktiḥ sthirā tvayi ।। tathā tvaṃ matprasādena nirvāṇaṃ param āpsyasi ।। sa cāpi punar āgamya vavande caraṇau pituḥ ।।
jīvasīty āha vatseti bāṣpārdranayano dvija ।। gurupitroś cakāraivaṃ śuśrūṣāṃ so api dharmavit ।। viṣṇunā so api daityānāṃ maitreyābhūt patis tataḥ ।। putrapautrāṃś ca subahūn avāpyaiśvaryam eva ca ।।
tadāsau bhagavaddhyānāt paraṃ nirvāṇam āptavān ।। prahlādo bhagavadbhakto yaṃ tvaṃ mām anupṛcchasi ।। śṛṇoti tasya pāpāni sadyo gacchanti saṃkṣayam ।। śṛṇvan paṭhaṃś ca maitreya vyapohati na saṃśayaḥ ।।
dvādaśyāṃ vā tad āpnoti gopradānaphalaṃ dvija ।। tathā rakṣati yas tasya śṛṇoti caritaṃ sadā ।। karuṇaṃ caraṇānamre cāruṇaṃ praṇatadruhi ।। prahlādavaradaṃ vande nṛsiṃhaghṛṇibhīṣaṇaṃ ।।
virocanas tu prāhlādir balir jajñe virocanāt ।। hiraṇyākṣasutāś cāsan sarva eva mahābalāḥ ।। mahānābho mahābāhuḥ kālanābhas tathāparaḥ ।। ayomukhaḥ śaṅkuśirāḥ kapilaḥ śambaras tathā ।।
svarbhānur vṛṣaparvā ca pulomā ca mahābalaḥ ।। ete danoḥ sutāḥ khyātā vipracittiś ca vīryavān ।। upadānavī hayaśirāḥ prakhyātā varakanyakāḥ ।। ubhe te tu mahābhāge mārīces tu parigrahaḥ ।।
paulomāḥ kālakeyāś ca mārīcatanayāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। siṃhikāyām athotpannā vipracitteḥ sutās tathā ।। vātāpir namuciś caiva ilvalaḥ khasṛmas tathā ।। svarbhānuś ca mahāvīryo vaktrayodhī mahāsuraḥ ।।
eteṣāṃ putrapautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। samutpannāḥ sumahatā tapasā bhāvitātmanaḥ ।। śukī śyenī ca bhāsī ca sugrīvī śucigṛdhrikā ।। śyenī śyenāṃs tathā bhāsī bhāsān gṛddhrāṃś ca gṛddhry api ।।
aśvān uṣṭrān gardabhāṃś ca tāmrāvaṃśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। suparṇaḥ patatāṃ śreṣṭho dāruṇaḥ pannagāśanaḥ ।। anekaśirasāṃ brahman khecarāṇāṃ mahātmanām ।। suparṇavaśagā brahmañ jajñire naikamastakāḥ ।।
śaṅkhaśveto mahāpadmaḥ kambalāśvatarāv ubhau ।। ete cānye ca bahavo dandaśūkā viṣolbaṇāḥ ।। sthalajāḥ pakṣiṇo abjāś ca dāruṇāḥ piśitāśanāḥ ।। krodhāt tu janayām āsa piśācāṃś ca mahābalān ।।
irāvṛkṣalatāvallīs tṛṇajātīś ca sarvaśaḥ ।। ariṣṭā tu mahāsattvān gandharvān samajījanat ।। teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। vaivasvate ca mahati vāruṇe vitate kratau ।।
pūrvaṃ yatra tu saptarṣīn utpannān sapta mānasān ।। gandharvabhogidevānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca sattama ।। tayā cārādhitaḥ samyak kaśyapas tapatāṃ varaḥ ।। putram indravadhārthāya samartham amitaujasam ।।
dattvā ca varam avyagraḥ kaśyapas tām uvāca ha ।। śakraṃ putro nihantā te yadi garbhaṃ śaracchatam ।। b saṃdhyāyāṃ naiva bhoktavyaṃ garbhiṇyā varavarṇini ।। b na sthātavyaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ vṛkṣamūleṣu sarvadā ।। b
samāhitātiprayatā śucinī dhārayiṣyasi ।। d dadhāra sā ca taṃ garbhaṃ samyak chaucasamanvitā ।। śuśrūṣus tām athāgacchad vinayād amarādhipaḥ ।। ūne varṣaśate cāsyā dadarśāntaram ātmavān ।।
nidrām āhārayām āsa tasyāḥ kukṣiṃ praviśya saḥ ।। sa pāṭyamāno vajreṇa prarurodātidāruṇam ।। so abhavat saptadhā garbhas tam indraḥ kupitaḥ punaḥ ।। maruto nāma devās te babhūvur ativeginaḥ ।।
devā ekonapañcāśat sahāyā vajrapāṇinaḥ ।। tataḥ krameṇa rājyāni dadau lokapitāmahaḥ ।। somaṃ rājye adadhad brahmā yajñānāṃ tapasām api ।। ādityānāṃ patiṃ viṣṇuṃ vasūnām atha pāvakam ।।
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca prahlādam adhipaṃ dadau ।। marutāṃ ditiputrāṇāṃ vāsavam adhipaṃ dadau ।। airāvataṃ gajendrāṇām aśeṣāṇāṃ patiṃ dadau ।। uccaiḥśravasam aśvānāṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tu gavām api ।।
himālayaṃ sthāvaraṇāṃ munīnāṃ kapilaṃ munim ।। śeṣaṃ tu nāgarājānaṃ mṛgāṇāṃ siṃham īśvaram ।। b mṛgāṇām api sarveṣāṃ rājye siṃhaṃ dadau vibhuḥ ।। b kravyādānāṃ daṃṣṭriṇāṃ ca mṛgāṇāṃ vyāghram īśvaram ।। b
vanaspatīnāṃ rājānaṃ plakṣam evābhyaṣecayat ।। d evaṃ vibhajya jātīnāṃ prādhānyenākarot prabhūn ।। prajāpatipatir brahmā sthāpayām āsa sarvataḥ ।। diśāpālaṃ sudhanvānaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।।
putraṃ śaṅkhapadaṃ nāma rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। ketumantaṃ mahātmānaṃ rājānam abhiṣiktavān ।। udīcyāṃ diśi durdharṣaṃ rājānaṃ so abhyaṣecayat ।। yathāpradeśam adyāpi dharmataḥ paripālyate ।।
vibhūtibhūtā rājāno ye cānye munisattama ।। te sarve sarvabhūtasya viṣṇor aṃśā dvijottama ।। dānavānāṃ ca ye nāthā ye nāthāḥ piśitāśinām ।। manuṣyāṇāṃ ca sarpāṇāṃ nāgānāṃ cādhipās tu ye ।।
te sarve sarvabhūtasya viṣṇor aṃśasamudbhavāḥ ।। sthitau sthitaṃ mahāprājña bhavaty anyasya kasyacit ।। hanti caivāntakatve ca rajaḥsattvādisaṃśrayaḥ ।। pralayaṃ ca karoty ante caturbhedo janārdanaḥ ।।
marīcimiśrāḥ patayaḥ prajānām anyabhāgataḥ ।। itthaṃ caturdhā saṃsṛṣṭau vartate asau rajoguṇaḥ ।। manvādirūpī cānyena kālarūpo apareṇa ca ।। sattvaṃ guṇaṃ samāśritya jagataḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।।
rudrasvarūpī bhagavān ekāṃśena bhavaty ajaḥ ।। kālasvarūpo bhāgo anyaḥ sarvabhūtāni cāparaḥ ।। vibhāgakalpanā brahman kathyate sārvakālikī ।। vibhūtayo harer etā jagataḥ sṛṣṭihetavaḥ ।।
sthiter nimittabhūtasya viṣṇor etā vibhūtayaḥ ।। caturdhā pralayāyaitā janārdanavibhūtayaḥ ।। dhātrā marīcimiśraiś ca kriyate jantubhis tathā ।। utpādayanty apatyāni jantavaś ca pratikṣaṇam ।।
na prajāpatayaḥ sarve na caivākhilajantavaḥ ।। caturdhā devadevasya maitreya pralaye tathā ।। tasya sṛjyasya saṃbhūtau tat sarvaṃ vai hares tanuḥ ।। janārdanasya tad raudraṃ maitreyāntakaraṃ vapuḥ ।।
jagadbhakṣayitā devaḥ samastasya janārdanaḥ ।। guṇapravṛttyā paramaṃ padaṃ tasyāguṇaṃ mahat ।। catuṣprakāraṃ tad api svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।। tvām ācakṣva yathānyāyaṃ yad uktaṃ paramaṃ padam ।।
sādhyaṃ ca vastv abhimataṃ yat sādhayitum ātmanaḥ ।। sādhyaṃ ca paramaṃ brahma punar nāvartate yataḥ ।। sa bhedaḥ prathamas tasya jñānabhūtasya vai mune ।। tadālambanavijñānaṃ dvitīyo aṃśo mahāmune ।।
vijñānam advaitamayaṃ tadbhāgo anyo mayoditaḥ ।। tan nirākaraṇadvāradarśitātmasvarūpavat ।। ātmasaṃbodhaviṣayaṃ sattāmātram alakṣaṇam ।। viṣṇor jñānamayasyoktaṃ taj jñānaṃ paramaṃ padam ।।
saṃsārakarṣaṇoptau te yānti nirbījatāṃ dvija ।। samastaheyarahitaṃ viṣṇvākhyaṃ paramaṃ padam ।। apuṇyapuṇyoparame kṣīṇakleśo atinirmalaḥ ।। kṣarākṣarasvarūpe te sarvabhūteṣu ca sthite ।।
parasya brahmaṇaḥ śaktis tathaitad akhilaṃ jagat ।। jyotsnābhedo asti tacchaktes tadvan maitreya vidyate ।। tataś ca devā maitreya nyūnā dakṣādayas tataḥ ।। nyūnā nyūnatarāś caiva vṛkṣagulmādayas tataḥ ।।
āvirbhāvatirobhāvajanmanāśavikalpavat ।। mūrtaṃ yad yogibhiḥ pūrvaṃ yogārambheṣu cintyate ।। manasy avyāhate samyag yuñjatāṃ jāyate mune ।। mūrtaṃ brahma mahābhāga sarvabrahmamayo hariḥ ।।
tato jagaj jagat tasmin sa jagac cākhilaṃ mune ।। puruṣāvyākṛtamayaṃ bhūṣaṇāstrasvarūpavat ।। bibharti bhagavān viṣṇus tan mamākhyātum arhasi ।। kathayāmi yathākhyātaṃ vasiṣṭhena mamābhavat ।।
bibharti kaustubhamaṇisvarūpaṃ bhagavān hariḥ ।। asya jagata ātmānaṃ puruṣaṃ śuddhaṃ kṣatrajñam ।। pradhānaṃ buddhir apy āste gadārūpeṇa mādhave ।। bibharti śaṅkharūpeṇa śārṅgarūpeṇa ca sthitam ।।
cakrasvarūpaṃ ca mano dhatte viṣṇukare sthitam ।। sā bhūtahetusaṃghātā bhūtamālā ca vai dvija ।। śararūpāṇy aśeṣāṇi tāni dhatte janārdanaḥ ।। vidyāmayaṃ tu taj jñānam avidyācarmasaṃsthitam ।।
vidyāvidye ca maitreya sarvam etat samāśritam ।। bibharti māyārūpo asau śreyase prāṇināṃ hariḥ ।। bibharti puṇḍarīkākṣas tad evaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ sarvabhūteśe maitreya madhusūdane ।।
kālasvarūpo bhagavān apāro harir avyayaḥ ।। mahar janas tapaḥ satyaṃ saptalokān imān vibhuḥ ।। ādhāraḥ sarvavidyānāṃ svayam eva hariḥ sthitaḥ ।। sthitaḥ sarveśvaro ananto bhūtamūrtir amūrtimān ।।
itihāsopavedāś ca vedānteṣu tathoktayaḥ ।। śāstrāṇy aśeṣāṇy ākhyānāny anuvākāś ca ye kvacit ।। śabdamūrtidharasyaitad vapur viṣṇor mahātmanaḥ ।। santi vai vastujātāni tāni sarvāṇi tadvapuḥ ।।
īdṛṅ mano yasya na tasya bhūyo bhavodbhavā dvandvagadā bhavanti ।। yathāvat kathito yasmiñ śrute pāpair vimucyate ।। tad asya śravaṇe sarvaṃ maitreyāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। bhavanti śṛṇvataḥ puṃso devādyā varadā mune ।।
jagataḥ sargasaṃbandhi yat pṛṣṭo asi guro mayā ।। tatrāhaṃ śrotum icchāmi bhūyo api munisattama ।। tayor uttānapādasya dhruvaḥ putras tvayoditaḥ ।। tām ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi prasanno vaktum arhasi ।।
samrāṭ kukṣiś ca tatkanye daśaputrās tathāpare ।। priyavratasutāḥ khyātās teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। medhā medhātithir bhavyaḥ savanaḥ putra eva ca ।। priyavratasya putrāṇāṃ prakhyātā balavīryataḥ ।।
jātismarā mahābhāgā na rājyāya mano dadhuḥ ।। cakruḥ kriyā yathānyāyam aphalākāṅkṣiṇo hi te ।। vibhajya sapta dvīpāni maitreya sumahātmanām ।। medhātithes tathā prādāt plakṣadvīpam athāparam ।।
jyotiṣmantaṃ kuśadvīpe rājānaṃ kṛtavān prabhuḥ ।। śākadvīpeśvaraṃ cāpi bhavyaṃ cakre priyavrataḥ ।। tasya putrā babhūvus te prajāpatisamā nava ।। ketumālas tathaivānyaḥ sādhuceṣṭo nṛpo abhavat ।।
pitrā dattaṃ himāhvaṃ tu varṣaṃ nābhes tu dakṣiṇam ।। tṛtīyaṃ naiṣadhaṃ varṣaṃ harivarṣāya dattavān ।। nīlācalāśritaṃ varṣaṃ ramyāya pradadau pitā ।। śvetaṃ yad uttaraṃ tasmāt pitrā dattaṃ hiraṇvate ।।
meroḥ pūrveṇa yad varṣaṃ bhadrāśvāya pradattavān ।। ity etāni dadau tebhyaḥ putrebhyaḥ sa nareśvaraḥ ।। sālagrāmaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ maitreya tapase yayau ।। teṣāṃ svābhāvikī siddhiḥ sukhaprāyā hy ayatnataḥ ।।
dharmādharmau na teṣv āstāṃ nottamādhamamadhyamāḥ ।। tasyarṣabho abhavat putro merudevyāṃ mahādyutiḥ ।। kṛtvā rājyaṃ svadharmeṇa tatheṣṭvā vividhān makhān ।। tapase sa mahābhāgaḥ pulahasyāśramaṃ yayau ।।
tapas tepe yathānyāyam iyāja sa mahīpatiḥ ।। nagno vīṭāṃ mukhe dattvā vīrādhvānaṃ tato gataḥ ।। bharatāya yataḥ pitrā dattaṃ prātiṣṭhatā vanam ।। kṛtvā samyag dadau tasmai rājyam iṣṭamakhaḥ pitā ।।
yogābhyāsarataḥ prāṇān sālagrāme atyajan mune ।। maitreya tasya caritaṃ kathayiṣyāmi te punaḥ ।। parameṣṭhī tatas tasmāt pratihāras tadanvayaḥ ।। bhuvas tasmād athodgīthaḥ prastāvas tatsuto vibhuḥ ।।
naro gayasya tanayas tatputro abhūd virāṭ tataḥ ।। mahānto api tataś cābhūn manasyus tasya cātmajaḥ ।। śatajid rajasas tasya jajñe putraśataṃ mune ।। tair idaṃ bhārataṃ varṣaṃ navabhedam alaṃkṛtam ।।
kṛtatretādisargeṇa yugākhyā hy ekasaptatiḥ ।। vārāhe tu mune kalpe pūrvamanvantarādhipaḥ ।। śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ tvattaḥ sakalaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhuvaḥ ।। vanāni saritaḥ puryo devādīnāṃ tathā mune ।।
saṃsthānam asya ca mune yathāvad vaktum arhasi ।। nāsya varṣaśatenāpi vaktuṃ śaknomi vistaram ।। kuśaḥ krauñcas tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraś caiva saptamaḥ ।। lavaṇekṣusurāsarpirdadhidugdhajalaiḥ samam ।।
tasyāpi merur maitreya madhye kanakaparvataḥ ।। caturaśītisāhasro yojanair asya cocchrayaḥ ।। mūle ṣoḍaśasāhasro vistāras tasya sarvataḥ ।। bhūpadmasyāsya śailo asau karṇikākārasaṃsthitaḥ ।।
nīlaḥ śvetaś ca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ ।। sahasradvitayocchrāyās tāvadvistāriṇaś ca te ।। harivarṣaṃ tathaivānyan meror dakṣiṇato dvija ।। uttarāḥ kuravaś caiva yathā vai bhārataṃ tathā ।।
ilāvṛtaṃ ca tanmadhye sauvarṇo merur ucchritaḥ ।। ilāvṛtaṃ mahābhāga catvāraś cātra parvatāḥ ।। viṣkambhā racitā meror yojanāyutam ucchritāḥ ।। b sarvaiḥ sarobhiś ca samaṃ dikṣv ete kesarācalāḥ ।। b
pūrveṇa mandaro nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ ।। d vipulaḥ paścime pārśve supārśvaś cottare smṛtaḥ ।। f ekādaśaśatāyāmāḥ pādapā giriketavaḥ ।। patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvataḥ ।।
sarit pravartate sā ca pīyate tannivāsibhiḥ ।। tatpānāt svacchamanasāṃ janānāṃ tatra jāyate ।। jāmbūnadākhyaṃ bhavati suvarṇaṃ siddhabhūṣaṇam ।। varṣe dve tu muniśreṣṭha tayor madhyam ilāvṛtam ।।
vaibhrājaṃ paścime tadvad uttare nandanaṃ smṛtam ।। sarāṃsy etāni catvāri devabhogyāni sarvadā ।। vaikaṅkapramukhā meroḥ pūrvataḥ kesarācalāḥ ।। niṣadhādyā dakṣiṇatas tasya kesaraparvatāḥ ।।
jārudhipramukhās tadvat paścime kesarācalāḥ ।। kālañjanādyāś ca tadā uttare kesarācalāḥ ।। kesarās tu tathocchrāyas te aśītipṛthulāyatāḥ ।। meror upari maitreya brahmaṇaḥ prathitā divi ।।
indrādilokapālānāṃ prakhyātāḥ pravarāḥ puraḥ ।। samantād brahmaṇaḥ puryāṃ gaṅgā patati vai divaḥ ।। sītā cālakanandā ca cakṣur bhadrā ca vai kramāt ।। tataś ca pūrvavarṣeṇa bhadrāśvenaiti sārṇavam ।।
prayāti sāgaraṃ bhūtvā saptabhedā mahāmune ।। paścimaṃ ketumālākhyaṃ varṣaṃ gatvaiti sāgaram ।। atītyottaram ambhodhiṃ samabhyeti mahāmune ।। tayor madhyagato meruḥ karṇikākārasaṃsthitaḥ ।।
