patrāṇi lokapadmasya maryādāśailabāhyataḥ ।। tau dakṣiṇottarāyāmāv ānīlaniṣadhāyatau ।। aśītiyojanāyāmāv arṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।। meroḥ paścimadigbhāge yathāpūrvau tathā sthitau ।।
pūrvapaścāyatāv etāv arṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।। jaṭharādyāḥ sthitā meros yeṣāṃ dvau dvau caturdiśam ।। śailānām antaradroṇyaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitāḥ ।। tāsv āyatanavaryāṇi juṣṭāni varakiṃnaraiḥ ।।
krīḍanti tāsu ramyāsu śailadroṇīṣv aharniśam ।। naiteṣu pāpakartāro yānti janmaśatair api ।। varāhaḥ ketumāle tu bhārate kūrmarūpadhṛk ।। viśvarūpeṇa sarvatra sarvaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ ।।
sarvasyādhārabhūto asau maitreyāste akhilātmakaḥ ।। na teṣu śoko nāyāso nodvegaḥ kṣudbhayādikam ।। daśa dvādaśavarṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi sthirāyuṣaḥ ।। kṛtatretādikā naiva teṣu sthāneṣu kalpanā ।।
nadyaś ca śataśas tebhyaḥ prasūtā yā dvijottama ।। varṣaṃ tad bhārataṃ nāma bhāratī yatra saṃtatiḥ ।। karmabhūmir iyaṃ svargam apavargaṃ ca gacchatām ।। vindhyaś ca pāriyātraś ca saptātra kulaparvatāḥ ।।
tiryaktvaṃ narakaṃ cāpi yānty ataḥ puruṣā mune ।। na khalv anyatra martyānāṃ karma bhūmau vidhīyate ।। indradvīpaḥ kaseruś ca tāmraparṇo gabhastimān ।। ayaṃ tu navamas teṣāṃ dvīpaḥ sāgarasaṃvṛtaḥ ।।
pūrve kirātā yasyānte paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ ।। ijyāyudhavaṇijyādyair vartayanto vyavasthitāḥ ।। vedasmṛtimukhāś cānyāḥ pāriyātrodbhavā mune ।। tāpīpayoṣṇīnirvindhyāpramukhā ṛkṣasaṃbhavāḥ ।।
sahyapādodbhavā nadyaḥ smṛtāḥ pāpabhayāpahāḥ ।। trisāmā ṛṣikulyādyā mahendraprabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। āsāṃ nadyupanadyaś ca santy anyāś ca sahasraśaḥ ।। pūrvadeśādikāś caiva kāmarūpanivāsinaḥ ।।
tathāparāntāḥ saurāṣṭrāḥ śūrābhīrās tathārbudāḥ ।। sauvīrāḥ saindhavā hūṇāḥ sālvāḥ śākalavāsinaḥ ।। samīpato mahābhāgā hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulāḥ ।। kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliś cānyatra na kvacit ।।
dānāni cātra dīyante paralokārtham ādarāt ।। yajñair yajñamayo viṣṇur anyadvīpeṣu cānyathā ।। yato hi karmabhūr eṣā hy ato anyā bhogabhūmayaḥ ।। kadācil labhate jantur mānuṣyaṃ puṇyasaṃcayāt ।।
svargāpavargāspadahetubhūte bhavanti bhūyaḥ puruṣāḥ suratvāt ।। avāpya tāṃ karmamahīm anante tasmiṃl layaṃ ye tv amalāḥ prayānti ।। prāpsyāma dhanyāḥ khalu te manuṣyā ye bhārate nendriyaviprahīnāḥ ।। lakṣayojanavistāraṃ saṃkṣepāt kathitaṃ tava ।।
maitreya valayākāraḥ sthitaḥ kṣārodadhir bahiḥ ।। saṃveṣṭya kṣāram udadhiṃ plakṣadvīpas tathā sthitaḥ ।। atha plakṣādikadvīpān varṣādrisaridabdhibhiḥ ।। varṇarūpādibhedena varṇayaty ākaṭāhataḥ ।।
sa evaṃ dviguṇo brahman plakṣadvīpa udāhṛtaḥ ।। jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayo nāma śiśiras tadanantaraḥ ।। dhruvaś ca saptamas teṣāṃ plakṣadvīpeśvarā hi te ।। ānandaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva kṣemakaṃ dhruvam eva ca ।।
saptaiva teṣāṃ nāmāni śṛṇuṣva munisattama ।। somakaḥ sumanāḥ śailo vaibhrājaś caiva saptamaḥ ।। vasanti devagandharvasahitāḥ satataṃ prajāḥ ।। nādhayo vyādhayo vāpi sarvakālasukhaṃ hi tat ।।
nāmatas tāḥ pravakṣyāmi śrutāḥ pāpaṃ haranti yāḥ ।। amṛtā sukṛtā caiva saptaitās tatra nimnagāḥ ।। tāḥ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭā nadīr janapadās tu te ।। na tv evāsti yugāvasthā teṣu sthāneṣu saptasu ।।
plakṣadvīpādiṣu brahmañ śākadvīpāntikeṣu vai ।। dharmaḥ pañcasv athaiteṣu varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ ।। varṇāś ca tatra catvāras tān nibodha vadāmi te ।। viprakṣatriyavaiśyās te śūdrāś ca munisattama ।।
plakṣas tannāmasaṃjño ayaṃ plakṣadvīpo dvijottama ।। somarūpī jagatsraṣṭā sarvaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ ।। tathaivekṣurasodena pariveṣānukāriṇā ।। saṃkṣepeṇa mayā bhūyaḥ śālmalaṃ me niśāmaya ।।
yeṣāṃ tu nāmasaṃjñāni sapta varṣāṇi tāni vai ।। vaidyuto mānasaś caiva suprabhaś ca mahāmune ।। vistāradviguṇenātha sarvataḥ saṃvṛtaḥ sthitaḥ ।। varṣābhivyañjakās te tu tathā saptaiva nimnagāḥ ।।
droṇo yatra mahauṣadhyaḥ sa caturtho mahīdharaḥ ।। kakudmān parvatavaraḥ sarinnāmāni me śṛṇu ।। nivṛttiḥ saptamī tāsāṃ smṛtās tāḥ pāpaśāntidāḥ ।। saptaitāni tu varṣāṇi cāturvarṇyayutāni vai ।।
kapilāś cāruṇāḥ pītāḥ kṛṣṇāś caiva pṛthak pṛthak ।। vāyubhūtaṃ makhaśreṣṭhair yajvino yajñasaṃsthitam ।। śālmaliś ca mahāvṛkṣo nāma nirvṛtikārakaḥ ।। vistārāc chālmalasyaiva samena tu samantataḥ ।।
śālmalasya tu vistārād dviguṇena samantataḥ ।। jyotiṣmataḥ kuśadvīpe sapta putrān śṛṇuṣva tān ।। prabhākaro atha kapilas tannāmā varṣapaddhatiḥ ।। tathaiva devagandharvayakṣakiṃpuruṣādayaḥ ।।
daminaḥ śuṣmiṇaḥ snehā mandehāś ca mahāmune ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś cānukramoditāḥ ।। yajantaḥ kṣapayanty ugram adhikāraphalapradam ।। kuśeśayo hariś caiva saptamo mandarācalaḥ ।।
nadyaś ca sapta tāsāṃ tu śṛṇu nāmāny anukramāt ।। vidyud ambhā mahī cānyā sarvapāpaharās tv imāḥ ।। kuśadvīpe kuśastambaḥ saṃjñayā tasya tat smṛtam ।। ghṛtodaś ca samudro vai krauñcadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ ।।
kuśadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇo yasya vistaraḥ ।। tannāmāni ca varṣāṇi teṣāṃ cakre mahīpatiḥ ।। muniś ca dundubhiś caiva saptaite tatsutā mune ।। varṣācalā mahābuddhe teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।।
caturtho ratnaśailaś ca svāhinī hayasaṃnibhaḥ ।। dvīpā dvīpeṣu ye śailā yathā dvīpāni te tathā ।। nivasanti nirātaṅkāḥ saha devagaṇaiḥ prajāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāś cānukramoditāḥ ।।
sapta pradhānāḥ śataśas tatrānyāḥ kṣudranimnagāḥ ।। khyātiś ca puṇḍarīkā ca saptaitā varṣanimnagāḥ ।। yāgai rudrasvarūpastha ijyate yajñasaṃnidhau ।। āvṛtaḥ sarvataḥ krauñcadvīpatulyena mānataḥ ।।
krauñcadvīpasya vistārād dviguṇena mahāmune ।। saptaiva tanayās teṣāṃ dadau varṣāṇi sapta saḥ ।। kusumodaḥ sumodākiḥ saptamaś ca mahādrumaḥ ।। tatrāpi parvatāḥ sapta varṣavicchedakāriṇaḥ ।।
āmbikeyas tathā ramyaḥ kesarī parvatottamaḥ ।। nivasanti mahātmāno nirātaṅkā nirāmayāḥ ।। yatpatravātasaṃsparśād āhlādo jāyate paraḥ ।। nadyaś cātra mahāpuṇyāḥ sarvapāpabhayāpahāḥ ।।
ikṣuś ca dhenukā caiva gabhastī saptamī tathā ।। mahīdharās tathā santi śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। varṣeṣu te janapadāḥ svargād abhyetya medinīm ।। maryādāvyutkramo vāpi teṣu deśeṣu saptasu ।।
vaiśyās tu mānasās teṣāṃ śūdrās teṣāṃ tu mandagāḥ ।। yathoktair ijyate samyak karmabhir niyatātmabhiḥ ।। śākadvīpapramāṇena valayeneva veṣṭitaḥ ।। dvīpena śākadvīpāt tu dviguṇena samantataḥ ।।
puṣkareṇāvṛto brahman kṣīrodusāpi sarvataḥ ।। mahāvīraṃ tathaivānyad dhātakīkhaṇḍasaṃjñitam ।। mānasottarasaṃjño vai madhyato valayākṛtiḥ ।। tāvad eva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।।
sthito asau tena vicchinnaṃ jātaṃ varṣadvayaṃ mune ।। valayākāram ekaikaṃ tayor varṣaṃ tathā giriḥ ।। nirāmayā viśokāś ca rāgadveṣavivarjitāḥ ।। nerṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ roṣo doṣo lobhādiko na ca ।।
mānasottaraśailasya devadaityādisevitam ।। na tatra nadyaḥ śailā vā dvīpe varṣadvayānvite ।। tulyaveṣās tu manujā devais tatraikarūpiṇaḥ ।। trayīvārtādaṇḍanītiśuśrūṣārahitaṃ ca yat ।।
puṣkare dhātakīṣaṇḍe mahāvīre ca vai mune ।। tasmin nivasati brahmā pūjyamānaḥ surāsuraiḥ ।। samena puṣkarasyaiva vistārān maṇḍalāt tathā ।। dvīpaś caiva samudraś ca samānau dviguṇau parau ।।
nyūnātiriktatā teṣāṃ kadācin naiva jāyate ।। tathenduvṛddhau salilam ambhodhau munisattama ।। udayāstamayeṣv indoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ।। apāṃ vṛddhikṣayau dṛṣṭau sāmudrīṇāṃ mahāmune ।।
ṣaḍrasaṃ bhuñjate vipra prajāḥ sarvāḥ sadaiva hi ।। dviguṇā kāñcanī bhūmiḥ sarvajantuvivarjitā ।। ucchrāyeṇāpi tāvanti sahasrāṇy acalo hi saḥ ।। tamaś cāṇḍakaṭāhena samantāt pariveṣṭitam ।।
kvacit kvacit purāṇeṣu virodho yadi lakṣyate ।। kalpabhedādibhis tatra vyavasthā sadbhir iṣyate ।। sahaivāṇḍakaṭāhena sadvīpābdhimahīdharā ।। ādhārabhūtā sarveṣāṃ maitreya jagatām iti ।।
saptatis tu sahasrāṇi dvijocchrāyo api kathyate ।। saptabhūmikavistāraḥ prāsādavad adhobhuvaḥ ।। saptapātālavyaktis tu varṇyate anantamastake ।। mahākhyaṃ sutalaṃ cāgryaṃ pātālaṃ cāpi saptamam ।।
bhūmayo yatra maitreya varaprāsādaśobhitāḥ ।। nivasanti mahānāgajātayaś ca mahāmune ।। prāha svargasadāṃ madhye pātālābhyāgato divi ।। nāgābharaṇabhūṣāsu pātālaṃ kena tatsamam ।।
pātāle kasya na prītir vimuktasyāpi jāyate ।। śaśinaś ca na śītāya niśi dyotāya kevalam ।। yatra na jñāyate kālo gato api danujādibhiḥ ।। puṃskokilābhilāpāś ca manojñāny ambarāṇi ca ।।
vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgānāṃ svanās tūryāṇi ca dvija ।। daityoragaiś ca bhujyante pātālāntaragocaraiḥ ।। śeṣākhyā yadguṇān vaktuṃ na śaktā daityadānavāḥ ।। sahasraśirasā vyaktasvastikāmalabhūṣaṇaḥ ।।
sarvān karoti nirvīryān hitāya jagato asurān ।। kirīṭī sragdharo bhāti sāgniḥ śveta ivācalaḥ ।। sābhragaṅgāprapāto asau kailāsādrir ivonnataḥ ।। upāsyate svayaṃ kāntyā yo vāruṇyā ca mūrtayā ।।
saṃkarṣaṇātmako rudro niṣkramyātti jagattrayam ।। āste pātālamūlasthaḥ śeṣo aśeṣasurārcitaḥ ।। na hi varṇayituṃ śakyaṃ jñātuṃ vā tridaśair api ।। āste kusumamāleva kas tadvīryaṃ vadiṣyati ।।
tadā calati bhūr eṣā sādritoyā sakānanā ।। nāntaṃ guṇānāṃ gacchanti tenānanto ayam avyayaḥ ।। muhuḥ śvāsānilāpāstaṃ yāti dikṣūdavāsatām ।। jñātavān sakalaṃ caiva nimittapaṭhitaṃ phalam ।।
bibharti mālāṃ lokānāṃ sadevāsuramānuṣām ।। pāpino yeṣu pātyante tāñ chṛṇuṣva mahāmune ।। mahājvālas taptakumbho lavaṇo atha vilohitaḥ ।। asipatravanaṃ kṛṣṇo lālābhakṣaś ca dāruṇaḥ ।।
saṃdaṃśaḥ kṛṣṇasūtraś ca tamaś cāvīcir eva ca ।। ity evamādayaś cānye narakā bhṛśadāruṇāḥ ।। patanti yeṣu puruṣāḥ pāpakarmaratās tu ye ।। yaś cānyad anṛtaṃ vakti sa naro yāti rauravam ।।
yānti te narakaṃ rodhaṃ yaś cocchvāsanirodhakaḥ ।। prayāti narake yaś ca taiḥ saṃsargam upaiti vai ।। taptakumbhe svasāgāmī hanti rājabhaṭāṃś ca yaḥ ।। taptalohe patanty ete yaś ca bhaktaṃ parityajet ।।
avamantā gurūṇāṃ yo yaś cākroṣṭā narādhamaḥ ।। agamyagāmī yaś ca syāt te yānti lavaṇaṃ dvija ।। cauro vimohe patati maryādādūṣakas tathā ।। sa yāti kṛmibhakṣe vai kṛmiśe ca duriṣṭakṛt ।।
lālābhakṣe sa yāty ugre śarakartā ca vedhake ।। prayānty ete viśasane narake bhṛśadāruṇe ।। ayājyayājakas tatra tathā nakṣatrasūcakaḥ ।। vegī pūyavahaṃ caiko yāti miṣṭānnabhuṅ naraḥ ।।
vikretā brāhmaṇo yāti tam eva narakaṃ dvija ।। poṣayan narakaṃ yāti tam eva dvijasattama ।। apūpavikrayāc caiva tathā pustakavikrayāḥ ।। sūcī māhiṣikaś caiva parvagāmī ca yo dvijaḥ ।।
rudhirāndhe patanty ete somaṃ vikrīṇate ca ye ।। madhuhā grāmahantā ca yāti vaitaraṇīṃ naraḥ ।। te kṛṣṇe yānty aśaucāś ca kuhakājīvinaś ca ye ।। aurabhriko mṛgavyādho vahnijvāle patanti vai ।।
yānty ete dvija tatraiva yaś cāpākeṣu vahnidaḥ ।। saṃdaṃśayātanāmadhye patatas tāv ubhāv api ।। putrair adhyāpitā ye ca te patanti śvabhojane ।। yeṣu duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ pacyante yātanāgatāḥ ।।
bhujyante yāni puruṣair narakāntaragocaraiḥ ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā nirayeṣu patanti te ।। devāś cādhomukhān sarvān adhaḥ paśyanti nārakān ।। dhārmikās tridaśās tadvan mokṣiṇaś ca yathākramam ।।
sarve hy ete mahābhāga yāvan muktisamāśrayāḥ ।। pāpakṛd yāti narakaṃ prāyaścittaparāṅmukhaḥ ।। tathā tathaiva saṃsmṛtya proktāni paramarṣibhiḥ ।। prāyaścittāni maitreya jaguḥ svāyaṃbhuvādayaḥ ।।
yāni teṣām aśeṣāṇāṃ kṛṣṇānusmaraṇaṃ param ।। prāyaścittaṃ tu tasyaikaṃ harisaṃsmaraṇaṃ param ।। nārāyaṇam avāpnoti sadyaḥ pāpakṣayaṃ naraḥ ।। muktiṃ prayāti svargāptis tasya vighno anumīyate ।।
tasyāntarāyo maitreya devendratvādikaṃ phalam ।। kva japo vāsudeveti muktibījam anuttamam ।। na yāti narakaṃ śuddhaḥ saṃkṣīṇākhilapātakaḥ ।। narakasvargasaṃjñe vai pāpapuṇye dvijottama ।।
kopāya ca yatas tasmād vastu vastvātmakaṃ kutaḥ ।। tad eva kopāya yataḥ prasādāya ca jāyate ।। manasaḥ pariṇāmo ayaṃ sukhaduḥkhādilakṣaṇaḥ ।। jñānātmakam idaṃ viśvaṃ na jñānād vidyate param ।।
vidyāvidyeti maitreya jñānam evopadhāraya ।। pātālāni ca sarvāṇi tathaiva narakā dvija ।। saṃkṣepāt sarvam ākhyātaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi ।। bhuvarlokādikāṃl lokāñ śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ mune ।।
samācakṣva mahābhāga mahyaṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchate ।। sasamudrasaricchailā tāvatī pṛthivī smṛtā ।। nabhas tāvatpramāṇaṃ vai vyāsamaṇḍalato dvija ।। lakṣe divākarasyāpi maṇḍalaṃ śaśinaḥ sthitam ।।
nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnam upariṣṭāt prakāśate ।। tāvatpramāṇabhāge tu budhasyāpy uśanā sthitaḥ ।। lakṣadvaye tu bhaumasya sthito devapurohitaḥ ।। saptarṣimaṇḍalaṃ tasmāl lakṣam ekaṃ dvijottama ।।
meḍhībhūtaḥ samastasya jyotiścakrasya vai dhruvaḥ ।। ijyāphalasya bhūr eṣā ijyā cātra pratiṣṭhitā ।। ekayojanakoṭī tu maharloko abhidhīyate ।। sanandanādyāḥ kathitā maitreyāmalacetasaḥ ।।
vairājā yatra te devāḥ sthitā dāhavivarjitāḥ ।। apunarmārakā yatra brahmaloko hi sa smṛtaḥ ।। sa bhūrlokaḥ samākhyāto vistaro asya mayoditaḥ ।। bhuvarlokas tu so apy ukto dvitīyo munisattama ।।
svarlokaḥ so api gadito lokasaṃsthānacintakaiḥ ।। janas tapas tathā satyam iti cākṛtakaṃ trayam ।। śūnyo bhavati kalpānte yo atyantaṃ na vinaśyati ।। pātālāni ca saptaiva brahmāṇḍasyaiṣa vistaraḥ ।।
kapitthasya yathā bījaṃ sarvato vai samāvṛtam ।। sarvo ambuparidhāno asau vahninā veṣṭito bahiḥ ।। daśottarāṇy aśeṣāṇi maitreyaitāni sapta vai ।। anantasya na tasyāntaḥ saṃkhyānaṃ vāpi vidyate ।।
hetubhūtam aśeṣasya prakṛtiḥ sā parā mune ।। īdṛśānāṃ tathā tatra koṭikoṭiśatāni ca ।। pradhāne avasthito vyāpī cetanātmātmavedanaḥ ।। viṣṇuśaktyā mahābuddhe vṛtau saṃśrayadharmiṇau ।।
kṣobhakāraṇabhūtā ca sargakāle mahāmate ।। śaktiḥ sāpi tathā viṣṇoḥ pradhānapuruṣātmakam ।। ādibījāt prabhavati bījāny anyāni vai tataḥ ।। te api tallakṣaṇadravyakāraṇānugatā mune ।।
tebhyaś ca putrās teṣāṃ ca putrāṇām apare sutāḥ ।। bhūtānāṃ bhūtasargeṇa naivāsty apacayas tathā ।। tathaivāpariṇāmena viśvasya bhagavān hariḥ ।। kāṇḍakoṣas tathā puṣpaṃ kṣīraṃ tadvac ca taṇḍulāḥ ।।
prarohahetusāmagrīm āsādya munisattama ।। viṣṇuśaktiṃ samāsādya praroham upayānti vai ।। jagac ca yo yatra cedaṃ yasmiṃś ca layam eṣyati ।। yasya sarvam abhedena jagad etac carācaram ।।
tasminn eva layaṃ sarvaṃ yāti tatra ca tiṣṭhati ।। srugādi yat sādhanam apy aśeṣato harer na kiṃcid vyatiriktam asti vai ।। tataḥ pramāṇasaṃsthāne sūryādīnāṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।। īṣādaṇḍas tathaivāsya dviguṇo munisattama ।।
yojanānāṃ tu tasyākṣas tatra cakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। saṃvatsaramaye kṛtsnaṃ kālacakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। pañcānyāni tu sārdhāni syandanasya mahāmate ।। dvitīye akṣe tu tac cakraṃ saṃsthitaṃ mānasācale ।।
anuṣṭup paṅktir ity uktāś chandāṃsi harayo raveḥ ।। uttareṇa ca somasya tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। purī sukhā jaleśasya somasya ca vibhāvarī ।। maitreya bhagavān bhānur jyotiṣāṃ cakrasaṃyutaḥ ।।
devayānaḥ paraḥ panthā yogināṃ kleśasaṃkṣaye ।। sarvadvīpeṣu maitreya niśārdhasya ca saṃmukhaḥ ।। diśāsv aśeṣāsu tathā maitreya vidiśāsu ca ।। tirobhāvaṃ ca yatraiti tatraivāstamanaṃ raveḥ ।।
udayāstamanākhyaṃ hi darśanādarśanaṃ raveḥ ।। vikarṇau dvau vikarṇasthas trīn koṇān dve pure tathā ।। tataḥ paraṃ hrasantībhir gobhir astaṃ niyacchati ।। yāvat purastāt tapati tāvat pṛṣṭhe ca pārśvayoḥ ।।
te te nirastās tadbhāsā pratīpam upayānti vai ।। sarveṣāṃ dvīpavarṣāṇāṃ merur uttarato yataḥ ।। viśaty agnim ato rātrau vahnir dūrāt prakāśate ।। atīva vahnisaṃyogād ataḥ sūryaḥ prakāśate ।।
parasparānupraveśād āpyāyete divāniśam ।। ahorātraṃ viśaty ambhas tamaḥprākāśyaśīlavat ।। tasmāc chuklībhavanty āpo naktam ahnaḥ praveśanāt ।। triṃśadbhāgaṃ tu medinyās tadā mauhūrtikī gatiḥ ।।
karoty ahas tathā rātriṃ vimuñcan medinīṃ dvija ।। tataḥ kumbhaṃ ca mīnaṃ ca rāśe rāśyantaraṃ dvija ।। prayāti savitā kurvann ahorātraṃ tataḥ samam ।। tato rātriḥ kṣayaṃ yāti vardhate anudinaṃ dinam ।।
rāśiṃ karkaṭakaṃ prāpya kurute dakṣiṇāyanam ।। dakṣiṇe prakrame sūryas tathā śīghraṃ pravartate ।। tasmāt prakṛṣṭāṃ bhūmiṃ tu kālenālpena gacchati ।। muhūrtais tāvadṛkṣāṇi naktam aṣṭādaśaiś caran ।।
tathodagayane sūryaḥ sarpate mandavikramaḥ ।। aṣṭādaśamuhūrtaṃ yad uttarāyaṇapaścimam ।। ahar bhavati tatrāpi carate mandavikramaḥ ।। muhūrtais tāvadṛkṣāṇi rātrau dvādaśabhiś caran ।।
mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho dhruvo bhramati vai tathā ।। dhruvas tathā hi maitreya tatraiva parivartate ।। divā naktaṃ ca sūryasya mandā śīghrā ca vai gatiḥ ।। śīghrā niśi yadā cāsya tadā mandā divā gatiḥ ।।
ahorātreṇa yo bhuṅkte samastā rāśayo dvija ।। ṣaḍ eva rāśayo bhuṅkte rātrāv anyāṃś ca ṣaḍ divā ।। tathā niśāyāṃ rāśīnāṃ pramāṇair laghudīrghatā ।। uttare prakrame śīghrā niśi mandā gatir divā ।।
dakṣiṇe tv ayane caiva viparītā vivasvataḥ ।। procyate ca tathā saṃdhyā uṣāvyuṣṭyor yad antaram ।। mandehā rākṣasā ghorāḥ sūryam icchanti khāditum ।। akṣayatvaṃ śarīrāṇāṃ maraṇaṃ ca dine dine ।।
tato dvijottamās toyaṃ yat kṣipanti mahāmune ।। tena dahyanti te pāpā vajrībhūtena vāriṇā ।। sūryo jyotiḥ sahasrāṃśus tayā dīpyati bhāskaraḥ ।। taduccāraṇatas te tu vināśaṃ yānti rākṣasāḥ ।।
abhidhāyaka oṃkāras tasya sa prerakaḥ paraḥ ।। dahaty aśeṣarakṣāṃsi mandehākhyāny aghāni vai ।। sa hanti sūryaṃ saṃdhyāyā nopāstiṃ kurute hi yaḥ ।। vālakhilyādibhiś caiva jagataḥ pālanodyataḥ ।।
prabhur vaikhānasair api ।। mahātmabhir mahātmā vai ।। triṃśatkalāś caiva bhaven muhūrtas tais triṃśatā rātryahanī samete ।। saṃdhyā muhūrtamātrā vai hrāsavṛddhau samā smṛtā ।।
prātaḥ smṛtas tataḥ kālo bhāgaś cāhnaḥ sa pañcamaḥ ।। madhyāhnas trimuhūrtas tu tasmāt kālāt tu saṃgavāt ।। traya eva muhūrtās tu kālabhāgaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ ।। daśapañcamuhūrtāho muhūrtās traya eva ca ।।
daśapañcamuhūrtaṃ vai ahar vaiṣuvataṃ smṛtam ।। ahas tu grasate rātriṃ rātrir grasati vāsaram ।। tulāmeṣagate bhānau samarātridinaṃ tu tat ।। uttarāyaṇam apy uktaṃ makarasthe divākare ।।
tāni pañcadaśa brahman pakṣa ity abhidhīyate ।। ṛtutrayaṃ cāpy ayanaṃ dve ayane varṣasaṃjñite ।। niścayaḥ sarvakālasya yugam ity abhidhīyate ।। vatsaraḥ pañcamaś cātra kālo ayaṃ yugasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
trīṇi tasya tu śṛṅgāṇi yair asau śṛṅgavān smṛtaḥ ।। meṣādau ca tulādau ca maitreya viṣuvatsthitaḥ ।। daśapañcamuhūrtaṃ vai tad etad ubhayaṃ smṛtam ।। viśākhānāṃ caturthe aṃśe mune tiṣṭhaty asaṃśayam ।।
tadā candraṃ vijānīyāt kṛttikāśirasi sthitam ।। tadā dānāni deyāni devebhyaḥ prayatātmabhiḥ ।। dattadānas tu viṣuve kṛtakṛtyo abhijāyate ।। sinīvālī kuhūś caiva rākā cānumatis tathā ।।
nabho nabhasyo atha iṣaś ca sorjaḥ sahaḥsahasyāv iti dakṣiṇaṃ syāt ।। lokapālās tu catvāras tatra tiṣṭhanti suvratāḥ ।। hiraṇyaromā caivānyaś caturthaḥ ketumān api ।। lokapālāḥ sthitā hy ete lokāloke caturdiśam ।।
pitṛyānaḥ sa vai panthā vaiśvānarapathād bahiḥ ।। lokārambhaṃ prārabhante teṣāṃ panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ ।। saṃtatyā tapasā caiva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca ।। paścimāś caiva pūrveṣāṃ jāyante nidhaneṣv iha ।।
savitur dakṣiṇaṃ mārgaṃ śritā hy ācandratārakam ।। uttaraḥ savituḥ panthā devayānas tu sa smṛtaḥ ।। saṃtatiṃ te jugupsanti tasmān mṛtyur jitaś ca taiḥ ।। udakpanthānam aryamṇaḥ śritā hy ābhūtasaṃplavāt ।।
icchādveṣāpravṛttyā ca bhūtārambhavivarjanāt ।। ity ebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ śuddhās te amṛtatvaṃ hi bhejire ।। trailokyasthitikālo ayam apunarmāra ucyate ।। ābhūtasaṃplavāntāntaṃ phalam uktaṃ tayor dvija ।।
kṣayam āyāti tāvat tu bhūmer ābhūtasaṃplave ।। etad viṣṇupadaṃ divyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vyomni bhāsvaram ।। sthānaṃ tat paramaṃ vipra puṇyapāpaparikṣaye ।। yatra gatvā na śocanti tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।।
tatsārṣṭyotpannayogeddhās tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। bhāvyaṃ ca viśvaṃ maitreya tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। vivekajñānadṛṣṭaṃ ca tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। dhruve ca sarvajyotīṃṣi jyotiṣv ambhomuco dvija ।।
āpyāyanaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ devādīnāṃ mahāmune ।। vṛṣṭeḥ kāraṇatāṃ yānti bhūtānāṃ sthitaye punaḥ ।। ādhārabhūtaṃ lokānāṃ trayāṇāṃ vṛṣṭikāraṇam ।। gaṅgā devāṅganāṅgānām anulepanapiñjarā ।।
viṣṇor bibharti yāṃ bhaktyā śirasāharniśaṃ dhruvaḥ ।। tiṣṭhanti vīcimālābhir uhyamānajaṭājale ।। bhūyo adhikatarāṃ kāntiṃ vahaty etad upakṣayam ।। jagataḥ pāvanārthāya yā prayāti caturdiśam ।।
ekaiva yā caturbhedā digbhedagatilakṣaṇā ।। dadhāra śirasā prītyā varṣāṇām adhikaṃ śatam ।। plāvayitvā divaṃ ninye yā pāpān sagarātmajān ।। apūrvapuṇyaprāptiś ca sadyo maitreya jāyate ।।
samātrayaṃ prayacchanti tṛptiṃ maitreya durlabhām ।। dvijabhūpāḥ parām ṛddhim avāpur divi ceha ca ।। keśavāsaktamanasaḥ prāptā nirvāṇam uttamam ।। yā pāvayati bhūtāni kīrtitā ca dine dine ।।
sthitair uccāritaṃ hanti pāpaṃ janmatrayārjitam ।। samudbhūtā paraṃ tat tu tṛtīyaṃ bhagavatpadam ।। divi rūpaṃ harer yat tu tasya pucche sthito dhruvaḥ ।। bhramantam anu taṃ yānti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat ।।
vātānīkamayair bandhair dhruve baddhāni tāni vai ।। śiśumārākṛti proktaṃ yad rūpaṃ jyotiṣāṃ divi ।। b ity evaṃ vāyavaḥ sapta vahanti bhuvanatrayam ।। b nārāyaṇo ayanaṃ dhāmnāṃ tasyādhāraḥ svayaṃ hṛdi ।। d
satārāśiśumārasya dhruvaḥ pucche vyavasthitaḥ ।। dhruvasya śiśumāraś ca dhruve bhānur vyavasthitaḥ ।। tadādhāraṃ jagac cedaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। varṣaty ambu tataś cānnam annād apy akhilaṃ jagat ।।
nālair vikṣipate abhreṣu dhūmāgnyanilamūrtiṣu ।। saṃskāraṃ kālajanitaṃ maitreyāsādya nirmalāḥ ।। catuṣprakārā bhagavān ādatte savitā mune ।। anabhragatam evorvyāṃ sadyaḥ kṣipati raśmibhiḥ ।।
na yāti narakaṃ martyo divyaṃ snānaṃ hi tat smṛtam ।। ākāśagaṅgāsalilaṃ tad gobhiḥ kṣipyate raveḥ ।। dṛṣṭārkaṃ patitaṃ jñeyaṃ tad gāṅgaṃ diggajojjhitam ।। tat sūryaraśmibhiḥ sadyaḥ samādāya nirasyate ।।
ākāśagaṅgāsalilaṃ divyaṃ snānaṃ mahāmune ।। puṣṇāty oṣadhayaḥ sarvā jīvanāyāmṛtaṃ hi tat ।। sādhakaḥ phalapākāntaḥ prajānāṃ dvija jāyate ।। kurvanty aharahas taiś ca devān āpyāyayanti te ।।
sarve devanikāyāś ca paśubhūtagaṇāś ca ye ।। sāpi niṣpādyate vṛṣṭiḥ savitrā munisattama ।। dhruvasya śiśumāro asau so api nārāyaṇāśrayaḥ ।। bibhartā sarvabhūtānām ādibhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
ārohaṇāvarohābhyāṃ bhānor abdena yā gatiḥ ।। gandharvair apsarobhiś ca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ ।। rathakṛd grāmaṇīr hetis tumburuś caiva saptamaḥ ।। maitreya syandane bhānoḥ sapta māsādhikāriṇaḥ ।।
prahetiḥ kacchanīraś ca nāradaś ca rathe raveḥ ।। mādhave nivasanty ete śucisaṃjñe nibodha me ।। hāhā rathasvanaś caiva maitreyaite vasanti vai ।। rathacitras tathā śukre vasanty āṣāḍhasaṃjñite ।।
pramlocā ca nabhasy ete sarpaś cārke vasanti vai ।। umlocā śaṅkhapālaś ca vyāghro bhādrapade tathā ।। suṣeṇo anyo ghṛtācī ca vasanty āśvayuje ravau ।। viśvācī senajic cāpi kārttike cādhikāriṇaḥ ।।
citrasenas tathā vidyun mārgaśīrṣādhikāriṇaḥ ।। ariṣṭanemiś caivānyā pūrvacittir varāpsarāḥ ।। lokaprakāśanārthāya vipravaryādhikāriṇaḥ ।। brahmāpeto atha ṛtajid dhṛtarāṣṭraś ca saptamaḥ ।।
śrūyatāṃ cāpare sūrye phālgune nivasanti ye ।। viśvāmitras tathā rakṣo yajñopeto mahāmune ।। savitur maṇḍale brahman viṣṇuśaktyupabṛṃhitāḥ ।। nṛtyanty apsaraso yānti sūryasyānu niśācarāḥ ।।
vahanti pannagā yakṣaiḥ kriyate abhīṣusaṃgrahaḥ ।। vālakhilyās tathaivainaṃ parivārya samāsate ।। himoṣṇavārivṛṣṭīnāṃ hetuḥ svasamayaṃ gataḥ ।। maṇḍale himatāpādeḥ kāraṇaṃ tan mayā śrutam ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ vālakhilyānāṃ tathaivāpsarasāṃ guro ।। kiṃ tvādityasya yat karma tan nātroktaṃ tvayā mune ।। tat kim atra raver yena vṛṣṭiḥ sūryād itīryate ।। bravīty etat samaṃ karma yadi saptagaṇasya tat ।।
yathā saptagaṇe apy ekaḥ prādhānyenādhiko raviḥ ।। saiṣā trayī tapaty aṃho jagataś ca hinasti yat ।। ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūto antaḥ savitur dvija tiṣṭhati ।। trayīmayī viṣṇuśaktir avasthānaṃ karoti vai ।।
bṛhadrathantarādīni sāmāny ahnaḥ kṣaye ravau ।। viṣṇuśaktir avasthānaṃ sadāditye karoti sā ।। brahmātha puruṣo rudras trayam etat trayīmayam ।। rudraḥ sāmamayo antāya tasmāt tasyāśucir dhvaniḥ ।।
ātmasaptagaṇasthaṃ taṃ bhāsvantam adhitiṣṭhati ।। tamaḥ samastajagatāṃ nāśaṃ nayati cākhilam ।। nṛtyanty apsaraso yānti tasya cānu niśācarāḥ ।। vālakhilyās tathaivainaṃ parivārya samāsate ।।
viṣṇur viṣṇoḥ pṛthak tasya gaṇaḥ saptavidho apy ayam ।। chāyādarśanasaṃyogaṃ sa saṃprāpnoty athātmanaḥ ।। māsānumāsaṃ bhāsvantam adhyāste tatra saṃsthitam ।। parivartaty ahorātrakāraṇaṃ savitā dvija ।।
kṛṣṇapakṣe amaraiḥ śaśvat pīyate vai sudhāmayaḥ ।। pibanti pitaras teṣāṃ bhāskarāt tarpaṇaṃ tathā ।। tam utsṛjati bhūtānāṃ puṣṭyarthaṃ sasyavṛddhaye ।। pitṛdevamanuṣyādīn evam āpyāyayaty asau ।।
śaśvat tṛptiṃ ca martyānāṃ maitreyārkaḥ prayacchati ।। vāmadakṣiṇato yuktā daśa tena caraty asau ।। hrāsavṛddhikramas tasya raśmīnāṃ savitur yathā ।। kalpam ekaṃ muniśreṣṭha vārigarbhasamudbhavāḥ ।।
maitreyaikakalaṃ santaṃ raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ ।। āpyāyayaty anudinaṃ bhāskaro vāritaskaraḥ ।। pibanti devā maitreya sudhāhārā yato amarāḥ ।। trayas triṃśat tathā devāḥ pibanti kṣaṇadākaram ।।
amākhyaraśmau vasati amāvāsyā tataḥ smṛtā ।। tato vīrutsu vasati prayāty arkaṃ tataḥ kramāt ।। patraṃ vā pātayaty ekaṃ brahmahatyāṃ sa vindati ।। aparāhṇe pitṛgaṇā jaghanyaṃ paryupāsate ।।
sudhāmṛtamayī puṇyā tām indoḥ pitaro mune ।। saumyā barhiṣadaś caiva agniṣvāttāś ca te tridhā ।। vīrudhaś cāmṛtamayaiḥ śītair apparamāṇubhiḥ ।। āpyāyayati śītāṃśuḥ prākāśyāhlādanena tu ।।
piśaṅgais turagair yuktaḥ so aṣṭābhir vāyuvegibhiḥ ।। sopāsaṅgapatākas tu śukrasyāpi ratho mahān ।। padmarāgāruṇair aśvaiḥ saṃyukto vahnisaṃbhavaiḥ ।। tasmiṃs tiṣṭhati varṣaṃ vai rāśau rāśau bṛhaspatiḥ ।।
samāruhya śanair yāti mandagāmī śanaiścaraḥ ।। sakṛdyuktās tu maitreya vahanty avirataṃ sadā ।। ādityam eti somāc ca punaḥ saureṣu parvasu ।। palāladhūmavarṇābhā lākṣārasanibhāruṇāḥ ।।
sarve dhruve mahābhāga prabaddhā vāyuraśmibhiḥ ।। bhramanty ucitacāreṇa maitreyānilaraśmibhiḥ ।। sarve dhruve nibaddhās te bhramanto bhrāmayanti tam ।। tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vātaviddhāni sarvaśaḥ ।।
yasmāj jyotīṃṣi vahati pravahas tena sa smṛtaḥ ।। saṃniveśaṃ ca tasyāpi śṛṇuṣva munisattama ।। tāvanty eva tu varṣāṇi jīvaty abhyadhikāni ca ।। yajño adharaś ca vijñeyo dharmo mūrdhānam āśritaḥ ।।
varuṇaś cāryamā caiva paścime tasya sakthinī ।। śiśnaṃ saṃvatsaras tasya mitro apānaṃ samāśritaḥ ।। tārakā śiśumārasya nāstam eti catuṣṭayam ।। dvīpānām udadhīnāṃ ca parvatānāṃ ca kīrtitaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ svarūpam ākhyātaṃ saṃkṣepāc chrūyatāṃ punaḥ ।। padmākārā samudbhūtā parvatābdhyādisaṃyutā ।। nadyaḥ samudrāś ca sa eva sarvaṃ yad asti yan nāsti ca vipravarya ।। tato hi śailābdhidharādibhedāñ jānīhi vijñānavijṛmbhitāni ।।
tadā hi saṃkalpataroḥ phalāni bhavanti no vastuṣu vastubhedāḥ ।। yac cānyathātvaṃ dvija yāti bhūyo na tat tathā tatra kuto hi tattvam ।। janaiḥ svakarmastimitātmaniścayair ālakṣyate brūhi kim atra vastu ।। vijñānam ekaṃ nijakarmabheda vibhinnacittair bahudhābhyupetam ।।
ekaṃ sadaikaṃ paramaḥ pareśaḥ sa vāsudevo na yato anyad asti ।। etat tu yat saṃvyavahārabhūtaṃ tatrāpi coktaṃ bhuvanāśritaṃ te ।। ityādikarmāśritamārgadṛṣṭaṃ bhūrādibhogāś ca phalāni teṣām ।। jñātvaivaṃ dhruvam acalaṃ sadaikarūpaṃ tat kuryād viśati hi yena vāsudevam ।।
bhūsamudrādisaritāṃ saṃsthānaṃ grahasaṃsthitiḥ ।। paramārthaś ca me prokto yathā jñānaṃ pradhānataḥ ।। kathayiṣyāmi caritaṃ tan mamākhyātum arhasi ।। yogayuktaḥ samādhāya vāsudeve manaḥ sadā ।।
kathaṃ tu nābhavan muktir yadābhūt sa dvijaḥ punaḥ ।। pūrvakarmasvabhāvena tan mamākhyātum arhasi ।। uvāsa suciraṃ kālaṃ maitreya pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। avāpa paramāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ manasaś cāpi saṃyame ।।
kṛṣṇa viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśety āha rājā sa kevalam ।। vāsudeva namo astu te ।। iti rājāha bharato ।। etat padaṃ tadarthaṃ ca vinā nānyad acintayat ।।
nānyāni cakre karmāṇi niḥsaṅgo yogatāpasaḥ ।। sasnau tatra tadā cakre snānasyānantarakriyāḥ ।। āsannaprasavā brahmann ekaiva hariṇī vanāt ।। siṃhasya nādaḥ sumahān sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkaraḥ ।।
atyuccārohaṇenāsyā nadyāṃ garbhaḥ papāta saḥ ।। jagrāha sa nṛpo garbhāt patitaṃ mṛgapotakam ।। maitreya sāpi hariṇī papāta ca mamāra ca ।। mṛgapotaṃ samādāya punar āśramam āgataḥ ।।
poṣaṇaṃ puṣyamāṇaś ca sa tena vavṛdhe mune ।। dūraṃ gatvā ca śārdūlatrāsād abhyāyayau punaḥ ।। punaś ca bharatasyābhūd āśramasyoṭajājire ।। āsīc cetaḥ samāsaktaṃ na yayāv anyato dvija ।।
mamatvaṃ sa cakāroccais tasmin hariṇabālake ।। cirāyamāṇe niṣkrānte tasyāsīd iti mānasam ।। eṣā vasumatī tasya khurāgrakṣatakarburā ।। kṣemeṇābhyāgato araṇyād api māṃ sukhayiṣyati ।।
kuśakāśā virājante baṭavaḥ sāmagā iva ।। prītiprasannavadanaḥ pārśvasthe cābhavan mṛge ।। saṃtyaktarājyabhogarddhisvajanasyāpi bhūpateḥ ।। mṛgapote abhavac cittaṃ sthairyavat tasya bhūpateḥ ।।
piteva sāsraṃ putreṇa mṛgapotena vīkṣitaḥ ।। tanmayatvena maitreya nānyat kiṃcid acintayat ।। jambūmārge mahāraṇye jajñe jātismaro mṛgaḥ ।। vihāya mātaraṃ bhūyaḥ sālagrāmam upāyayau ।।
mṛgatvahetubhūtasya karmaṇo niṣkṛtiṃ yayau ।। sadācāravatāṃ śuddhe yogināṃ pravare kule ।। apaśyat sa ca maitreya ātmānaṃ prakṛteḥ param ।। sarvabhūtāny abhedena dadarśa sa mahāmatiḥ ।।
na dadarśa ca karmāṇi śāstrāṇi jagṛhe na ca ।। tad apy asaṃskāraguṇaṃ grāmyavākyoktisaṃśritam ।। klinnadantāntaraḥ sarvaiḥ paribhūtaḥ sa nāgaraiḥ ।। janenāvamato yogī yogasiddhiṃ ca vindati ।।
janā yathāvamanyeran gaccheyur naiva saṃgatim ।। ātmānaṃ darśayām āsa jaḍonmattākṛtiṃ jane ।। yad yad āpnoti subahu tad atte kālasaṃyamam ।। kāritaḥ kṣetrakarmādi kadannāhārapoṣitaḥ ।।
sarvalokopakaraṇaṃ babhūvāhāravetanaḥ ।। kṣattā sauvīrarājasya viṣṭiyogyam amanyata ।। kālyai paśum ayojayat ।। rātrau taṃ samalaṃkṛtya vaiśaṃsanavidhānataḥ ।।
adhiṣṭhitaṃ mahākālī jñātvā yogeśvaraṃ tadā ।। tataḥ khaḍgaṃ samādāya niśitaṃ niśi sā tadā ।। kṣattāraṃ krūrakarmāṇam acchinat kaṇṭhamūlataḥ ।। piśitārthaparikaraiḥ papau rudhiram ulbaṇam ।।
tataḥ sauvīrarājasya prayātasya mahātmanaḥ ।। viṣṭikartātha taṃ tatra viṣṭiyogyo ayam ity api ।। kṣattā sauvīrarājasya ।। babhūvekṣumatītīre kapilarṣer varāśramam ।।
praṣṭuṃ taṃ mokṣadharmajñaṃ kapilākhyaṃ mahāmunim ।। nṛṇāṃ viṣṭigṛhītānām anyeṣāṃ so api madhyagaḥ ।। jātismaro asau pāpasya kṣayakāma uvāha tām ।। kurvan matimatāṃ śreṣṭhas te tv anye tvaritaṃ yayuḥ ।।
kim etad ity āha samaṃ gamyatāṃ śibikāvahāḥ ।। nṛpaḥ kim etad ity āha bhavadbhir gamyate anyathā ।। śibikodvāhakāḥ procur ayaṃ yātīty asatvaram ।। kim āyāsasaho na tvaṃ pīvān asi nirīkṣyase ।।
na śrānto asmi na cāyāsaḥ soḍhavyo asti mahīpate ।। śramaś ca bhārodvahane bhavaty eva hi dehinām ।। balavān abalaś ceti vācyaṃ paścād viśeṣaṇam ।। mithyaitad atra tu bhavāñ śṛṇotu vacanaṃ mama ।।
ūrū jaṅghādvayāvasthau tadādhāraṃ tathodaram ।। skandhāśriteyaṃ śibikā mama bhāro atra kiṃ kṛtaḥ ।। tatra tvam aham apy atra procyate cedam anyathā ।। guṇapravāhapatito bhūtavargo api yāty ayam ।।
avidyāsaṃcitaṃ karma tac cāśeṣeṣu jantuṣu ।। pravṛddhyapacayau nāsya ekasyākhilajantuṣu ।। tadā pīvān asītītthaṃ kayā yuktyā tvayeritam ।। śibikeyaṃ yadā skandhe tadā bhāraḥ samas tvayā ।।
śailadrumagṛhottho api pṛthivīsaṃbhavo api vā ।। voḍhavyas tu tadā bhāraḥ katamo nṛpate mayā ।। bhavato me akhilasyāsya mamatvenopabṛṃhitaḥ ।। so api rājāvatīryorvyāṃ tatpādau jagṛhe tvaran ।।
kathyatāṃ ko bhavān atra jālmarūpadharaḥ sthitaḥ ।। tat sarvaṃ kathyatāṃ vidvan mahyaṃ śuśrūṣave tvayā ।। upabhoganimittaṃ ca sarvatrāgamanakriyā ।। dharmādharmodbhavau bhoktuṃ jantur dehādim ṛcchati ।।
dharmādharmau yatas tasmāt kāraṇaṃ pṛcchyate kutaḥ ।। upabhoganimittaṃ ca dehīdeśāntarāgamaḥ ।। vaktuṃ na śakyate śrotuṃ tan mamecchā pravartate ।। ātmany eva na doṣāya śabdo aham iti yo dvija ।।
anātmany ātmavijñānaṃ śabdo vā bhrāntilakṣaṇaḥ ।। ete nāhaṃ yataḥ sarve vāṅniṣpādanahetavaḥ ।। tathāpi vāṅ nāham etad vaktum itthaṃ na yujyate ।। tato aham iti kutraitāṃ saṃjñāṃ rājan karomy aham ।।
tadaiṣo aham ayaṃ cānyo vaktum evam apīṣyate ।। tadā hi ko bhavān ko aham ity etad viphalaṃ vacaḥ ।। ayaṃ ca bhavato loko na sad etan nṛpocyate ।। kva vṛkṣasaṃjñā yātā syād dārusaṃjñātha vā nṛpa ।।
na ca dāruṇi sarvas tvāṃ bravīti śibikāgatam ।। anviṣyatāṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha tadbhede śibikā tvayā ।। kva yātaṃ chatram ity eṣa nyāyas tvayi tathā mayi ।। deheṣu lokasaṃjñeyaṃ vijñeyā karmahetuṣu ।।
śarīrākṛtibhedās tu bhūpaite karmayonayaḥ ।। tathānyac ca nṛpetthaṃ tan na satsaṃkalpanāmayam ।। pariṇāmādisaṃbhūtaṃ tad vastu nṛpa tac ca kim ।। patnyāḥ patiḥ pitā sūnoḥ kaṃ tvāṃ bhūpa vadāmy aham ।।
kim u pādādikaṃ tvaṃ vai tavaitat kiṃ mahīpate ।। ko aham ity eva nipuṇo bhūtvā cintaya pārthiva ।। pṛthakkaraṇaniṣpādyaṃ śakyate nṛpate katham ।। praśrayāvanato bhūtvā tam āha nṛpatir dvijam ।।
nāham ityādivākyena pramāṇāsaṃbhave gate ।। prameyāsaṃbhavāśaṅkī bhūyo bhūyo atha pṛcchati ।। śrute tasmin bhramantīva manaso mama vṛttayaḥ ।। bhavatā darśitaṃ vipra tat paraṃ prakṛter mahat ।।
śarīram anyad asmatto yeneyaṃ śibikā dhṛtā ।। pravartante guṇāś caite kiṃ mameti tvayoditam ।। mano vihvalatām eti paramārthārthitāṃ gatam ।। praṣṭum abhyudyato gatvā śreyaḥ kiṃ nv ity asaṃśayam ।।
tenaiva paramārthārthaṃ tvayi cetaḥ pradhāvati ।। viṣṇor aṃśo jaganmohanāśāyorvīm upāgataḥ ।। pratyakṣatām atra gato yathaitad bhavatocyate ।। tad vadākhilavijñānajalavīcyudadhir bhavān ।।
śreyāṃsy aparamārthāni aśeṣāṇy eva bhūpate ।। putrān icchati rājyaṃ ca śreyas tatprāptilakṣaṇam ।। śreyaḥ pradhānaṃ ca phale tad evānabhisaṃhite ।। śreyas tasyaiva saṃyogaḥ śreyo yaḥ paramātmanaḥ ।।
santy atra paramārthās tu na tv ete śrūyatāṃ ca me ।। vyayaś ca kriyate kasmāt kāmaprāptyupalakṣaṇaḥ ।। paramārthabhūtaḥ so anyasya paramārtho hi tatpitā ।। paramārtho hi kāryāṇi kāraṇānām aśeṣataḥ ।।
paramārthā bhavanty atra na bhavanti ca vai tataḥ ।। paramārthabhūtaṃ tatrāpi śrūyatāṃ gadato mama ।। tat kāraṇānugamanāj jñāyate nṛpa mṛṇmayam ।। niṣpādyate kriyā yā tu sā bhavitrī vināśinī ।।
tat tu nāśi na saṃdeho nāśidravyopapāditam ।। muktisādhanabhūtatvāt paramārtho na sādhanam ।। bhedakāri parebhyas tat paramārtho na bhedavān ।। mithyaitad anyadravyaṃ hi naiti taddravyatāṃ yataḥ ।।
paramārthas tu bhūpāla saṃkṣepāc chrūyatāṃ mama ।। janmavṛddhyādirahita ātmā sarvagato avyayaḥ ।। na yogavān na yukto abhūn naiva pārthiva yokṣyati ।। vijñānaṃ paramārtho asau dvaitino atattvadarśinaḥ ।।
abhedavyāpino vāyos tathā tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। devādibhede apadhvaste nāsty evāvaraṇo hi saḥ ।। pratyuvācātha vipro asāv advaitāntargatāṃ kathām ।। avabodhaṃ janayatā nidāghasya dvijanmanaḥ ।।
vijñātatattvasadbhāvo nisargād eva bhūpate ।। pramāṇatarkataḥ samyak māne meye api niścite ।। prādād aśeṣavijñānaṃ sa tasmai parayā mudā ।। sa ṛbhus tarkayām āsa nidāghasya nareśvara ।।
samṛddham atiramyaṃ ca pulastyena niveśitam ।। nidāgho nāma yogajña ṛbhuśiṣyo avasat purā ।। jagāma sa ṛbhuḥ śiṣyaṃ nidāgham avalokitum ।। sthitas tena gṛhītārgho nijaveśmapraveśitaḥ ।।
uvāca sa dvijaśreṣṭho bhujyatām iti sādaram ।। tat kathyatāṃ kadanneṣu na prītiḥ satataṃ mama ।। yad rocate dvijaśreṣṭha tat tvaṃ bhuṅkṣva yathecchayā ।। saṃyāvapāyasādīni drapsaphāṇitavanti ca ।।
bhakṣyopasādhanaṃ miṣṭaṃ tenāsyānnaṃ prasādhaya ।। prasādhitavatī tad vai bhartur vacanagauravāt ।। nidāghaḥ prāha bhūpāla praśrayāvanataḥ sthitaḥ ।। api te mānasaṃ svastham āhāreṇa kṛtaṃ dvija ।।
āgamyate ca bhavatā yatas tac ca dvijocyatām ।। na me kṣud abhavat tṛptiṃ kasmān māṃ paripṛcchasi ।। bhavaty ambhasi ca kṣīṇe nṛṇāṃ tṛḍ api jāyate ।। tataḥ kṣutsaṃbhavābhāvāt tṛptir asty eva me sadā ।।
cetaso yasya tat pṛccha pumān ebhir na yujyate ।। kutaś cāgamyate tatra tritaye api nibodha me ।। kutaḥ kutra kva gantāsīty etad apy arthavat katham ।। tvaṃ cānye ca na ca tvaṃ ca nānye naivāham apy aham ।।
kiṃ vakṣyatīti tatrāpi śrūyatāṃ dvijasattama ।। mṛṣṭam eva yadāmṛṣṭaṃ tad evodvegakāraṇam ।। ādimadhyāvasāneṣu kim annaṃ rucikārakam ।। pārthivo ayaṃ tathā dehaḥ pārthivaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ ।।
ālipta āpyāyayataḥ puṃso bhogo atra kiṃ kṛtaḥ ।। guḍaṃ phalādīni tathā pārthivāḥ paramāṇavaḥ ।। tan manaḥ samatālambi kāryaṃ sāmyaṃ hi muktaye ।। praṇipatya mahābhāgo nidāgho vākyam abravīt ।।
naṣṭo mohas tavākarṇya vacāṃsy etāni me dvija ।। ihāgato ahaṃ yāsyāmi paramārthas tavoditaḥ ।। vāsudevābhidheyasya svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।। pūjitaḥ parayā bhaktyā icchātaḥ prayayāv ṛbhuḥ ।।
nidāghajñānadānāya tad eva nagaraṃ yayau ।। mahābalaparīvāre puraṃ viśati pārthive ।। kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭham āyāntam araṇyāt sasamitkuśam ।। uvāca kasmād ekānte sthīyate bhavatā dvija ।।
pravivikṣau puraṃ ramyaṃ tenātra sthīyate mayā ।। kathyatāṃ me dvijaśreṣṭha tvam abhijño mato mama ।। adhirūḍho narendro ayaṃ parilokas tathetaraḥ ।। bhavatā na viśeṣeṇa pṛthakcihnopalakṣaṇau ।।
jñātum icchāmy ahaṃ ko atra gajaḥ ko vā narādhipaḥ ।। vāhyavāhakasaṃbandhaṃ ko na jānāti vai dvija ।। adhaḥśabdanigadyaṃ kiṃ kiṃ cordhvam abhidhīyate ।। śrūyatāṃ kathayāmy eṣa yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi ।।
avabodhāya te brahman dṛṣṭānto darśito mayā ।। tad eva tvaṃ mamācakṣva katamas tvam ahaṃ tathā ।। nidāghaḥ prāha bhagavān ācāryas tvam ṛbhur dhruvam ।। yathācāryasya tena tvāṃ manye prāptam ahaṃ gurum ।।
gurus te aham ṛbhur nāmnā nidāgha samupāgataḥ ।। paramārthasārabhūtaṃ yad advaitam aśeṣataḥ ।। nidāgho apy upadeśena tenādvaitaparo abhavat ।। tathā brahma tato muktim avāpa paramāṃ dvijaḥ ।।
bhava sarvagataṃ jānann ātmānam avanīpate ।। bhrāntadṛṣṭibhir ātmāpi tathaikaḥ san pṛthak pṛthak ।। so ahaṃ sa ca tvaṃ sa ca sarvam etad ātmasvarūpaṃ tyaja bhedamoham ।। sa cāpi jātismaraṇāptabodhas tatraiva janmany apavargam āpa ।।
sa vimalamatir eti nātmamohaṃ bhavati ca saṃsaraṇeṣu muktiyogyaḥ ।। sūryādīnāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ jyotiṣām api vistarāt ।। cāturvarṇyasya cotpattis tiryagyonigatasya ca ।। manvantarāṇy aśeṣāṇi śrotum icchāmy anukramāt ।।
bhavatā kathitān etāñ śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ guro ।। tāny ahaṃ bhavate samyak kathayāmi yathākramam ।। uttamas tāmasaś caiva raivataś cākṣuṣas tathā ।। vaivasvato ayaṃ yasyaitat saptamaṃ vartate antaram ।।
devās tatrarṣayaś caiva yathāvat kathitā mayā ।। manvantarādhipān samyag devarṣīṃs tatsutāṃs tathā ।। vipaścit tatra devendro maitreyāsīn mahābalaḥ ।। niścaraś cārvarīvāṃś ca tatra saptarṣayo abhavan ।।
dvitīyam etat kathitam antaraṃ śṛṇu cottaram ।। suśāntir nāma devendro maitreyābhūt sureśvaraḥ ।। vaśavartinaś ca pañcaite gaṇā dvādaśakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ajaḥ paraśudivyādyās tathottamamanoḥ sutāḥ ।।
satyāś ca sudhiyaś caiva saptaviṃśatikā gaṇāḥ ।। saptarṣayaś ca ye teṣāṃ tatra nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। pīvaraś carṣayo hy ete sapta tatrāpi cāntare ।। putrās tu tāmasasyāsan rājānaḥ sumahābalāḥ ।।
manur vibhuś ca tatrendro devāṃś caivāntare śṛṇu ।। ete devagaṇās tatra caturdaśa caturdaśa ।। ete saptarṣayo vipra tatrāsan raivate antare ।। narendrāḥ sumahāvīryā babhūvur munisattama ।।
priyavratānvayā hy ete catvāro manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। manvantarādhipān etāṃl labdhavān ātmavaṃśajān ।। manojavas tathaivendro devān api nibodha me ।। mahānubhāvā lekhāś ca pañcaite hy aṣṭakā gaṇāḥ ।।
atināmā sahiṣṇuś ca saptāsann iti carṣayaḥ ।। cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthivīpatayo abhavan ।। manuḥ saṃvartate dhīmān sāmprataṃ saptame antare ।। puraṃdaras tathaivātra maitreya tridaśeśvaraḥ ।।
viśvāmitrabharadvājau sapta saptarṣayo atra tu ।। nariṣyantaś ca vikhyāto nābhāgo diṣṭa eva ca ।। manor vaivasvatasyaite nava putrāḥ sudhārmikāḥ ।। manvantareṣv aśeṣeṣu devatvenādhitiṣṭhati ।।
ākūtyāṃ mānaso deva utpannaḥ prathame antare ।। tuṣitāyāṃ samutpanno hy ajitas tuṣitaiḥ saha ।। satyāyām abhavat satyaḥ satyaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ ।। haryāyāṃ haribhiḥ sārdhaṃ harir eva babhūva ha ।।
saṃbhūto rājasaiḥ sārdhaṃ devair devavaro hariḥ ।। vikuṇṭhāyām asau jajñe vaikuṇṭhair daivataiḥ saha ।। vāmanaḥ kaśyapād viṣṇur adityāṃ saṃbabhūva ha ।। puraṃdarāya trailokyaṃ dattaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam ।।
saptasv evābhavan vipra yābhiḥ saṃrakṣitāḥ prajāḥ ।। tasmāt sa procyate viṣṇur viśer dhātoḥ praveśanāt ।। indraś ca yo yas tridaśeśabhūto viṣṇor aśeṣās tu vibhūtayas tāḥ ।। bhaviṣyāṇy api viprarṣe mamākhyātuṃ tvam arhasi ।।
manur yamo yamī caiva tadapatyāni vai mune ।। bhartuḥ śuśrūṣaṇe araṇyaṃ svayaṃ ca tapase yayau ।। śanaiścaraṃ manuṃ cānyaṃ tapatīṃ cāpy ajījanat ।। tadānyeyam asau buddhir ity āsīd yamasūryayoḥ ।।
samādhidṛṣṭyā dadṛśe tām aśvāṃ tapasi sthitām ।। janayām āsa revantaṃ retaso ante ca bhāskaraḥ ।। tejasaḥ śamanaṃ cāsya viśvakarmā cakāra ha ।। kṛtavān aṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ na vyaśātayatāvyayam ।।
jājvalyamānam apatat tad bhūmau munisattama ।। triśūlaṃ caiva śarvasya śibikāṃ dhanadasya ca ।। tat sarvaṃ tejasā tena viśvakarmā vyavardhayat ।। pūrvajasya savarṇo asau sāvarṇis tena kathyate ।।
tac chṛṇuṣva mahābhāga bhaviṣyaṃ kathayāmi te ।। sutapāś cāmitābhāś ca mukhyāś cāpi tadā surāḥ ।। saptarṣīn api vakṣyāmi bhaviṣyān munisattama ।। matputraś ca tathā vyāsa ṛśyaśṛṅgaś ca saptamaḥ ।।
virocanasutas teṣāṃ balir indro bhaviṣyati ।। sāvarṇes tu manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti nareśvarāḥ ।। navamo dakṣasāvarṇir maitreya bhavitā manuḥ ।। bhaviṣyanti tadā devā ekaiko dvādaśo gaṇaḥ ।।
teṣām indro mahāvīryo bhaviṣyaty adbhuto dvija ।। jyotiṣmān saptamaḥ satyas tatraite ca maharṣayaḥ ।। pṛthuśravādyāś ca tathā dakṣasāvarṇikātmajāḥ ।। sudhāmāno viruddhāś ca śatasaṃkhyās tathā surāḥ ।।
saptarṣayo bhaviṣyanti ye tadā tāñ chṛṇuṣva ca ।। nābhāgo apratimaujāś ca satyaketus tathaiva ca ।। brahmasāvarṇiputrās tu rakṣiṣyanti vasuṃdharām ।। ekādaśaś ca bhavitā dharmasāvarṇiko manuḥ ।।
ekaikas triṃśakas teṣāṃ gaṇaś cendraś ca vai vṛṣaḥ ।। haviṣmān anaghaś caite bhavyāḥ saptarṣayas tathā ।। bhaviṣyanti manos tasya tanayāḥ pṛthivīśvarāḥ ।। ṛtadhāmā ca tatrendro bhavitā śṛṇu me surān ।।
sukarmāṇaḥ supārāś ca daśakāḥ pañca vai gaṇāḥ ।। tapodhṛtir dyutiś cānyaḥ saptamas tu tapodhanaḥ ।। manos tasya mahāvīryā bhaviṣyanti sutā nṛpāḥ ।। trayodaśo raucyanāmā bhaviṣyati mune manuḥ ।।
trayas triṃśadvibhedās te devānāṃ ye tu vai gaṇāḥ ।। divaspatir mahāvīryas teṣām indro bhaviṣyati ।। saptarṣayas tv ime tasya putrān api nibodha me ।। citrasenavicitrādyā bhaviṣyanti mahīkṣitaḥ ।।
śucir indraḥ suragaṇās tatra pañca śṛṇuṣva tān ।। vācāvṛddhāś ca vai devāḥ saptarṣīn api me śṛṇu ।। yuktas tathā jitaś cānyo manuputrān ataḥ śṛṇu ।। kathitā muniśārdūla pālayiṣyanti ye mahīm ।।
pravartayanti tān etya bhuvi saptarṣayo divaḥ ।। devā yajñabhujas te tu yāvan manvantaraṃ tu tat ।। tadanvayodbhavaiś caiva tāvad bhūḥ paripālyate ।। manvantare bhavanty ete śakraś caivādhikāriṇaḥ ।।
sahasrayugaparyantaḥ kalpo niḥśeṣa ucyate ।। brahmarūpadharaḥ śete śeṣāhāv ambusaṃplave ।। svamāyāsaṃsthito vipra sarvabhūto janārdanaḥ ।। sṛṣṭiṃ karoty avyayātmā kalpe kalpe rajoguṇaḥ ।।
sāttviko aṃśaḥ sthitikaro jagato dvijasattama ।। yugavyavasthāṃ kurute yathā maitreya tac chṛṇu ।। dadāti sarvabhūtātmā sarvabhūtahite rataḥ ।। duṣṭānāṃ nigrahaṃ kurvan paripāti jagattrayam ।।
karoti bahulaṃ bhūyo vedavyāsasvarūpadhṛk ।। kalkisvarūpī durvṛttān mārge sthāpayati prabhuḥ ।। hanti cānteṣv anantātmā nāsty asmād vyatireki yat ।। tad atrānyatra vā vipra sadbhāvaḥ kathitas tava ।।
manvantarādhipāṃś caiva kim anyat kathayāmi te ।। viṣṇur viṣṇau viṣṇutaś ca na paraṃ vidyate tataḥ ।। vedavyāsasvarūpeṇa yathā tena yuge yuge ।। taṃ tam ācakṣva bhagavañ śākhābhedāṃś ca me vada ।।
na śakyo vistaro vaktuṃ saṃkṣepeṇa śṛṇuṣva tam ।। vedam ekaṃ sa bahudhā kurute jagato hitaḥ ।। hitāya sarvabhūtānāṃ vedabhedān karoti saḥ ।। vedavyāsābhidhānā tu sā mūrtir madhuvidviṣaḥ ।।
yathā ca bhedaḥ śākhānāṃ vyāsena kriyate mune ।। vaivasvate antare tasmin dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।। caturdhā yaiḥ kṛto vedo dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।। dvitīye dvāpare caiva vedavyāsaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
savitā pañcame vyāso mṛtyuḥ ṣaṣṭhe smṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ।। sārasvataś ca navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ ।। trayodaśe cāntarikṣo varṇī cāpi caturdaśe ।। kratuṃjayaḥ saptadaśe ṛṇajyo aṣṭādaśe smṛtaḥ ।।
gautamād uttamo vyāso haryātmā yo abhidhīyate ।। somaḥ śuṣmāyaṇas tasmāt tṛṇabindur iti smṛtaḥ ।। tasmād asmatpitā śaktir vyāsas tasmād ahaṃ mune ।। aṣṭāviṃśatir ity ete vedavyāsāḥ purātanāḥ ।।
eko vedaś caturdhā tu yaiḥ kṛto dvāparādiṣu ।। vyatīte mama putre asmin kṛṣṇadvaipāyane munau ।। bṛhatvād bṛṃhaṇatvāc ca tad brahmety abhidhīyate ।। ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvāṇaṃ yat tasmai brahmaṇe namaḥ ।।
mahataḥ paramaṃ guhyaṃ tasmai subrahmaṇe namaḥ ।। saṃprakāśapravṛttibhyāṃ puruṣārthaprayojanam ।। yat tad avyaktam amṛtaṃ pravṛttir brahma śāśvatam ।। avibhāgaṃ tathā śukram akṣaraṃ bahudhātmakam ।।
yad rūpaṃ vāsudevasya paramātmasvarūpiṇaḥ ।। sarvabhūteṣv abhedo asau bhidyate bhinnabuddhibhiḥ ।। ṛgyajuḥsāmasārātmā sa evātmā śarīriṇām ।। śākhāpraṇetā sa samastaśākhā jñānasvarūpo bhagavān anantaḥ ।।
tato daśaguṇaḥ kṛtsno yajño ayaṃ sarvakāmadhuk ।। vedam ekaṃ catuṣpādaṃ caturdhā vyabhajat prabhuḥ ।। vedās tathā samastais tair vyastā vyāsais tathā mayā ।। caturyugeṣu racitān samasteṣv avadhāraya ।।
ko anyo hi bhuvi maitreya mahābhāratakṛd bhavet ।। dvāpare hy atra maitreya tan me śṛṇu yathārthataḥ ।। atha śiṣyān sa jagrāha caturo vedapāragān ।। vaiśampāyananāmānaṃ yajurvedasya cāgrahīt ।।
sumantus tasya śiṣyo abhūd vedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ ।। sūtaṃ jagrāha śiṣyaṃ sa itihāsapurāṇayoḥ ।। ārṣādi bahudhā sthānaṃ devarṣiracitāśrayam ।। itihāsam iti proktaṃ sthaviṣṭhādbhutakarmayuk ।।
cāturhotram abhūd yasmiṃs tena yajñam athākarot ।। audgātraṃ sāmabhiś cakre brahmatvaṃ cāpy atharvabhiḥ ।। yajūṃṣi ca yajurvedaṃ sāmavedaṃ ca sāmabhiḥ ।। kārayām āsa maitreya brahmatvaṃ ca yathāsthitiḥ ।।
caturdhā tu tato jātaṃ vedapādapakānanam ।। indrapramataye prādād bāṣkalāya ca saṃhite ।। baudhyādibhyo dadau tās tu śiṣyebhyaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ ।। pratiśākhās tu śākhāyās tasyās te jagṛhur mune ।।
māṇḍukeyaṃ mahātmānaṃ maitreyādhyāpayat tadā ।। tasya śiṣyapraśiṣyebhyaḥ putraśiṣyān kramād yayau ।। cakāra saṃhitāḥ pañca śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau ca tāḥ ।। śiśiraḥ pañcamaś cāsīt maitreya sumahāmuniḥ ।।
etāni pañcanāmāni saṃhitāyāḥ samāśritāḥ ।। niruktam akarot tadvac caturthaṃ munisattama ।। niruktaś ca caturtho abhūd vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।। śiṣyaḥ kālāyanir gārgyas tṛtīyaś ca tathā javaḥ ।।
ity ete bahvṛcāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ pravartitāḥ ।। vaiśampāyananāmāsau vyāsaśiṣyaś cakāra vai ।। śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau tāś ca jagṛhus te apy anukramāt ।। śiṣyaḥ paramadharmajño guruvṛttiparaḥ sadā ।।
tasya vai saptarātrāt tu brahmahatyā bhaviṣyati ।। vaiśampāyana ekas tu taṃ vyatikrāntavāṃs tadā ।। svasrīyaṃ bālakaṃ so atha padā spṛṣṭam aghātayat ।। caradhvaṃ matkṛte sarve na vicāryam idaṃ tathā ।।
kleśitair alpatejobhiś cariṣye aham idaṃ vratam ।। mucyatāṃ yat tvayādhītaṃ matto viprāvamānaka ।। tena śiṣyeṇa nārtho asti mamājñābhaṅgakāriṇā ।। mamāpy alaṃ tvayādhītaṃ yan mayā tad idaṃ dvija ।।
chardayitvā dadau tasmai yayau ca svecchayā muniḥ ।। jagṛhus tittirībhūtvā taittirīyās tu te tataḥ ।। carakādhvaryavas te tu caraṇān munisattama ।। tuṣṭāva praṇataḥ sūryaṃ yajūṃṣy abhilaṣaṃs tataḥ ।।
ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūtāya trayīdhāmavate namaḥ ।। bhāskarāya paraṃ tejaḥ sauṣumṇam uru bibhrate ।। dhyeyāya viṣṇurūpāya paramākṣararūpiṇe ।। svadhāmṛtena ca pitṝṃs tasmai tṛptyātmane namaḥ ।।
namo agnīsomabhūtāya sarvasiddhikarāya ca ।। tasmai trikālabhūtāya namaḥ sūryāya vedhase ।। sattvadhāmadharo devo namas tasmai vivasvate ।। yasminn anudite tasmai namo devāya bhāsvate ।।
pavitratākāraṇāya tasmai śuddhātmane namaḥ ।। ādityāyādibhūtāya devādīnāṃ namo namaḥ ।। vahanti bhuvanālokacakṣuṣas taṃ namāmy aham ।। vājirūpadharaḥ prāha vrīyatām iti vāñchitam ।।
yajūṃṣi tāni me dehi yāni santi na me gurau ।। ayātayāmasaṃjñāni yāni vetti na tadguruḥ ।। vājinas te samākhyātāḥ sūryo aśvaḥ so abhavad yataḥ ।। kaṇvādyāḥ sumahābhāgā yājñavalkyapravartitāḥ ।।
krameṇa yena maitreya bibheda śṛṇu tan mama ।। ṛgyajuḥśākhiśākho ayaṃ śākhāsaṃkhyyā prapañcitā ।। sāmātharvapurāṇoktaṃ śākhāsaṃjñātha kathyate ।। adhītavantāv ekaikāṃ saṃhitāṃ tau mahāmunī ।।
cakāra taṃ ca tacchiṣyau jagṛhāte mahāvratau ।। putram adhyāpayām āsa sumantum atha jaiminiḥ ।। sumantuś capi sumulaṃ putram adhyāpayan muniḥ ।। udīcyāḥ sāmagāḥ śiṣyās tasya pañcadaśa smṛtāḥ ।।
gṛhītās te api cocyante paṇḍitaiḥ prācyasāmagāḥ ।। pauṣpiñjiśiṣyās tadbhedaiḥ saṃhitā bahulīkṛtāḥ ।। provāca kṛtināmāsau śiṣyebhyaḥ sumahāmatiḥ ।। atharvavedaṃ sa muniḥ sumantur amitadyutiḥ ।।
kṛtvā tu devadarśāya tathā pathyāya dattavān ।। śaulkāyaniḥ pippalādas tathānyo munisattama ।। jājaliḥ kumudādiś ca tṛtīyaḥ śaunako dvija ।। dvitīyāṃ saṃhitāṃ prādāt saindhavāya ca saṃjñine ।।
nakṣatrakalpo vedānāṃ saṃhitānāṃ tathaiva ca ।। śreṣṭhās tv atharvaṇām ete saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakāḥ ।। purāṇasaṃhitāṃ cakre purāṇārthaviśāradaḥ ।। svayaṃ dṛṣṭvārthakathanaṃ prāhur ākhyānakaṃ budhāḥ ।।
śrutasyārthasya kathanam upākhyānaṃ pracakṣate ।। purāṇasaṃhitāṃ tasmai dadau vyāso mahāmuniḥ ।। akṛtavraṇo atha sāvarṇiḥ ṣaṭ śiṣyās tasya cābhavan ।। romaharṣaṇikā cānyā tisṝṇāṃ mūlasaṃhitā ।।
catuṣṭayenāpy etena saṃhitānām idaṃ mune ।। aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni purāṇajñāḥ pracakṣate ।। tathānyaṃ nāradīyaṃ ca mārkaṇḍeyaṃ ca saptamam ।। daśamaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ laiṅgam ekādaśaṃ smṛtam ।।
mātsyaṃ ca gāruḍaṃ caiva brahmāṇḍaṃ ca tataḥ param ।। mahāpurāṇāny etāni hy aṣṭādaśa mahāmune ।। tathā copapurāṇāni munibhiḥ kathitāni ca ।। sarveṣv eteṣu kathyante vaṃśānucaritaṃ ca yat ।।
etad vaiṣṇavasaṃjñaṃ vai pādmasya samanantaram ।। kathyate bhagavān viṣṇur aśeṣeṣv eva sattama ।। purāṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca vidyā hy etāś caturdaśa ।। arthaśāstraṃ caturthaṃ tu vidyā hy aṣṭādaśaiva tāḥ ।।
rājarṣayaḥ punas tebhya ṛṣiprakṛtayas trayaḥ ।। kartāraś caiva śākhānāṃ bhedahetus tathoditaḥ ।। sarvamanvantareṣv evaṃ śākhābhedāḥ samāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। prājāpatyā śrutir nityā tadvikalpās tv ime dvija ।।
maitreya vedasaṃbaddhaṃ kim anyat kathayāmi te ।। śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ tv ekaṃ tad bhavān prabravītu me ।। vedarāśir apāro asāv uktaḥ śākhāvibhāgataḥ ।। xxxx paro dharmo varṇādīnām athocyate ।।
sapta lokāś ca ye antaḥsthā brahmāṇḍasyāsya sarvataḥ ।। sthūlaiḥ sthūlataraiś caitat sarvaṃ prāṇibhir āvṛtam ।। na santi prāṇino yatra karmabandhanibandhanāḥ ।। āyuṣo ante tato yānti yātanās tatpracoditāḥ ।।
jantavaḥ parivartante śāstrāṇām eṣa nirṇayaḥ ।। na bhavanti narā yena tat karma kathayāmalam ।। pṛṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ prāha bhīṣmo yat tac chṛṇuṣva me ।। mām uvāca sa pṛṣṭo vai mayā jātismaro muniḥ ।।
tathā ca tad abhūd vatsa yathoktaṃ tena dhīmatā ।। yad yad āha na tad dṛṣṭam anyathā hi mayā kvacit ।। prāha kāliṅgako vipraḥ smṛtvā tasya muner vacaḥ ।। yamakiṃkarayor yo abhūt saṃvādas taṃ bravīmi te ।।
narake pacyamānas tu yamena paribhāṣitaḥ ।। kiṃ tvayā nārcito devaḥ keśavaḥ kleśanāśanaḥ ।। parihara madhusūdanaprapannān prabhur aham anyanṛṇāṃ na vaiṣṇavānām ।। aham amaragaṇārcitena dhātrā yama iti lokahitāhite niyuktaḥ ।। b
sugatim abhilaṣāmi vāsudevād aham api bhāgavatasthitāntarātmā ।। b hariguruvaśago asmi na svatantraḥ prabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi viṣṇuḥ ।। d bhagavati vimukhasya nāsti siddhir viṣam amṛtaṃ bhavatīti naitad asti ।। bhavati hi harau sthitāntarātmā bhṛśamalino api virājate manuṣyaḥ ।।
mahad api suvicārya lokatantraṃ bhagavadupāsyam ṛte na siddhir asti ।। avihatagataye sanātanāya prathamajagatpataye namo astv ajāya ।। surapaśumanujādikalpanābhir harir akhilābhir udīryate tathaikaḥ ।। surapaśumanujādayas tathānte guṇakaluṣeṇa sanātanena tena ।।
tam apagatasamastapāpabandhaṃ vraja parihṛtya yathāgnim ājyasiktam ।। kathaya mama vibho samastadhātur bhavati hareḥ khalu yādṛśo asya bhaktaḥ ।। na harati na ca hanti kiṃcid uccaiḥ sitamanasaṃ tam avaihi viṣṇubhaktam ।। manasi kṛtajanārdanaṃ manuṣyaṃ satatam avaihi harer atīva bhaktam ।।
bhavati ca bhagavaty ananyacetāḥ puruṣavaraṃ tam avaihi viṣṇubhaktam ।। na hi tuhinamayūkharaśmipuñje bhavati hutāśanadīptijaḥ pratāpaḥ ।। priyahitavacano astamānamāyo vasati sadā hṛdi tasya vāsudevaḥ ।। kṣitirasam atiramyam ātmano antaḥ kathayati cārutayaiva śālapotaḥ ।।
apagatamadamānamatsarāṇāṃ vraja bhaṭa dūratareṇa mānavānām ।। tadagham aghavighātakartṛbhinnaṃ bhavati kathaṃ sati cāndhakāram arke ।। aśubhajanitadurmadasya puṃsaḥ kaluṣamater hṛdi tasya nāsty anantaḥ ।। na yajati na dadāti yaś ca santaṃ manasi na tasya janārdano adhamasya ।।
śaṭhamatir upayāti yo arthatṛṣṇāṃ tam adhamaceṣṭam avaihi nāsya bhaktam ।। anudinakṛtapāpabandhayatnaḥ puruṣapaśur na hi vāsudevabhaktaḥ ।। iti matir amalā bhavaty anante hṛdayagate vraja tān vihāya dūrāt ।। bhava śaraṇam itīrayanti ye vai tyaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa tān apāpān ।।
tava gatir athavā mamāsti cakra pratihatavīryabalasya so anyalokyaḥ ।। mama kathitam idaṃ ca tena tubhyaṃ kuruvara samyag idaṃ mayāpi coktam ।। kaliṅgadeśād abhyetya prīyatā sumahātmanā ।। yathā viṣṇum ṛte nānyat trāṇaṃ saṃsārasāgare ।।
samarthās tasya yasyātmā keśavālambanaḥ sadā ।। tvatpraśnānugataṃ samyak kim anyac chrotum icchasi ।। samākhyāhi jagannātho viṣṇur ārādhyate yathā ।। viṣṇubhaktādicihnaṃ yo nijadharmaḥ puroditaḥ ।।
tam evātisphuṭaṃ vaktuṃ pañcādhyāyī vidhīyate ।। yat prāpyate phalaṃ śrotuṃ tac cecchāmi mahāmune ।। aurvaḥ prāha yathā pṛṣṭas tan me kathayataḥ śṛṇu ।। viṣṇor ārādhanopāyasaṃbandhaṃ munisattama ।।
sa cāha pṛṣṭo yat tena tan maitreyākhilaṃ śṛṇu ।। prāpnoty ārādhite viṣṇau nirvāṇam api cottamam ।। tat tad āpnoti rājendra bhūri svalpam athāpi vā ।। tad ahaṃ sakalaṃ tubhyaṃ kathayāmi nibodha me ।।
viṣṇur ārādhyate panthā nānyas tattoṣakāraṇam ।। ghnaṃs tathānyān hinasty enaṃ sarvabhūto yato hariḥ ।। ārādhyate svavarṇoktadharmānuṣṭhānakāriṇā ।। svadharmatatparo viṣṇum ārādhayati nānyathā ।।
anyodvegakaraṃ vāpi toṣyate tena keśavaḥ ।। na karoti pumān bhūpa toṣyate tena keśavaḥ ।। yo manuṣyo manuṣyendra toṣyate tena keśavaḥ ।। toṣyate tena govindaḥ puruṣeṇa nareśvara ।।
hitakāmo haris tena toṣyate sarvadā sukham ।। viśuddhacetasā viṣṇus toṣyate tena sarvadā ।। teṣu tiṣṭhan naro viṣṇum ārādhayati nānyathā ।। tathaivāśramadharmāṃś ca dvijavarya bravīhi tān ।।
tvam ekāgramanā bhūtvā śṛṇu dharmān mayoditān ।। nityodakī bhaved vipraḥ kuryāc cāgniparigraham ।। kuryāt pratigrahādānaṃ gurvarthaṃ nyāyato dvijaḥ ।। maitrī samastabhūteṣu brāhmaṇasyottamaṃ dhanam ।।
ṛtāv abhigamaḥ patnyāṃ śasyate cāsya pārthiva ।। yajec ca vividhair yajñair adhīyīta ca pārthivaḥ ।। tasyāpi prathame kalpe pṛthivīparipālanam ।। bhavanti nṛpater aṃśā yato yajñādikarmaṇām ।।
prāpnoty abhimatāṃl lokān varṇasaṃsthākaro nṛpaḥ ।। vaiśyāya jīvikāṃ brahmā dadau lokapitāmahaḥ ।। nityanaimittikādīnām anuṣṭhānaṃ ca karmaṇām ।। krayavikrayajair vāpi dhanaiḥ kārūdbhavena vā ।।
śūdrasya sannatiḥ śaucaṃ sevā svāminy amāyayā ।। amantrayajñā hy aste ayaṃ tatsaṅgo viprarakṣaṇam ।। pitryādikaṃ ca vai sarvaṃ śūdraḥ kurvīta tena vai ।। ṛtukālābhigamanaṃ svadāreṣu mahīpate ।।
satyaṃ śaucam anāyāso maṅgalaṃ priyavāditā ।। śarīraṃ yā tṛtīyena svaśubhenāpi karmaṇā ।। atyantaṃ na tu kartavyam anāyāsaḥ sa ucyate ।। anasūyā ca sāmānyā varṇānāṃ kathitā guṇāḥ ।।
guṇāṃs tathāpaddharmāṃś ca viprādīnām imāñ chṛṇu ।। rājanyasya ca vaiśyoktaṃ śūdrakarma na caitayoḥ ।। tad evāpadi kartavyaṃ na kuryāt karmasaṃkaram ।। dharmam āśramiṇāṃ samyag bruvato me niśāmaya ।।
gurugehe vased bhūpa brahmacārī samāhitaḥ ।। vratāni caratā grāhyo vedaś ca kṛtabuddhinā ।। upatiṣṭhet tathā kuryād guror apy abhivādanam ।। śiṣyo gurau nṛpaśreṣṭha pratikūlaṃ na saṃcaret ।।
anujñātaś ca bhikṣānnam aśnīyād guruṇā tataḥ ।। samijjalādikaṃ cāsya kālyaṃ kālyam upānayet ।। gārhasthyam āvaset prājño niṣpannaguruniṣkṛtiḥ ।। gṛhasthakāryam akhilaṃ kuryād bhūpāla śaktitaḥ ।।
annair munīṃś ca svādhyāyair apatyena prajāpatim ।। prāpnoti lokān puruṣo nijakarmasamārjitān ।। te apy atraiva pratiṣṭhante gārhasthyaṃ tena vai param ।। aṭanti vasudhāṃ viprāḥ pṛthivīdarśanāya ca ।।
teṣāṃ gṛhasthaḥ sarveṣāṃ pratiṣṭhā yonir eva ca ।। gṛhāgatānāṃ dadyāc ca śayanāsanabhojanam ।। sa dattvā duṣkṛtaṃ tasmai puṇyam ādāya gacchati ।। paritāpopaghātau ca pāruṣyaṃ ca na śasyate ।।
sarvabandhavimukto asau lokān āpnoty anuttamān ।। putreṣu bhāryāṃ nikṣipya vanaṃ gacchet sahaiva vā ।। bhūmiśāyī bhavet tatra muniḥ sarvātithir nṛpa ।। tadvat triṣavaṇaṃ snānaṃ śastam asya nareśvara ।।
bhikṣābalipradānaṃ ca śastam asya nareśvara ।। tapasyataś ca rājendra śītoṣṇādisahiṣṇutā ।। sa dahaty agnivad doṣāñ jayel lokāṃś ca śāśvatān ।। tasya svarūpaṃ gadato mama śrotuṃ nṛpārhasi ।।
caturtham āśramasthānaṃ gacchen nirdhūtamatsaraḥ ।। mitrādiṣu samo maitraḥ samasteṣv eva jantuṣu ।। yuktaḥ kurvīta na drohaṃ sarvasaṅgāṃś ca varjayet ।। tathā tiṣṭhed yathā prītir dveṣo vā nāsya jāyate ।।
kāle praśastavarṇānāṃ bhikṣārthaṃ paryaṭed gṛhān ।। tāṃs tu doṣān parityajya parivrāḍ nirmamo bhavet ।। na tasya sarvabhūtebhyo bhayam utpadyate kvacit ।। vipras tu bhikṣopagatair havirbhiś citāgninā sa vrajati sma lokān ।।
anindhanaṃ jyotir iva praśāntaḥ sa brahmalokaṃ śrayate dvijātiḥ ।। puṃsaḥ kriyām ahaṃ śrotum icchāmi dvijasattama ।। samākhyāhi bhṛguśreṣṭha sarvajño hy asi me mataḥ ।। tad ahaṃ kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanā nṛpa ।।
putrasya kurvīta pitā śrāddhaṃ cābhyudayātmakam ।। yathāvṛtti tathā kuryād daivaṃ pitryaṃ dvijanmanām ।। nāndīmukhebhyas tīrthena dadyād daivena pārthiva ।। kurvīta tat tathāśeṣavṛddhikāleṣu bhūpate ।।
devapūrvaṃ narākhyaṃ hi śarmavarmādisaṃyutam ।। nāmadheyaṃ daśamyāṃ tu kecid icchanti pārthiva ।। dvādaśyām athavā rājan māse pūrṇe athavā pare ।। guptadāsātmakaṃ nāma praśastaṃ vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ ।।
nāmaṅgalyaṃ jugupsyaṃ vā nāma kuryāt samākṣaram ।। sukhoccāryaṃ tu tan nāma kuryād yat pravaṇākṣaram ।। yathoktaṃ vidhim āśritya kuryād vidyāparigraham ।। gārhasthyam icchan bhūpāla kuryād dāraparigraham ।।
guroḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ kuryāt tatputrāder athāpi vā ।। pūrvasaṃkalpitaṃ yādṛk tādṛk kuryān mahīpate ।। nātikeśām akeśāṃ vā nātikṛṣṇāṃ na piṅgalām ।। nāviśuddhāṃ saromāṃ vā akulajāṃ vātirogiṇīm ।।
na śmaśruvyañjanavatīṃ na caiva puruṣākṛtim ।। nātibaddhekṣaṇāṃ tadvad vṛttākṣīṃ nodvahet striyam ।। kūpo yasyā hasantyāś ca gaṇḍayos tāṃ ca nodvahet ।। nodvahet tādṛśīṃ kanyāṃ prājñaḥ kāryaviśāradaḥ ।।
āpīnahastapādāṃ ca na kanyām udvahed budhaḥ ।। na cāticchidradaśanāṃ na karālamukhīṃ naraḥ ।। gṛhasthas tūdvahet kanyāṃ nyāyyena vidhinā nṛpa ।। gāndharvarākṣasau cānyau paiśācaś cāṣṭamo adhamaḥ ।।
yajñeṣu ṛtvije daiva ādāyārṣas tu godvayam ।। sahau tau caratāṃ dharmaṃ prājāpatyo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। kurvīta dārāharaṇaṃ tenānyaṃ parivarjayet ।। samudvahed dadāty etat samyagūḍhaṃ mahāphalam ।।
lokād asmāt parasmāc ca yam ātiṣṭhan na hīyate ।। sadācāravatā puṃsā jitau lokāv ubhāv api ।। teṣām ācaraṇaṃ yat tu sadācāraḥ sa ucyate ।। sadācārasya vaktāraḥ kartāraś ca mahīpate ।।
vibuddhaś cintayed dharmam arthaṃ cāsyāvirodhinam ।। dṛṣṭādṛṣṭavināśāya trivarge samadarśitā ।। dharmam apy asukhodarkaṃ lokavikruṣṭam eva ca ।। tataḥ kalyaṃ samutthāya kuryān maitraṃ nareśvara ।।
dūrād āvasathān mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca samutsṛjet ।। pādāvasecanocchiṣṭe prakṣipen na gṛhāṅgaṇe ।। guruṃ dvijātīṃś ca budho na meheta kadācana ।। na vartmani na nadyāditīrtheṣu puruṣarṣabha ।।
utsargaṃ vai purīṣasya mūtrasya ca visarjanam ।। kurvītānāpadi prājño mūtrotsargaṃ ca pārthiva ।। tiṣṭhen nāticiraṃ tatra naiva kiṃcid udīrayet ।। śaucāvaśiṣṭāṃ gehāc ca nādadyāl lepasaṃbhavām ।।
parityajen mṛdaś caitāḥ sakalāḥ śaucasādhane ।। ekā liṅge gude tisro daśa vāmakare nṛpa ।। b ubhayor mṛdvayaṃ smṛtam ।। pañcāpāne gṛhasthasya ।।
hastadvaye ca saptānyā mṛdaḥ śaucopapādikāḥ ।। d ācāmeta mṛdaṃ bhūyas tathā dadyāt samāhitaḥ ।। triḥ pibet salilaṃ tena tathā dviḥ parimārjayet ।। bāhū nābhiṃ ca toyena hṛdayaṃ cāpi saṃspṛśet ।।
prakṣālya pādau hastau ca triḥ pibed ambu vīkṣitam ।। saṃvṛtyāṅguṣṭhamūlena dviḥ pramṛjet tato mukham ।। saṃhatābhis tribhiḥ pūrvaṃ soṣṭaṃ tu samupaspṛśet ।। aṅguṣṭhena pradeśinyā xxxxxxxx [lacuna] ।।
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ ca cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhato nābhiṃ hṛdayaṃ tu talena vai ।। sarvāṅgeṣu śiraḥ paścāc cāśreṇa [??] saṃspṛśed iti ।। ādarśāñjanamāṅgalyaṃ durvādyālambhanāni ca ।।
kurvīta śraddhāsaṃpanno yajec ca pṛthivīpate ।। dhane yato manuṣyāṇāṃ yatetāto dhanārjane ।। nityakriyārthaṃ snāyīta giriprasravaṇeṣu ca ।। snāyītoddhṛtatoyena athavā bhuvy asaṃbhave ।।
teṣām eva hi tīrthena kurvīta susamāhitaḥ ।। tatharṣīṇāṃ yathānyāyaṃ sakṛc cāpi prajāpateḥ ।। pitāmahebhyaś ca tathā prīṇayet prapitāmahān ।। dadyāt paitreṇa tīrthena kāmyaṃ cānyac chṛṇuṣva me ।।
gurave mātulādīnāṃ snigdhamitrāya bhūbhuje ।। upakārāya bhūtānāṃ kṛtadevāditarpaṇaḥ ।। piśācā guhyakāḥ siddhāḥ kūṣmāṇḍās taravaḥ khagāḥ ।। tṛptim ete prayāntv āśu maddattenāmbunākhilāḥ ।।
teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā ।। te tṛptim akhilā yāntu ye cāsmattoyakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। idam apy akṣayaṃ cāstu mayā dattaṃ tilodakam ।। jagadāpyāyanodbhūtaṃ puṇyam āpnoti cānagha ।।
ācamya ca tato dadyāt sūryāya salilāñjalim ।। jagatsavitre śucaye savitre karmadāyine ।। jalābhiṣekapuṣpāṇāṃ dhūpādeś ca nivedanaiḥ ।। apūrvam agnihotraṃ ca kuryāt prāg brahmaṇe tataḥ ।।
gṛhebhyaḥ kāśyapāyātha tato anumataye kramāt ।। dvāre dhātur vidhātuś ca madhye ca brahmaṇaḥ kṣipet ।। gṛhasya puruṣavyāghra digdevān api me śṛṇu ।। prācyādiṣu budho dadyād dhutaśeṣātmakaṃ balim ।।
nirvaped vaiśvadevaṃ ca karma kuryād ataḥ param ।। brahmaṇe cāntarikṣāya bhānave ca kṣiped balim ।। yakṣmāṇaṃ ca samuddiśya baliṃ dadyān nareśvara ।। dadyād aśeṣabhūtebhyaḥ svecchayā tatsamāhitaḥ ।।
pretāḥ piśācās taravaḥ samastā ye cānnam icchanti mayā pradattam ।। prayāntu te tṛptim idaṃ mayānnaṃ tebhyo visṛṣṭaṃ sukhino bhavantu ।। tattṛptaye annaṃ bhuvi dattam etat te yāntu tṛptiṃ muditā bhavantu ।। tasmād ahaṃ bhūtanikāyabhūtam annaṃ prayacchāmi bhavāya teṣām ।।
tṛptyartham annaṃ hi mayā nisṛṣṭaṃ teṣām idaṃ te muditā bhavantu ।। bhuvi bhūtopakārāya gṛhī sarvāśrayo yataḥ ।। ye cānye patitāḥ kecid apātrā bhuvi mānavāḥ ।। atithigrahaṇārthāya tadūrdhvaṃ vā yathecchayā ।।
tathāsanapradānena pādaprakṣālanena ca ।। gacchataś cānuyānena prītim utpādayed gṛhī ।। pūjayed atithiṃ samyaṅ naikagrāmanivāsinam ।। asaṃpūjyātithiṃ bhuñjan bhoktukāmaṃ vrajaty adhaḥ ।।
hiraṇyagarbhabuddhyā taṃ manyetābhyāgataṃ gṛhī ।। taddeśyaṃ viditācārasaṃbhūtiṃ pāñcayajñikam ।। nirvāpabhūtaṃ bhūpāla śrotriyāyopapādayet ।। icchayā ca budho dadyād vibhave saty avāritam ।।
caturaḥ pūjayed etān nṛyajñarṇāt pramucyate ।। sa dattvā duṣkṛtaṃ tasmai puṇyam ādāya gacchati ।। praviśyātithim ete vai bhuñjante annaṃ nareśvara ।। ye ca viṣṇuparā nityaṃ ye ca vikhānasāśramāḥ ।।
pañcarātraṃ vidhānajñā ye ca viṣṇuparāyaṇāḥ ।। viṣṇurūpadharā ye te viṣṇum eva samāśritāḥ ।। sarvo viṣṇumayo loka iti matvā sthitāś ca ye ।। sarva ete hy atithayo mṛṣyā vai sārvakālikam ।।
eteṣām ekam atithiṃ pūjayet puṇyalokabhāk ।। sa kevalam aghaṃ bhuṅkte yo bhuṅkte tv atithiṃ vinā ।। bhojayet saṃskṛtānnena prathamaṃ caramaṃ gṛhī ।। mṛtaś ca narakaṃ gatvā śleṣmabhug jāyate naraḥ ।।
asaṃskṛtānnabhuṅ mūtraṃ bālādiprathamaṃ śakṛt ।। abhūtāśī kṛmiṃ bhuṅkte adātā viṣam aśnute ।। bhuñjataś ca yathā puṃsaḥ pāpabandho na jāyate ।। bhavaty ariṣṭaśāntiś ca vairipakṣābhicārikā ।।
praśastaratnapāṇiś ca bhuñjīta prayato gṛhī ।। puṇyagandhadharaḥ śastamālyadhārī nareśvara ।। viśuddhavadanaḥ prīto bhuñjīta na vidiṅmukhaḥ ।। annaṃ praśastaṃ pathyaṃ ca prokṣitaṃ prokṣaṇodakaiḥ ।।
dattvā tu bhuktaṃ śiṣyebhyaḥ kṣudhitebhyas tathā gṛhī ।। praśastaśuddhapātreṣu bhuñjītākupito nṛpa ।। nākāle nātisaṃkīrṇe dattvāgraṃ ca naro agnaye ।। anyatra phalamāṃsebhyaḥ śuṣkaśākādikāṃs tathā ।।
bhuñjītoddhṛtasārāṇi na kadācin nareśvara ।। madhvambudadhisarpibhyaḥ saktubhyaś ca vivekavān ।। lavaṇāmlau tathā madhye kaṭutiktādikaṃ tataḥ ।। punar ante dravāśī tu balārogye na muñcati ।।
pañcagrāsaṃ mahāmaunaṃ prāṇādyāpyāyanāya tat ।। yathāvat punar ācāmet pāṇī prakṣālya mūlataḥ ।। abhīṣṭadevatānāṃ tu kurvīta smaraṇaṃ naraḥ ।। dattāvakāśaṃ nabhasā jarayatv astu me sukham ।।
bhavatv etat pariṇatau mamāstv avyāhataṃ sukham ।। annaṃ puṣṭikaraṃ cāstu mamāstv avyāhataṃ sukham ।। sukhaṃ ca me tatpariṇāmasaṃbhavaṃ yacchantv arogo mama cāstu dehe ।। deheṣu sarveṣu yathā ca dehī ।।
satyena tenānnam aśeṣam etad ārogyadaṃ me pariṇāmam etu ।। satyena tena vai bhuktaṃ jīryatv annam idaṃ tathā ।। anāyāsapradāyīni kuryāt karmāṇy atandritaḥ ।। dinaṃ nayet tataḥ saṃdhyām upatiṣṭhet samāhitaḥ ।।
upatiṣṭhed yathānyāyaṃ samyag ācamya pārthiva ।। anyatrasūtakāśaucavibhramāturabhītitaḥ ।। anyatrāturabhāvāt tu prāyaścittīyate naraḥ ।। upatiṣṭhen naraḥ saṃdhyām asvapaṃś ca dināntajām ।।
vrajanti te durātmānas tāmisraṃ narakaṃ nṛpa ।। vaiśvadevanimittaṃ vai patny amantraṃ baliṃ haret ।। tatrāpi śvapacādibhyas tathaivānnāpavarjanam ।। tataś cānnapradānena śayanena ca pārthiva ।।
tad evāṣṭaguṇaṃ puṃsāṃ sūryoḍhe vimukhe gate ।। pūjayet pūjite tasmin pūjitāḥ sarvadevatāḥ ।। śayanaprastaramahīpradānair athavāpi tam ।। gacched asphuṭitāṃ śayyām api dārumayīṃ nṛpa ।।
na ca jantumayīṃ śayyām adhitiṣṭhed anāstṛtām ।। sadaiva svapataḥ puṃso viparītaṃ tu rogadam ।। punnāmarkṣe śubhe kāle jyeṣṭhayugmāsu rātriṣu ।। nāniṣṭāṃ na prakupitāṃ nāpraśastāṃ na garbhiṇīm ।।
kṣutkṣāmām atibhuktāṃ vā svayaṃ caibhir guṇair yutaḥ ।। sakāmaḥ sānurāgaś ca vyavāyaṃ puruṣo vrajet ।। parvāṇy etāni rājendra ravisaṃkrāntir eva ca ।। viṇmūtrabhojanaṃ nāma prayāti narakaṃ mṛtaḥ ।।
bhāvyaṃ sacchāstradevejyādhyānajapyaparair naraiḥ ।। devadvijagurūṇāṃ ca vyavāyī nāśraye bhavet ।। naiva śmaśānopavane salileṣu mahīpate ।। gacched vyavāyaṃ matimān na mūtroccārapīḍitaḥ ।।
bhuvi rogaprado nṝṇām apraśasto jalāśaye ।। kim u vācāsthibandho api nāsti teṣu vyavāyinām ।। paradāraratiḥ puṃsām ubhayatrāpi bhītidā ।। yathoktadoṣahīneṣu sakāmeṣv anṛtāv api ।।
dvikālaṃ ca namet saṃdhyām agnīn upacaret tathā ।। gāruḍāni ca ratnāni bibhṛyāt prayato naraḥ ।। sitāḥ sumanaso hṛdyā bibhṛyāc ca naraḥ sadā ।। priyaṃ ca nānṛtaṃ brūyān nānyadoṣān udīrayet ।।
na duṣṭayānam ārohet kūlacchāyāṃ na saṃśrayet ।। bandhakībandhakībhartṛkṣudrānṛtakathaiḥ saha ।। budho maitrīṃ na kurvīta naikaḥ panthānam āśrayet ।। pradīptaṃ veśma na viśen nārohec chikharaṃ taroḥ ।।
nāsaṃvṛtamukho jṛmbhec śvāsakāsau ca varjayet ।। nakhān na khādayec chindyān na tṛṇaṃ na mahīṃ likhet ।। jyotīṃṣy amedhyaḥ śastāni nābhivīkṣeta ca prabho ।। na huṃkuryāc chavaṃ caiva śavagandho hi somajaḥ ।।
duṣṭastrīsaṃnikarṣaṃ ca varjayen niśi sarvadā ।। naikaḥ śūnyāṭavīṃ gacchen na ca śūnyagṛhe vaset ।। snānārdradharaṇīṃ caiva dūrataḥ parivarjayet ।। upasarpeta na vyālāṃś ciraṃ tiṣṭhen na cotthitaḥ ।।
na seveta tathā śayyāṃ vyāyāmaṃ ca nareśvara ।। avaśyāyaṃ ca rājendra puro vātātapau tathā ।। muktakacchaś ca nācāmed devādyarcāṃ ca varjayet ।। naikavastraḥ pravarteta dvijavācanake jape ।।
sadvṛttasaṃnikarṣo hi kṣaṇārdham api śasyate ।। vivāhaś ca vivādaś ca tulyaśīlair nṛpeṣyate ।। apy alpahāniḥ soḍhavyā vaireṇārthāgamaṃ tyajet ।। na ca nirdhūnayet keśān nācāmec caiva cotthitaḥ ।।
vīrāsanaṃ guror agre bhajeta vinayānvitaḥ ।। māṅgalyapūjyāṃś ca tato viparītān na dakṣiṇam ।। kuryāt ṣṭhīvanaviṇmūtrasamutsargaṃ ca paṇḍitaḥ ।। śleṣmaviṇmūtraraktāni sarvadaiva na laṅghayet ।।
balimaṅgalajapyādau na home na mahājane ।। na caiverṣyur bhavet tāsu nādhikuryāt kadācana ।। na niṣkramed gṛhāt prājñaḥ sadācāraparo nṛpa ।। dīnān abhyuddharet sādhūn upāsīta bahuśrutān ।।
satkartā cātithīnāṃ yaḥ sa lokān uttamān vrajet ।। adhyātmayoge yatamānasasya mokṣo dhruvaṃ nityam ahiṃsakasya ।। sa yāti lokān āhlādahetubhūtān nṛpākṣayān ।। vidyābhijanavṛddhānāṃ yāti lokān anuttamān ।।
anadhyāyaṃ budhaḥ kuryād uparāgādike tathā ।। bhītāśvāsanakṛt sādhuḥ svargas tasyālpakaṃ phalam ।। śarīratrāṇakāmo vai sopānatkaḥ sadā vrajet ।। yugamātraṃ mahīpṛṣṭhaṃ naro gacched vilokayan ।।
tasya dharmārthakāmānāṃ hānir nālpāpi jāyate ।। sadācārarataḥ prājño vidyāvinayaśikṣitaḥ ।। maitrīdravāntaḥkaraṇas tasya muktiḥ kare sthitā ।। sadācārasthitās teṣām anubhāvair dhṛtā mahī ।।
satyaṃ yat paraduḥkhāya tatra maunaparo bhavet ।। śreyas tatra hitaṃ vākyaṃ yady apy atyantam apriyam ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā tad eva matimān bhajet ।। jātakarma tathā kuryāc śrāddham abhyudaye ca yat ।।
pūjayed bhojayec caiva tanmanā nānyamānasaḥ ।। devatīrthena vai piṇḍān dadyāt kāyena vā nṛpa ।। prīyate tat tu kartavyaṃ puruṣaiḥ sarvavṛddhiṣu ।। nāmakarmaṇi bālānāṃ cūḍākarmādike tathā ।।
nāndīmukhaṃ pitṛgaṇaṃ pūjayet prayato gṛhī ।। śrūyatām avanīpāla pretakarmakriyāvidhiḥ ।। dagdhvā grāmād bahiḥ snātvā sacailāḥ salilāśaye ।। dakṣiṇābhimukhā dadyur bāndhavāḥ salilāñjalim ।।
kaṭadharmāṃs tataḥ kuryur bhūmau prastaraśāyinaḥ ।। divā ca bhaktaṃ bhoktavyam amāṃsaṃ manujarṣabha ।। pretas tṛptiṃ tathā yāti bandhuvargeṇa bhuñjatā ।। vastratyāgaṃ bahiḥsnānaṃ kṛtvā dadyāt tilodakam ।।
tato anubandhuvargas tu bhuvi dadyāt tilodakam ।। tadūrdhvam aṅgasparśaś ca sapiṇḍānām apīṣyate ।। anulepanapuṣpādibhogād anyatra pārthiva ।। bhasmāsthicayanād ūrdhvaṃ saṃyogo na tu yoṣitām ।।
sadyaḥ śaucaṃ tathecchāto jalāgnyudbandhanādiṣu ।। dānaṃ pratigraho yajñaḥ svādhyāyaś ca nivartate ।। ardhamāsaṃ tu vaiśyasya māsaṃ śūdrasya śuddhaye ।। dadyād darbheṣu piṇḍaṃ ca pretāyocchiṣṭasaṃnidhau ।।
spraṣṭavyo anantaraṃ varṇaiḥ śudhyeraṃs te tataḥ kramāt ।। tān kurvīta pumāñ jīven nijadharmārjanais tathā ।। āhvānādikriyādaivaniyogarahitaṃ hi tat ।। pretāya piṇḍo dātavyo bhuktavatsu dvijātiṣu ।।
akṣayyam amukasyeti vaktavyaṃ viratau tathā ।। sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tasmin kāle rājendra tac chṛṇu ।। ekoddiṣṭavidhānena kāryaṃ tad api pārthiva ।। b saṃvatsare atha ṣaṣṭhe vā māsi vā dvādaśe ahni vā ।। b
tilagandhodakair yuktaṃ tatra pātracatuṣṭayam ।। d secayet pitṛpātreṣu pretapātraṃ nṛpa triṣu ।। śrāddhadharmair aśeṣais tu tatpūrvān arcayet pitṝn ।। sapiṇḍasaṃtatir vāpi kriyārho nṛpa jāyate ।।
mātṛpakṣasya piṇḍena saṃbaddhā ye jalena vā ।। utsannabandhurikthānāṃ kārayed avanīpatiḥ ।। triḥprakārāḥ kriyā hy etās tāsāṃ bhedaṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।। tāḥ pūrvā madhyamā māsi māsy ekoddiṣṭasaṃjñitāḥ ।।
kriyante yāḥ kriyāḥ pitryāḥ procyante tā nṛpottarāḥ ।। tatsaṃghātagataiś caiva rājñā vā dhanahāriṇā ।। dauhitrair vā naraśreṣṭha kāryās tattanayais tathā ।। pratisaṃvatsaraṃ rājann ekoddiṣṭavidhānataḥ ।।
yadā yadā ca kartavyā vidhinā yena cānagha ।। viśvedevān ṛṣigaṇān vayāṃsi manujān paśūn ।। śrāddhaṃ śraddhānvitaḥ kurvan tarpayaty akhilaṃ jagat ।। tathāṣṭakāsu kurvīta kāmyān kālāñ chṛṇuṣva me ।।
śrāddhaṃ kurvīta vijñāya vyatīpāte ayane tathā ।। samasteṣv eva bhūpāla rāśiṣv arke ca gacchati ।। icchāśrāddhāni kurvīta navasasyāgame tathā ।। śrāddhaiḥ pitṛgaṇas tṛptiṃ tathāpnoty aṣṭavārṣikīm ।।
dvādaśābdaṃ tadā tṛptiṃ prayānti pitaro arcitāḥ ।। vāruṇe cāpy amāvāsyā devānām api durlabhā ।। tadā tṛptipradaṃ śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ śṛṇu cāparam ।। pṛcchate pitṛbhaktāya śraddhayāvanatāya ca ।।
nabhasyamāsasya tu kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśī pañcadaśī ca māghe ।। etā yugādyās tithayaś catasro apy anantapuṇyā nṛpa saṃpradiṣṭāḥ ।। b dve śukle dve tathā kṛṣṇe yugādye munayo viduḥ ।। b śukle pūrvāhnike grāhye kṛṣṇe caivāparāhnike ।। b
yugādyeṣu yugānteṣu dattam akṣayam iṣyate ।। b upaplave candramaso raveś ca triṣv aṣṭakāsv apy ayanadvaye ca ।। d manvantarādyās tithayas tathaiva chāyāgajasya vyatipātakālaḥ ।। śrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena samāḥ sahasraṃ rahasyam etat pitaro vadanti ।।
ṛkṣeṇa kālaḥ sa paraḥ pitṝṇāṃ na hy alpapuṇyair nṛpa labhyate asau ।। dattaṃ jalānnaṃ pradadāti tṛptiṃ varṣāyutaṃ tatkulajair manuṣyaiḥ ।। śrāddhaṃ parāṃ tṛptim upetya tena yugaṃ samagraṃ pitaraḥ svapanti ।। tato avagāhyārcanam ādareṇa kṛtvā pitṝṇāṃ duritāni hanti ।।
māghāsitānte śubhatīrthatoyair yāsyāma tṛptiṃ tanayādidattaiḥ ।। pātraṃ yathoktaṃ paramā ca bhaktir nṛṇāṃ prayacchaty abhivāñchitāni ।। śrutvā tathaiva bhavatā bhāvyaṃ tatrādṛtātmanā ।। akurvan vittaśāṭhyaṃ yaḥ piṇḍānno nirvapiṣyati ।।
vibhave sati viprebhyo yo asmān uddiśya dāsyati ।। bhojayiṣyati viprāgryāṃs tanmātravibhavo naraḥ ।। pradāsyati dvijāgrebhyaḥ svalpālpāṃ vāpi dakṣiṇām ।। praṇamya dvijamukhyāya kasmaicid bhūpa dāsyati ।।
bhaktinamraḥ samuddiśya bhuvy asmākaṃ pradāsyati ।। abhāve prīṇayann asmāñ śraddhāyuktaḥ pradāsyati ।। sūryādilokapālānām idam uccair paṭhiṣyati ।। tṛpyantu bhaktyā pitaro mayaitau kṛtau bhujau vartmani mārutasya ।।
yaḥ karoti kṛtaṃ tena śrāddhaṃ bhavati pārthiva ।। brāhmaṇān bhojayec chrāddhe yadguṇāṃs tān nibodha me ।। vedavic chrotriyo yogī tathā vai jyeṣṭhasāmagaḥ ।। śiṣyāḥ saṃbandhinaś caiva mātāpitṛrataś ca yaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇān pitṛpuṣṭyartham anukalpeṣv anantarān ।। kanyādūṣayitā vahnivedojjhaḥ somavikrayī ।। bhṛtakādhyāpakas tadvad bhṛtakādhyāpitaś ca yaḥ ।। parapūrvāpatiś caiva mātāpitros tathojjhakaḥ ।। b
tathā bhrātṛparityāgī dūṣakaḥ sarvanindakaḥ ।। b vṛṣalīsūtipoṣṭā ca vṛṣalīpatir eva ca ।। d tathā devalakaś caiva śrāddhe nārhati ketanam ।। kathayec ca tadaivaiṣāṃ niyogān pitṛdaivikān ।।
yajamāno na kurvīta doṣas tatra mahān ayam ।। vyavāyī retaso garte majjayaty ātmanaḥ pitṝn ।। animantrya dvijān geham āgatān bhojayed yatīn ।। pādaśaucādinā geham āgatān pūjayed dvijān ।।
pitṝṇām ayujo yugmān devānām icchayā dvijān ।। devānām ekam ekaṃ vā pitṝṇāṃ ca niyojayet ।। kurvīta bhaktisaṃpannas tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikam ।। pitṛpaitāmahānāṃ ca bhojayec cāpy udaṅmukhān ।।
ekatraikena pākena vadanty anye maharṣayaḥ ।। kuryād āvāhanaṃ prājño devānāṃ tadanujñayā ।। sraggandhadhūpadīpāṃś ca dattvā tebhyo yathāvidhi ।। anujñāṃ ca tataḥ prāpya dattvā darbhān dvidhākṛtān ।।
tilāmbunā cāpasavyaṃ dadyād arghyādikaṃ nṛpa ।। brāhmaṇair abhyanujñātaḥ kāmaṃ tam api bhojayet ।। bhramanti pṛthivīm etām avijñātasvarūpiṇaḥ ।। śrāddhakriyāphalaṃ hanti narendrāpūjito atithiḥ ।।
anujñāto dvijais tais tu trikṛtvaḥ puruṣarṣabha ।। somāya vai pitṛmate dātavyā tadanantaram ।। hutāvaśiṣṭam alpālpaṃ viprapātreṣu nirvapet ।। dattvā juṣadhvam icchāto vācyam etad aniṣṭhuram ।।
akrudhyatā cātvaratā deyaṃ tenāpi bhaktitaḥ ।। kṛtvā dhyeyāḥ svapitaras ta eva dvijasattamāḥ ।। mama tṛptiṃ prayāntv adya vipradeheṣu saṃsthitāḥ ।। mama tṛptiṃ prayāntv agnihomāpyāyitamūrtayaḥ ।।
tṛptiṃ prayāntu piṇḍena mayā dattena bhūtale ।। tṛptiṃ prayāntu me bhaktyā yan mayaitad ihāhṛtam ।। viśve ca devāḥ paramāṃ prayāntu tṛptiṃ praṇaśyantu ca yātudhānāḥ ।। tatsaṃnidhānād apayāntu sadyo rakṣāṃsy aśeṣāṇy asurāś ca sarve ।।
dadyāc cācamanārthāya tebhyo vāri sakṛt sakṛt ।। satilena tataḥ piṇḍān samyag dadyāt samāhitaḥ ।। mātāmahebhyas tenaiva piṇḍāṃs tīrthena nirvapet ।। dakṣiṇāpravaṇaṃ caiva prayatnenopapādayet ।।
avakāśeṣu cokṣeṣu jalatīreṣu caiva hi ।। svapitre prathamaṃ piṇḍaṃ dadyād ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau ।। darbhamūle lepabhujaḥ prīṇayel lepagharṣaṇaiḥ ।। pūjayitvā dvijāgryāṇāṃ dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ ।।
susvadhety āśiṣā yuktāṃ dadyāc chaktyā ca dakṣiṇām ।। prīyantām iti ye viśvedevās tena itīrayet ।। paścād visarjayed devān pūrvaṃ paitrān mahāmate ।। bhojane ca svaśaktyā ca dāne tadvad visarjane ।।
visarjanaṃ tu prathamaṃ paitraṃ mātāmaheṣu vai ।। nivartetābhyanujñāta ādvārāt tān anuvrajet ।। bhuñjīyāc ca samaṃ pūjyabhṛtyabandhubhir ātmanaḥ ।। śrāddhair āpyāyitā dadyuḥ sarvakāmān pitāmahāḥ ।।
rajatasya tathā dānaṃ kathāsaṃdarśanādikam ।। bhoktur apy atra rājendra trayam etan na śasyate ।। kulaṃ cāpyāyyate puṃsāṃ sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ prakurvatām ।। śrāddhe yoginiyogas tu tasmād bhūpāla śasyate ।।
sarvān bhoktṝṃs tārayati yajamānaṃ tathā nṛpa ।। saukaracchāgalaiṇeyarauravair gavayena ca ।। prayānti tṛptiṃ māṃsais tu nityaṃ vārdhrīṇasām iṣaiḥ ।। śastāni karmaṇy atyantatṛptidāni nareśvara ।।
saphalaṃ tasya taj janma jāyate pitṛtuṣṭidam ।। vanyauṣadhīpradhānās tu śrāddhārhāḥ puruṣarṣabha ।। niṣpāvāḥ kovidārāś ca sarṣapāś cātra śobhanāḥ ।। rājamāṣān aṇūṃś caiva masūrāṃś ca vivarjayet ।।
gandhārakaṃ karambhāṇi lavaṇāny auṣarāṇi ca ।। varjyāny etāni vai śrāddhe yac ca vācā na śasyate ।। durgandhi phenilaṃ cāmbu śrāddhayogyaṃ na pārthiva ।। mārgaṃ ca māhiṣaṃ caiva varjayec chrāddhakarmaṇi ।।
kṛkavākuśvanagnaiś ca vānaragrāmasūkaraiḥ ।। śrāddhe surā na pitaro bhuñjate puruṣarṣabha ।। urvyāṃ ca tilavikṣepād yātudhānān nivārayet ।। na caivābhiṣavair miśram annaṃ paryuṣitaṃ tathā ।।
yadāhārās tu te jātās tadāhāratvam eti tat ।। ikṣvākor manuputrasya kalāpopavane purā ।। gayām upetya ye piṇḍān dāsyanty asmākam ādarāt ।। pāyasaṃ madhusarpibhyāṃ varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca ।।
yajeta vāśvamedhena vidhivad dakṣiṇāvatā ।। sadācārān purā samyaṅ maitreya paripṛcchate ।। evaṃ navabhir adhyāyais trayīdharmaḥ prapañcitaḥ ।। tatparityāganindārtham adhyāyadvayam uttaram ।।
samullaṅghya sadācāraṃ kaścin nāpnoti śobhanam ।। udakyādyāś ca ye sarve nagnam icchāmi veditum ।। nagnasvarūpam icchāmi yathāvat gaditaṃ tvayā ।। śrotuṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha na hy asty aviditaṃ tava ।।
etām ujjhati yo mohāt sa nagnaḥ pātakī smṛtaḥ ।। nagno bhavaty ujjhitāyām atas tasyām asaṃśayam ।। kathayām āsa dharmajño vasiṣṭho asmatpitāmahaḥ ।। nagnasaṃbandhi maitreya yat pṛṣṭo aham iha tvayā ।।
tasmin parājitā devā daityair hrādapurogamaiḥ ।। viṣṇor ārādhanārthāya jaguś cemaṃ stavaṃ tadā ।। vakṣyāmo bhagavān ādyas tayā viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu ।। yasmiṃś ca layam eṣyanti kas taṃ saṃstotum īśvaraḥ ।।
tvāṃ stoṣyāmas tavoktīnāṃ yāthārthyaṃ naiva gocare ।। samastam antaḥkaraṇaṃ pradhānaṃ tatparaḥ pumān ।। ābrahmastambaparyantaṃ sthānakālavibhedavat ।। rūpaṃ sargopakārāya tasmai brahmātmane namaḥ ।।
vayam evaṃ svarūpaṃ te tasmai devātmane namaḥ ।। yad rūpaṃ tava govinda tasmai daityātmane namaḥ ।। śabdādilobhi yat tasmai tubhyaṃ yakṣātmane namaḥ ।। niśācarātmane tasmai namas te puruṣottama ।।
dharmākhyaṃ ca tathā rūpaṃ namas tasmai janārdana ।। siddhātmaṃs tava yad rūpaṃ tasmai siddhātmane namaḥ ।। dvijihvaṃ tava yad rūpaṃ tasmai sarpātmane namaḥ ।। ṛṣirūpātmane tasmai viṣṇo rūpāya te namaḥ ।।
tvadrūpaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa tasmai kālātmane namaḥ ।। nṛtyaty ante ca yad rūpaṃ tasmai rudrātmane namaḥ ।। janārdana namas tasmai tvadrūpāya narātmane ।। unmārgagāmi sarvātmaṃs tasmai paśvātmane namaḥ ।।
vṛkṣādibhedair yad bhedi tasmai mukhyātmane namaḥ ।। rūpaṃ tavādeḥ sarvasya tasmai sarvātmane namaḥ ।। rūpaṃ tavādyaṃ na yad anyatulyaṃ tasmai namaḥ kāraṇakāraṇāya ।। śuddhātiśuddhaṃ paramarṣidṛśyaṃ rūpāya tasmai bhagavan natāḥ smaḥ ।।
yasmāc ca nānyad vyatiriktam asti brahmasvarūpāya natāḥ sma tasmai ।। tam anidhanam aśeṣabījabhūtaṃ prabhum amalaṃ praṇatāḥ sma vāsudevam ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ garuḍasthaṃ surā harim ।। prasīda deva daityebhyas trāhīti śaraṇārthinaḥ ।।
hṛtaṃ no brahmaṇo apy ājñām ullaṅghya parameśvara ।। tathāpy avidyābhedena bhinnaṃ paśyāmahe jagat ।। na śakyās te arayo hantum asmābhis tapasānvitāḥ ।। yena tān asurān hantuṃ bhavema bhagavan kṣamāḥ ।।
samutpādya dadau viṣṇuḥ prāha cedaṃ surottamān ।। tato vadhyā bhaviṣyanti vedamārgabahiṣkṛtāḥ ।। brahmaṇo hy adhikārasya devā daityādikāḥ surāḥ ।। gacchatv adyopakārāya bhavatāṃ bhavitā surāḥ ।।
māyāmoho api taiḥ sārdhaṃ yayau yatra mahāsurāḥ ।। maitreya dadṛśe gatvā narmadātīrasaṃśrayān ।। māyāmoho asurān ślakṣṇam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। aihikaṃ vātha pāratryaṃ tapasaḥ phalam icchatha ।।
asmābhir iyam ārabdhā kiṃ vā te atra vivakṣitam ।। arhadhvaṃ dharmam etaṃ ca muktidvāram asaṃvṛtam ।। atraivāvasthitāḥ svargaṃ vimuktiṃ vā gamiṣyatha ।। arhadhvaṃ dharmam etaṃ ca sarve yūyaṃ mahābalāḥ ।।
māyāmohena daityās te vedamārgād apākṛtāḥ ।। vimuktaye tv idaṃ naitad vimuktiṃ saṃprayacchati ।। paramārtho ayam atyarthaṃ paramārtho na cāpy ayam ।। digvāsasām ayaṃ dharmo dharmo ayaṃ bahuvāsasām ।।
tena darśayatā daityāḥ svadharmāṃs tyājitā dvija ।। proktās tam āśritā dharmam arhatās tena te abhavan ।। kāritās tanmayā hy āsaṃs tathānye tatprabodhitāḥ ।। alpair ahobhiḥ saṃtyaktā tair daityaiḥ prāyaśas trayī ।।
anyān āhāsurān gatvā mṛdvalpamadhurākṣaram ।। tad alaṃ paśughātādiduṣṭadharmaṃ nibodhata ।। budhyadhvaṃ me vacaḥ samyag budhair evam udīritam ।। rāgādiduṣṭam atyarthaṃ bhrāmyate bhavasaṃkaṭe ।।
māyāmohaḥ sa daityeyān dharmam atyājayan nijam ।। tathā tathāvadad dharmaṃ tatyajus te yathā yathā ।। maitreya tatyajur dharmaṃ vedasmṛtyuditaṃ param ।। daiteyān mohayām āsa māyāmoho atimohakṛt ।।
mohitās tatyajuḥ sarvāṃ trayīmārgāśritāṃ kathām ।। yajñakarmakalāpasya tathānye ca dvijanmanām ।। havīṃṣy analadagdhāni phalāyety arbhakoditam ।। śamyādi yadi cet kāṣṭhaṃ tadvaraṃ patrabhuk paśuḥ ।।
bhaved yajñasya sādhanam ।। tadāhāras tadā nityaṃ ।। svapitā yajamānena kiṃ nu tasmān na hanyate ।। dadyāc chrāddhaṃ śraddhayānnaṃ na vaheyuḥ pravāsinaḥ ।।
upekṣā śreyasī vākyaṃ rocatāṃ yan mayeritam ।। yuktimad vacanaṃ grāhyaṃ mayānyaiś ca bhavadvidhaiḥ ।। vyutthāpitā yathā naiṣāṃ trayīṃ kaścid arocayat ।। udyogaṃ paramaṃ kṛtvā yuddhāya samupasthitāḥ ।।
hatāś ca te asurā devaiḥ sanmārgaparipanthinaḥ ।। tena rakṣābhavat pūrvaṃ neśur naṣṭe ca tatra te ।। nagnās te tair yatas tyaktaṃ trayīsaṃvaraṇaṃ vṛthā ।। kṛtāś ca te asurā devair nānāvedavinindakāḥ ।।
parivrāḍ vā caturtho atra pañcamo nopapadyate ।। parivrāḍ vāpi maitreya sa nagnaḥ pāpakṛn naraḥ ।। akurvan vihitaṃ karma śaktaḥ patati taddine ।। pakṣaṃ nityakriyāhāneḥ kartā maitreya mānavaḥ ।।
tasyāvalokanāt sūryo nirīkṣyaḥ sādhubhiḥ sadā ।। puṃso bhavati tasyoktā na śuddhiḥ pāpakarmaṇaḥ ।। prayānty anarcitāny atra na tasmāt pāpakṛn naraḥ ।। na tena saṃkaraṃ kuryād gṛhāsanaparicchadaiḥ ।।
jāyate tulyatā puṃsas tenaiva dvija vatsaram ।। śete cāpy ekaśayane sa sadyas tatsamo bhavet ।। bhuṅkte sa pātakaṃ bhuṅkte niṣkṛtis tasya kīdṛśī ।। yānti te nagnasaṃjñāṃ tu hīnakarmasv avasthitāḥ ।।
tatrāsyā sādhuvṛttīnām upaghātāya jāyate ।। yo bhuṅkte tasya saṃbhāṣāt patanti narake narāḥ ।। sarvadā varjayet prājña ālāpasparśanādiṣu ।। na prīṇayati tac chrāddhaṃ yady ebhir avalokitam ।।
patnī ca śaibyā tasyābhūd atidharmaparāyaṇā ।। sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā saṃpannā vinayena ca ।। ārādhayām āsa vibhuṃ parameṇa samādhinā ।। pūjābhiś cānudivasaṃ tanmanā nānyamānasaḥ ।।
pāṣaṇḍinam apaśyetām āyāntaṃ saṃmukhaṃ dvija ।। atas tadgauravāt tena sahālāpam athākarot ।। upoṣitāsmīti raviṃ tasmin dṛṣṭe dadarśa ca ।। viṣṇoḥ pūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtavantau dvijottama ।।
anvāruroha taṃ devī citāsthaṃ bhūpatiṃ patim ।। upoṣitena pāṣaṇḍasaṃbhāṣo yaḥ kṛto abhavat ।। sarvavijñānasaṃpannā sarvalakṣaṇabhūṣitā ।। tayaiva tanvyā virato vivāhārambhato nṛpaḥ ।।
vaidiśākhyaṃ puraṃ gatvā tadavasthaṃ dadarśa tam ।। dadau tasmai varāhāraṃ satkārapravaṇaṃ śubham ।। śvajātilalitaṃ kurvan bahu cāṭu cakāra vai ।। praṇāmapūrvam āhedaṃ dayitaṃ taṃ kuyonijam ।।
yena śvayonim āpanno mama cāṭukaro bhavān ।। prāpto asi kutsitāṃ yoniṃ kiṃ na smarasi tat prabho ।। dadhyau ciram athāvāpa nirvedam atidurlabham ।। maruprapatanaṃ kṛtvā śārgālīṃ yonim āgataḥ ।।
jñātvā sṛgālaṃ taṃ draṣṭuṃ yayau kolāhalaṃ girim ।। bhartāram api cārvaṅgī tanayā pṛthivīkṣitaḥ ।। proktaṃ te pūrvacaritaṃ pāṣaṇḍālāpasaṃśrayam ।। kānane sa nirāhāras tatyāja svaṃ kalevaram ।।
smārayām āsa bhartāraṃ pūrvavṛttam aninditā ।। śvā bhūtvā tvaṃ śṛgālo abhūr vṛkatvaṃ sāmprataṃ gataḥ ।। apāpā sā punaś cainaṃ bodhayām āsa bhāminī ।। pāṣaṇḍālāpajāto ayaṃ doṣo yad gṛdhratāṃ gataḥ ।।
uvāca tanvī bhartāram upalabhyātmayogataḥ ।। sa tvaṃ kākatvam āpanno jāto adya balibhuk prabho ।। tatyāja bhūpatiḥ prāṇān mayūratvam avāpa ca ।। dattaiḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ bhojyair bālā tajjātibhojanaiḥ ।।
cakāra tasyāvabhṛthe snāpayām āsa taṃ tadā ।। yathāsau śvaśṛgālādyā yonīr jagrāha pārthivaḥ ।। jajñe ca janakasyaiva putro asau sumahātmanaḥ ।। sa cāpi kārayām āsa pitā tasyāḥ svayaṃvaram ।।
