varayām āsa bhūyo api bhartṛbhāvena bhāminī ।। pitary uparate rājyaṃ videheṣu cakāra saḥ ।। putrān utpādayām āsa yuyudhe ca sahāribhiḥ ।। tatyāja sa priyān prāṇān saṃgrāme dharmato nṛpaḥ ।।
anvāruroha vidhivad yathāpūrvaṃ mudāvatī ।। aindrān atītya vai lokāṃl lokān kāmaduho akṣayān ।। prāptaṃ puṇyaphalaṃ prāpya saṃśuddhiṃ tāṃ dvijottama ।। tathāśvamedhāvabhṛthasnānamāhātmyam eva ca ।।
viśeṣataḥ kriyākāle yajñādau cāpi dīkṣitaḥ ।। tasyāvalokanāt sūryaṃ paśyeta matimān naraḥ ।। parānnabhojibhiḥ pāpair vedavādavirodhibhiḥ ।। sahālāpas tu saṃsargaḥ sahāsyā cātipāpinī ।।
pāṣaṇḍibhir durācārais tasmāt tān parivarjayet ।। haitukān bakavṛttīṃś ca vāṅmātreṇāpi nārcayet ।। bhraṣṭaḥ svadharmāt pāṣaṇḍo vikarmastho niṣiddhakṛt ।। yasya dharmasya yo nityaṃ suradhvaja ivocchritaḥ ।।
pracchannāni ca pāpāni baiḍālaṃ nāma tadvratam ।। priyaṃ vakti puro anyatra vipriyaṃ kurute bhṛśam ।। tyaktāparādhaceṣṭaś ca śaṭho ayaṃ kathito budhaiḥ ।। saṃdehakṛd dhetubhir yaḥ satkarmasu sa haitukaḥ ।।
arvāgdṛṣṭir nikṛtikāḥ svārthasādhanatatparāḥ ।। śaṭho mithyāvinītaś ca bakavṛttir udāhṛtaḥ ।। pāṣaṇḍibhir durācārais tasmāt tān parivarjayet ।। yeṣāṃ saṃbhāṣaṇāt puṃsāṃ dinapuṇyaṃ praṇaśyati ।।
puṇyaṃ naśyati saṃbhāṣād eteṣāṃ taddinodbhavam ।। toyapradānapitṛpiṇḍabahiṣkṛtānāṃ saṃbhāṣaṇād api narā narakaṃ prayānti ।। tan mahyaṃ guruṇākhyātaṃ nityanaimittikātmakam ।। śrotum icchāmy ahaṃ vaṃśāṃs tāṃs tvaṃ prabrūhi me guro ।।
maitreya śrūyatām ayam anekayajvivīraśūrabhūpālālaṃkṛto brahmādir mānavo vaṃśaḥ ।। tathā coktam । tasya vaṃśasamucchedo na kadācid bhaviṣyati ।। tad asya vaṃśasyānupūrvīm aśeṣapāpaprakṣālanāya maitreya tāṃ śṛṇu ।।
tad yathā sakalajagatām anādir ādibhūta-ṛgyajuḥsāmādimayo bhagavadviṣṇumayasya brahmaṇo mūrtaṃ rūpaṃ hiraṇyagarbho brahmāṇḍato bhagavān brahmā prāg babhūva ।। brahmaṇaś ca dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhajanmā dakṣaḥ prajāpatir dakṣasyāditir aditer vivasvān vivasvato manuḥ ।। manor ikṣvākunṛgadhṛṣṭaśaryātinariṣyantaprāṃśunābhāganediṣṭakarūṣapṛṣadhrākhyā daśa putrā babhūvuḥ ।। iṣṭiṃ ca mitrāvaruṇayor manuḥ putrakāmaś cakāra ।।
tatrāpahute hotur apacārād ilā nāma kanyā babhūva ।। saiva ca mitrāvaruṇayoḥ prasādāt sudyumno nāma manoḥ putro maitreyāsīt ।। punaś ceśvarakopāt strī satī somasūnor budhasyāśramasamīpe babhrāma ।। sānurāgaś ca tasyāṃ budhaḥ purūravasam ātmajam utpādayām āsa ।।
jāte ca tasminn amitatejobhiḥ paramarṣibhir ṛṅmayo yajurmayaḥ sāmamayo atharvamayaḥ sarvamayo manomayo jñānamayo na kiṃcinmayo bhagavān yajñapuruṣasvarūpī sudyumnasya puṃstvam abhilaṣadbhir yathāvad iṣṭas tatprasādāc cāsāv ilā punar api sudyumno abhavat ।। tasyāpy utkalagayavinatasaṃjñās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ ।। sudyumnas tu strīpūrvakatvād rājyabhāgaṃ na lebhe ।। tatpitrā tu vasiṣṭhavacanāt pratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma nagaraṃ sudyumnāya dattaṃ tac cāsau purūravase prādāt ।।
pṛṣadhras tu manoḥ putro gurugovadhāc chūdratvam agamat ।। karūṣāt kārūṣāḥ kṣatriyā mahābalaparākramā babhūvuḥ ।। nābhāgo nediṣṭaputras tu vaiśyatām agamat । tasmād bhalandanaḥ putro abhavat ।। bhalandanād vatsaprir udārakīrtiḥ ।।
vatsapreḥ prāṃśur abhavat ।। prajāniś ca prāṃśor eko abhavat ।। tataś ca khanitras tasmāc cakṣupaḥ cakṣupāc cātibalaparākramo viṃśo abhavat ।। tato viviṃśas tasmāc ca khaninetras tataś cātivibhūtiḥ ।।
ativibhūter bhūribalaparākramaḥ karaṃdhamaḥ putro abhavat tasmād apy avikṣir avikṣer apy atibalaḥ putro marutto abhavad yasyemāv adyāpi ślokau gīyete ।। sarvaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ yasya yajñavastv atiśobhanam ।। marutaḥ pariveṣṭāraḥ sadasyāś ca divaukasaḥ ।। maruttaś cakravartī nariṣyantanāmānaṃ putram avāpa ।।
tasmāc ca damo damasya putro rājyavardhano jajñe ।। rājyavardhanāt sudhṛtir abhūt tataś ca naras tasmāc ca kevalaḥ kevalād bandhumān bandhumato vegavān vegavato budhaś tataś ca tṛṇabinduḥ ।। tasyāpy ekā kanyā ilavilā nāma ।। taṃ cālambuṣā nāma varāpsarās tṛṇabinduṃ bheje ।।
tasyām asya viśālo jajñe yaḥ purīṃ vaiśālīṃ nāma nirmame ।। hemacandro viśālasya putro abhavat ।। tasmāc ca sucandras tattanayo dhūmrāśvas tasyāpi sṛñjayo abhūt ।। sṛñjayāt sahadevaḥ । tataḥ kṛśāśvo nāma putro abhavat ।।
somadattaḥ kṛśāśvāj jajñe yo daśāśvamedhān ājahāra ।। tatputraś ca janamejayaḥ । janamejayāt sumatiḥ । ete vaiśālikā bhūbhṛtaḥ ।। śloko apy atra gīyate । dīrghāyuṣo mahātmāno vīryavanto atidhārmikāḥ ।।
śaryāteḥ kanyā sukanyā nāmābhavad yām upayeme cyavanaḥ ।। ānartaś ca nāma dhārmikaḥ śaryātiputro abhūt ।। ānartasyāpi revato nāma putro jajñe yo asāv ānartaviṣayaṃ bubhuje purīṃ ca kuśasthalīm adhyuvāsa ।। revatasyāpi raivataḥ putraḥ kakudmī nāma dharmātmā bhrātṛśatasya jyeṣṭho abhavat ।।
tasya ca revatī nāma kanyā । tām ādāya kasyeyam arhatīti bhagavantam abjayoniṃ praṣṭuṃ brahmalokaṃ jagāma ।। tāvac ca brahmaṇo antike hāhāhūhūsaṃjñābhyāṃ gandharvābhyām atitānaṃ nāma divyaṃ gāndharvam agīyata ।। tāvac ca trimārgaparivartair anekayugaparivṛttitiṣṭhann api raivataḥ śṛṇvan muhūrtam iva mene ।।
gītāvasāne ca bhagavantam abjayoniṃ praṇamya raivataḥ kanyāyogyaṃ varam apṛcchat ।। taṃ cāha bhagavān kathaya yo abhimatas te vara iti ।। punaś ca praṇamya bhagavate tasmai yathābhimatān ātmanaḥ sa varān kathayām āsa । ka eṣāṃ bhagavato abhimato yasmai kanyām imāṃ prayacchāmīti ।।
tataḥ kiṃcidavanataśirāḥ sasmitaṃ bhagavān abjayonir āha ।। ya ete bhavato abhimatā naiteṣāṃ sāmpratam apatyāpatyasaṃtatir apy avanītale asti ।। bahūni hi tavātraiva gāndharvaṃ śṛṇvataś caturyugāny atītāni ।। sāmprataṃ hi bhūtale aṣṭāviṃśatitamasya manoś caturyugam atītaprāyam āsanno hi tatra kaliḥ ।।
anyasmai kanyāratnam idaṃ bhavataikākinā deyam ।। bhavato api mitramantribhṛtyakalatrabandhubalakośādayaḥ samastāḥ kālenaitenātyantam atītāḥ ।। tataḥ punar utpannasādhvasaḥ sa rājā bhagavantaṃ praṇamya papraccha ।। bhagavann evam avasthite mayeyaṃ kasmai deyeti ।।
tataḥ sa bhagavān kiṃcidavanamrakandharaṃ kṛtāñjalibhūtaṃ sarvalokagurur abjayonir āha ।। na ca svarūpaṃ na paraṃ svabhāvaṃ na caiva sāraṃ parameśvarasya ।। ajanmanāśasya samastamūrter anāmarūpasya sanātanasya ।। krodhāc ca rudraḥ sthitihetubhūto yasmāc ca madhye puruṣaḥ parasmāt ।।
rudrasvarūpeṇa ca yo atti viśvaṃ dhatte tathānantavapuḥ samastam ।। pākāya yo agnitvam upetya lokān bibharti pṛthvīvapur avyayātmā ।। dadāti viśvasthitisaṃsthitas tu sarvāvakāśaṃ ca nabhaḥsvarūpī ।। viśvātmanā saṃhriyate antakārī pṛthak trayasyāsya ca yo avyayātmā ।।
sa sarvabhūtaprabhavo dharitryāṃ svāṃśena viṣṇur nṛpate avatīrṇaḥ ।। sā dvārakā saṃprati tatra cāste sa keśavāṃśo baladevanāmā ।। ślāghyo varo asau tanayā taveyaṃ strīratnabhūtā sadṛśo hi yogaḥ ।। dadarśa hrasvān puruṣān aśeṣān alpaujasaḥ svalpavivekavīryān ।।
sīradhvajāya sphaṭikācalābha vakṣaḥsthalāyātuladhīr narendraḥ ।। vināmayām āsa tataś ca sāpi babhūva sadyo vanitā yathānyā ।। dattvā ca kanyāṃ sa nṛpo jagāma himālayaṃ vai tapase dhṛtātmā ।। yāvac ca brahmalokāt kakudmī raivato nābhyeti tāvat puṇyajanasaṃjñā rākṣasās tām asya purīṃ kuśasthalīṃ jaghnuḥ ।।
tac cāsya bhrātṛśataṃ puṇyajanatrāsād diśo bheje ।। tadanvayāś ca kṣatriyāḥ sarvadikṣv abhavan ।। dhṛṣṭasyāpi dhārṣṭakaṃ kṣatram abhavat ।। nabhagasyātmajo nābhāgasaṃjño abhavat । tasya ambarīṣaḥ । ambarīṣasyāpi virūpo abhavat ।।
virūpāt pṛṣadaśvo jajñe tataś ca rathītaraḥ ।। tatrāyaṃ ślokaḥ । ete kṣatraprasūtā vai punaś cāṅgirasāḥ smṛtāḥ । rathītarāṇāṃ pravarāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayaḥ ।।
kṣuvataś ca manor ikṣvākur ghrāṇataḥ putro jajñe ।। tasya putraśatapravarā vikukṣinimidaṇḍākhyās trayaḥ putrā । śakunipramukhāḥ pañcāśat putrāḥ uttarāpatharakṣitāro babhūvuḥ । catvāriṃśad aṣṭau ca dakṣiṇāpathabhūpālāḥ ।। sa cekṣvākur aṣṭakāyām utpādya śrāddhārhaṃ māṃsam ānayeti vikukṣim ājñāpayām āsa । sa tatheti gṛhītājño vanam abhyetyānekān mṛgān hatvātiśrānto atikṣutparīto vikukṣir ekaṃ śaśam abhakṣayat । śeṣaṃ ca māṃsam ānīya pitre nivedayām āsa ।। ikṣvākukulācāryas tatprokṣaṇāya vasiṣṭhaś coditaḥ prāha । alam anenāmedhyenāmiṣeṇa durātmanānena te putreṇaitan māṃsam upahataṃ yato anena śaśo bhakṣitaḥ ।।
tataś cāsau vikukṣir guruṇaivam uktaḥ śaśādasaṃjñām avāpa pitrā ca parityaktaḥ ।। pitary uparate cākhilām etāṃ pṛthvīṃ dharmataḥ śaśāsa ।। śaśādasya puraṃjayo nāma putro abhavat ।। idaṃ cānyat purā hi tretāyāṃ devāsuram atīva bhīṣaṇaṃ yuddham āsīt । tatra cātibalibhir asurair amarāḥ parājitā bhagavantaṃ viṣṇum ārādhayāṃ cakruḥ ।।
prasannaś ca devānām anādinidhanaḥ sakalajagatparāyaṇo nārāyaṇaḥ prāha । jñātam eva mayā yuṣmābhir yad abhilaṣitaṃ tadartham idaṃ śrūyatām । puraṃjayo nāma śaśādasya ca rājarṣes tanayaḥ kṣatriyavaryas taccharīre aham aṃśena svayam evāvatīrya tān aśeṣān asurān nihaniṣyāmi tad bhavadbhiḥ puraṃjayo asuravadhārthāya kāryodyogaḥ kārya iti etac ca śrutvā praṇamya bhagavantaṃ viṣṇum amarāḥ puraṃjayasakāśam ājagmuḥ ।। ūcuś cainaṃ । bho bhoḥ kṣatriyavaryāsmābhir abhyarthitena bhavatāsmākam arātivadhodyatānāṃ sāhāyyaṃ kṛtam icchāmaḥ । tad bhavatāsmākam abhyāgatānāṃ praṇayabhaṅgo na kāryaḥ । ity uktaḥ puraṃjayaḥ prāha । sakalatrailokyanātho yo ayaṃ yuṣmākam indraḥ śatakratur asya yady ahaṃ skandhārūḍho yuṣmadarātibhiḥ saha yotsye tadāhaṃ bhavatāṃ sahāyaḥ । ity ākarṇya samastadevair indreṇa ca bāḍham ity evaṃ samanvicchitam ।। tataś ca śatakrator vṛṣabharūpadhāriṇaḥ kakutstho atiharṣasamanvito bhagavataś carācaraguror acyutasya tejasāpyāyito devāsurasaṃgrāme samastān evāsurān nijaghāna ।। yataś ca vṛṣabhakakutsthena rājñā niṣūditam asurabalam ataś cāsau kakutsthasaṃjñām avāpa ।।
kakutsthasyāpy anenāḥ putro abhūt pṛthur anenasaḥ pṛthor viśvagaśvas tasyāpi cāndro yuvanāśvaś cāndrasya tasya yuvanāśvasya śrāvasto yaḥ purīṃ śrāvastīṃ niveśayām āsa ।। śrāvastasya bṛhadaśvas tasyāpi kuvalayāśvo yo asāv uttaṅkasya maharṣer apakāriṇaṃ dhundhunāmānam asuraṃ vaiṣṇavena tejasāpyāyitaḥ putrasahasrair ekaviṃśatibhiḥ parivṛto jaghāna dhundhumārasaṃjñāṃ cāvāpa ।। tasya ca samastā eva putrā dhundhumukhaniḥśvāsāgninā vipluṣṭā vineśuḥ ।। dṛḍhāśvacandrāśvakapilāśvās trayaḥ kevalaṃ avaśeṣitāḥ ।।
dṛḍhāśvād dharyaśvas tasmān nikumbho nikumbhāt saṃhitāśvaḥ । tataś ca kṛśāśvas । tasmāc ca prasenajit tato yuvanāśvo abhavat ।। tasya cāputrasyātinirvedān munīnām āśramamaṇḍale nivasataḥ kṛpālubhis tair munibhir apatyotpādanāya iṣṭiḥ kṛtā । tasyāṃ ca madhyarātrinivṛttāyāṃ mantrapūtajalapūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ vedimadhye niveśya te munayaḥ suṣupuḥ ।। teṣu ca supteṣv atitṛṭparītaḥ sa bhūpālas tam āśramaṃ viveśa ।। suptāṃś ca tān ṛṣīn naivotthāpayām āsa । tac ca kalaśajalam aparimeyamāhātmyaṃ mantrapūtaṃ papau ।।
prabuddhāś ca ṛṣayaḥ papracchuḥ kenaitan mantrapūtaṃ vāri pītam ।। atra hi pīte rājño yuvanāśvasya patnī mahābalaparākramaṃ putraṃ janayiṣyatīty ākarṇya sa rājā ajānatā mayā pītam ity āha ।। garbhaś ca yuvanāśvasyodare abhavat krameṇa ca vavṛdhe ।। prāptasamayaś ca dakṣiṇakukṣim avanīpater nirbhidya niścakrāma na cāsau rājā mamāra ।।
jāto nāmaiṣa kaṃ dhāsyatīti munayaḥ procuḥ ।। athāgamya devarāḍ abravīt mām ayaṃ dhāsyatīti ।। tato māṃdhātā nāmato abhavat । vaktre cāsya pradeśinī devarājena nyastā tāṃ papau । tāṃ cāmṛtasrāviṇīm āsvādyāhnaiva sa vyavardhata ।। sa tu māṃdhātā cakravartī saptadvīpāṃ mahīṃ bubhuje ।।
bhavati cātra ślokaḥ । yāvat sūrya udeti sma yāvac ca pratitiṣṭhati । sarvaṃ tad yauvanāśvasya māṃdhātuḥ kṣetram ucyate ।। māṃdhātā śaśabindor duhitaraṃ bindumatīm upayeme । purukutsam ambarīṣaṃ ca mucakundaṃ ca tasyāṃ putratrayam utpādayām āsa ।। pañcāśac ca duhitaras tasya nṛpater babhūvuḥ ।। bahvṛcaś ca saubharir nāma ṛṣir antarjale dvādaśābdaṃ kālam uvāsa ।।
tatra cāntarjale saṃmado nāmātibahuprajo atipramāṇo mīnādhipatir āsīt । tasya ca putrapautradauhitrāḥ pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhato agrato vakṣaḥpucchaśirasāṃ copari bhramantas tenaiva sahāharniśam atinirvṛtā remire ।। sa cāpi tatsparśopacīyamānaharṣaprakarṣo bahuprakāraṃ tasya ṛṣeḥ paśyatas tair ātmajapautradauhitrādibhiḥ sahānudinaṃ bahuprakāraṃ reme ।। athāntarjalāvasthitaḥ sa saubharir ekāgratāsamādhānam apahāyānudinaṃ tat tasya matsyasyātmajapautradauhitrādibhiḥ sahātiramaṇīyaṃ lalitam avekṣyācintayat । aho dhanyo ayam īdṛśam apy anabhimataṃ yonyantaram avāpyaibhir ātmajapautrādibhiḥ saha ramamāṇo atīvāsmākaṃ spṛhām utpādayati । vayam apy evaṃ putrādibhiḥ saha ramiṣyāmaḥ । ity evam abhisamīkṣya sa tasmād antarjalān niṣkramya nirveṣṭukāmaḥ kanyārthaṃ māṃdhātāraṃ rājānam agacchat ।। āgamanaśravaṇasamanantaraṃ cotthāya tena rājñā samyag arghādinā pūjitaḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ saubharir uvāca ।।
na hy arthinaḥ kāryavaśābhyupetāḥ kakutsthagotre vimukhāḥ prayānti ।। kiṃtv arthinām arthitadānadīkṣā kṛtavrataṃ ślāghyam idaṃ kulaṃ te ।। yat prārthanābhaṅgabhayād bibhemi tasmād ahaṃ rājavarātiduḥkhāt ।। iti ṛṣivacanam ākarṇya sa rājā jarājarjaritadehaṃ tam ṛṣim ālokya pratyākhyānakātaras tasmāc ca bhagavataḥ śāpato bibhyatkiṃcidadhomukhaś ciraṃ dadhyau ।।
yāvaśyadeyā tanayā tayaiva kṛtārthatā no yadi kiṃ na labdham ।। atha tasya śāpabhītaḥ sapraśrayam uvācāsau rājā ।। bhagavann asmatkulasthitir iyaṃ ya eva kanyāyā abhirucito abhijanavān varas tasmai kanyā pradīyate । bhagavadājñāsmanmanorathānām apy agocaravartinī । katham apy eṣā saṃjātā tad evam upasthite na vidmaḥ kiṃ kurma ity etan mayā cintyate । ity abhihite ca tena bhūbhujā munir acintayat । aho ayam anyo asmatpratyākhyānopāyo vṛddho ayam anabhimataḥ strīṇāṃ kim uta kanyānām ity amunā saṃcintyaivam abhihitam । evam astu tathā kariṣyāmīti saṃcintya māṃdhātāram uvāca ।।
yady evaṃ tadādiśyatām asmākaṃ praveśāya kanyāntaḥpuravarṣavaraḥ । yadi kanyaiva kācin mām abhilaṣati tadāhaṃ dārasaṃgrahaṃ kariṣyāmīty anyathā cet tad alam asmākam etenātītakālārambhenety uktvā virarāma ।। tataś ca māṃdhātrā muniśāpaśaṅkitena kanyāntaḥpuravarṣavaraḥ samājñaptaḥ ।। kanyāntaḥpuraṃ praviśann eva bhagavān akhilasiddhagandharvamanuṣyebhyo atiśayena kamanīyaṃ rūpam akarot ।। praveśya ca tam ṛṣim antaḥpuravarṣavaras tāḥ kanyakāḥ prāha ।।
bhavatīnāṃ janayitā mahārājaḥ samājñāpayati । ayam asmān brahmarṣiḥ kanyārthī samabhyāgato mayā cāsya pratijñātaṃ yady asmatkanyakā kācid bhagavantaṃ varayati tat kanyāyāś chande nāhaṃ paripanthānaṃ kariṣyāmīty ākarṇya sarvā eva tāḥ kanyāḥ sānurāgāḥ samanmathāḥ kareṇava ivebhayūthapatiṃ tam ṛṣim ahamahamikayā varayāṃ babhūvuḥ ।। mamaiva bhartā vidhinaiṣa sṛṣṭaḥ sṛṣṭāham asyopaśamaṃ prayāhi ।। mayā mayeti kṣitipātmajānāṃ tadartham atyarthakalir babhūva ।। tadā sa kanyādhikṛto nṛpāya yathāvad ācaṣṭa vinamramūrtiḥ ।।
tadavagamāt kiṃ kim etat kathaya kiṃ karomīti kiṃ mayābhihitam ity ākulamatir anicchann api kathamapi rājānumene ।। kṛtānurūpavivāhaś ca maharṣiḥ sakalā eva tāḥ kanyāḥ svam āśramam anayat ।। tatra cāśeṣaśilpiśilpapraṇetāraṃ dhātāram ivānyaṃ viśvakarmāṇam āhūya sakalakanyānām ekaikasyāḥ protphullapaṅkajāḥ kūjatkalahaṃsakāraṇḍavādi vihaṃgamābhirāmajalāśayāḥ sopavanāḥ sāvakāśāḥ sādhuśayyāparicchadāḥ prāsādāḥ kriyantām ity ādideśa ।। tac ca tathaivānuṣṭhitam aśeṣaśilpaviśeṣācāryas tvaṣṭā darśitavān ।।
tataś ca paramarṣiṇā saubhariṇājñaptas teṣu gṛheṣv anapāyī nandanāmā mahānidhir āsāṃ cakre ।। tato anavaratabhakṣyabhojyalehyādyupabhogair āgatānugatabhṛtyādīn aharniśam aśeṣagṛheṣu tāḥ kṣitīśaduhitaro bhojayām āsuḥ ।। ekadā tu duhitṛsnehākṛṣṭahṛdayaḥ sa mahīpatir atiduḥkhitās tāḥ sukhitā veti vicintya tasya maharṣer āśramam upetya sphuradaṃśumālāṃ sphaṭikamayīṃ prāsādamālām atiramyopavanajalāśayāṃ dadarśa ।। praviśya caikaṃ prāsādam ātmajāṃ pariṣvajya kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ pravṛddhasnehanayanāmbugarbhanayano abravīt ।।
apy atra vatse bhavatyāḥ sukham uta kiṃcid asukham api te maharṣiḥ snehavān uta saṃsmaryate asmadgṛhavāsasyety uktā tattanayā pitaram āha ।। tātātiramaṇīyaḥ prāsādo atrātimanojñam upavanam atikalavākyavihaṃgābhirutāḥ protphullapadmākarā jalāśayāḥ । manonukūlabhakṣyabhojyānulepanavastra bhūṣaṇādibhogopabhogā mṛdūni śayanāni sarvasaṃpatsamavetam etad gārhasthyam tathāpi kena vā janmabhūmir na smaryate ।। tvatprasādād idam aśeṣam atiśobhanam ।। kiṃtv ekaṃ mamaitad duḥkhakāraṇaṃ yad asmadgṛhān maharṣir ayaṃ madbhartā na niṣkrāmati mamaiva kevalam atiprītyā samīpavartī nānyāsām asmadbhaginīnām ।।
evaṃ ca mama sahodaryā duḥkhitā ity evam atiduḥkhakāraṇam ity uktas tayā dvitīyaṃ prāsādam upetya svatanayāṃ pariṣvajyopaviṣṭas tathaiva pṛṣṭavān ।। tayāpi tathaiva sarvam etat prāsādādyupabhogasukham ākhyātaṃ mamaiva kevalam atiprītyā pārśvavartī nāsmadbhaginīnām ity evamādi śrutvā samastaprāsādeṣu rājā praviveśa tanayās tathaivāpṛcchat ।। sarvābhiś ca tābhis tathaivābhihitaḥ paritoṣavismayanirbharavivaśahṛdayo bhagavantaṃ saubharim ekāntāvasthitam upetya kṛtapūjo abravīt ।। dṛṣṭas te bhagavan sumahān eṣa siddhiprabhāvo naivaṃvidham anyasya kasyacid asmābhir vibhūtivilasitam upalakṣitaṃ । kiyad etad bhagavaṃs tapasaḥ phalam ity abhipūjya tam ṛṣiṃ tatraiva tena ṛṣivaryeṇa saha kiṃcit kālam abhimatopabhogaṃ bubhuje svapuraṃ ca jagāma ।।
kālena gacchatā tasya rājatanayāsu putraśataṃ sārdham abhavat ।। anudinānurūḍhasnehaprasaraś ca sa tatrātīva mamatākṛṣṭahṛdayo abhavat ।। apy ete asmatputrāḥ kalabhāṣiṇaḥ padbhyāṃ gaccheyuḥ । apy ete yauvanino bhaveyuḥ । api kṛtadārān etān paśyeyam । apy eṣāṃ putrā bhaveyuḥ । apy etatputrān putrasamanvitān paśyeyam evamādimanorathān anudinakālasaṃpattivṛttim avetyaitat saṃcintayām āsa । aho me mohasyātivistāraḥ ।। pūrṇeṣu pūrṇeṣu punar navānām utpattayaḥ santi manorathānām ।।
dṛṣṭāḥ sutās tattanayaprasūtiṃ draṣṭuṃ punar vāñchati me antarātmā ।। pūrṇe api tatrāpy aparasya janma nivāryate kena manorathasya ।। manorathāsaktiparasya cittaṃ na jāyate vai paramārthasaṅgi ।। parigrahaḥ saṅgakṛto mamāyaṃ parigrahotthā ca mahāvidhitsā ।।
parigraheṇa kṣitipātmajānāṃ sutair anekair bahulīkṛtaṃ tat ।। vistāram eṣyaty atiduḥkhahetuḥ parigraho vai mamatānidhānam ।। matsyasya saṅgād abhavac ca yo me sutādirāgo muṣito asmi tena ।। ārūḍhayogo api nipātyate adhaḥ saṅgena yogī kim utālpasiddhiḥ ।।
yathā hi bhūyaḥ parihīnadoṣo janasya duḥkhair bhavitā na duḥkhī ।। sitāsitaṃ ceśvaram īśvarāṇām ārādhayiṣye tapasaiva viṣṇum ।। mamācalaṃ cittam apetadoṣaṃ sadāstu viṣṇāv abhavāya bhūyaḥ ।। yasmān na kiṃcit tam ahaṃ gurūṇāṃ paraṃ guruṃ saṃśrayam emi viṣṇum ।।
ity ātmānam ātmanaivābhidhāyāsau saubharir apahāya putragṛhāsanaparicchadādikam aśeṣam arthajātaṃ sakalabhāryāsamaveto vanaṃ praviveśa ।। tatrāpy anudinaṃ vaikhānasaniṣpādyam aśeṣaṃ kriyākalāpaṃ niṣpādya kṣapitasakalapāpaḥ paripakvamanovṛttir ātmany agnīn samāropya bhikṣur abhavat ।। bhagavaty āsajyākhilakarmakalāpaṃ ajam avikāram amaraṇādidharmam avāpa paraṃ paravatām acyutapadam ।। ity etan māṃdhātur duhitṛsaṃbandhād ākhyātam ।।
yaś caitat saubharicaritam anusmarati paṭhati śṛṇoti avadhārayati lekhayati tasyāṣṭau janmany asanmatir asaddharmo vā manaso asanmārgācaraṇam aśeṣaheyeṣu vā mamatvaṃ na bhavati ।। ato māṃdhātuḥ putrasaṃtatir abhidhīyate ।। ambarīṣasya māṃdhātus tanayasya yuvanāśvaḥ putro abhūt ।। tasmād dharīto yato aṅgiraso hārītāḥ ।।
rasātale ca mauneyā nāma gandharvāḥ ṣaṭkoṭisaṃkhyās tair aśeṣāṇi nāgakulāny apahṛtapradhānaratnādhipatyāny akriyanta ।। taiś ca gandharvavīryāvadhūtair urageśvarair bhagavān aśeṣadeveśastavaśravaṇonmīlitonnidrapuṇḍarīkanayano jalaśayano nidrāvasānād vibuddhaḥ praṇipatyābhihitaḥ । bhagavann apy asmākam etebhyo gandharvebhyo bhayam upaśamam eṣyatīti āha bhagavān anādipuruṣaḥ puruṣottamo yauvanāśvasya māṃdhātuḥ purukutsanāmā putras tam aham anupraviśya tān aśeṣaduṣṭagandharvān upaśamaṃ nayiṣyāmi ।। ity ākarṇya bhagavate kṛtapraṇāmāḥ punar nāgalokam āgatāḥ pannagapatayo narmadāṃ ca purukutsānayanāya codayām āsuḥ ।। sā cainaṃ rasātalaṃ nītavatī ।।
rasātalagataś cāsau bhagavattejasāpyāyitātmavīryaḥ sakalagandharvāñ jaghāna । punaś ca svabhavanam ājagāma ।। sakalapannagapatayaś ca narmadāyai varaṃ daduḥ । yas te anusmaraṇasamavetaṃ nāmagrahaṇaṃ kariṣyati na tasya sarpaviṣabhayaṃ bhaviṣyatīti ।। atra ca ślokaḥ । namo astu narmade tubhyaṃ trāhi māṃ viṣasarpataḥ ।। ।
ity uccāryāharniśam andhakārapraveśe vā na sarpair daśyate na cāpi kṛtānusmaraṇabhujo viṣam api bhuktam upaghātāya bhaviṣyati ।। purukutsāya ca saṃtativicchedo na bhavato bhaviṣyatīty uragapatayo varaṃ daduḥ ।। purukutso narmadāyāṃ trasadasyum ajījanat ।। trasadasyutaḥ saṃbhūtas tato anaraṇyas taṃ rāvaṇo digvijaye nijaghāna । anaraṇyasya pṛṣadaśvaḥ pṛṣadaśvasya haryaśvaḥ putro abhavat । tataś ca vasumanās tasyāpi tridhanvā tridhanvanas trayyāruṇaḥ ।।
tasmāt satyavrato yo asau triśaṅkusaṃjñām avāpa । caṇḍālatām upagataś ca ।। dvādaśavārṣikyām anāvṛṣṭyāṃ viśvāmitrakalatrāpatyapoṣaṇārthaṃ cāṇḍālapratigrahapariharaṇāya jāhnavītīranyagrodhe mṛgamāṃsam anudinaṃ babandha ।। parituṣṭena viśvāmitreṇa saśarīraḥ svargam āropitaḥ ।। triśaṅkor hariścandras tasmād rohitāśvas tataś ca harito haritāc cañcuś cañcor vijayasudevau ruruko vijayād rurukasya vṛkaḥ ।।
tato bāhur yo asau haihayatālajaṅghādibhir avajito antarvatnyā mahiṣyā saha vanaṃ viveśa ।। tasyāś ca sapatnyā garbhastambhanāya garo dattaḥ ।। tenāsyā garbhaḥ saptavarṣāṇi jaṭhara eva tasthau । sa ca bāhur vṛddhabhāvād aurvāśramasamīpe mamāra ।। sā tasya bhāryā citāṃ kṛtvā tam āropyānumaraṇakṛtaniścayābhūt ।।
athaitām atītānāgatavartamānakālavedī bhagavān aurvaḥ svāśramān nirgatyābravīt । alam anenāsadgrāheṇākhilabhūmaṇḍalapatir ativīryaparākramo naikayajñakṛd arātipakṣakṣayakartā tavodare cakravartī tiṣṭhati ।। maivaṃ maivaṃ sāhasādhyavasāyinī bhavetyukte ca sā tasmād anumaraṇanirbandhād virarāma ।। tenaiva bhagavatā svāśramam ānīyata । katipayadinābhyantare ca sahaiva tena gareṇātitejasvī bālako jajñe । tasyaurvo jātakarmādikriyāṃ niṣpādya sagara iti nāma cakāra ।। kṛtopanayanaṃ cainam aurvo vedaśāstrāṇy astraṃ cāgneyaṃ bhārgavākhyam adhyāpayām āsa ।।
utpannabuddhiś ca mātaram apṛcchat । amba katham atra vayaṃ kva tāto asmākam ity evamādi pṛcchatas tanmātā sarvam avocat ।। tataḥ pitṛrājyaharaṇāmarṣito haihayatālajaṅghādivadhāya pratijñām akarot । prāyaśaś ca haihayāñ jaghāna ।। śakayavanakāmbojapāradapahlavā hanyamānās tatkulaguruṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। athaitān vasiṣṭho jīvanmṛtakān kṛtvā sagaram āha । vatsālam ebhir jīvanmṛtakair anumṛtaiḥ ।।
ete ca mayaiva tvatpratijñāparipālanāya nijadharmadvijasaṅgaparityāgaṃ kāritāḥ ।। sa tatheti tad guruvacanam abhinandya teṣāṃ veṣānyatvam akārayat yavanān muṇḍitaśiraso ardhamuṇḍāñ chakān pralambakeśān pāradān pahlavāṃś ca śmaśrudharān niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārān etān anyāṃś ca kṣatriyāṃś cakāra ।। te ca nijadharmaparityāgād brāhmaṇaiś ca parityaktā mlecchatāṃ yayuḥ ।। sagaro api svam adhiṣṭhānam āgamya askhalitacakraḥ saptadvīpavatīm imām urvīṃ praśaśāsa ।।
kāśyapaduhitā sumatir vidarbharājatanayā keśinī ca dve bhārye sagarasyāstām ।। tābhyāṃ cāpatyārtham ārādhita aurvaḥ parameṇa samādhinā varam adāt ।। ekā vaṃśadharam ekaṃ putram aparā ṣaṣṭiṃ putrasahasrāṇi janayiṣyati ।। yasyā yad abhimataṃ tad icchayā gṛhyatām ity ukte keśinī putram ekaṃ sumatiḥ putrasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiṃ vavre ।।
tatheti ca ṛṣiṇābhihite alpair evāhobhiḥ keśinī putram ekam asamañjasaṃ nāma vaṃśadharam asūta । vinatātanayāyās tu sumatyāḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ putrasahasrāṇy abhavan ।। tasmād asamañjaso aṃśumān nāma kumāro jajñe ।। sa tv asamañjā bālyād evāpavṛttaḥ pitā cāsyācintayad ayam atītabālyo buddhimān bhaviṣyatīti ।। atha tatrāpi vayasy atīte tac caritam evainaṃ pitā tatyāja ।।
tāny api ṣaṣṭiḥ kumārasahasrāṇy asamañjasaś caritam anucakruḥ ।। tataś cāsamañjasaś caritānukāribhiḥ sāgarair apadhvastayajñādisanmārge jagati devāḥ sakalavidyāmayam asaṃspṛṣṭam aśeṣadoṣair bhagavataḥ puruṣottamasyāṃśabhūtaṃ kapilaṃ praṇamya tad artham ūcuḥ ।। bhagavann ebhiḥ sagaratanayair asamañjasaś caritam anugamyate । katham evam ebhir anusaradbhir jagad bhaviṣyatīty ārtajagatparitrāṇāya ca bhagavato atra śarīragrahaṇam ity ākarṇya bhagavān alpair eva dinair ete vinaṅkṣyantīty uktavān ।। tatrāntare ca sagaro hayamedham ārebhe tatra ca putrair adhiṣṭhitam asyāśvaṃ ko apy apahṛtya bhuvo bilaṃ praviveśa ।।
tataś cāśvānveṣaṇāya tanayān yuyoja tatas tattanayāś cāśvakhurapadavīm anusaranto atinirbandhena vasudhātalam ekaiko yojanaṃ yojanam avaneś cakhāna ।। pātāle cāśvaṃ paribhramantaṃ tam avanīpatitanayās te dadṛśuḥ ।। nātidūrāvasthitaṃ ca bhagavantam apaghane śaratkāle arkam iva tejobhir anavaratam ūrdhvam adhaś cāśeṣadiśaś codbhāsayamānaṃ kapilarṣim apaśyan ।। tataś codyatāyudhā durātmāyam asmadapakārī yajñavighātakartā hayahartā hanyatāṃ hanyatām ity avocan । tatas tenāpi bhagavatā kiṃcidīṣatparivartitalocanenāvalokitāḥ svaśarīrasamutthenāgninā dahyamānā vineśuḥ ।।
sagaro apy avagamyāśvānusāri tat putrabalam aśeṣaṃ paramarṣikapilatejasā dagdham aṃśumantam asamañjasaḥ putram aśvānayanāya codayām āsa ।। sa tu sagaratanayakhātamārgeṇa kapilam upagamya bhaktinamras tathā tuṣṭāva yathainaṃ bhagavān āha gacchainaṃ pitāmahāyāśvaṃ prāpaya varaṃ vṛṇīṣva ca putrapautraś ca te svargād gaṅgāṃ ānayiṣyatīti ।। athāṃśumān api brahmadaṇḍahatānām asmatpitṝṇām asvargayogyānāṃ svargaprāptikaraṃ varam asmākaṃ bhagavān prayacchatv iti pratyāha ।। taṃ cāha bhagavān uktam evaitan mayā pautras te tridivād gaṅgāṃ bhuvam ānayiṣyatīti । tadambhasā saṃspṛṣṭeṣv asthibhasmasv ete svargam ārokṣyanti । bhagavadviṣṇupādāṅguṣṭhavinirgatasya jalasya hi tanmāhātmyam ।।
yan na kevalam abhisaṃdhipūrvakaṃ snānādyupabhogeṣūpakārakam anabhisaṃhitam apy apetaprāṇasyāsthicarmasnāyukeśādyutsṛṣṭaṃ śarīrajam yad bhūpatitam śarīriṇaṃ sadyaḥ svargaṃ nayatīty uktaḥ praṇamya ca bhagavate aśvam ādāya pitāmahayajñam ājagāma ।। sagaro apy aśvam āsādya taṃ yajñaṃ samāpayām āsa ।। sāgaraṃ cātmajaprītyā putratve kalpayām āsa ।। tasyāṃśumato dilīpaḥ putro abhavat ।।
dilīpasya bhagīratho yo asau gaṅgāṃ svargād ihānīya bhāgīrathīsaṃjñāṃ cakāra ।। bhagīrathāc chrutas tasyāpi nābhāgas tato ambarīṣas tasmāt sindhudvīpaḥ । sindhudvīpād ayutāyus tatputraś ca ṛtuparṇo nalasahāyo akṣahṛdayajño abhūt ।। ṛtuparṇaputraḥ sarvakāmas tattanayaḥ sudāsaḥ sudāsāt saudāso mitrasahanāmā ।। sa cāṭavyāṃ mṛgayāṃ gato vyāghradvayam apaśyat ।।
tābhyāṃ ca tad vanam apamṛgaṃ kṛtaṃ sa caikaṃ tayor bāṇena jaghāna ।। mriyamāṇaś cāsāv atibhīṣaṇākṛtir atikarālavadano rākṣaso abhavat ।। dvitīyo api pratikriyāṃ te kariṣyāmīty uktvāntardhānaṃ jagāma ।। kālena gacchatā sa saudāso yajñam ayajat । pariniṣṭhitayajñe cācārye vasiṣṭhe niṣkrānte tad rakṣo vasiṣṭharūpam āsthāya yajñāvasāne mama samāṃsaṃ bhojanaṃ deyaṃ tat saṃskriyatāṃ kṣaṇād ihāgamiṣyāmīty uktvā niṣkrāntaḥ ।।
bhūyaś ca sūdaveṣaṃ kṛtvā rājājñayā mānuṣamāṃsaṃ saṃskṛtya rājñe nyavedayat ।। asāv api hiraṇyapātrasthitaṃ māṃsam ādāya vasiṣṭhāgamanapratīkṣo abhavat । āgatāya ca vasiṣṭhāya niveditavān ।। sa cāpy acintayad aho asya rājño dauḥśīlyaṃ yenaitan māṃsam asmākaṃ prayacchati kim etad dravyajātam iti dhyānaparo abhūt । apaśyac ca tan mānuṣamāṃsam । tataś ca krodhakaluṣīkṛtacetā rājānaṃ prati śāpam utsasarja । yasmād abhojyam etad asmadvidhānāṃ tapasvinām avagacchann api bhavān mahyaṃ dadāti tasmāt tavaivātra lolupā buddhir bhaviṣyatīti ।। anantaraṃ ca tenāpi bhagavataivābhihito asmīty ukte kiṃ kiṃ mayaivābhihitam iti saṃcintya munir api samādhau tasthau ।।
samādhivijñānāvagatārthaś cānugrahaṃ tasmai cakāra । nātyantikam etad dvādaśābdaṃ tava bhojanaṃ bhaviṣyatīti ।। asāv api tu pragṛhyodakāñjaliṃ muniśāpapradānāyodyato bhagavān asmadgurur nārhasy enaṃ kuladevatābhūtam ācāryaṃ śaptum iti madayantyā svapatnyā prasāditaḥ । sasyāmbudarakṣaṇārthaṃ tac chāpāmbu norvyāṃ na cākāśe cikṣepa tenaiva svapadau siṣeca ।। tena krodhāśritenāmbhasā dagdhacchāyau tatpādau kalmāṣatām upagatau । tataḥ sa kalmāṣapādasaṃjñām avāpa ।। vasiṣṭhaśāpāc ca ṣaṣṭhe kāle rākṣasabhāvam upetyāṭavyāṃ paryaṭann anekaśo mānuṣān abhakṣayat ।।
ekadā tu kaṃcin munim ṛtukāle bhāryayā saha saṃgataṃ dadarśa । tayoś ca tam atibhīṣaṇaṃ rākṣasam avalokya trāsāt pradhāvitayor dampatyor brāhmaṇaṃ jagrāha ।। tataḥ sā brāhmaṇī bahuśas taṃ yācitavatī । prasīdekṣvākukulatilakabhūtas tvaṃ mahārāja mitrasaho na rākṣaso nārhasi strīdharmasukhābhijño mayy akṛtārthāyām imaṃ madbhartāram attum ity evaṃ bahuprakāraṃ tasyāṃ vilapantyāṃ vyāghraḥ paśum iva taṃ brāhmaṇam abhakṣayat ।। tataś cātikopasamanvitā brāhmaṇī taṃ rājānaṃ yasmād evaṃ mayy atṛptāyāṃ tvayāyaṃ matpatir bhakṣitaḥ । tasmāt tvam apy antaṃ kāmopabhogapravṛttaḥ prāpsyasīti śaśāpa । agniṃ praviveśa ca ।। tatas tasya dvādaśābdaviparyaye vimuktaśāpasya strīviṣayābhilāṣiṇo madayantī smārayām āsa ।।
tataḥ param asau strībhogaṃ tatyāja । vasiṣṭhaś cāputreṇa rājñā putrārtham abhyarthito madayantyāṃ garbhādhānaṃ cakāra । yadā ca saptavarṣāṇy asau garbho na jajñe tatas taṃ garbham aśmanā sā devī jaghāna । putraś cājāyata tasya cāśmaka eva nāmābhavat ।। aśmakasya mūlako nāma putro abhavat । yo asau niḥkṣatre kṣmātale asmin kriyamāṇe strībhir vivastrābhiḥ parivārya rakṣitaḥ tatas taṃ nārīkavacam udāharanti ।। mūlakād daśarathas tasmād ilivilas tataś ca viśvasahaḥ । tasmāc ca khaṭvāṅgo dilīpaḥ yo asau devāsurāṇāṃ saṃgrāme devair abhyarthito asurāñ jaghāna । svarge ca kṛtapriyair devair varagrahaṇāya coditaḥ prāha । yady avaśyaṃ varo grāhyas tan mamāyuḥ kathyatām iti । anantaraṃ ca tair uktam ekamuhūrtapramāṇaṃ tavāyur ity ukto athāskhalitagatinā vimānena laghimaguṇo martyalokam āgamyedam āha । yathā na brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sakāśād ātmāpi me priyataraḥ । na ca svadharmollaṅghanaṃ mayā kadācid apy anuṣṭhitam । na ca sakaladevamānuṣapaśuvṛkṣādike apy acyutavyatirekavatī dṛṣṭir mamābhūt । tathā tam eva devaṃ munijanānusmṛtaṃ bhagavantam askhalitagatiḥ prāpayeyam ity aśeṣadevagurau bhagavaty anirdeśyavapuṣi sattāmātrātmany ātmānaṃ paramātmani vāsudevākhye yuyoja । tatraiva ca layam avāpa ।। khaṭvāṅgena samo nānyaḥ kaścid urvyāṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
trayo abhisaṃdhitā lokā buddhyā dānena caiva hi ।। khaṭvāṅgād dīrghabāhuḥ putro abhavat । tato raghus tasmād apy ajaḥ । ajād daśaratho daśarathasyāpi bhagavān abjanābho jagatsthityartham ātmāṃśena rāmalakṣmaṇabharataśatrughnarūpiṇā caturdhā putratvam āyāsīt । rāmo api bāla eva viśvāmitrayajñarakṣaṇāya gacchaṃs tāṭakāṃ jaghāna ।। yajñe ca mārīcam iṣupātāhataṃ dūraṃ cikṣepa subāhupramukhāṃś ca kṣayam anayat । darśanamātreṇaivāhalyām apāpāṃ cakāra । janakagṛhe ca māheśvaraṃ cāpam anāyāsenaiva babhañja । sītāṃ ca ayonijāṃ janakarājatanayāṃ vīryaśulkāṃ lebhe ।। sakalakṣatrakṣayakāriṇam aśeṣahaihayakuladhūmaketubhūtaṃ ca paraśurāmam apāstavīryabalāvalepaṃ cakāra ।।
pitṛvacanāc cāgaṇitarājyābhilāṣo bhrātṛbhāryāsamaveto vanaṃ viveśa ।। virādhakharadūṣaṇādīn kabandhavālinau ca nijaghāna ।। baddhvā cāmbhonidhim aśeṣarākṣasakulakṣayaṃ kṛtvā daśānanāpahṛtāṃ tadvadhāpahatakalaṅkām apy analapraveśaśuddhām aśeṣadeveśasaṃstūyamānāṃ sītāṃ janakarājatanayām ayodhyām āninye ।। viśvāmitrabharadvājāgastyaprabhṛtibhir munivaraiḥ ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvaiḥ saṃstūyamāno nṛtyagītavādyākhilalokamaṅgalavādyair vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgabherīpaṭahaśaṅkhakāhalagomukhaprabhṛtibhiḥ sunādaiḥ samastabhūbhṛtāṃ madhye sakalalokarakṣārthaṃ yathocitam abhiṣikto dāśarathiḥ kosalendro raghukulatilako jānakīpriyo bhrātṛtrayapriyaḥ siṃhāsanagato dvādaśābdasahasraṃ rājyam akarot ।।
bharato api gandharvaviṣayasādhanāyogragandharvakoṭīs tisro jaghāna । śatrughnenāpy atibalaparākramo madhuputro lavaṇo nāma rākṣaseśvaro nihato madhurā ca niveśitā ।। ity evamādiatulabalaparākramair atiduṣṭanibarhaṇair aśeṣasyāsya jagato niṣpāditasthitayo rāmalakṣmaṇabharataśatrughnāḥ punar api divam ārūḍhāḥ ।। ye api teṣu bhagavadaṃśeṣv anurāgiṇaḥ kosalanagarajanapadās te api tanmanasas tatsalokatām avāpuḥ ।। rāmasya tu kuśalavau putrau lakṣmaṇasyāṅgadacandraketū takṣapuṣkarau bharatasya subāhuśūrasenau śatrughnasya kuśasyātithir atither api niṣadhaḥ putro abhavat । niṣadhasyāpi nalas tasya api nabho nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīkaḥ । tattanayaḥ kṣemadhanvā tasya ca devānīkas tasyāpy ahīnagus tato rurus tasya ca pāriyātraḥ pāriyātrād dalo dalāc chalas tasyāpy uktha ukthād vajranābhas tasmāc chaṅkhanābhas tato vyutthitāśvas tataś ca viśvasaho jajñe ।।
hiraṇyanābhas tato mahāyogīśvaro jaiminiśiṣyo yato yājñavalkyo yogam avāpa ।। hiraṇyanābhasya putraḥ puṣyas tasmād dhruvasaṃdhis tataḥ sudarśanas tasmād agnivarṇas tataś ca śīghragas tasyāpi maruḥ putro abhūt yo asau yogam āsthāyādyāpi kalāpagrāmam āśritas tiṣṭhati । āgāmiyuge sūryavaṃśakṣatrapravartayitā bhaviṣyati । prasuśrutas tasyātmajas tasyāpi susaṃdhis tataś cāpy amarṣas tasya ca mahasvāṃs tataś ca viśrutavāṃs tato bṛhadbalo yo arjunatanayenābhimanyunā bhāratayuddhe kṣayam anīyata ।। eteṣāṃ caritaṃ śṛṇvan sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। ikṣvākutanayo yo asau nimir nāmā sa tu sahasrasaṃvatsaraṃ satram ārebhe vasiṣṭhaṃ ca hotāraṃ varayām āsa ।।
tam āha vasiṣṭho aham indreṇa pañcavarṣaśataṃ yāgārthaṃ prathamataraṃ vṛtas tadanantaraṃ pratipālyatām āgatas tavāpi ṛtvig bhaviṣyāmīty ukte sa pṛthivīpatir na kiṃcid uktavān ।। vasiṣṭho apy anena samanvicchitam ity amarapater yāgam akarot ।। so api tatkālam evānyair gautamādibhir yāgam akārayat । samāpte cāmarapater yāge tvarāvān vasiṣṭho nimeḥ karma kariṣyāmīty ājagāma । tatkarmakartṛtvaṃ ca tatra gautamasya dṛṣṭvātha svapate tasmai rājñe mām apratyākhyāyaitad anena gautamāya karmāntaraṃ samarpitaṃ yasmāt tasmād ayaṃ videho bhaviṣyatīti śāpaṃ dadau ।। pratibuddhaś cāsāv avanipatir api prāha । yasmān mām asaṃbhāṣyājñānata eva śayānasya śāpotsargam asau duṣṭaguruś cakāra tasmāt tasyāpi dehaḥ patito bhaviṣyatīti pratiśāpaṃ dattvā deham atyajat ।।
tasmāc chāpāc ca mitrāvaruṇayos tejasi vasiṣṭhatejaḥ praviṣṭam । urvaśīdarśanād udbhūtabījaprapātayos sakāśād vasiṣṭho deham aparaṃ lebhe ।। nimer api taccharīram atimanoharatailagandhādibhir upasaṃskriyamāṇaṃ naiva kledādikaṃ doṣam avāpa sadyomṛtam iva tasthau । yajñasamāptau bhāgagrahaṇāyāgatān devān v devān āgatān ṛtvija ūcuḥ । yajamānāya varo dīyatām iti devaiś ca chandito asau nimir āha ।। bhagavanto akhilasaṃsāraduḥkhasaṃghātasya chettāro na hy etāvaj jagaty anyad duḥkham asti yac charīrātmanor viyoge bhavati । tad aham icchāmi sakalalokalocaneṣu vastuṃ na punaḥ śarīragrahaṇaṃ kartum ity evam uktair devair asāv aśeṣabhūtānāṃ netreṣv avatāritaḥ ।। tato bhūtāny unmeṣanimeṣaṃ cakruḥ । aputrasya tasya bhūbhujaḥ śarīram arājakabhīravas te munayo araṇyā mamanthuḥ ।।
tatra ca kumāro jajñe jananāj janakasaṃjñāṃ cāvāpa ।। abhūd videho asya piteti vaideho mathanān mithir abhūt । tasyodāvasuḥ putro abhavat । udāvasor nandivardhanas tataḥ suketuḥ tasmāc ca devarātas tataś ca bṛhadukthas tasya ca mahāvīryas tasyāpi satyadhṛtis dhṛtiḥ tataś ca dhṛṣṭaketur ajāyata dhṛṣṭaketor haryaśvas tasya ca marur maroḥ pratibandhakas tasmāt kṛtarathas tasmāt kṛtis tasya vibudhaḥ tasyāpi mahādhṛtis tataś ca kṛtirātas tato mahāromā । tasya suvarṇaromā tasyāpi hrasvaromā tataḥ sīradhvajo abhūt । tasya putrārthaṃ yajanabhuvaṃ kṛṣataḥ sīre sītā duhitā samutpannā । sīradhvajasya bhrātā sāṃkāśyādhipatiḥ kuśadhvajanāmā । sīradhvajasyāpatyaṃ bhānumān bhānumataḥ śatadyumnaḥ tasya śucis tasmād ūrjavaho putro jajñe ।। tasyāpi śatadhvajaḥ tataḥ kuṇiḥ kuṇer añjanas tatputra ṛtujit tato ariṣṭanemis tasmāc chrutāyuḥ śrutāyuṣaḥ supārvas tasmāt saṃjayas tataḥ kṣemāris tasmād anenās tasmād mīnarathas tasya satyarathas tasya sātyarathiḥ sātyarather upagus tasmāc chāśvatas tasmāt sudhanvā tasyāpi subhāṣaḥ tataḥ suśrutas tasmāj jayo jayaputro vijayas tasya ca ṛto nāma suśrutaḥ tasmāt suśrutāj jayaḥ tasya putro vijayaḥ vijayasya ṛtaḥ ṛtāt sunayas tato vītahavyas tasmād dhṛtir dhṛter bahulāśvas tasya putraḥ kṛtiḥ kṛtau saṃtiṣṭate ayaṃ janakavaṃśaḥ ।। ity ete maithilāḥ prācuryeṇa teṣām ātmavidyāśrayiṇo bhūpālā bhaviṣyantīti ।।
somasya vaṃśe tv akhilāñ śrotum icchāmi pārthivān ।। prasādasumukhas tan me brahmann ākhyātum arhasi ।। śrūyatāṃ muniśārdūla vaṃśaḥ prathitatejasaḥ । somasyānukramāt khyātā yatrorvīpatayo abhavan ।। ayaṃ hi vaṃśo atibalaparākramadyutiśīlaceṣṭāvadbhir atiguṇānvitair nahuṣayayātikārtavīryārjunādibhir bhūpālair alaṃkṛtaḥ । tam ahaṃ kathayāmi śrūyatām ।।
akhilajagatsraṣṭur bhagavannārāyaṇanābhisarojinīsamudbhavābjayoner brahmaṇaḥ putro atrir atreḥ somaḥ ।। taṃ ca bhagavān abjayonir aśeṣauṣadhīdvijanakṣatrāṇām ādhipatye abhyaṣecayat ।। sa ca rājasūyam akarot । tatprabhāvād atyutkṛṣṭādhipatyādhiṣṭhātṛtvāc cainaṃ mada āviveśa ।। madāvalepāc cāsau sakaladevaguror bṛhaspates tārāṃ nāma patnīṃ jahāra ।।
bahuśas tu bṛhaspaticoditena bhagavatā brahmaṇā codyamānaḥ sakalaiś ca devarṣibhir yācyamāno api na mumoca ।। tasya ca bṛhaspatidveṣād uśanā pārṣṇigrāho abhavat ।। aṅgiraḥ sakāśād upalabdhavidyo bhagavān rudro bṛhaspateḥ sahāyyam akarot ।। yataś cośanā tato jambhakumbhādyāḥ samastā eva daityadānavanikāyā mahāntam udyamaṃ cakruḥ । bṛhaspater api sakaladevasainyasahāyaḥ śakro abhavat ।।
evaṃ ca tayor atīvograḥ saṃgrāmas tārānimittas tārakāmayo nāmābhavat । tataḥ samastaśastrāṇy asureṣu rudrapurogamā devā deveṣu cāśeṣadānavā mumucuḥ ।। evaṃ ca devāsurāhavakṣobhakṣubdhahṛdayam aśeṣaṃ eva jagad brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagāma ।। tataś ca bhagavān apy uśanasaṃ śaṃkaram asurān devāṃś ca nivārya bṛhaspataye tārām adadāt । tāṃ cāntaḥprasavām avalokya bṛhaspatir āha ।। naiṣa mama kṣetre bhavatyānyasya suto dhāryaḥ samutsṛjainam alam atidhārṣṭyeneti ।।
sā ca tenaivam uktātipativratā bhartṛvacanāt tam īṣikāstambe garbham utsasarja ।। sa cotsṛṣṭamātra evātitejasā devānāṃ tejāṃsy ācikṣepa ।। bṛhaspatim induṃ ca tasya kumārasyāticārutayā sābhilāṣau dṛṣṭvā devāḥ samutpannasaṃdehās tārāṃ papracchuḥ ।। satyaṃ kathayāsmākam atisubhage kasyāyam ātmajaḥ somasyātha bṛhaspateḥ putraḥ । ityuktāpi sā tārā hriyā na kiṃcid uvāca । bahuśo apy abhihitā yadāsau devebhyo nācacakṣe tataś ca sa kumāras tāṃ śaptum udyataḥ prāha ca । duṣṭe kasmān mama tātaṃ nākhyāsi । adyaiva te alīkalajjāvatyās tathā śāstim ayam ahaṃ karomi yathā naivam anyāpy atimantharavacanā bhaviṣyatīti atha bhagavān pitāmahas taṃ kumāraṃ saṃnivārya svayam apṛcchat tārām । kathaya vatse kasyāyam ātmajaḥ somasya atha bṛhaspater ity uktā lajjājaḍam āha somasyeti ।।
tataḥ sphuraducchvasitāmalakapolakāntir bhagavān uḍupatis tam āliṅgya kumāraṃ sādhu sādhu vatsa prājño asīti budha iti nāma cakre ।। sa cākhyātam evaitad yathelāyām ātmajapurūravasam utpādayām āsa । purūravās tv atidānaśīlo atiyajvātitejasvī yaṃ satyavādinam atirūpiṇaṃ mitrāvaruṇaśāpān mānuṣe loke mayā vastavyam iti kṛtamatir urvaśī dadarśa ।। dṛṣṭamātre ca yasminn apahāya mānam aśeṣasvargābhilāṣam apāsya tanmanaskā bhūtvā tam evopatasthe ।। so api ca tām atiśayitasakalalokastrīkāntisaukumāryalāvaṇyagativilāsahāsādiguṇām avalokya tadāyattacittavṛttir babhūva ।।
ubhayam api tanmanaskam ananyadṛṣṭi parityaktasamastānyatprayojanam abhūt ।। rājā tu prāgalbhyāt tām āha ।। subhru tvām aham atikāmo asmi । prasīdānurāgam udvahety uktā lajjāvakhaṇḍitam urvaśī prāha ।। bhavatv evaṃ yadi me samayaparipālanaṃ bhavān karoti ।।
ākhyāhi me samayam ity atha pṛṣṭā punar abravīt । śayanasamīpe mamoraṇakadvayaṃ putrabhūtaṃ nāpaneyam । bhavāṃś ca mayā nagno na draṣṭavyaḥ । ghṛtamātraṃ ca mamāhāra ity evam eveti bhūpatir āha । tayā ca sahāvanīpatir alakāyāṃ caitrarathādivaneṣv amalapadmaṣaṇḍeṣu saraḥsv abhiramamāṇa ekaṣaṣṭivarṣāṇy anudinapravardhamānapramodo anayat ।। urvaśī ca tadupabhogāt pratidinapravardhamānānurāgā amaralokavāse api na spṛhāṃ cakāra ।। vinā corvaśyā suraloko apsarasāṃ siddhagandharvāṇāṃ ca nātiramaṇīyo abhavat ।। tataś corvaśīpurūravasoḥ samayavid viśvāvasur gandharvasamaveto niśi śayanābhyāśād ekam uraṇakaṃ jahāra ।।
tasyākāśe nīyamānasyorvaśī śabdam aśṛṇot । āha ca mamānāthāyāḥ putraḥ kenāpy'pahriyate kaṃ śaraṇam upayāmīty v iti ākarṇya rājā nagnaṃ māṃ devī drakṣyatīti na yayau । athānyam apy uraṇakam ādāya gandharvā yayuḥ । tasyāpy apahriyamāṇasyaśabdam ākarṇya'kāśe punar apy anāthāsmy aham abhartṛkā kupuruṣāśrayety ārtarāviṇī babhūva ।। rājāpy amarṣavaśād andhakāram etad iti khaḍgam ādāya duṣṭa duṣṭa hato asīti vyāharann abhyadhāvat ।। tāvac ca gandharvair atīvojjvalā vidyuj janitā । tatprabhayā corvaśī rājānam apagatāmbaraṃ dṛṣṭvāpavṛttasamayā tatkṣaṇād evāpakrāntā ।। parityajya tāv uraṇakau gandharvāḥ suralokam upagatāḥ ।।
rājāpi ca tau meṣāv ādāya hṛṣṭamanāḥ svaśayanam āyāto norvaśīṃ dadarśa ।। tāṃ cāpaśyann apagatāmbara evonmattarūpo babhrāma । kurukṣetre cāmbhojasarasy anyābhiś catasṛbhir apsarobhiḥ samavetām urvaśīṃ dadarśa । tataś conmattarūpo jāye he tiṣṭha manasi ghore tiṣṭha vacasīty anekaprakāraṃ sūktam avocat ।। āha corvaśī । mahārājālam anenāvivekaceṣṭitenāntarvatny aham abdānte bhavatātrāgantavyaṃ kumāras te bhaviṣyatīty ekāṃ ca niśām ahaṃ tvayā saha vatsyāmīty uktaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ svapuraṃ jagāma ।। tāsāṃ cāpsarasām urvaśī kathayām āsa । ayaṃ sa puruṣotkarṣṭo yenāham etāvantaṃ kālam anurāgākṛṣṭamānasā sahoṣitety evam uktās tām apsarasa ūcuḥ । sādhu sādhv asya rūpam anena sahāsmākam api sarvakālam abhirantuṃ spṛhā bhavet । ity abde ca pūrṇe sa rājā tatrājagāma । kumāraṃ cāyuṣam asmai tadorvaśī dadau ।।
ekāṃ ca niśāṃ tena rājñā sahoṣitvā pañcaputrotpattaye garbham avāpa ।। uvāca cainaṃ rājānam asmatprītyā mahārājāya sarva eva gandharvā varadāḥ saṃvṛttā vriyatāṃ vara iti ।। āha rājā । vijitasakalārātir avihatendriyasāmarthyo bandhumān amitabalakośo nānyad asmākam urvaśīsālokyād aprāpyam asti । tad aham anayā sahorvaśyā kālaṃ netum abhilaṣāmi ।। ity ukte gandharvā rājñe agnisthālīṃ daduḥ ।।
ūcuś cainam agnim āmnāyānusārī bhūtvā tridhā kṛtvorvaśīsalokatāmanoratham uddiśya samyag yajethās tato avaśyam abhilaṣitam avāpsyasīty uktas tām agnisthālīm ādāyājagāma antar aṭavyām acintayad aho me atimūḍhatā yad agnisthalī mayānītā norvaśīti । athainām aṭavyām evāgnisthālīṃ tatyāja svapuraṃ cājagāma ।। vyatītārdharātrasamaye vinidraś cācintayat । mamorvaśīsālokyaprāptyartham agnisthālī gandharvair dattā sā ca mayāṭavyāṃ parityaktā । tad ahaṃ tatra tadāharaṇāya yāsyāmīty utthāya tatrāpy upagato nāgnisthālīm apaśyat । śamīgarbhaṃ cāśvattham agnisthālīsthāne dṛṣṭvācintayat । mayātra sthālī nikṣiptā sā cāśvatthaḥ śamīgarbho abhūt । tad enam evāham agnirūpam ādāya svapuram abhigamyāraṇīṃ kṛtvā tadutpannāgner upāstiṃ kariṣyāmīty evam eva svapuram upagato araṇiṃ cakāra ।। tatpramāṇaṃ cāṅgulaiḥ kurvan gāyatrīm apaṭhat । paṭhataś cākṣarasaṃkhyāny evāṅgulāny araṇy abhavat । tatrāgniṃ nirmathyāgnitrayam āmnāyānusārī bhūtvā juhāva urvaśīsālokyaṃ ca phalam abhisaṃhitavān ।। tenaivāgnividhinā bahuvidhān yajñān iṣṭvā gāndharvalokān avāpyorvaśyā saha viyogaṃ nāvāpa ।।
eko agnir ādāv abhavad ailena tv atra manvantare tredhā pravartita iti ।। tasyāpy āyur dhīmān amāvasur viśvāvasuḥ śatāyur śrutāyuḥ saṃjñāḥ ṣaḍ abhavan putrāḥ ।। amāvasor bhīmo nāma putro abhavat ।। bhīmasya kāñcanaḥ kāñcanāt suhotras tasyāpi jahnuḥ । yo asau yajñavāṭam akhilaṃ gaṅgāmbhasā plāvitam ālokya krodhasaṃraktanayano bhagavantaṃ yajñapuruṣam ātmani parameṇa samādhinā samāropyākhilām eva gaṅgām apibat ।।
athainaṃ devarṣayaḥ prasādayām āsuḥ । duhitṛtve cāsya gaṅgām anayan ।। jahnoś ca sumantur nāma putro abhavat । tasyāpy ajakas tato balākāśvas tasmāt kuśaḥ kuśasya kuśāmbakuśanābhāmūrtarayāmāvasavaś catvāraḥ putrā babhūvuḥ ।। teṣāṃ kuśāmbaḥ śakratulyo me putro bhaved iti tapaś cakāra । taṃ cogratapasam avalokya mā bhavatv anyo asmattulyavīrya ity ātmanaivāsyendraḥ putratvam agacchat ।। gādhir nāma sa kauśiko abhavat । gādhiś ca satyavatīṃ kanyām ajanayat । tāṃ ca bhārgava ṛcīko vavre ।।
gādhir apy atiroṣaṇāyātivṛddhāya ca brāhmaṇāya dātum anicchann ekataḥ śyāmakarṇānām induvarcasām anilaraṃhasām aśvānāṃ sahasraṃ kanyāśulkam ayācata ।। tenāpy ṛṣiṇā varuṇasakāśād upalabhyāśvatīrthotpannaṃ tādṛgaśvasahasraṃ dattam । tatas tām ṛcīkaḥ kanyām upayeme । ṛcīkaś ca tasyāś carum apatyārthaṃ cakāra ।। tatprasāditaś ca tanmātre kṣatravaraputrotpattaye carum aparaṃ sādhayām āsa ।। eṣa carur bhavatyāyam aparas tvanmātrā samyag upayojya ity uktvā vanaṃ jagāma ।।
upayogakāle ca tāṃ mātā satyavatīm āha । putri sarva evātmaputram atiguṇaṃ samabhilaṣati nātmajāyābhrātṛguṇeṣv atīvādṛto bhavati ।। ato arhasi mamātmīyaṃ caruṃ dātuṃ madīyaṃ carum ātmanopayoktum ।। matputreṇa hi sakalabhūmaṇḍalaparipālanaṃ kāryaṃ kiyad vā brāhmaṇasya balavīryasaṃpad ity uktvā sā svacaruṃ mātre dattavatī ।। atha vanād apy āgamya satyavatīm ṛṣir apaśyat ।।
āha cainām atipāpe kim idam akāryaṃ bhavatyā kṛtam । atiraudraṃ te vapur ālakṣyate । nūnaṃ tvayā tvanmātṛsātkṛtaś carur upayukto na yuktam etat ।। mayā hi tatra carau sakalaiva śauryavīryabalasaṃpad āropitā । tvadīye carāv apy akhilaśāntijñānatitikṣādikī brāhmaṇasaṃpat । etac ca viparītaṃ kurvantyās tavātiraudrāstradhāraṇamāraṇaniṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyācāraḥ putro bhaviṣyaty asyā । copaśamarucir brāhmaṇācāra ity ākarṇyaiva sā tasya pādau jagrāha ।। praṇipatya cainam āha । bhagavan mayaitad ajñānād anuṣṭhitam । prasādaṃ me kuru । maivaṃvidhaḥ putro bhavatu । kāmam evaṃvidhaḥ pautro bhavatv ity ukto munir apy āhaivam astv iti ।। anantaraṃ ca sā jamadagnim ajījanat । tanmātā ca viśvāmitraṃ janayām āsa । satyavatī ca kauśikī nāma nady abhavat । jamadagnir ikṣvākuvaṃśodbhavasya reṇos tanayāṃ reṇukām upayeme । tasyāṃ cāśeṣakṣatrahantāraṃ paraśurāmasaṃjñaṃ bhagavataḥ sakalalokaguror nārāyaṇasyāṃśaṃ jamadagnir ajījanat ।।
viśvāmitraputras tu bhārgava eva śunaḥśepo devair dattaḥ । tataś ca devarātanāmābhavat । tataś cānye madhucchandajayakṛtadevāṣṭakakacchapahārītakākhyā viśvāmitraputrā babhūvuḥ ।। teṣāṃ ca bahūni kauśikagotrāṇy ṛṣyantareṣu vaivāhyāni bhavantīti ।। purūravaso jyeṣṭhaputro yas tv āyurnāmā sa rāhor duhitaram upayeme ।। tasyāṃ sa pañca putrān utpādayām āsa । nahuṣakṣatravṛddharambharajisaṃjñās tathaivānenāḥ pañcamaḥ putro abhūt । kṣatravṛddhāt suhotraḥ putro abhavat ।।
kāśyaleśagṛtsamadās tasya putrās trayo abhavan । gṛtsamadasya śaunakaś cāturvarṇyapravartayitābhūt ।। kāśyasya kāśīrājas tato dīrghatamāḥ putro abhavat । dhanvantaris tu dīrghatamaso abhavat । sa hi saṃsiddhakāryakaraṇaḥ sakalasaṃbhūtiṣv aśeṣajñānavid bhagavatā nārāyaṇena cātītasaṃbhūtāv asmai varo dattaḥ ।। kāśīrājagotre avatīrya tvam aṣṭadhā samyag āyurvedaṃ kariṣyasi yajñabhāk ca bhaviṣyasīti abhihitaḥ ।। tasya ca dhanvantareḥ putraḥ ketumān ketumato bhīmarathaḥ । tasyāpi divodāsas tataḥ pratardanaḥ । sa ca bhadraśreṇyavaṃśavināśād aśeṣāḥ śatravo anena jitā iti śatrujid abhavat ।।
tena ca prītimatātmaputro vatsa vatsety abhihitas tato vatso sāv abhavat । satyaparatayā ṛtadhvajasaṃjñām avāpa । punaś ca kuvalayanāmānam aśvaṃ lebhe tataḥ kuvalayāśva ity asyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ prathitaḥ ।। tasya ca vatsasya putro alarko nāmābhavat । yasyāyam adyāpi śloko gīyate । alarkād aparo nānyo bubhuje medinīṃ yuvā ।। tasyāpy alarkasya sannatir nāmātmajo abhavat । tataḥ sunīthas tasya suketus tato dharmaketuḥ । tataḥ satyaketus tasmād vibhus tattanayaḥ suvibhus tataś ca sukumāras tasyāpi dṛṣṭaketuḥ । tataś ca vainahotras tataś ca bhargo bhārgasya bhārgabhūmiḥ । tataś cāturvarṇyapravṛttiḥ ity ete kāśayo bhūpatayaḥ kathitāḥ । rajes tu saṃtatiḥ śrūyatām iti ।।
rajeḥ pañca putraśatāny atulavīryasārāṇy āsan ।। devāsurasaṃgrāmārambhe parasparavadhepsavo devāś cāsurāś ca brahmāṇam papracchuḥ ।। bhagavann asmākam atra virodhe kataraḥ pakṣo jetā bhaviṣyatīti ।। athāha bhagavān yeṣām arthe rajir āttāyudho yotsyatīti । atha daityair upetya rajir ātmasāhāyyadānāyābhyarthitaḥ prāha । yotsye ahaṃ bhavatām arthe yady aham amarajayād bhavatām indro bhaviṣyāmīty ākarṇyaitat tair abhihito na vayam anyathā vadiṣyāmo anyathā kariṣyāmo asmākam indraḥ prahlādas tadartham ayam udyama ity uktvā gateṣv asureṣu devair apy asāv avanīpatir evam evoktas tenāpi ca tathaivokte devair indras tvaṃ bhaviṣyasīti samanvicchitam ।।
rajināpi devasainyasahāyenānekair mahāstrais tad aśeṣam asurabalaṃ niṣūditam ।। avajitārātipakṣaś cendro rajicaraṇayugalam ātmaśirasā nipīḍyāha । bhayatrāṇadānād asmatpitā bavān aśeṣalokānām uttamo bhavān yasyāhaṃ putras trilokendraḥ ।। sa cāpi rājā prahasyāha । evam evāstv anatikramaṇīyā hi vairipakṣād apy anekavidhacāṭuvākyagarbhā praṇatir ity uktvā svapuraṃ jagāma ।। śatakratur apīndratvaṃ cakāra ।।
svaryāte tu rajau nāradarṣicoditā rajisutāḥ śatakratum ātmapitṛputraṃ ācārād rājyaṃ yācitavantaḥ ।। apradāne cāvajityendram atibalinaḥ svayam indratvaṃ cakruḥ ।। tataś ca bahutithe kāle vyatīte bṛhaspatim ekānte dṛṣṭvāpahṛtatrailokyayajñabhāgaḥ śatakratur uvāca ।। badarīphalamātram apy arhasi mamāpyāyanāya puroḍāśakhaṇḍaṃ dātum ity ukto bṛhaspatir uvāca । yady evaṃ pūrvam eva tvayāhaṃ coditaḥ syāṃ tan mayā tvadarthaṃ kim akartavyam iti । svalpair evāhobhis tvāṃ nijaṃ padaṃ prāpayiṣyāmīty abhidhāya teṣām anudinābhicārikaṃ buddhimohāya śakrasya ca tejobhivṛddhaye juhāva । te cāpi tena buddhimohenābhibhūyamānā brahmadviṣo dharmatyāgino vedavādaparāṅmukhā babhūvuḥ ।।
tataś ca tān apetadharmācārān indro jaghāna । purohitāpyāyitatejāś ca tridivam ākramat । etad indrasya svapadacyāvanārohaṇaṃ śrutvā puruṣaḥ svapadabhraṃśaṃ daurātmyaṃ ca nāpnoti ।। rambhas tv anapatyo abhavat । kṣatravṛddhasutaḥ pratikṣatras ।। tatputraḥ saṃjayas tasyāpi jayas tataś ca vijayas tasmāc ca jajñe kṛtaḥ । tasya harṣavardhano harṣavardhanasutaḥ sahadevas tasmād adīnas tasya jayatsenaḥ tataś ca saṃkṛtis tatputraḥ kṣatradharmā ity ete kṣatravṛddhasyāto nahuṣavaṃśaṃ pravakṣyāmīti ।। yatiyayātisaṃyātyāyātiviyātikṛtisaṃjñā nahuṣasya ṣaṭ putrā mahābalaparākramā babhūvuḥ ।।
yatis tu rājyaṃ naicchat । yayātis tu bhūbhṛd abhavat ।। uśanasaś ca duhitaraṃ devayānīṃ śarmiṣṭhāṃ ca vārṣaparvaṇīm upayeme । atrānuvaṃśaśloko bhavati ।। yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva devayānī vyajāyata । druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī ।। kāvyaśāpāc cākālenaiva yayātir jarām avāpa ।।
prasannaśukravacanāc ca svajarāṃ saṃkrāmayituṃ jyeṣṭhaputraṃ yadum uvāca ।। tvanmātāmahaśāpād iyam akālenaiva jarā mām upasthitā । tām ahaṃ tasyaivānugrahād bhavataḥ saṃcārayāmy ekaṃ varṣasahasram atṛpto asmi viṣayeṣu tvadvayasā viṣayān ahaṃ bhoktum icchāmi । nātra bhavatā pratyākhyānaṃ kartavyam ity uktaḥ sa naicchat tāṃ jarām ādātum । taṃ cāpi pitā śaśāpa । tvatprasūtir na rājyārhā bhaviṣyatīti ।। anantaraṃ ca durvasuṃ druhyum anuṃ ca pṛthivīpatir jarāgrahaṇārthaṃ svayauvanapradānāya cābhyarthayām āsa । tair apy ekaikaśyena pratyākhyātas tāñ chaśāpa ।। atha śarmiṣṭhātanayam aśeṣakanīyāṃsaṃ pūruṃ tathaivāha । sa cātipravaṇamatiḥ praṇamya pitaraṃ sabahumānaṃ mahān prasādo ayam asmākam ity udāram abhidhāya jarāṃ pratijagrāha । svakīyaṃ ca yauvanaṃ pitre dadau ।।
so api pauravaṃ yauvanam āsādya dharmāvirodhena yathākāmaṃ yathākālopapannaṃ yathotsāhaṃ viṣayāṃś cacāra । samyak ca prajāpālanam akarot ।। viśvācyā devayānyā ca sahopabhogaṃ bhuktvā kāmānām antam avāpsyāmīty anudinaṃ tanmanasko babhūva ।। anudinaṃ copabhogataḥ kāmān atīvābhiramyān mene ।। tataś caivam agāyata ।
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate ।। ekasyāpi na paryāptaṃ tasmāt tṛṣṇāṃ parityajet ।। samadṛṣṭes tadā puṃsaḥ sarvāḥ sukhamayā diśaḥ ।। tāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ saṃtyajet prājñaḥ sukhenaivābhipūryate ।।
dhanāśā jīvitāśā ca jīryato api na jīryataḥ ।। tathāpy anudinaṃ tṛṣṇā mamaiteṣv eva jāyate ।। nirdvandvo nirmamo bhūtvā cariṣyāmi mṛgaiḥ saha ।। rājye abhiṣicya pūruṃ ca prayayau tapase vanam ।।
pratīcyāṃ ca tathā druhyuṃ dakṣiṇāyāṃ tato yadum ।। sarvapṛthvīpatiṃ pūruṃ so abhiṣicya yayau vanam ।। ataḥ paraṃ yayāteḥ prathamaputrasya yador vaṃśam ahaṃ kathayāmi । yatrāśeṣalokanivāsimanuṣyasiddhagandharvayakṣarākṣasaguhyakakiṃpuruṣāpsaroragavihagadaityadānavarudravasvaśvi maruddevarṣidvijarṣimumukṣibhir dharmārthakāmamokṣārthibhis tattatphalalābhāya sadābhiṣṭutāparicchedyamāhātmyenāṃśena bhagavān anādinidhano viṣṇur avatatāra ।। atra ca ślokaḥ । yador vaṃśaṃ naraḥ śrutvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate । yatrāvatīrṇaṃ viṣṇvākhyaṃ paraṃ brahma nirākṛti ।।
sahasrajitkroṣṭunalaraghusaṃjñāś catvāro yaduputrā babhūvuḥ । sahasrajitputraḥ śatajit । tasya haihayahehayaveṇuhayās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ । haihayaputro dharmas tasyāpi dharmanetras tataḥ kuntiḥ kunteḥ sāhaṃjit । tattanayo mahiṣmān ।। tasmād bhadraśreṇyas tato durdamas tasmād dhanakaḥ । dhanakasya kṛtavīryakṛtāgnikṛtadharmakṛtaujasaś catvāraḥ putrāḥ । kṛtavīryād arjunaḥ saptadvīpapatir bāhusahasrī jajñe । yo asau bhagavadaṃśam atrikulaprasūtaṃ dattātreyākhyam ārādhya bāhusahasram adharmasevānivāraṇaṃ dharmeṇa pṛthivījayaṃ dharmataś cānupālanam arātibhyo aparājayam akhilajagatprakhyātapuruṣāc ca mṛtyum ity etān varān abhilaṣitavāṃl lebhe ca ।। teneyam aśeṣadvīpavatī pṛthivī samyak paripālitā । daśa yajñasahasrāṇy asāv ayajat ।। tasya ca śloko adyāpi gīyate ।
yajñair dānais tapobhir vā praśrayeṇa śrutena ca ।। anaṣṭadravyatā ca tasya rājye abhavat । evaṃ pañcāśītivarṣasahasrāṇy avyāhatārogyaśrībalaparākramo rājyam akarot ।। māhiṣmatyāṃ digvijayābhyāgato narmadājalāvagāhanakrīḍātipānamadākulenāyatnenaiva tenāśeṣadevadaityagandharveśajayodbhūtamadāvalepo api rāvaṇaḥ paśur iva baddhvā svanagaraikānte sthāpitaḥ ।। yaś ca pañcāśītivarṣasahasropalakṣaṇakālāvasāne bhagavannārāyaṇāṃśena paraśurāmeṇopasaṃhṛtaḥ । tasya ca putraśatapradhānāḥ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ । śūraśūrasenavṛṣaṇamadhujayadhvajasaṃjñāḥ ।।
jayadhvajāt tālajaṅghaḥ putro abhavat । tālajaṅghasya tālajaṅghākhyaṃ putraśatam āsīt । yeṣāṃ jyeṣṭho vītihotras tathānyo bharataḥ । bharatād vṛṣasujātau ca । vṛṣasya putro madhur abhavat । tasyāpi vṛṣṇipramukhaṃ putraśatam āsīt । yato vṛṣṇisaṃjñām etad gotram avāpa ।। madhusaṃjñāhetuś ca madhur abhavat । yādavāś ca yadunāmopalakṣaṇāt ।। kroṣṭoś ca yaduputrasyātmajo vṛjinīvān । tataś ca svāhis tato ruṣaṅkuḥ । ruṣaṅkoś citrarathaḥ । tattanayaḥ śaśabinduś caturdaśamahāratnaś cakravarty abhavat । tasya ca śatasahasraṃ patnīnām abhavat । daśalakṣasaṃkhyāś ca putrāḥ ।। teṣāṃ ca pṛthuyaśāḥ pṛthukarmā pṛthujayaḥ pṛthukīrtiḥ pṛthudānaḥ pṛthuśravāś ca ṣaṭ putrāḥ pradhānāḥ ।।
pṛthuśravasaś ca putras tamaḥ । tasmād uśanā yo vājimedhānāṃ śatam ājahāra । tasya ca śitapur nāma putro abhūt । tasyāpi rukmakavacaḥ । tataḥ parāvṛt parāvṛto rukmeṣupṛthujyāmaghapālitaharitasaṃjñās tasya pañcātmajā babhūvuḥ ।। atrāpy ayam adyāpi jyāmaghasya śloko gīyate । teṣāṃ tu jyāmaghaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ śaibyāpatir abhūn nṛpaḥ ।। apatyakāmo api bhayān nānyāṃ bhāryām avindata ।।
sa tv ekadā atiprabhūtagajaturagarathasaṃmardātidāruṇe mahāhave yudhyamānaḥ sakalam evārāticakram ajayat । tac cāricakram apāstaputrakalatrabandhubalakośaṃ svam adhiṣṭhānaṃ parityajya diśaḥ pravidrutam ।। tasmiṃś ca vidrute atitrāsalolāyatalocanayugalaṃ trāhi trāhi tātāmba bhrātar ity ākulavilāpavidhuraṃ rājakanyāratnam adrākṣīt ।। taddarśanāc ca tasyām anurāgānugatāntarātmā sa nṛpo acintayat । sādhv idaṃ mamāpatyavirahitasya vandhyābhartuḥ sāmprataṃ vidhināpatyakāraṇaṃ kanyāratnam upapāditam । tad etat udvahāmy athaināṃ syandanam āropya svam adhiṣṭhānaṃ nayāmi ।। tayaiva devyā śaibyayāham anujñātaḥ samudvakṣyāmīty athaināṃ ratham āropya svanagaram agacchat ।।
vijayinaṃ ca rājānam aśeṣapaurabhṛtyaparijanāmātyasamavetā śaibyā draṣṭum adhiṣṭhānadvāram āgatā ।। sā cāvalokya rājñaḥ savyapārśvavartinīṃ kanyām īṣadudbhūtāmarṣasphuradadharapallavā rājānam avocat । aticapalacittātra syandane keyam āropitety asāv apy anālocitottaravacano atibhayāt tām āha snuṣā mameyam iti ।। athainaṃ śaibyovāca । snuṣāsaṃbandhatā hy eṣā katamena sutena te ।।
ity ātmerṣyākopakaluṣitavacanamuṣitavivekatayā duruktaparihārārtham idam avanīpatir āha । yas te janiṣyaty ātmajas tasyeyam anāgata eva bhāryā nirūpitety ākarṇyodbhūtamṛduhāsā tathety āha praviveśa ca rājñā sahādhiṣṭhānam ।। anantaraṃ cātiśuddhalagnahorāṃśakāvayavoktakṛtaputrajanmālāpaguṇād vayasaḥ pariṇāmam upagatāpi śaibyā svalpair evāhobhir garbham avāpa ।। kālena ca kumāram ajījanat । tasya ca vidarbha iti pitā nāma cakre । sa ca tāṃ snuṣām upayeme ।। tasyāṃ cāsau krathakaiśikasaṃjñau putrāv ajanayat । punas tṛtīyaṃ romapādasaṃjñaṃ kumāram ajījanat । romapādād babhruḥ babhroḥ putro dhṛtiḥ । dhṛteḥ kaiśikaḥ kaiśikasyāpi cediḥ putro abhūd yasya saṃtatau caidyā bhūpālāḥ । krathasya snuṣāputrasya kuntir abhavat ।।
kunter vṛṣṇir vṛṣṇer nirvṛtiḥ । nirvṛter daśārhas tataś ca vyomaḥ । tasmād api jīmūtas tato vikṛtis tataś ca bhīmarathaḥ । tasmān navarathas tasyāpi daśarathas tataś ca śakunis tattanayaḥ karambhiḥ karambher devarāto abhavat । tasyāpi devakṣatro devakṣatrān madhur madhor anavaratho anavarathāt kuruvatsas tataś cānurathaḥ tataḥ puruhotro jajñe । tataś cāṃśus tataś ca satvataḥ satvatād ete sātvatāḥ ity etāṃ jyāmaghasaṃtatiṃ samyag chraddhāsamanvitaḥ śrutvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। bhajanabhajamānadivyāndhakadevāvṛdhamahābhojavṛṣṇi saṃjñāḥ satvatasya putrā babhūvuḥ ।। bhajamānasya nimikṛkaṇavṛṣṇayas tathānye tadvaimātrāḥ śatajitsahasrajidayutajitsaṃjñāḥ devāvṛdhasyāpi babhruḥ putro abhūt । tayoś cāyaṃ śloko gīyate । yathaiva śṛṇumo dūrāt saṃpaśyāmas tathāntikāt । babhruḥ śreṣṭho manuṣyāṇāṃ devair devāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ ।। puruṣāḥ ṣaṭ ca ṣaṣṭiś ca ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi cāṣṭa ca । ye amṛtatvam anuprāptā babhror devāvṛdhād api ।।
mahābhojas tv atidharmātmā tasyānvaye bhojā mārtikāvatā babhūvuḥ ।। vṛṣṇeḥ sumitro yudhājic ca putrāv abhūtām । tataś cānamitraśinī tathānamitrān nighno nighnasya prasenasatrājitau । tasya satrājitasya bhagavān ādityaḥ sakhābhavat । ekadā tv ambhonidhitīrasaṃśrayaḥ sūryaṃ satrājitas tuṣṭāva tanmanaskatayā ca bhāsvān abhiṣṭūyamāno agratas tasya tasthau । aspaṣṭamūrtidharaṃ cainam ālokya satrājitaḥ sūryam āha । yathaiva vyomni vahnipiṇḍopamam aham apaśyaṃ tathaivādyāgrato gatam apy atra na kiṃcid bhagavatā prasādīkṛtaṃ viśeṣam upalakṣayāmi ।। ityevam ukte bhagavatā sūryeṇa nijakaṇṭhād unmucya syamantakanāmā mahāmaṇir avatāryaikānte nyastaḥ ।। tatas tam ātāmrojjvalahrasvavapuṣam īṣadāpiṅgalanayanam ādityam adrākṣīt । kṛtapraṇipātastavādikaṃ ca satrājitam āha । bhagavān varam asmatto abhimataṃ vṛṇīṣveti । sa ca tad eva maṇiratnam ayācata । sa cāpi tasmai tad dattvā viyati svadhiṣṇyam āruroha ।।
satrājito apy amalamaṇiratnasanāthakaṇṭhatayā sūrya iva tejobhir aśeṣadigantarāṇy udbhāsayan dvārakāṃ viveśa ।। dvārakāvāsijanapadas tu tam āyāntam avekṣya bhagavantam ādipuruṣaṃ puruṣottamam avanibhārāvataraṇāyāṃśena mānuṣarūpadhāriṇaṃ praṇipatyāha । bhagavan bhagavantam ayaṃ nūnaṃ draṣṭum āyāty āditya ity ākarṇya prahasya ca tān āha । bhagavān nāyam ādityaḥ satrājito yam ādityadattaṃ syamanatakākhyaṃ mahāmaṇiṃ bibhrad atropayāti । tad enaṃ visrabdhāḥ paśyata ity uktās te yayuḥ । sa ca taṃ syamantakākhyaṃ mahāmaṇim ātmaniveśane cakre ।। pratidinaṃ ca tan maṇiratnapravaram aṣṭau kanakabhārān sravati । tatprabhāvāc ca sakalasyaiva rāṣṭrasyopasargānāvṛṣṭivyālāgnitoyadurbhikṣādibhayaṃ na bhavati ।। acyuto api tad ratnam ugrasenasya bhūpater yogyam etad iti lipsāṃ cakre । gotrabhedabhayāc chakto api na jahāra ।।
satrājito apy acyuto mām etad yācayiṣyatīty avagataratnalobhaḥ svabhrātre prasenāya tad ratnam dattavān । tac ca śucinā dhriyamāṇam aśeṣam eva suvarṇasrāvādikaṃ guṇam utpādayati । anyathā ya enaṃ dhārayati tam eva hantīty । asāv api prasenaḥ syamantakena kaṇṭhāsaktenāśvam āruhyāṭavyāṃ mṛgayām agacchat । tatra ca siṃhād vadham avāpa । sāśvaṃ ca taṃ nihatya siṃho apy amalamaṇiratnam āsyāgreṇādāya gantum udyata ṛkṣādhipatinā jāmbavatā dṛṣṭo ghātitaś ca । jāmbavān apy amalaṃ tan maṇiratnam ādāya svabilaṃ praviveśa । sukumārasaṃjñāya ca bālakāya krīḍanakam akarot ।। anāgacchati ca tasmin prasene kṛṣṇo maṇiratnam abhilaṣitavān । na ca prāptavān nūnam etad asya karmety akhila eva yadulokaḥ parasparaṃ karṇākarṇy'kathayat ।। viditalokāpavādavṛttāntaś ca bhagavān yadusainyaparivāraḥ prasenāśvapadavīm anusasāra । dadarśa cāśvasametaṃ prasenaṃ nihataṃ siṃhenākhilajanapadamadhye siṃhapadadarśanakṛtapariśuddhiḥ siṃhapadam anusasāra ।। ṛkṣavinihataṃ ca siṃham apy alpe bhūmibhāge dṛṣṭvā tataś ca tadratnagauravād ṛkṣasyāpi padāny anuyayau । giritaṭe ca sakalam eva yadusainyam avasthāpya tatpadānusārī ṛkṣabilaṃ praviveśa । ardhapraviṣṭaś ca dhātryāḥ sukumārakam ullāpayantyā vāṇīṃ śuśrāva । siṃhaḥ prasenam avadhīt siṃho jāmbavatā hataḥ । sukumāraka mā rodīs tava hy eṣa syamantakaḥ ।।
ity ākarṇyalabdhasyamantakodantaḥ praviṣṭaḥ kumārakrīḍanakīkṛtaṃ ca dhātryā haste tejobhir jājvalyamānaṃ syamantakaṃ dadarśa ।। taṃ ca syamantakābhilāṣicakṣuṣam apūrvapuruṣam āgataṃ samavekṣya dhātrī trāhi trāhīti vyājahāra ।। tadārtanādaśravaṇānantaraṃ cāmarṣapūrṇahṛdayaḥ sa jāmbavān ājagāma । tayoś ca parasparam yudhyator dvayor yuddham ekaviṃśatidināny abhavat । te ca yadusainikās tatra saptāṣṭa dināni tanniṣkrāntim udīkṣamāṇās tasthuḥ । aniṣkramamāṇe ca madhuripāv asāv avaśyam atra bile atyantaṃ nāśam āpto bhaviṣyaty anyathā tasya jīvataḥ katham etāvanti dināni śatrujaye vyākṣepo bhavatīti kṛtādhyavasāyā dvārakām āgatya hataḥ kṛṣṇa iti kathayām āsuḥ ।। tadbāndhavāś ca tatkālocitam akhilam uparatakriyākalāpaṃ cakruḥ । tatrāsya yuddhyamānasyātiśraddhādattaviśiṣṭapātropayuktānnatoyādinā kṛṣṇasya balaprāṇapuṣṭir abhūt ।।
itarasyānudinam atigurupuruṣabhidyamānasyātiniṣṭhuraprahārapīḍitākhilāvayavasya nirāhāratayā balahāniḥ । nirjitaś ca bhagavatā jāmbavān praṇipatyāha v vyājahāra । asurasurayakṣagandharvarākṣasādibhir apy akhilair bhagavān na jetuṃ śakyaḥ । kim utāvanigocarair alpavīryair narair narāvayavabhūtaiś ca tiryagyonyanusṛtibhiḥ kiṃ punar asmadvidhaiḥ । avaśyaṃ bhagavato asmatsvāmino nārāyaṇasya sakalajagatparāyaṇasyāṃśena bhagavatā bhavitavyam ity uktas tasmai bhagavān akhilāvanibhārāvatāram ācacakṣe । prītyābhyañjitakaratalasparśanena cainam apagatayuddhakhedaṃ cakāra ।। sa ca praṇipatyainaṃ punar api prasādya jāmbavatīṃ nāma kanyāṃ gṛhāgamanārghyabhūtāṃ grāhayām āsa ।। syamantakamaṇim apy asau praṇipatya tasmai pradadau । acyuto apy atipraṇatāt tasmād agrāhyam api tan maṇiratnam ātmasaṃśodhanāya jagrāha ।। saha jāmbavatyā sa dvārakām ājagāma । bhagavadāgamanodbhūtaharṣotkarṣasya dvārakāvāsijanasya kṛṣṇāvalokanāt tatkṣaṇam evātipariṇatavayaso api navayauvanam ivābhavat । ānakadundubhiṃ ca diṣṭyā diṣṭyeti sakalayādavāḥ striyaś ca sabhājayām āsuḥ । bhagavān api yathānubhūtam aśeṣayādavasamāje yathāvad ācacakṣe । syamantakaṃ ca satrājitāya dattvā mithyābhiśastiviśuddhim avāpa ।।
jāmbavatīṃ cāntaḥpure niveśayām āsa । satrājito api mayāsyābhūtamalinam āropitam iti jātasaṃtrāsaḥ svasutāṃ satyabhāmāṃ bhagavate bhāryāṃ dadau । tāṃ cākrūrakṛtavarmaśatadhanvapramukhā yādavāḥ pūrvaṃ varayāṃ āsuḥ । tatas tatpradānād avajñātam ivātmānaṃ manyamānāḥ satrājite vairānubandhaṃ cakruḥ ।। akrūrakṛtavarmapramukhāś ca śatadhanvānam ūcuḥ । ayam atidurātmā satrājito yo asmābhir bhavatā ca abhyarthito apy ātmajām asmān bhavantaṃ cāvigaṇayya kṛṣṇāya dattavān । tad alam anena jīvatā ghātayitvainaṃ tan mahāratnaṃ tvayā kiṃ na gṛhyate । vayam abhyupapatsyāmo yady acyutas tavopari vairānubandhaṃ kariṣyatīti ।। evam uktas tathety asāv apy āha । jatugṛhadagdhānāṃ pāṇḍutanayānāṃ viditaparamārtho api bhagavān duryodhanaprayatnaśaithilyakaraṇārtham ānukūlyakaraṇāya vāraṇāvataṃ gataḥ ।। gate ca tasmin suptam eva satrājitaṃ śatadhanvā jaghāna maṇiratnaṃ cādade । pitṛvadhāmarṣapūrṇā ca satyabhāmā śīghraṃ syandanam ārūḍhā vāraṇāvataṃ gatvā bhagavate ahaṃ pratipāditety akṣāntimatā śatadhanvanāsmatpitā vyāpāditaḥ । tac ca syamantakamaṇiratnam apahṛtam । tad iyam asyāvahāsanā । tad ālocya yad atra yuktaṃ tat kriyatām iti kṛṣṇam āha ।।
tayā caivam uktaḥ parituṣṭāntaḥkaraṇo api kṛṣṇaḥ satyabhāmām amarṣatāmralocanaḥ prāha । satye mamaivaiṣāvahāsanā । nāham etāṃ tasya durātmanaḥ sahiṣye । na hy anullaṅghya varapādapaṃ tatkṛtanīḍāśrayiṇo vihaṃgā vadhyante । tad alam atyartham amunāsmatpurataḥ śokapreritavākyaparikareṇety uktvā dvārakām abhyetya baladevam ekānte vāsudevaḥ prāha । mṛgayāgataṃ prasenam aṭavyāṃ mṛgapatir jaghāna । satrājito apy adhunā śatadhanvanā nidhanaṃ prāpitaḥ । tadubhayavināśāt tan maṇiratnam āvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। tad uttiṣṭhāruhyatāṃ rathaḥ śatadhanvanidhanāyodyamaṃ kurv ity abhihitas tatheti samanvicchitavān । kṛtodyogau ca tāv ubhāv upalabhya śatadhanvā kṛtavarmāṇam upetya pārṣṇipūraṇakarmanimittam acodayat । āha cainaṃ kṛtavarmā । nāhaṃ balabhadravāsudevābhyāṃ saha virodhāyālam ity uktaś cākrūram acodayat । asāv apy āha । na hi kaścid bhagavatā pādaprahāraparikampitajagattrayeṇāsurapuravanitāvaidhavyakāriṇā prabalaripucakrāpratihatacakreṇa cakriṇā madamuditanayanāvalokitāribalaviśātanenātiguruvairi vāraṇāpakarṣaṇāviṣkṛtamahimorusīreṇa sīriṇā ca saha sakalajagadvandyānām amaravarāṇām api yoddhuṃ samarthaḥ kim utāhaṃ tadanyataḥ śaraṇam abhilaṣyatām ।। ity uktaḥ śatadhanvāha । yady asmatparitrāṇāsamarthaṃ bhavān ātmānam avagacchati tad ayam asmanmaṇiḥ saṃgṛhya rakṣyatām ityuktaḥ so apy āha । yady antāyām apy avasthāyāṃ na kasmaicid bhavān kathayiṣyati tad aham enaṃ grahīṣyāmīti । tathety ukte cākrūras tan maṇiratnaṃ jagrāha ।। śatadhanvāpy atulavegāṃ śatayojanavāhinīṃ vaḍavām āruhyāpakrāntaḥ । śaibyasugrīvameghapuṣpabalāhakāśvacatuṣṭayayuktarathāvasthitau baladevavāsudevau tam anuprayātau ।।
sā ca vaḍavā śatayojanapramāṇamārgam atītya punar api vāhyamānā mithilāvanoddeśe prāṇān utsasarja । śatadhanvāpi tāṃ parityajya padātir evādravat ।। kṛṣṇo api balabhadram āha । tāvad atraiva syandane bhavatā stheyam aham enam adhamācāraṃ padātinam anugamya yāvad ghātayāmi । atra hi bhūbhāge dṛṣṭadoṣā hayāḥ । naite aśvā bhavatemaṃ bhūmibhāgam ullaṅghya neyāḥ ।। tathety uktvā balabhadro ratha eva tasthau । kṛṣṇo api dvikrośamātraṃ bhūmibhāgam anusṛtya dūrasthitasyaiva cakraṃ kṣiptvā śatadhanvanaḥ śiraś ciccheda । taccharīrāmbarādiṣu ca bahuprakāram anviṣyann api syamantakaṃ maṇiṃ nāvāpa yadā tadopagamya balabhadram āha । vṛthaivāsmābhir ghātitaḥ śatadhanvā । na prāptam akhilajagatsārabhūtaṃ tan maṇiratnaṃ । ity ākarṇyodbhūtakopo balabhadro vāsudevam āha । dhik tvāṃ yas tvam evam arthalipsur etac ca te bhrātṛtvān marṣaye । tad ayaṃ panthāḥ svecchayā gamyatāṃ । na me dvārakayā na bandhubhiḥ kāryam alam ebhir mamāgrato alīkaśapathair ity ākṣipya taṃ kathaṃcit prasādyamāno api na tasthau । videhapurīṃ praviveśa ।। janakaś cārghyapūrvakam enaṃ gṛhaṃ praveśayām āsa । tatraiva ca tasthau । vāsudevo api dvārakām ājagāma । yāvac ca janakarājagṛhe balabhadro avatasthe tāvad dhārtarāṣṭro duryodhanas tatsakāśād gadāśikṣām aśikṣata । varṣatrayānte ca babhrūgrasenaprabhṛtibhir yādavair na tad ratnaṃ kṛṣṇenāpahṛtam iti kṛtāvagatibhir videhapurīṃ gatvā baladevaḥ saṃpratyāyya dvārakām ānītaḥ ।।
akrūro apy uttamamaṇisamudbhūtasuvarṇadhyānaparas tato yajñān īje । savanagatau hi kṣatriyavaiśyau nighnan brahmahā bhavatīty ato dīkṣākavacaṃ praviṣṭa eva tasthau । dviṣaṣṭivarṣāṇy evaṃ tanmaṇiprabhāvāt tatropasargadurbhikṣamarakādikaṃ nābhūt ।। athākrūrapakṣīyair bhojaiḥ śatrughne sātvatasya prapautre vyāpādite bhojaiḥ sahākrūro dvārakām apahāyāpakrāntaḥ ।। tadapakrāntidinād ārabhya tatropasargavyālānāvṛṣṭimarakādyupadrāvā babhūvuḥ । atha yādavabalabhadrograsenasamaveto amantrayad bhagavān uragāriketanaḥ । kim yad idam ekadaiva pracuropadravāgamanam etad ālocyatām ।। ity ukte andhakanāmā yaduvṛddhaḥ prāha । asyākrūrasya pitā śvaphalko yatra yatrābhūt tatra tatra durbhikṣamarakānāvṛṣtyādikaṃ nābhūt ।।
kāśīrājasya viṣaye atyantānāvṛṣṭyāṃ śvaphalko anīyata । tatas tatkṣaṇād eva devo vavarṣa । kāśīrājapatnyāś ca garbhe kanyāpūrvam āsīt ।। sāpi pūrṇe api prasūtikāle naiva niścakrāma । evaṃ ca tasya garbhasya dvādaśa varṣāṇy aniṣkrāmato yayuḥ । kāśīrājaś ca garbhasthāṃ tām ātmajām āha । putri kasmān na jāyase niṣkramyatām āsyaṃ te draṣṭum icchāmy ahaṃ svakāṃ ca mātaraṃ kim iti ciraṃ kleśayiṣyasīty ukte garbhasthaiva vyājahāra । tāta yady ekaikāṃ gāṃ dine dine brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchasi tad aham anyais tribhir varṣair asmād garbhād avaśyaṃ niṣkramiṣyāmīti । etac ca tadvacanam ākarṇya rājā dine dine brāhmaṇāya gāṃ prādāt । sāpi tāvatā kālena jātā । tatas tasyāḥ pitā gāndinīti nāma cakāra । tāṃ ca gāndinīṃ kanyāṃ śvaphalkāya priyopakāriṇe gṛhāgatāyārghabhūtāṃ prādāt ।। tasyām ayam akrūraḥ śvaphalkāj jajñe । tad asyaivaṃguṇamithunād utpattiḥ ।। katham asminn apakrānte marakadurbhikṣādyupadravā na bhaviṣyanti । tad ayam ānīyatām ity alam atiguṇavaty aparādhānveṣaneneti ।।
yaduvṛddhasyāndhakasyaitad vacanam ākarṇya keśavograsenabalabhadrapurogamair yadubhiḥ kṛtāparādhatitikṣābhavam abhayaṃ dattvā śvāphalkiḥ svapuram ānītaḥ । tatra cāgatamātra eva tasya tatsthasya maṇer anubhāvad anāvṛṣṭimarakadurbhikṣavyālādyupadravaḥ śaśāma । kṛṣṇaś ca cintayām āsa । svalpam etat kāraṇaṃ yad ayaṃ gāndinyāṃ śvaphalkenākrūro jātaḥ । sumahāṃś cāyam anāvṛṣṭidurbhikṣamarakādyupadravaśamanakārī prabhāvaḥ ।। tan nūnam asya sakāśe sa mahāmaṇiḥ syamantakākhyas tiṣṭhati । tasya hy evaṃvidhāḥ prabhāvāḥ śrūyante । ayam api ca yajñād anantaram anyat kratvantaraṃ anantaram ca tasmād yajñāntaraṃ yajatīti । alpopādānaṃ cāsyā saṃśayam atrāsau varamaṇis tiṣṭhatīti kṛtādhyavasāyo anyat prayojanam uddiśya sakalayādavasamājam ātmageha evācīkarat ।। tatra copaviṣṭeṣv akhileṣu yādaveṣu pūrvaprayojanam upanyasya paryavasite ca tasmin prasaṅgāgataparihāsakathām akrūreṇa saha kṛtvā janārdanas tam akrūram āha ।। dānapate jānīma eva vayaṃ yathā śatadhanvanā tad akhilajagatsārabhūtaṃ syamantakaratnaṃ bhavataḥ samarpitaṃ tad etad rāṣṭropakārakaṃ bhavataḥ sakāśe tiṣṭhatīti । tiṣṭhatu sarva eva vayaṃ tatprabhāvaphalabhujaḥ kiṃ tv eṣa balabhadro asmān āśaṅkitavāṃs tad asmatprītaye darśayety abhihitaḥ saratnaḥ so acintayat ।।
kim atrānuṣṭheyam anyathā ced bravīmy ahaṃ tat kevalāmbaratirodhānam anviṣyanto ratnam etad drakṣyantīty anveṣaṇaṃ na kṣemam iti saṃcintya tam akhilajagatkāraṇabhūtaṃ nārāyaṇam āhākrūraḥ । bhagavan mamaitat syamantakaratnaṃ śatadhanvanā samarpitam ।। apagate ca tasminn adya śvaḥ paraśvo vā bhagavān māṃ yācayiṣyatīti etāvantaṃ kālam atikṛcchreṇādhārayam । tasya ca dhāraṇakleśenāham aśeṣopabhogeṣv asaṅgimānaso na vedmi svasukhakalām api ।। etāvanmātram apy aśeṣarāṣṭropakārī dhārayituṃ na śaknotīti māṃ bhavān maṃsyata ity ātmanā na coditam ।। tad idaṃ syamantakaratnaṃ gṛhyatām icchayā yasyābhimataṃ tasya samarpyatām । tataḥ so adharavastranigopitātilaghukanakasamudgakaṃ pragaṭīkṛtavān ।।
tataś ca niṣkrāmya syamantakamaṇiṃ tasmin yadusamāje mumoca । muktamātre ca tenātikāntyā tad akhilam āsthānam uddyotitam ।। athāhākrūraḥ । sa eṣa maṇir yaḥ śatadhanvanāsmākaṃ samarpito yasyāyaṃ sa enaṃ gṛhṇātv iti । tam ālokya sarvayādavānāṃ sādhu sādhv iti vismitavacasāṃ vāco aśrūyanta । tam ālokyamamāyam acyutenaiva sāmānyaḥ samanvicchita iti balabhadraḥ saspṛho abhavat ।। mamedaṃ pitṛdhanam ity atīva ca satyabhāmā spṛhāṃ cakāra । balabhadrasatyānanāvalokanāt kṛṣṇo apy ātmānaṃ cakrāntarāvasthitam iva mene । sakalayādavapratyakṣaṃ cākrūram āha । etad dhi maṇiratnam ātmasaṃśodhanāya eṣāṃ yadūnāṃ darśitam etac ca mama balabhadrasya ca sāmānyaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ caitat satyabhāmāyā nānyasya ।। etat sarvakālaṃ śucinā brahmacaryeṇa dhriyamāṇam aśeṣarāṣṭrasyopakārakam aśucinā dhriyamāṇam ādhāram eva hanti ।।
ato aham asya ṣoḍaśastrīsahasraparigrahād asamartho dhāraṇe । katham caitat satyabhāmā svīkarotu । āryabalabhadreṇāpi madirāpānādyaśeṣopabhogaparityāgaḥ kathaṃ kāryaḥ । tad ayaṃ yaduloko ahaṃ balabhadraḥ satyā ca tvāṃ dānapate prārthayāmaḥ । etad bhavān eva dhārayituṃ samarthaḥ । tvadsthaṃ cāsya rāṣṭrasyopakārakaṃ tad bhavān aśeṣarāṣṭropakāranimittam etat pūrvavad dhārayatu । tvayānyan na vaktavyam ity ukto dānapatis tathety uktvā jagrāha ca tan mahāratnam । tataḥ prabhṛti ca akrūraḥ prakaṭenaivātitejasā jājjvalyamānenātmakaṇṭhāsaktenāditya ivāṃśumālī cacāra ।। ity etāṃ bhagavato mithyābhiśastikṣālanāṃ yaḥ smarati na tasya kadācid alpāpi mithyābhiśastir bhavati । avyāhatendriyaś cākhilapāpamokṣam avāpnotīti ।। anamitrasya sutaḥ śinir nāmābhavat । tasyāpi satyakaḥ satyakāt sātyakir yuyudhānanāmā । tasmād apy asaṅgas tatputraś ca tūṇis tūṇer yugaṃdharaḥ । iti śaineyāḥ ।। anamitrasyaivānvaye vṛṣṇiḥ । tasmāc ca śvaphalkas tatprabhāvaḥ kathita eva । śvaphalkasya kanīyāṃś citrako nāmābhavad bhrātā । śvaphalkād akrūro gāndinyām abhavat । tathopamadgur upamadgor mṛduraviśārimejayagirikṣatropakṣatraśatrughnārimardanadharmadṛgdṛṣṭavarmagandhamojavāhaprativāhākhyāḥ putrāḥ sutārākhyā ca kanyā । devavān upadevaś cākrūraputrau । pṛthuvipṛthupramukhāś citrakasya putrā bahavo abhavan kukurabhajamānaśucikambalabarhiṣākhyās tathāndhakasya catvāraḥ putrāḥ ।।
kukurād dhṛṣṭas tasmāc ca kapotaromā tataś ca vilomā । tasmād api tumburusakhā bhavasaṃjñaś candanodakadundubhiḥ । tataś cābhijit tataḥ punarvasuḥ । tasyāpy āhukaḥ putra āhukī ca kanyā ।। āhukasya devakograsenau dvau putrau । devavān upadevaḥ sahadevo devarakṣito devakasyāpi catvāraḥ putrāḥ । teṣāṃ ca vṛkadevopadevā devarakṣitā śrīdevā śāntidevā sahadevā devakī ca sapta bhaginyaḥ । tāś ca sarvā eva vasudeva upayeme । ugrasenasyāpi kaṃsanyagrodhasunāmakaṅkaśaṅkusubhūmirāṣṭrapālayuddhamuṣṭituṣṭimatsaṃjñāḥ putrāḥ । kaṃsā kaṃsavatī sutanū rāṣṭrapālī kaṅkī ca ugrasenatanūjāḥ । bhajamānāc ca vidūrathaḥ putro abhavat । vidūrathāc chūraḥ śūrāc chamī śaminaḥ pratikṣatraḥ । tasmāt svayaṃbhojas tataś ca hṛdikaḥ ।। tasyāpi kṛtavarmaśatadhanurdevamīḍhuṣākhyāḥ putrā babhūvuḥ ।। devamīḍhuṣasya śūrasya māriṣā nāma patny abhavat ।।
tasyāṃ cāsau daśa putrān ajanayad vasudevapūrvān । vasudevasya jātamātrasyaiva tadgṛhe bhagavadaṃśāvatāram avyāhatadṛṣṭyā paśyadbhir devair divyānakadundubhayaś ca vāditāḥ । tatas tadaivānakadundubhisaṃjñām avāpa । tasyāpi devabhāgadevaśravānādhṛṣṭikarundhakavatsabālakasṛñjayaśyāmaśamīkagaṇḍūṣasaṃjñā nava bhrātaro babhūvuḥ । pṛthā śrutadevā śrutakīrtiḥ śrutaśravā rājādhidevī ca vasudevādīnāṃ pañca bhaginyo abhavan ।। śūrasya kuntir nāma sakhābhavat । tasmai cāputrāya pṛthām ātmajāṃ vidhinā śūro dattavān । tāṃ ca pāṇḍur uvāha । tasyāṃ ca dharmānilaśakrair yudhiṣṭhirabhīmārjunākhyās trayaḥ putrāḥ samutpāditāḥ । pūrvam anūḍhāyāś ca bhagavatā bhāsvatā kānīnaḥ karṇo nāma putro ajanyata ।। tasyāś ca sapatnī mādrī nāmābhavat । nāsatyadasrābhyāṃ tasyām api nakulasahadevau pāṇḍoḥ putrau janitau । śrutadevāṃ tu vṛddhaśarmā nāma kārūśa upayeme । tasyāṃ dantavakro nāma mahāsuro jajñe । śrutakīrtim api kaikeyarāja upayeme । tasyāṃ saṃtardanādayaḥ kaikeyāḥ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ । rājādhidevyām āvantyau vindānuvindau jajñāte । śrutaśravasam api cedirājo damaghoṣanāmopayeme । tasyāṃ śiśupālam utpādayām āsa । sa hi pūrvam apy anācāravikramasaṃpanno daityānām ādipuruṣo hiraṇyakaśipur abhūt ।। yaś ca bhagavatā sakalalokaguruṇā ghātitaḥ । punar apy akṣatavīryaśauryasaṃpatparākramaguṇaḥ samākrāntasakalatrailokyeśvarapratāpo daśānano abhavat ।।
bahukālopabhuktabhagavatsakāśād avāptaśarīrapātodbhavapuṇyaphalo atha bhagavatāeva rāghavarūpiṇā so api nidhanam upapāditaḥ । cedirājadamaghoṣātmajaś cedipatiḥ śiśupālanāmābhavat ।। śiśupālatve api bhagavato bhūbhārāvatāraṇāyāvatīrṇāṃśasya puṇḍarīkanayanākhyasyopari dveṣānubandham atitarāñ cakāra । bhagavatā ca nidhanam upanītas tatraiva paramātmabhūte manasas tadekāgratayā tatraiva sāyujyam avāpa ।। bhagavān hi prasanno yathābhilaṣitaṃ dadāty aprasanno api nighnan divyam anupamaṃ sthānaṃ prayacchatīti ।। avāpa nihato bhogān aprāpyān amarair api ।।
saṃprāptaḥ śiśupālatve sāyujyaṃ śāśvate harau ।। kautūhalapareṇaitat pṛṣṭo me vaktum arhasi ।। daityeśvarasya tu vadhāyākhilalokotpattisthitivināśakāriṇāpūrvaṃ tanugrahaṇaṃ kurvatā nṛsiṃharūpam āviṣkṛtam । tatra tu hiraṇyakaśipor viṣṇur ayam ity etan na manasy abhūt ।। niratiśayapuṇyajātasamudbhūtam etat sattvam iti rajodrekapreritaikāgramatis tadbhāvanāyogāt tato avāptavadhahaitukīṃ niratiśayām evākhilatrailokyādhikyadhāriṇīṃ daśānanatve bhogasaṃpadam avāpa ।।
nātas tasminn anādinidhane parabrahmabhūte bhagavaty anālambanīkṛte manasas tallayam । daśānanatve apy anaṅgaparādhīnatayā jānakīsaktacetaso dāśarathirūpadhāriṇas tadrūpadarśanam evāsin nāyam acyuta ity āsaktir vipadyato antaḥkaraṇasya mānuṣabuddhir eva kevalam asyābhūt ।। punar apy acyutavinipātamātraphalam akhilabhūmaṇḍalaślāghyacedirājakule janmāvyāhataṃ aiśvaryaṃ śiśupālatve cāvāpa ।। tatra tv akhilāny eva bhagavannāmakāraṇāny abhavan । tataś ca tatkāraṇakṛtānāṃ teṣām aśeṣāṇām evācyutanāmnām anavaratam anekajanmasaṃvardhitavidveṣānubandhicitto vinindanasaṃtarjanādiṣūccāraṇam akarot ।। tac ca rūpam utphullapadmadalāmalākṣam atyujjvalapītavastradhāry amalakirīṭakeyūrakaṭakopaśobhitam udārapīvaracaturbāhuśaṅkhacakragadādharam atiprauḍhavairānubhāvād aṭanabhojanasnānāsanaśayanādiṣv aśeṣāvasthāntareṣu naivāpayayāv asyātmacetasaḥ ।।
tam evākrośeṣūccārayaṃs tam eva hṛdayena dhārayann ātmavadhāya bhagavadastacakrāṃśumālojjvalam akṣayatejaḥsvarūpaṃ paraṃ brahmasvarūpam apagatarāgadveṣādidoṣaṃ bhagavantam adrākṣīt ।। tāvac ca bhagavaccakreṇāśu vyāpāditas tena tatsmaraṇadagdhākhilāghasaṃcayo bhagavataivāntam upanītas tasminn eva layam upayayau । etat tavākhilaṃ mayābhihitam । ayaṃ hi bhagavān kīrtitaḥ saṃsmṛtaś ca dveṣānubandhenāpy akhilasurāsurādidurlabhaṃ phalaṃ prayacchati kim uta samyag bhaktimatām । vasudevasyānakadundubheḥ pauravīrohiṇīmadirābhadrādevakīpramukhā bahvyaḥ patnyo abhavan ।। balabhadrasāraṇaśaṭhadurmadādīn putrān rohiṇyām ānakadundubhir utpādayām āsa । balabhadro api revatyāṃ niśaṭholmukau putrāv ajanayat । mārṣṭimārṣimacchiśiśiśusatyadhṛtipramukhāḥ sāraṇasyātmajāḥ । bhadrāśvabhadrabāhudurdamabhūtādyā rohiṇyāḥ kulajāḥ ।। nandopanandakṛtakādyā madirāyās tanayāḥ । bhadrāyāś copanidhigadādyāḥ । vaiśālyāṃ ca kauśikam ekam ajanayat । ānakadundubhir devakyām api kīrtimatsuṣeṇodāyibhadrasenarjudāsabhadradevākhyāḥ ṣaṭ putrā jajñire ।।
tāṃś ca sarvān eva kaṃso ghātitavān । anantaraṃ ca saptamaṃ garbham ardharātre bhagavatprahitā yoganidrā rohiṇyā jaṭharam avakṛṣya nītavatī ।। karṣaṇāc cāsāv api saṃkarṣaṇākhyām avāpa ।। tataś ca sakalajaganmahātarumūlabhūto bhūtātītabhaviṣyādisakalasurāsuramunimanujamanasām apy agocaro abjabhavapramukhair analapramukhaiś ca praṇamyāvanibhāraharaṇāya prasādito bhagavān anādimadhyo devakīgarbhe samavatatāra vāsudevaḥ ।। tatprasādavivardhitamānābhimānā ca yoganidrā nandagopapatnyā yaśodāyā garbham adhiṣṭhitavatī ।।
suprasannādityacandrādigraham avyālādibhayaṃ svasthamānasam akhilam evaitaj jagad apāstādharmam abhavat tasmiṃś ca puṇḍarīkanayane jāyamāne ।। jātena ca tenākhilam evaitat sanmārgavarti jagad akriyata । bhagavato apy atra martyaloke avatīrṇasya ṣoḍaśasahasrāṇy ekottaraśatādhikāni bhāryāṇām abhavan । tāsāṃ ca rukmiṇīsatyabhāmājāmbavatīcāruhāsinīpramukhā hy aṣṭau patnyaḥ pradhānā । tāsu cāṣṭāyutāni lakṣaṃ ca putrāṇāṃ bhagavān akhilamūrtir anādimān ajanayat ।। teṣāṃ ca pradyumnacārudeṣṇasāmbādayas trayodaśa pradhānāḥ । pradyumno api rukmiṇas tanayāṃ kakudvatīṃ nāmopayeme । tasyām asyāniruddho jajñe । aniruddho api rukmiṇa eva pautrīṃ subhadrāṃ nāmopayeme । tasyām asya vajro abhavat । vajrasya pratibāhus tasyāpi sucāruḥ । evam anekaśatasāhasrapuruṣasaṃkhyasya yadukulasya puruṣasaṃkhyā varṣaśatair api jñātuṃ na śakyate ।। yato hi ślokāv atra caritārthau ।।
kumārāṇāṃ gṛhācāryāś cāpayogyāsu ye ratāḥ ।। yatrāyutānām ayutaṃ lakṣeṇāste sadāhukaḥ ।। te cotpannā manuṣyeṣu janopadravakāriṇaḥ ।। avatīrṇāḥ kulaśataṃ yatraikābhyadhikaṃ dvija ।।
nideśasthāyinas tasya babhūvuḥ sarvayādavāḥ ।। sa sarvaiḥ pātakair mukto viṣṇulokaṃ prapadyate ।। ity eṣa samāsatas te kathito yador vaṃśaḥ । turvasor vaṃśam avadhāraya ।। turvasor vahnir ātmajo vahner gobhānus tataś ca traiśānus tasmāc ca karaṃdhamaḥ । tasyāpi maruttaḥ । so anapatyo abhavat । tataś ca pauravaṃ duṣyantaṃ putram akalpayat । evaṃ yayātiśāpāt tadvaṃśaḥ pauravam vaṃśaṃ samāśritavān ।।
druhyos tu tanayo babhruḥ ।। tataḥ setuḥ । setuputra āradvānnāmā । tadātmajo gāndhāraḥ । tato dharmo dharmād dhṛto dhṛtād durdamaḥ । tataḥ pracetāḥ । pracetasaḥ putraśatam adharmabahulānāṃ mlecchānām udīcyānām ādhipatyam akarot ।। yayāteś caturthasyaputrasyānoḥ sabhānaracakṣuparamekṣusaṃjñās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ । sabhānaraputraḥ kālānaraḥ kālānarāt sṛñjayaḥ sṛñjayāt puraṃjayaḥ । tasmāj janamejayas tato mahāśālas tasmāc ca mahāmanāḥ । tasmād apy uśīnaratitikṣū dvau putrāv utpannau । uśīnarasyāpi śibinṛganarakṛmidarvākhyāḥ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ । vṛṣadarbhasuvīrakaikeyamadrakāś catvāraḥ śibiputrāḥ । titikṣor api ruśadrathaḥ putro abhūt । tato api hemo hemāt sutapās tasmād baliḥ । yasya kṣetre dīrghatamasā aṅgavaṅgakaliṅgasuhyapauṇḍrākhyaṃ bāleyaṃ kṣatram ajanyata ।। tannāmasaṃtatisaṃjñāś ca pañca viṣayāḥ babhūvuḥ । aṅgasya tv anapānas tasyātmajo divirathas tasmād dharmarathaḥ । tataś citraratho romapādasaṃjñaḥ । yasya putro daśaratho jajñe । yasmai ajaputro daśarathaḥ śāntāṃ nāma kanyām anapatyāya duhitṛtve yuyoja ।।
romapādāc caturaṅgas tasmāc ca pṛthulākṣaḥ । tataś campo yaś campāṃ niveśayām āsa । campasya haryaṅgas tato bhadrarathas tato bṛhadrathas tato bṛhatkarmā bṛhatkarmaṇaś ca bṛhadbhānus tasmād bṛhanmanās tato jayadrathaḥ । jayadratho brahmakṣatrāntarālasaṃbhūtyāṃ patnyāṃ vijayaṃ nāma putram ajījanat ।। vijayaś ca dhṛtiṃ putram avāpa । tasyāpi dhṛtavrataḥ putro abhūt । dhṛtavratāt satyakarmā satyakarmaṇas tv adhirathaḥ । yo asau gaṅgāṃ gato mañjūṣāgataṃ pṛthāpaviddhaṃ karṇaṃ putram avāpa । karṇād vṛṣasena ity ete aṅgāḥ ।। ataś ca puror vaṃśaṃ śrotum arhasīti ।। pūror janamejayaḥ putras tasyāpi pracinvān pracinvataḥ pravīraḥ । tasmān manasyur manasyoś cābhayadas tasyāpi sudyuḥ sudyor bahugavaḥ । tasyāpi saṃyātiḥ saṃyāter ahaṃyātiḥ tato raudrāśvaḥ । ṛteyuḥ kakṣeyuḥ sthaṇḍileyur dhṛteyur jaleyuḥ sthaleyur dharmeyuḥ saṃnateyur dhaneyur vaneyur nāmāno raudrāśvasya daśātmajā v putrā babhūvuḥ । ṛteyo rantināraḥ putro abhūt । sumatim apratirathaṃ dhruvaṃ ca rantināraḥ putrān avāpa । apratirathāt kaṇvas tasyāpi medhātithiḥ । yataḥ kaṇvāyanā dvijā babhūvuḥ । apratirathasyāparaḥ putro abhūd ailīnaḥ । tato duṣyantādyāś catvāraḥ putrā babhūvuḥ । duṣyantāc cakravartī bharato abhavat yannāmahetur devaiḥ śloko gīyate । mātā bhastrā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa eva saḥ । bharasva putraṃ duṣyanta māvamaṃsthāḥ śakuntalām ।।
