retodhāḥ putro nayati naradeva yamakṣayāt । tvaṃ cāsya dhātā garbhasya satyam āha śakuntalā ।। bharatasya patnitraye nava putrā babhūvuḥ । naite mamānurūpā ity abhihitās tanmātaro jaghnuḥ parityāgabhayāt । tato asya vitathe putrajanmani putrārthino marutsomayājino dīrghatamasā pārṣṇyapāstabṛhaspativīryād utathyapatnīmamatāsamutpanno bharadvājākhyaḥ putro marudbhir dattaḥ ।। tasyāpi nāmanirvacanaślokaḥ paṭhyate ।। mūḍhe bhara dvājam imaṃ bhara dvājaṃ bṛhaspate । yātau yad uktvā pitarau bharadvājas tatas tv ayam ।।
iti bharadvājaś ca tasya vitathe putrajanmani marudbhir dattas tato vitathasaṃjñām avāpa ।। vitathasya bhavan manyuḥ putro abhūt । bṛhatkṣatramahāvīryanaragargā abhavan manyuputrāḥ । narasya saṃkṛtiḥ saṃkṛte ruciradhīrantidevau । gargāc chinis tato gārgyāḥ śainyāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayo babhūvuḥ ।। mahāvīryād durukṣayo nāma putro abhūt tasya trayyāruṇapuṣkariṇau kapiś ca putratrayam abhūt । tac ca tritayam api paścād vipratām upajagāma । bṛhatkṣatrasya suhotraḥ suhotrād dhastī ya idaṃ hastināpuram āropayām āsa । ajamīḍhadvimīḍhapurumīḍhās trayo hastinas tanayāḥ । ajamīḍhāt kaṇvaḥ kaṇvān medhātithiḥ । yataḥ kaṇvāyanā dvijāḥ ।। ajamīḍhasyānyaḥ putro bṛhadiṣuḥ । tato bṛhaddhanus tataś ca bṛhatkarmā tasmāj jayadrathas tato api viśvajit । tataḥ senajit । rucirāśvakāśyadṛḍhahanuvatsahanusaṃjñāḥ senajitaḥ putrāḥ । rucirāśvataḥ pṛthusenaḥ । tasmāt pāraḥ pārān nīpaḥ । tasyaikaśataṃ putrāṇām । teṣāṃ pradhānaḥ kāmpilyādhipatiḥ samaraḥ ।।
samarasyāpi pārasupārasadaśvās trayaḥ putrāḥ । pārāt pṛthuḥ pṛthoḥ sukṛtiḥ sukṛter vibhrājaḥ । tataś cāṇuho yaḥ śukaduhitaraṃ kṛtvīṃ nāmopayeme ।। aṇuhād brahmadattaḥ । tato viṣvaksenas tasyodaksenaḥ । bhallāṭas tasyātmajaḥ । dvimīḍhasya tu yavīnarasaṃjñas tasyāpi dhṛtimāṃs tataḥ satyadhṛtis tataś ca dṛḍhanemiḥ tasmāc ca supārśvas tataḥ sumatis tataś ca sannatimān sannatimataḥ kṛto abhūt । yaṃ hiraṇyanābho yogam adhyāpayām āsa । yaś caturviṃśati prācyasāmagānāṃ saṃhitāś cakāra ।। kṛtāc cogrāyudho yena prācuryeṇa nīpakṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। ugrāyudhāt kṣemyaḥ kṣemyāt suvīras tasmād ripuṃjayas tasmāc ca bahuratha ity ete pauravāḥ । ajamīḍhasya nalinī nāma patnī tasyāṃ nīlasaṃjñaḥ putro abhavat । tasmād api śāntiḥ śānteḥ suśāntiḥ suśānteḥ purujānuḥ । tataś cakṣus tato haryaśvaḥ । haryaśvān mudgalasṛñjayabṛhadiṣupravīrakāmpilyāḥ । pañcānām eteṣāṃ viṣayāṇāṃ rakṣaṇāyālam ete matputrā iti pitrābhihitam । ataḥ pāñcālāḥ ।।
mudgalāc ca maudgalyāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayo babhūvuḥ । mudgalād vadhyaśvo vadhyaśvād divodāso ahalyā ca mithunam abhūt । śaradvato ahalyāyāṃ śatānando abhavat । śatānandāt satyadhṛtir dhanurvedāntago jajñe । satyadhṛtes tu varāpsarasam urvaśīṃ dṛṣṭvā retaḥ skannaṃ śarastambe papāta ।। tac ca dvidhā gatam apatyadvayaṃ kumāraḥ kanyakā cābhavat । mṛgayām upagataḥ śāntanur dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā jagrāha ।। tataḥ sa kumāraḥ kṛpaḥ kanyā cāśvatthāmno jananī kṛpī droṇasya patny abhavat । divodāsasyāpi mitrāyuḥ putro mitrāyoś cyavano nāma rājā cyavanāt sudāsaḥ । tataḥ saudāsaḥ sahadevas tasyāpi somakaḥ । tato jantuḥ putraśatajyeṣṭho abhavat । teṣāṃ yavīyān pṛṣataḥ pṛṣatād drupadas tasmād dhṛṣṭadyumnas tato dhṛṣṭaketuḥ । ajamīḍhasyānya ṛkṣanāmā putro abhūt । ṛkṣāt saṃvaraṇaḥ saṃvaraṇāc ca kuruḥ । ya idaṃ dharmakṣetraṃ kurukṣetraṃ cakāra ।। sudhanurjahnuparīkṣitpramukhāḥ kuroḥ putrāḥ babhūvuḥ । sudhanuṣaḥ putraḥ suhotraḥ tasmāc cyavanaś cyavanāt kṛtakaḥ । tataś coparicaro vasuḥ । bṛhadrathapratyagrakuśāmbamāvellamatsyapramukhāḥ vasoḥ putrāḥ saptājāyanta । bṛhadrathāt kuśāgras tasmād ṛṣabhas tataḥ puṣpavān । tasmāt satyahitas tasmāt sudhanvā tasya ca jantuḥ । bṛhadrathāc cānyaḥ śakaladvayajanmā jarayā saṃdhito jarāsaṃdhanāmā । tasmāt sahadevas tataḥ somapis tataḥ śrutaśravāḥ । ity ete māgadhā bhūbhṛtaḥ ।।
parīkṣito janamejayaśrutasenograsenabhīmasenāś catvāraḥ putrāḥ ।। jahnos tu suratho nāmātmajo babhūva ।। tasya ca vidūrathaḥ । vidūrathasya sārvabhaumaḥ sārvabhaumāj jayatsenas tasmād ārādhitas tataś cāyutāyur ayutāyor akrodhanaḥ । tasmād devātithiḥ । tato ṛkṣaḥ ।। ṛkṣād bhīmasenas tataś ca dilīpaḥ । dilīpāt pratīpaḥ । tasyāpi devāpiśāṃtanubāhlīkasaṃjñās trayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ । devāpir bāla evāraṇyaṃ viveśa ।।
śāṃtanus tu mahīpālo abhavat । ayaṃ ca tasya ślokaḥ pṛthivyāṃ gīyate । śāntiṃ cāpnoti yenāgryāṃ karmaṇā tena śāṃtanuḥ ।। tasya śāṃtano rāṣṭre dvādaśavarṣāṇi devo na vavarṣa ।। tataś cāśeṣarāṣṭravināśam avekṣyāsau rājā brāhmaṇān apṛcchat । kasmād asmadrāṣṭre devo na varṣati ko mamāparādha iti । te tam ūcuḥ । agrajasya te arheyam avanis tvayā bhujyate parivettā tvam ity uktaḥ sa punas tān apṛcchat । kiṃ mayā vidheyam iti । te punar apy ūcuḥ । yāvad devāpir na patanādibhir doṣair abhibhūyate tāvat tasyārhaṃ rājyam । tad alam etena tasmai dīyatām ity ukte tasya mantripravareṇāśmasāriṇātatrāraṇye tapasvino vedavādavirodhavaktāraḥ prayuktāḥ ।।
tair asyātiṛjumater mahīpatiputrasya buddhir vedavirodhamārgānusāriṇy akriyata ।। rājā ca śāṃtanur dvijavacanotpannaparivedanaśokas tān brāhmaṇān agraṇīkṛtyāgrajarājyapradānāyāraṇyaṃ jagāma । tadāśramam upagatāś ca tam avanīpatiputraṃ devāpim upatasthuḥ । te brāhmaṇā vedavādānubaddhāni vacāṃsi rājyam agrajena kartavyam ity arthavanti tam ūcuḥ । asāv api devāpir vedavādavirodhiyuktidūṣitam anekaprakāraṃ tān āha । tatas te brāhmaṇāḥ śāṃtanum ūcuḥ । āgaccha bho rājann alam atrātinirbandhena praśānta evāsāv anāvṛṣṭidoṣaḥ patito ayam anādikālam ahitavedavacanadūṣaṇoccāraṇāt । patite cāgraje naiva pārivedyaṃ bhavatīty uktaḥ śāṃtanuḥ svapuram āgatya rājyam akarot । vedavādavirodhivacanoccāraṇadūṣite ca tasmin devāpāv akhilasya niṣpattaye vavarṣa bhagavān parjanyaḥ । bāhlīkasya somadattaḥ putro abhūt ।। somadattasyāpi bhūribhūriśravaḥśalyasaṃjñās trayaḥ putrāḥ । śāṃtanor apy amaranadyāṃ gaṅgāyām udārakīrtir aśeṣaśāstrārthavid bhīṣmaḥ putro abhūt । satyavatyāṃ ca citrāṅgadavicitravīryau putrāv utpādayām āsa śāṃtanuḥ । citrāṅgadas tu bāla eva citrāṅgadena gandharveṇāhave vinihataḥ । vicitravīryo api kāśīrājatanaye ambikāmbālike upayeme । tadupabhogātikhedāc ca yakṣmaṇā gṛhītaḥ pañcatvam agamat । satyavatīniyogāc ca tatputraḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyano mātur vacanam anatikramaṇīyam iti vicitravīryakṣetre dhṛtarāṣṭrapāṇḍū tatprahitabhujiṣyāyāṃ ca viduraṃ utpādayām āsa ।। dhṛtarāṣṭro api duryodhanaduḥśāsanādipradhānaṃ putraśatam utpādayām āsa । pāṇḍor apy araṇye mṛgaśāpopahataprajananasāmarthyasya dharmavāyuśakrair yudhiṣṭhirabhīmārjunāḥ kuntyāṃ nakulasahadevau cāśvibhyāṃ mādryāṃ pañca putrāḥ samutpāditāḥ । teṣāṃ ca draupadyāṃ pañca putrā babhūvuḥ । yudhiṣṭhirāt prativindhyo bhīmasenāc chrutasomaḥ śrutakīrtir arjunāc chatānīko nakulāc chrutakarmā sahadevāt । apare ca pāṇḍavānām ātmajās tad yathā । yaudheyī yudhiṣṭhirād devakaṃ putram avāpa । hiḍimbā ghaṭotkacaṃ bhīmasenāt putraṃ lebhe । kāśī ca bhīmasenād eva sarvatragaṃ putram avāpa । sahadevāc ca vijayā suhotraṃ nāma putraṃ prāptavatī । kareṇumatyāṃ ca nakulo api niramitram ajījanat ।।
arjunasyāpy ulūpyāṃ nāgakanyāyām irāvān nāma putro abhūt । maṇipurapatiputryāṃ ca putrikādharmeṇa babhruvāhanaṃ nāma putram arjuno ajanayat ।। subhadrāyāṃ cārbhakatve api yo asāv atibalaparākramasamastārātirathavijetā so abhimanyur ajāyata । abhimanyor uttarāyāṃ parikṣīṇeṣu kuruṣv aśvatthāmaprayuktabrahmāstreṇa garbha eva bhasmīkṛto bhagavataḥ sakalasurāsuravanditacaraṇayugalasyātmecchākāraṇamānuṣarūpadhāriṇo anubhāvāt punar jīvitam avāpya parīkṣij jajñe । yo ayaṃ sāmpratam etad bhūmaṇḍalam akhaṇḍitāyatidharmeṇa pālayati। ।। ataḥ paraṃ bhaviṣyān ahaṃ bhūpālān kīrtayiṣyāmi । yo ayaṃ sāmpratam avanīpatiḥ parīkṣit tasyāpi janamejayaśrutasenograsenabhīmasenāḥ putrāś catvāro bhaviṣyanti ।। tasyāparaḥ śatānīko bhaviṣyati । yo asau yājñavalkyād vedam adhītya kṛpād astrāṇy avāpya viṣayaviraktacittavṛttiś ca śaunakopadeśād ātmavijñānapravīṇaḥ paraṃ nirvāṇam āpsyati ।।
śatānīkād apy aśvamedhadatto bhavitā । tasmād apy adhisīmakṛṣṇaḥ adhisīmakṛṣṇān niścaknuḥ । yo gaṅgayāpahṛte hastināpure kauśāmbyāṃ nivatsyati । tasyāpy uṣṇaḥ putro bhavitā । uṣṇāc citrarathas tataḥ śucirathas tasmād vṛṣṇimāṃs tataḥ suṣeṇaḥ । tasmād api sunīthaḥ sunīthād ṛcas tato nṛcakṣus tasyāpi sukhibalas tasmād pariplavas tataś ca sunayas tato medhāvī । tato npaṃjayas tato mṛdus tasmāt tigmas tigmād bṛhadrathaḥ । tasmād vasudānas tato aparaḥ śatānīkaḥ । tasmāc codayana udayanād ahīnaras tataś ca daṇḍapāṇis tato niramitras tasmāc ca kṣemakaḥ । atrāyaṃ ślokaḥ । kṣemakaṃ prāpya rājānaṃ sa saṃsthāṃ prāpsyate kalau ।। ataś cekṣvākavo bhaviṣyāḥ pārthivāḥ kathyante । bṛhadbalasya putro bṛhatkṣaṇaḥ ।। tasmād urukṣayas tato vatso vatsād vatsavyūhaḥ । tataḥ prativyomas tasyāpi divākaras tasmāt sahadevaḥ ।।
tato bṛhadaśvas tatsūnur bhānurathas tasya pratītāśvas tasyāpi supratīkaḥ । tato marudevo marudevāt sunakṣatras tasmāt kiṃnaraḥ । kiṃnara-d antarikṣas tasmāt suvarṇas tataś cāmitrajit । tataś ca bṛhadrājas tasyāpi dharmī dharmiṇaḥ kṛtaṃjayaḥ । kṛtaṃjayād raṇaṃjayo raṇaṃjayāt saṃjayas tasmāc chākyaḥ । śākyāc chuddhodanas tasmād rāhulas tataḥ prasenajit । tataś ca kṣudrakas tataś ca kuṇḍakas tasmād api surathaḥ । tatputraś ca sumitro antya ity ete cekṣvākavo bṛhadbalānvayāḥ । atrānuvaṃśaślokaḥ । yatas taṃ prāpya rājānaṃ sa saṃsthāṃ prāpsyate kalau ।। māgadhānāṃ bārhadrathānāṃ bhaviṣyāṇām anukramaṃ kathayāmi । atra hi vaṃśe mahābalā jarāsaṃdhapradhānā babhūvuḥ ।। jarāsaṃdhasutāt sahadevāt somāpis tasmāc chṛtavāṃs tasyāpy ayutāyus tataś ca niramitras tattanayaḥ sukṣatras tasmād api bṛhatkarmā । tataś ca senajit tasmāc ca śrutaṃjayas tato vipras tasya putraḥ śucināmā bhaviṣyati । tasyāpi kṣemyas tataś ca suvrataḥ suvratād dharmas tataḥ suśramaḥ । tato dṛḍhasenas tataḥ sumatis tasmāt subalas tasya sunīto bhavitā । tataḥ satyajit satyajito viśvajit tasyāpi ripuṃjayaḥ putraḥ । ity ete bārhadrathā bhūpatayo varṣasahasram ekaṃ bhaviṣyantīti ।।
yo ayaṃ ripuṃjayo nāma bārhadratho antyas tasya muniko nāmāmātyo bhaviṣyati । sa cainaṃ svāminaṃ hatvā svaputraṃ pradyotanāmānam abhiṣekṣyati । tasyāpi pālako nāma putro bhavitā । tataś ca viśākhayūpas tatputro janakas tasya ca nandivardhanaḥ । ity ete aṣṭatriṃśaduttaram abdaśataṃ pañca pradyotāḥ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti ।। tataś ca śiśunāgas tatputraś ca kākavarṇo bhavitā । tatputraḥ kṣemadharmā tasyāpi kṣatraujāḥ । tatputro vidhisāras tataś cājātaśatruḥ । tasmāc ca darbhako darbhakāc codayanaḥ । tasmād api nandivardhanas tato mahānandī । ity ete śaiśunāgā daśa bhūmipālās trīṇi varṣaśatāni dviṣaṣṭyadhikāni bhaviṣyanti ।। mahānandisutaḥ śūdrāgarbhodbhavo atilubdho mahāpadmo nandaḥ paraśurāma ivāparo akhilakṣatrāntakārī bhavitā ।। tataḥprabhṛti śūdrā bhūmipālā bhaviṣyanti । sa caikacchatrām anullaṅghitaśāsano mahāpadmaḥ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyati ।।
tasyāpy aṣṭau sutāḥ sumālyādyā bhavitāraḥ । tasya ca mahāpadmasyānu pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti । mahāpadmas tatputrāś ca ekaṃ varṣaśatam avanīpatayo bhaviṣyanti । navaitān nandān kauṭilyo brāhmaṇaḥ samuddhariṣyati ।। teṣām abhāve mauryāḥ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti । kauṭilya eva candraguptaṃ rājye abhiṣekṣyati ।। tasyāpi putro bindusāro bhaviṣyati । tasyāpy aśokavardhanas tataḥ suyaśās tato daśarathas tataḥ saṃgatas tataḥ śāliśūkas tasmāt somaśarmā tasmāc chatadhanvā । tasyāpy'nu bṛhadrathanāmā bhavitā । evaṃ mauryā daśa bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti abdaśataṃ saptatriṃśaduttaram । teṣām ante pṛthivīṃ śuṅgā bhokṣyanti ।। puṣyamitraḥ senāpatiḥ svāminaṃ hatvā rājyaṃ kariṣyati ।।
asyātmajo agnimitras tasmāt sujyeṣṭhas tato vasumitras tasmād apy ardrakas tataḥ pulindakas tato ghoṣavasus tasmād api vajramitras tato bhāgavataḥ ।। tasmād devabhūtiḥ । ity ete daśa śuṅgā dvādaśottaraṃ varṣaśataṃ pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanti । tataḥ kaṇvān eṣā bhūr yāsyati ।। devabhūtiṃ tu śuṅgarājānaṃ vyasaninaṃ tasyaivāmātyaḥ kaṇvo vasudevanāmā nipātya svayam avanīṃ bhokṣyate । tasya putro bhūmitras tasyāpi nārāyaṇaḥ । nārāyaṇasyātmajaḥ suśarmā । ete kāṇvāyanāś catvāraḥ pañcacatvāriṃśad varṣāṇi bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti । suśarmāṇaṃ tu kāṇvaṃ svabhṛtyo balāt śiprakanāmā hatvāndhrajātīyo vasudhāṃ bhokṣyati । tataś ca kṛṣṇanāmā tadbhrātā bhūpatir bhāvī । tasya putraḥ śrīśātakarṇis tasyāpi pūrṇotsaṅgas tatputraś ca śātakarṇis tasmāc ca lambodaras tasmād divīlakas tato meghasvātis tataḥ paṭumān । tataś cāriṣṭakarmā tato hālo hālāt pattalakas tataḥ pravilla senas tataḥ sundaraḥ śātakarṇī tasmāc cakoraḥ śātakarṇī tataḥ śivasvātis tataś ca gomatīputras tatputraḥ pulimān । tasyāpi śātakarṇī tataḥ śivaśrīs tataḥ śivaskandhaḥ । tasmād yajñaśrīs tato vijayas tataś candraśrīs tasyāpi pulomāviḥ । evam ete triṃśac catvāry abdaśatāni ṣaṭpañcāśadadhikāni pṛthivīṃ bhokṣyanty āndhrabhṛtyāḥ ।। saptābhīrāḥ daśa gardabhilāś ca bhūbhujo bhaviṣyanti । tataḥ ṣoḍaśa śakā bhūpatayo bhavitāraḥ । tataś cāṣṭau yavanāś caturdaśa tuṣārā muṇḍāś ca trayodaśa ekādaśa maunāḥ । ete pṛthivīṃ trayodaśavarṣaśatāni navanavatyadhikāni bhokṣyanti ।।
tataś ca paurā ekādaśa bhūpatayo abdaśatāni trīṇi mahīṃ bhokṣyanti । teṣūtsanneṣu kailakilā yavanā bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanty amūrdhābhiṣiktāḥ । teṣāṃ vindhyaśaktiḥ ।। tataḥ puraṃjayas tato rāmacandras tasmād dharmo dharmād vaṅgaraḥ kṛtanandanaḥ suṣinandis tadbhrātā nandiyaśāḥ śiśukapravīrau caite varṣaśataṃ ṣaḍ varṣāṇi ca bhaviṣyanti । tatas tatputrās trayodaśaite bāhlikāś ca trayaḥ । tataḥ puṣyamitrapaṭumitrās trayodaśa mekalāś ca saptāndhrāḥ । kosalāyāṃ tu navaiva bhūpatayo bhaviṣyanti । naiṣadhās tu tāvanta eva ।। māgadhāyāṃ tu viśvasphaṭikasaṃjño anyān varṇān kariṣyati । kaivartapaṭupulindabrāhmaṇān rājye sthāpayiṣyati । utsādyākhilakṣatrajātim । nava nāgāḥ padmāvatyāṃ nāma puryāṃ mathurāyām anugaṅgāprayāgaṃ māgadhā guptāś ca bhokṣyanti । kośalauḍrapuṇḍratāmraliptān samudrataṭapurīṃ ca devarakṣito rakṣiṣyati । kaliṅgamāhiṣakamāhendrā bhaumāṃ guhāṃ bhokṣyanti । naiṣadhanaimiṣikakālatoyān janapadān maṇidhānakavaṃśyā bhokṣyanti । trairājyamūṣikajanapadān kanakāhvayā bhokṣyanti । saurāṣṭrāvantiśūdrān arbudamarubhūmiviṣayāṃś ca vrātyā dvijābhīraśūdrādyā bhokṣyanti । sindhutaṭadāvikorvīcandrabhāgākāśmīraviṣayāṃś ca vrātyā mlecchādayaḥ śūdrā bhokṣyanti । ete ca tulyakālāḥ sarve pṛthivyāṃ bhūbhṛto bhaviṣyanti । alpaprasādā bṛhatkopāḥ sarvakālam anṛtādharmarucayaḥ strībālagovadhakartāraḥ parasvādānarucayo alpasārā uditāstamitaprāyāḥ svalpāyuṣo mahecchā hy alpadharmāś ca bhaviṣyanti ।। taiś ca vimiśrā janapadās tacchīlavartino rājāśrayaśuṣmiṇo mlecchācāryāś ca viparyayeṇa vartamānāḥ prajāḥ kṣapayiṣyanti । tataś cānudinam alpālpahrāsavyavacchedād dharmārthayor jagataḥ saṃkṣayo bhaviṣyati ।।
tataś cārtha evābhijanahetuḥ । dhanam evāśeṣadharmahetuḥ । abhirucir eva dāmpatyasaṃbandhahetuḥ । strītvam evopabhogahetuḥ । anṛtam eva vyavahārajayahetuḥ । ratnatāmrabhāgitaiva pṛthivīhetuḥ । brahmasūtram eva vipratvahetuḥ । liṅgadhāraṇam evāśramahetuḥ । anyāya eva vṛttihetuḥ ।। daurbalyam evāvṛttihetuḥ । bhayagarbhoccāraṇam eva pāṇḍityahetuḥ । āḍhyataiva sādhutvahetuḥ ।। snānam eva prasādhanahetuḥ । dānam eva dharmahetuḥ । svīkaraṇam eva vivāhahetuḥ । sadveśadhāry eva pātram । dūrāyatanodakam eva tīrtham । ity evam anekadoṣottare bhūmaṇḍale sarvavarṇeṣv eva yo yo balavān sa sa bhūpatir bhaviṣyati । evaṃ cātilubdhakarabhārāsahāḥ śailānām antaradroṇīḥ prajāḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti । madhuśākamūlaphalapattrapuṣpādyāhārāś ca bhaviṣyanti । taruvalkalacīraprāvaraṇāś cātibahuprajāḥ śītavātātapavarṣasahā bhaviṣyanti । na ca kaścit trayoviṃśativarṣāṇi jīviṣyati anavarataṃ cātra kaliyuge kṣayam āyāty akhila evaiṣa janaḥ kṣayam upaiṣyati ।। śrautasmārtadharme viplavam atyantam upagate kṣīṇaprāye ca kalāv aśeṣajagatsraṣṭuś carācaraguror ādimayasyāntamayasya sarvamayasya brahmamayasyātmarūpiṇo bhagavato vāsudevasyāṃśaḥ śambalagrāmapradhānabrāhmaṇaviṣṇuyaśaso gṛhe aṣṭaguṇarddhisamanvitaḥ kalkirūpī jagaty atrāvatīrya sakalamlecchadasyuduṣṭācaraṇacetasām aśeṣāṇām aparicchinnamāhātmyaśaktiḥ kṣayaṃ kariṣyati । svadharmeṣu cākhilaṃ jagat saṃsthāpayiṣyati । anantaraṃ cāśeṣakaler avasāne niśāvasānaprabuddhānāṃ teṣām eva janapadānām amalasphaṭikaviśuddhā matayo bhaviṣyanti ।।
teṣāṃ ca bījabhūtānām aśeṣamanuṣyāṇāṃ pariṇatānām api tatkālakṛtānām apatyaprasūtir bhaviṣyati । tāni ca tadapatyāni kṛtayugadharmānusārīṇy eva bhaviṣyantīti ।। atrocyate । ekarāśau sameṣyanti bhaviṣyati tadā kṛtam ।। ete vaṃśeṣu bhūpālāḥ kathitā munisattama ।।
etad varṣasahasraṃ tu jñeyaṃ pañcadaśottaram ।। tena saptarṣayo yuktās tiṣṭhanty abdaśataṃ nṛṇām ।। tadā pravṛttaś ca kalir dvādaśābdaśatātmakaḥ ।। vasudevakulodbhūtas tadaivātrāgataḥ kaliḥ ।।
tāvat pṛthvīpariṣvaṅge samartho nābhavat kaliḥ ।। tatyāja sānujo rājyaṃ dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। yāte kṛṣṇe cakārātha so abhiṣekaṃ parīkṣitaḥ ।। tadā nandāt prabhṛty eṣa kalir vṛddhiṃ gamiṣyati ।।
pratipannaṃ kaliyugaṃ tasya saṃkhyāṃ nibodha me ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ caiva sahasrāṇi bhaviṣyaty eṣa vai kaliḥ ।। niḥśeṣeṇa tatas tasmin bhaviṣyati punaḥ kṛtam ।। yuge yuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।
punaruktabahutvāt tu na mayā parikīrtitā ।। mahāyogabalopetau kalāpagrāmasaṃśrayau ।। bhaviṣyato manor vaṃśabījabhūtau vyavasthitau ।। kṛtatretādisaṃjñāni yugāni trīṇi bhujyate ।।
yathaiva devāpimarū sāmprataṃ samavasthitau ।। nikhilo gadituṃ śakyo naiva janmaśatair api ।। kṛtaṃ mamatvaṃ mohāndhair nitye anityakalevaraiḥ ।। madvaṃśasyeti cintārtā jagmur antam ime nṛpāḥ ।।
bhaviṣyāś caiva yāsyanti teṣām anye ca ye adhy anu ।। puṣpaprahāsaiḥ śaradi hasatīva vasuṃdharā ।। yān āha dharmadhvajine janakāyāsito muniḥ ।। yena phenasadharmāṇo apy ativiśvastacetasaḥ ।।
tato bhṛtyāṃś ca paurāṃś ca jigīṣante tathā ripūn ।। ity āsaktadhiyo mṛtyuṃ na paśyanty avidūragam ।। kiyad ātmajayād etan muktir ātmajaye phalam ।। tāṃ mameti vimūḍhatvāj jetum icchanti pārthivāḥ ।।
jāyante atyantamohena mamatvādṛtacetasām ।। yo yo mṛto hy atra babhūva rājā kubuddhir āsīd iti tasya tasya ।। tasyānvayasthasya kathaṃ mamatvaṃ hṛdy āspadaṃ matprabhavaṃ karoti ।। narādhipās teṣu mamātihāsaḥ punaś ca mūḍheṣu dayābhyupaiti ।।
mamatvaṃ vilayaṃ yāti tāpanyastaṃ yathā himam ।। yatra sthitipravṛttasya viṣṇor aṃśāṃśakā nṛpāḥ ।। tasya pāpam aśeṣaṃ vai praṇaśyaty amalātmanaḥ ।। ikṣvākujahnumāndhātṛsagarāvikṣitān raghūn ।।
mahābalān mahāvīryān anantadhanasaṃcayān ।। kṛtān kālena balinā kathāśeṣān narādhipān ।। । dravyādau vā kṛtaprajño mamatvaṃ kurute naraḥ ।। iṣṭāś ca yajñā balino ativīryāḥ kṛtās tu kālena kathāvaśeṣāḥ ।।
sa kālavātābhihato vinaṣṭaḥ kṣiptaṃ yathā śālmalitūlam agnau ।। kathāprasaṅgeṣv abhidhīyamānaḥ sa eva saṃkalpavikalpahetuḥ ।। bhasmāpi jātaṃ na kathaṃ kṣaṇena bhrūbhaṅgapātena dhig antakasya ।। śrutvāpi taṃ ko hi karoti sādhur mamatvam ātmany api mandacetāḥ ।।
yudhiṣṭhirādyāś ca babhūvur ete satyaṃ na mithyā kva nu te na vidmaḥ ।। ye te tathānye ca tathābhidheyāḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti yathaiva pūrve ।। tiṣṭhantu tāvat tanayātmajāyāḥ kṣetrādayo ye tu śarīrato anye ।। śrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥ ।।
vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva yathāvad anuvarṇitam ।। viṣṇos taṃ vistareṇāhaṃ śrotum icchāmy aśeṣataḥ ।। aṃśāṃśenāvatīryorvyāṃ tatra tāni mune vada ।। viṣṇor aṃśāṃśasaṃbhūticaritaṃ jagato hitam ।।
upayeme mahābhāgāṃ devakīṃ devatopamām ।। vasudevasya devakyāḥ saṃyoge bhojavardhanaḥ ।। meghagambhīranirghoṣaṃ samābhāṣyedam abravīt ।। asyās tavāṣṭamo garbhaḥ prāṇān apahariṣyati ।।
devakīṃ hantum ārabdho vasudevo abravīd idam ।। samarpayiṣye sakalān garbhān asyāudarodbhavān ।। na ghātayām āsa ca tāṃ devakīṃ tasya gauravāt ।। jagāma dharaṇī merau samāje tridivaukasām ।।
kathayām āsa tat sarvaṃ khedāt karuṇabhāṣiṇī ।। mamāpy akhilalokānāṃ gurur nārāyaṇo guruḥ ।। kalākāṣṭhānimeṣātmā kālaś cāvyaktamūrtimān ।। tadaṃśabhūtaḥ sarveṣāṃ samūho vaḥ surottamāḥ ।।
pitaro ye ca lokānāṃ sraṣṭāro atripurogamāḥ ।। etat tasyāprameyasya rūpaṃ viṣṇor mahātmanaḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaś caiva rūpaṃ viṣṇor mahātmanaḥ ।। ahaṃ ca viṣayāś caitat sarvaṃ viṣṇumayaṃ jagat ।।
bādhyabādhakatāṃ yānti kallolā iva sāgare ।। martyalokaṃ samākramya bādhante aharniśaṃ prajāḥ ।। ugrasenasutaḥ kaṃsaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ sa mahāsuraḥ ।। sundo asuras tathātyugro bāṇaś cāpi baleḥ sutaḥ ।।
samutpannā durātmānas tān na saṃkhyātum utsahe ।। mahābalānāṃ dṛptānāṃ daityendrāṇāṃ mamopari ।। bibhartum ātmānam aham iti vijñāpayāmi vaḥ ।। yathā rasātalaṃ nāhaṃ gaccheyam ativihvalā ।।
bhuvo bhārāvatārārthaṃ brahmā prāha pracoditaḥ ।। ahaṃ bhavo bhavantaś ca sarvaṃ nārāyaṇātmakam ।। ādhikyanyūnatā bādhyabādhakatvena vartate ।। tatrārādhya hariṃ tasmai sarvaṃ vijñāpayāma vai ।।
svalpāṃśenāvatīryorvyāṃ dharmasya kurute sthitim ।। samāhitamatiś cainaṃ tuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam ।। ta eva bhavato rūpe mūrtāmūrtātmike prabho ।। śabdabrahmaparaṃ caiva brahma brahmamayasya yat ।।
śikṣā kalpo niruktaṃ ca chando jyotiṣam eva ca ।। mīmāṃsā nyāyikaṃ tadvad dharmaśāstrāṇy adhokṣaja ।। tad apy ādyapate nānyad adhyātmātmasvarūpavat ।। apāṇipādarūpaṃ ca viṣṇur nityaṃ parāt param ।।
apādahasto javano grahītā tvaṃ vetsi sarvaṃ na ca sarvavedyaḥ ।। dhīr asya dhīryasya bibharti nānyad vareṇyarūpāt parataḥ parātman ।। yad bhūtabhavyaṃ tad aṇor aṇīyaḥ pumāṃs tvam ekaḥ prakṛteḥ parastāt ।। tvaṃ viśvataś cakṣur anantamūrte tredhā padaṃ tvaṃ nidadhe vidhātaḥ ।।
tathā bhavān sarvagataikarūpo rūpāṇy anekāny anupuṣyatīśaḥ ।। tvatto nānyat kiṃcid asti svarūpaṃ yad vā bhūtaṃ yac ca bhavyaṃ parātman ।। sarvajñaḥ sarvadṛk sarvaśaktijñānabalarddhimān ।। klamatandrībhayakrodhakāmādibhir asaṃyutaḥ ।।
sarveśvara parādhāra dhāmnāṃ dhāmātmako akṣayaḥ ।। mahāvibhūtisaṃsthāna namas te puruṣottama ।। śarīragrahaṇaṃ vyāpin dharmatrāṇāya te param ।। brahmāṇam āha viśvātmā viśvarūpadharo hariḥ ।।
tad ucyatām aśeṣaṃ ca siddham evāvadhāryatām ।। tuṣṭāva bhūyo deveṣu sādhvasāvanatātmasu ।। namo namas te jagataḥ pravṛtti vināśasaṃsthānakarāprameya ।। pradhānabuddhīndriyavatpradhāna mūlāt parātman bhagavan prasīda ।।
parāyaṇaṃ tvāṃ jagatām upaiti bhārāvatārārtham apārapāram ।। ime ca rudrā vasavaḥ sasūryāḥ samīraṇāgnipramukhās tathānye ।। ājñāpayājñāṃ paripālayantas tathaiva tiṣṭhāma sadāstadoṣāḥ ।। ujjahārātmanaḥ keśau sitakṛṣṇau mahāmune ।।
avatīrya bhuvo bhārakleśahāniṃ kariṣyataḥ ।। kurvantu yuddham unmattaiḥ pūrvotpannair mahāsuraiḥ ।। prayāsyanti na saṃdeho maddṛkpātavicūrṇitāḥ ।। tasyāyam aṣṭamo garbho matkeśo bhavitā surāḥ ।।
kālanemiṃ samudbhūtam ity uktvāntardadhe hariḥ ।। merupṛṣṭhaṃ surā jagmur avateruś ca bhūtale ।। bhaviṣyatīty ācacakṣe bhagavān nārado muniḥ ।। devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca gṛhe guptāv adhārayat ।।
tathaiva vasudevo api putram arpitavān dvija ।। viṣṇuprayuktā tān nidrā kramād garbhe nyayojayat ।। avidyayā jagat sarvaṃ tām āha bhagavān hariḥ ।। ekaikaśyena ṣaḍ garbhān devakījaṭharaṃ naya ।।
aṃśāṃśenodare tasyāḥ saptamaḥ saṃbhaviṣyati ।। tasyāḥ sa saṃbhūtisamaṃ devi neyas tvayodaram ।। devakyāḥ patito garbha iti loko vadiṣyati ।। saṃjñām avāpsyate vīraḥ śvetādriśikharopamaḥ ।।
garbhe tvayā yaśodāyā gantavyam avilambitam ।। utpatsyāmi navamyāṃ ca prasūtiṃ tvam avāpsyasi ।। macchaktipreritamatir vasudevo nayiṣyati ।। prakṣepsyaty antarikṣe ca tvaṃ sthānaṃ samavāpsyasi ।।
praṇipātānataśirā bhaginītve grahīṣyati ।। sthānair anekaiḥ pṛthivīm aśeṣāṃ maṇḍayiṣyasi ।। lajjā puṣṭir uṣā yā ca kācid anyā tvam eva sā ।। yā ca kācana vidyeti matprasādāt tvam eva sā ।।
bhadreti bhadrakālīti kṣemyā kṣemakarīti ca ।। teṣāṃ hi prārthitaṃ sarvaṃ matprasādād bhaviṣyati ।। nṝṇām aśeṣakāmāṃs tvaṃ prasannā saṃpradāsyasi ।। asaṃdigdhā bhaviṣyanti gaccha devi yathoditam ।।
ṣaḍgarbhagarbhavinyāsaṃ cakre cānyasya karṣaṇam ।। lokatrayopakārāya devakyāḥ praviveśa vai ।। saṃbhūtā jaṭhare tadvad yathoktaṃ parameṣṭhinā ।। viṣṇor aṃśe bhuvaṃ yāte ṛtavaś cābhavan śubhāḥ ।।
jājvalyamānāṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā manāṃsi kṣobham āyayuḥ ।। bibhrāṇāṃ vapuṣā viṣṇuṃ tuṣṭuvus tām aharniśam ।। tato vāṇī jagaddhātur vedagarbhātiśobhane ।। bījabhūtā tu sarvasya yajñagarbhābhavas trayī ।।
aditir devagarbhā tvaṃ daityagarbhā tathā ditiḥ ।। nayagarbhadharā nītir lajjā tvaṃ praśrayodvahā ।। medhā ca bodhagarbhāsi dhairyagarbhodvahā dhṛtiḥ ।। etā vibhūtayo devi tathānyāś ca sahasraśaḥ ।।
grāmakharvaṭakheṭāḍhyā samastā pṛthivī śubhe ।। samastavahnayo ambhāṃsi sakalāś ca samīraṇāḥ ।। b mahoragās tathā yakṣā rākṣasāḥ pretaguhyakāḥ ।। b graharkṣatārakācitraṃ vimānaśatasaṃkulam ।। d
avakāśam aśeṣasya yad dadāti nabhaś ca tat ।। f tapaś ca brahmalokaś ca brahmāṇḍam akhilaṃ śubhe ।। mahoragās tathā yakṣā rākṣasāḥ pretaguhyakāḥ ।। tair antaḥsthair ananto asau sarveśaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ।।
yasyākhilapramāṇāni sa viṣṇur garbhagas tava ।। tvaṃ sarvalokarakṣārtham avatīrṇā mahītale ।। prītyā taṃ dhārayeśānaṃ dhṛtaṃ yenākhilaṃ jagat ।। garbheṇa puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ jagatāṃ trāṇakāraṇam ।।
devakīpūrvasaṃdhyāyām āvirbhūtaṃ mahātmanā ।। babhūva sarvalokasya kaumudī śaśino yathā ।। prasādaṃ nimnagā yātā jāyamāne janārdane ।। jagur gandharvapatayo nanṛtuś cāpsarogaṇāḥ ।।
jajvaluś cāgnayaḥ śāntā jāyamāne janārdane ।। mandaṃ jagarjur jaladāḥ puṣpavṛṣṭimuco dvija ।। śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ jātaṃ tuṣṭāvānakadundubhiḥ ।। vijñāpayām āsa tadā kaṃsād bhīto dvijottama ।।
divyaṃ rūpam idaṃ deva prasādenopasaṃhara ।। avatīrṇam iti jñātvā tvam asmin mama mandire ।। prasīdatām eṣa sa devadevaḥ svamāyayāviṣkṛtabālarūpaḥ ।। jānātu māvatāraṃ te kaṃso ayaṃ ditijātmajaḥ ।।
saphalaṃ devi saṃjātaṃ jāto ahaṃ yat tavodarāt ।। vasudevo api taṃ rātrāv ādāya prayayau bahiḥ ।। mathurādvārapālāś ca vrajaty ānakadundubhau ।। saṃcchādyānuyayau śeṣaḥ phaṇair ānakadundubhim ।।
vasudevo vahan viṣṇuṃ jānumātravahāṃ yayau ।। nandādīn gopavṛddhāṃś ca yamunāyāṃ dadarśa saḥ ।। tām eva kanyāṃ maitreya prasūtā mohite jane ।। yaśodāśayane tūrṇam ājagāmāmitadyutiḥ ।।
nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ tato atyarthaṃ mudaṃ yayau ।। devakīśayane nyasya yathāpūrvam atiṣṭhata ।। kaṃsāyāvedayām āsur devakīprasavaṃ dvija ।। muñca muñceti devakyā sannakaṇṭhyā nivāritaḥ ।।
avāpa rūpaṃ ca mahat sāyudhāṣṭamahābhujam ।। kiṃ mayā kṣiptayā kaṃsa jāto yas tvāṃ vadhiṣyati ।। tad etat saṃpradhāryāśu kriyatāṃ hitam ātmanaḥ ।। paśyato bhojarājasya stutā siddhair vihāyasā ।।
pralambakeśipramukhān āhūyāsurapuṃgavān ।। ariṣṭādyais tathā cānyaiḥ śrūyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama ।। madvīryatāpitair vīrā na tv etān gaṇayāmy aham ।। hariṇā vāpi kiṃ sādhyaṃ chidreṣv asuraghātinā ।।
kiṃ vānyair amaraiḥ sarvair madbāhubalanirjitaiḥ ।। pṛṣṭhenaiva vahan bāṇān apāgacchan na vakṣasā ।। madbāṇabhinnair jaladair āpo muktā yathepsitāḥ ।। na sarve sannatiṃ yātā jarāsaṃdham ṛte gurum ।।
hāsyaṃ me jāyate vīrās teṣu yatnapareṣv api ।। apakārāya daityendrā yatanīyaṃ durātmanām ।। kāryo devāpakārāya teṣāṃ sarvātmanā vadhaḥ ।। ity etad bālikā prāha devakīgarbhasaṃbhavā ।।
yatrodriktaṃ balaṃ bāle sa hantavyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।। mumoca vasudevaṃ ca devakīṃ ca nirodhataḥ ।। ko apy anya eva nāśāya bālo mama samudgataḥ ।। arbhakā yuvayoḥ ko vā nāyuṣo ante vihanyate ।।
antargṛhaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha praviveśa punaḥ svakam ।। prahṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭavān nandaṃ putro jāto mameti vai ।। vārddhake api samutpannas tanayo yat tavādhunā ।। yadartham āgatās tasmān nātra stheyaṃ mahādhanāḥ ।।
bhavadbhir gamyatāṃ nanda tac chīghraṃ nijagokulam ।। sa rakṣaṇīyo bhavatā yathāyaṃ tanayo nijaḥ ।। śakaṭāropitair bhāṇḍaiḥ karaṃ dattvā mahābalāḥ ।। suptaṃ kṛṣṇam upādāya rātrau tasmai dadau stanam ।।
tasya tasya kṣaṇenāṅgaṃ bālakasyopahanyate ।। gṛhītvā prāṇasahitaṃ papau kopasamanvitaḥ ।। papāta pūtanā bhūmau mriyamāṇātibhīṣaṇā ।। dadṛśuḥ pūtanotsaṅge kṛṣṇaṃ tāṃ ca nipātitām ।।
gopucchaṃ bhrāmya hastena bāladoṣam apākarot ।। kṛṣṇasya pradadau rakṣāṃ kurvaṃś caitad udīrayan ।। yasya nābhisamudbhūtapaṅkajād abhavaj jagat ।। varāharūpadhṛg devaḥ sa tvāṃ rakṣatu keśavaḥ ।।
nṛsiṃharūpī sarvatra sa tvāṃ rakṣatu keśavaḥ ।। trivikramakramākrāntatrailokyaḥ sphuradāyudhaḥ ।। guhyaṃ sajaṭharaṃ viṣṇur jaṅghe pādau janārdanaḥ ।। rakṣatv avyāhataiśvaryas tava nārāyaṇo avyayaḥ ।।
gacchantu pretakūṣmāṇḍarākṣasā ye tavāhitāḥ ।। hṛṣīkeśo ambare bhūmau rakṣatu tvāṃ mahīdharaḥ ।। śāyitaḥ śakaṭasyādho bālaparyaṅkikātale ।। mṛtāyāḥ paramaṃ trāsaṃ vismayaṃ ca tadā yayuḥ ।।
cikṣepa caraṇāv ūrdhvaṃ stanyārthī praruroda ca ।। vidhvastakumbhabhāṇḍaṃ tad viparītaṃ papāta ca ।। ājagāmātha dadṛśe bālam uttānaśāyinam ।। tatraiva bālakāḥ procur bālenānena pātitam ।।
śakaṭaṃ parivṛttaṃ vai naitad anyasya ceṣṭitam ।। nandagopo api jagrāha bālam atyantavismitaḥ ।। śakaṭaṃ cārcayām āsa dadhipuṣpaphalākṣataiḥ ।। pracchanna eva gopānāṃ saṃskārān akarot tayoḥ ।।
gargo matimatāṃ śreṣṭho nāma kurvan mahāmatiḥ ।। ghṛṣṭajānukarau vipra babhūvatur ubhāv api ।। na nivārayituṃ sehe yaśodā na ca rohiṇī ।। tadaharjātagovatsapucchākarṣaṇatatparau ।।
śaśāka no vārayituṃ krīḍantāv aticañcalau ।। yaśodā yaṣṭim ādāya kopenānugatā ca tam ।। kṛṣṇaṃ kamalapatrākṣaṃ tarjayantī ruṣā tadā ।। bahir āvaraṇaṃ nāsti yasya yenedam āvṛtam ।।
taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ dāmnā baddhuṃ pracakrame ।। kṛṣṇam akliṣṭakarmāṇam āha cedam amarṣitā ।। ity uktvā ca nijaṃ karma sā cakāra kuṭumbinī ।। yamalārjunamadhyena jagāma kamalekṣaṇaḥ ।।
bhagnāv uttuṅgaśākhāgrau tena tau yamalārjunau ।। ājagāma vrajajano dadṛśe ca mahādrumau ।। tayor madhyagataṃ baddhaṃ dāmnā gāḍhaṃ tathodare ।। tataś ca dāmodaratāṃ sa yayau dāmabandhanāt ।।
mantrayām āsur udvignā mahotpātātibhīravaḥ ।। utpātā bahavo hy atra dṛśyante nāśahetavaḥ ।। vinā vātādidoṣeṇa drumayoḥ patanaṃ tathā ।। yāvad bhaumamahotpātadoṣo nābhibhaved vrajam ।।
ūcuḥ svaṃ svaṃ kulaṃ śīghraṃ gamyatāṃ mā vilambyatām ।। yūthaśo vatsapālāṃś ca kālayanto vrajaukasaḥ ।। kākabhāsasamākīrṇaṃ vrajasthānam abhūd dvija ।। śubhena manasā dhyātaṃ gavāṃ vṛddhim abhīpsatā ।।
prāvṛṭkāla ivodbhūtaṃ navaśaṣpaṃ samantataḥ ।। śakaṭīvāṭaparyantaś candrārdhākārasaṃsthitiḥ ।। ekasthānasthitau goṣṭhe ceratur bālalīlayā ।। gopaveṇukṛtātodyau patravādyakṛtasvanau ।।
hasantau ca ramantau ca ceratus tan mahāvanam ।। gopaputraiḥ samaṃ vatsāṃś cārayantau viceratuḥ ।। sarvasya jagataḥ pālau vatsapālau babhūvatuḥ ।। babhūva vāridhārābhir aikyaṃ kurvan diśām iva ।।
tadā mārakatevāsīt padmarāgavibhūṣitā ।। manāṃsi durvinītānāṃ prāpya lakṣmīṃ navām iva ।। sadvākyavādo mūrkhāṇāṃ pragalbhābhir ivoktibhiḥ ।। avāpyatāvivekasya nṛpasyeva parigrahe ।।
durvṛtte vṛttaceṣṭeva kulīnasyātiśobhanā ।। maitrīva pravare puṃsi durjanena prayojitā ।। arthāntaram anuprāptāḥ prajaḍānām ivoktayaḥ ।। kṛṣṇarāmau mudā yuktau gopālaiś ceratuḥ saha ।।
ceratuḥ kvacid atyarthaṃ śītavṛkṣatalāśrayau ।। vicitrau kvacid āsātāṃ vividhair giridhātubhiḥ ।। kvacid garjati jīmūte hāhākāraravādṛtau ।। mayūrakekānugatau gopaveṇupravādakau ।।
krīḍantau tau vane tasmiñ ceratus tuṣṭamānasau ।। vikāle ca samaṃ gobhir gopavṛndasamanvitau ।। b ājagmatuḥ kṛṣṇabalau gopaveṣadharāv ubhau ।। b vikāle ca yathājoṣaṃ vrajam etya mahābalau ।। d
gopaiḥ samānaiḥ sahitau krīḍantāv amarāv iva ।। evaṃ tāv ūṣatus tatra rāmakṛṣṇau mahādyutī ।। vicacāra vṛto gopair vanyapuṣpasragujjvalaḥ ।। tīrasaṃlagnaphenaughair hasantīm iva sarvataḥ ।।
hradaṃ kāliyanāgasya dadṛśe atīva bhīṣaṇam ।। vātāhatāmbuvikṣepasparśadagdhavihaṃgamam ।। vilokya cintayām āsa bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ ।। yo mayā nirjitas tyaktvā duṣṭo naṣṭaḥ payonidhim ।।
na narair godhanair vāpi tṛṣārtair upabhujyate ।। ciram atra sukhaṃ yena careyur vrajavāsinaḥ ।। yad eṣām utpathasthānāṃ kāryā śāntir durātmanām ।। adhiruhyotpatiṣyāmi hrade asminn anilāśinaḥ ।।
nipapāta hrade tatra sarparājasya vegitaḥ ।। atyarthaṃ dūrajātāṃs tu tān asiñcan mahīruhān ।। jajvaluḥ pādapāḥ sadyo jvālāvyāptadigantarāḥ ।। tacchabdaśravaṇāc cāśu nāgarājo abhyupāgamat ।।
vṛto mahāviṣaiś cānyair uragair anilāśibhiḥ ।। prakampitatanukṣepacalatkuṇḍalakāntayaḥ ।। dadaṃśuś cāpi te kṛṣṇaṃ viṣajvālāvilair mukhaiḥ ।। gopā vrajam upāgamya cukruśuḥ śokalālasāḥ ।।
bhakṣyate sarparājena tad āgacchata paśyata ।। gopyaś ca tvaritā jagmur yaśodāpramukhā hradam ।। yaśodayā samaṃ bhrānto drutaṃ praskhalitaṃ yayau ।। tvaritaṃ yamunāṃ jagmuḥ kṛṣṇadarśanalālasāḥ ।।
niṣprayatnakṛtaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sarpabhogena veṣṭitam ।। yaśodā ca mahābhāgā babhūva munisattama ।। procuś ca keśavaṃ prītyā bhayakātaryagadgadam ।। nāgarājasya no gantum asmākaṃ yujyate vraje ।।
vinā vṛṣeṇa kā gāvo vinā kṛṣṇena ko vrajaḥ ।। araṇyaṃ nātisevyaṃ ca vārihīnaṃ yathā saraḥ ।। yatra nendīvaradalaprakhyakāntir ayaṃ hariḥ ।। b kenāyaṃ mānuṣo jāto na ca mānuṣaceṣṭitaḥ ।। b
tenāpi martyavāsena ratir astīti vismayaḥ ।। d apaśyanto hariṃ dīnāḥ kathaṃ goṣṭhe bhaviṣyatha ।। na vinā puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ yāsyāmo nandagokulam ।। smitaśobhimukhaṃ gopyaḥ kṛṣṇasyāsmadvilokane ।।
gopāṃś ca trāsavidhurān vilokya stimitekṣaṇaḥ ।। mūrcchākulāṃ yaśodāṃ ca kṛṣṇamāhātmyasaṃjñayā ।। vyajyate atyantam ātmānaṃ kim anantaṃ na vetsi yat ।। kartāpahartā pātā ca trailokye tvaṃ trayīmayaḥ ।।
cintyase tvam acintyātman samastaiś caiva yogibhiḥ ।। avatīrṇo atra martyeṣu tavāṃśaś cāham agrajaḥ ।। viḍambayantas tvallīlāṃ sarva eva sadāsate ।। krīḍārtham ātmanaḥ paścād avatīrṇo asi śāśvata ।।
gopyaś ca sīdataḥ kasmāt tvaṃ bandhūn samupekṣase ।। tad ayaṃ damyatāṃ kṛṣṇa duṣṭātmā daśanāyudhaḥ ।। āsphoṭya mocayām āsa svadehaṃ bhogabandhanāt ।। āruhyābhugnaśirasi prananartoruvikramaḥ ।।
yatronnatiṃ ca kurute nanāmāsya tataḥ śiraḥ ।। daṇḍapātanipātena vavāma rudhiraṃ bahu ।। vilokya śaraṇaṃ jagmus tatpatnyo madhusūdanam ।। paraṃ jyotir acintyaṃ yat tadaṃśaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।
svarūpavarṇanaṃ tasya kathaṃ yoṣit kariṣyati ।। brahmāṇḍam alpakāṃśāṃśaḥ stoṣyāmas taṃ kathaṃ vayam ।। paramārtham aṇor alpaṃ sthūlāt sthūlaṃ natāḥ sma tam ।। sthitikartā na cānyo asti yasya tasmai namaḥ sadā ।।
kāraṇaṃ kāliyasyāsya damane śrūyatām ataḥ ।। yatas tato asya dīnasya kṣamyatāṃ kṣamatāṃ vara ।। tvatpādapīḍito jahyān muhūrtārdhena jīvitam ।। prītidveṣau samotkṛṣṭagocarau ca yato avyaya ।।
prāṇāṃs tyajati nāgo ayaṃ bhartṛbhikṣā pradīyatām ।। vedāntavedya deveśa duṣṭadaityanibarhaṇa ।। prasīda deva deveti prāha vākyaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ ।। nirastātiśayaṃ yasya tasya stoṣyāmi kiṃ nv aham ।।
parasmāt paramo yas tvaṃ tasya stoṣyāmi kiṃ nv aham ।। vasavaś ca sahādityais tasya stoṣyāmi kiṃ nv aham ।। kalpanāvayavāṃśasya taṃ stoṣyāmi kathaṃ tv aham ।। nāgapatnībhir evaṃ vai stūyamānasya kāliyaḥ ।।
stotreṇa praṇipatyocet kṛtvā karatalāñjalim ।। namas te nātha bhagavan pītavastrācyuteśvara ।। prasīda me jagannātha na jñātaṃ kiṃ mayā prabho ।। paramārthaṃ na jānanti tasya stoṣyāmi kiṃ nv aham ।।
nandanādisamudbhūtaiḥ so arcyate vā kathaṃ mayā ।। na vetti paramaṃ rūpaṃ so arcyate vā kathaṃ mayā ।। yam arcayanti dhyānena so arcyate vā kathaṃ mayā ।। bhāvapuṣpādibhir nāthaḥ so arcyate vā kathaṃ mayā ।।
sāmarthyavān kṛpāmātramanovṛttiḥ prasīda me ।। tatsvabhāvo ayam atrāsti nāparādho mamācyuta ।। jātirūpasvabhāvāś ca sṛjyante sṛjatā tvayā ।। svabhāvena ca saṃyuktas tathedaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ mayā ।।
nyāyyo daṇḍanipāto vai tavaiva vacanaṃ yathā ।। sa soḍho ayaṃ varaṃ daṇḍas tvatto nānyatra me varaḥ ।। jīvitaṃ dīyatām ekam ājñāpaya karomi kim ।। sabhṛtyaparivāras tvaṃ samudrasalilaṃ vraja ।।
garuḍaḥ pannagaripus tvayi na prahariṣyati ।। praṇamya so api kṛṣṇāya jagāma payasāṃ nidhim ।। samastabhāryāsahitaḥ parityajya svakaṃ hradam ।। gopā mūrdhani govindaṃ siṣicur netrajair jalaiḥ ।।
tuṣṭuvur muditā gopā dṛṣṭvā śivajalāṃ nadīm ।। gīyamānaḥ sa gopībhiś caritaiś cāruceṣṭitaḥ ।। b sahito baladevena nandena ca yaśodayā ।। b saṃstūyamāno gopaiś ca kṛṣṇo vrajam upāgamat ।। d
bhramamāṇau vane tasmin ramyaṃ tālavanaṃ gatau ।। nṛgomāṃsakṛtāhāraḥ sadādhyāste kharākṛtiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā spṛhānvitā gopāḥ phalādāne abruvan vacaḥ ।। bhūpradeśo yatas tasmāt pakvānīmāni santi vai ।।
vayam etāny abhīpsāmaḥ pātyantāṃ yadi rocate ।। kṛṣṇaś ca pātayām āsa bhuvi tālaphalāni vai ।। etat kathavyam ityuktvā pātayām āsa tāni vai ।। ājagāma sa duṣṭātmā kopād daiteyagardabhaḥ ।।
jaghānorasi tābhyāṃ ca sa ca tenāpy agṛhyata ।। tasminn eva sa cikṣepa vegena tṛṇarājani ।। pṛthivyāṃ pātayām āsa mahāvāto ambudān iva ।। kṛṣṇaś cikṣepa tālāgre balabhadraś ca līlayā ।।
daityagardabhadehaiś ca maitreya śuśubhe adhikam ।। navaśaṣpaṃ sukhaṃ cerur yan na bhuktam abhūt purā ।। balaḥ praviśya bāhubhyām tālān saṃparikampayan ।। phalāni pātayām āsa mataṅgaja ivaujasā ।।
phalānāṃ patatāṃ śabdaṃ niśamyāsurarāsabhaḥ ।। abhyadhāvat kṣititalaṃ sa nagaṃ parikampayan ।। sametya tarasā pratyag dvābhyāṃ padbhyāṃ balaṃ balī ।। nihatyorasi kā śabdaṃ muñcan paryacarat kharaḥ ।।
punar āsādya saṃrabdha upakroṣṭāparāsthitaḥ ।। caraṇāv aparau rājan balāya prākṣipad ruṣā ।। sa taṃ gṛhītvā pradadau bhrāmayitvaikapāṇinā ।। cikṣepa tṛṇarājāgre bhrāmaṇatyaktajīvitam ।।
tenāhato mahātālo vepamāno bṛhacchirāḥ ।। pārśvasthaṃ xxx bhagnaḥ sa cānyaṃ so api cāparam ।। bālasya līlayotsṛṣṭas kharadehahatāhatāḥ ।। tālāś cakampire sarve mahāvāteritā iva ।।
naitac citraṃ bhagavati hy anante jagadīśvare ।। otaprotam idaṃ tasmiṃs tantuṣv aṅgau yathā paṭaḥ ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ ca rāmaṃ ca jñātayo dhenukasya ye ।। kroṣṭāro vyadravan sarve saṃrabdhā hatabāndhavāḥ ।।
tāṃs tān āpatataḥ kṛṣṇo rāmaś ca nṛpalīlayā ।। gṛhītapaścāccaraṇān prāhiṇot tṛṇarājasu ।। tayos tu sumahat karma niśamya vibudhādayaḥ ।। mumucuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi cakrur vādyāni tuṣṭuvuḥ ।।
atha tālaphalāny ādan manuṣyā gatasādhvasāḥ ।। tṛṇaṃ ca paśavaś cerur hatadhenukakānane ।। kṛṣṇaḥ kamalapatrākṣaḥ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanaḥ ।। stūyamānānugair gopaiḥ sāgrajo vrajam āviśat ।।
sevyaṃ gogopagopīnāṃ ramyaṃ tālavanaṃ babhau ।। hatvā dhenukadaiteyaṃ bhāṇḍīravaṭam āgatau ।। cārayantau ca gā dūre vyāharantau ca nāmabhiḥ ।। śuśubhāte mahātmānau bālaśṛṅgāv ivarṣabhau ।।
mahendrāyudhasaṃyuktau śvetakṛṣṇāv ivāmbudau ।। samastalokanāthānāṃ nāthabhūtau bhuvaṃ gatau ।। tajjātiguṇayuktābhiḥ krīḍābhiś ceratur vanam ।। vyāyāmaṃ cakratus tatra kṣepaṇīyais tathāśmabhiḥ ।।
ājagāma pralambākhyo gopaveṣatirohitaḥ ।। mānuṣaṃ vapur āsthāya pralambo dānavottamaḥ ।। kṛṣṇaṃ tato rauhiṇeyaṃ hantuṃ cakre manoratham ।। prakurvanto hi te sarve dvau dvau yugapad utpatan ।।
gopālair aparaiś cānye gopālāḥ saha pupluvuḥ ।। nidāghakāle saṃprāpte atha bhāṇḍīrakasaṃjñake ।। paśūṃś cārayato gopais tadvane rāmakṛṣṇayoḥ ।। goparūpī pralambo agād asuraḥ tajjihīrṣayā ।।
taṃ vidvān api dāśārho bhagavān sarvadarśanaḥ ।। anvamodata tatsakhyaṃ vadhaṃ tasya vicintayan ।। tatropahūya gopālān kṛṣṇaḥ prāha vihāravit ।। he gopā vihariṣyāmo dvandvībhūya yathāyatham ।।
tatra cakruḥ parivṛḍho gopā rāmajanārdanau ।। kṛṣṇasaṃghaṭṭinaḥ kecid āsan rāmasya cāpare ।। ācerur vividhāḥ krīḍā vāhyavāhakalakṣaṇāḥ ।। tatrāruhyanti jetāro vahanti ca parājitāḥ ।।
vahanto vāhayantaś ca cārayantaś ca godhanam ।। bhāṇḍirakaṃ nāma vaṭaṃ jagmuḥ kṛṣṇapurogamāḥ ।। rāmasaṃghaṭṭino ye hi śrīdāmavṛṣabhādayaḥ ।। krīḍāyāṃ jayinas tāṃs tān ūhuḥ kṛṣṇādayas tathā ।।
uvāha kṛṣṇaṃ bhagavān śrīdāmānaṃ parājitāḥ ।। ṛṣabhaṃ bhadrasenas tu pralambo rohiṇīsutam ।। jitavān kṛṣṇapakṣīyair gopair anye parājitāḥ ।। punar nivavṛtuḥ sarve ye ye tatra parājitāḥ ।।
na tasthau prajagāmaiva sacandra iva vāridaḥ ।। vavṛdhe sumahākāyaḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ ।। sragdāmalambābharaṇaṃ mukuṭāṭopimastakam ।। raudraṃ śakaṭacakrākṣaṃ pādanyāsacalatkṣitim ।। b
abhītamanasā tena rakṣasā rohiṇīsutaḥ ।। b hriyamāṇas tataḥ kṛṣṇam idaṃ vacanam abravīt ।। d kenāpi paśya daityena gopālachadmarūpiṇā ।। tat kathyatāṃ prayāty eṣa durātmātitvarānvitaḥ ।।
mahātmā rauhiṇeyasya balavīryapramāṇavit ।। sarvātman sarvaguhyānāṃ guhyaguhyātmanā tvayā ।। ātmānam ekaṃ tadvac ca jagaty ekārṇave ca yat ।। bhārāvatāraṇārthāya martyalokam upāgatau ।।
somo manas te śvasitaṃ samīro diśaś catasro avyaya bāhavas te ।। sahasrapadmodbhavayonir ādyaḥ sahasraśas tvāṃ munayo gṛṇanti ।। tavārcyate vetsi na kiṃ yad ante tvayy eva viśvaṃ layam abhyupaiti ।। kṛtādibhedair aja kālarūpo nimeṣapūrvo jagad etad atsi ।।
himācale bhānumato aṃśusaṅgāj jalatvam abhyeti punas tad eva ।। tathaiva sargāya samudyatasya jagattvam abhyety anukalpam īśa ।। jagato asya jagaty arthe bhedenāvāṃ vyavasthitau ।। mānuṣyam evāvalambya bandhūnāṃ kriyatāṃ hitam ।।
vihasya pīḍayām āsa pralambaṃ balavān balaḥ ।। tena cāsya prahāreṇa bahir yāte vilocane ।। nipapāta mahīpṛṣṭhe daityavaryo mamāra ca ।। prahṛṣṭās tuṣṭuvur gopāḥ sādhu sādhv iti cābruvan ।।
pralambe saha kṛṣṇena punar gokulam āyayau ।। prāvṛḍ vyatītā vikasatsarojā cābhavac charat ।। putrakṣetrādisaktena mamatvena yathā gṛhī ।। asāratāṃ parijñāya saṃsārasyeva yoginaḥ ।।
tatyajuś cāmbaraṃ meghā gṛhaṃ vijñānino yathā ।। bahvālambimamatvena hṛdayānīva dehinām ।। avabodhair manāṃsīva saṃbandham amalātmanām ।। candraś caramadehātmā yogī sādhukule yathā ।।
mamatvaṃ kṣetraputrādirūḍham uccair yathā budhāḥ ।। kleśaiḥ kuyogino aśeṣair antarāyahatā iva ।। kramāvāptamahāyogo niścalātmā yathā yatiḥ ।। jñāte sarvagate viṣṇau manāṃsīva sumedhasām ।।
yogāgnidagdhakleśaughaṃ yoginām iva mānasam ।। ahaṃkārodbhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ vivekaḥ sumahān iva ।। indriyāṇīndriyārthebhyaḥ pratyāhāra ivāharat ।। abhyasyate anudivasaṃ recakākumbhakādibhiḥ ।।
dadarśendramahārambhāy dyatāṃs tān vrajaukasaḥ ।। kautūhalād idaṃ vākyaṃ prāha vṛddhān mahāmatiḥ ।। prāha taṃ nandagopaś ca pṛcchantam atisādaram ।। tena saṃcoditā meghā varṣanty ambumayaṃ rasam ।।
vartayāmopabhuñjānās tarpayāmaś ca devatāḥ ।। tena saṃvardhitaiḥ sasyais tuṣṭāḥ puṣṭā bhavanti vai ।। dṛśyate yatra dṛśyante vṛṣṭimanto balāhakāḥ ।। parjanyaḥ sarvalokasya bhavāya bhuvi varṣati ।।
mahaiḥ sureśam arcanti vayam anye ca mānavāḥ ।। kopāya tridaśendrasya prāha dāmodaras tadā ।। gāvo asmaddaivataṃ tāta vayaṃ vanacarā yataḥ ।। ānvīkṣikyātmavijñānaṃ dharmādharmaṃ trayīsthitam ।।
arthānarthaunuvārtāyāṃ daṇḍanītyāṃ jayājayau ।। vidyācatuṣṭayaṃ caitad vārtām atra śṛṇuṣva me ।। vidyā hy ekā mahābhāga vārtā vṛttitrayāśrayā ।। asmākaṃ gauḥ parā vṛttir vārtābhedair iyaṃ tribhiḥ ।।
saiva pūjyārcanīyā ca saiva tasyopakārikā ।। iha ca pretya caivāsau tāta nāpnoti śobhanam ।। vanāntā girayaḥ sarve te cāsmākaṃ parā gatiḥ ।। sukhinas tv akhile loke yathā vai cakracāriṇaḥ ।।
tat tad rūpaṃ samāsthāya ramante sveṣu sānuṣu ।। tadā siṃhādirūpais tān ghātayanti mahīdharāḥ ।। kim asmākaṃ mahendreṇa gāvaḥ śailāś ca devatāḥ ।। girigoyajñaśīlāś ca vayam adrivanāśrayāḥ ।।
arcyatāṃ pūjyatāṃ medhyaṃ paśuṃ hatvā vidhānataḥ ।। bhojyantāṃ tena vai viprās tathā ye cābhivāñchakāḥ ।। śaratpuṣpakṛtāpīḍāḥ parigacchantu gogaṇāḥ ।। tataḥ kṛtā bhavet prītir gavām adres tathā mama ।।
prītyutphullamukhā vipra sādhu sādhv ity athābruvan ।। tat kariṣyāmahe sarvaṃ giriyajñaḥ pravartyatām ।। dadhipāyasamāṃsādyair daduḥ śailabaliṃ tataḥ ।। dvijāṃś ca bhojayām āsuḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।।
anyān apy āgatān itthaṃ kṛṣṇenoktaṃ yathā purā ।। ṛṣabhāś cāpi nardantaḥ satoyā jaladā iva ।। bubhuje annaṃ bahu tadā gopavaryāhṛtaṃ dvija ।। adhiruhyārcayām āsa dvitīyām ātmanas tanum ।।
kṛtvā girimahaṃ goṣṭhaṃ nijam abhyāyayuḥ punaḥ ।। saṃvartakaṃ nāma gaṇaṃ toyadānām athābravīt ।। ājñānantaram evāśu kriyatām avicāritam ।। kṛṣṇāśrayabalādhmāto mahabhaṅgam acīkarat ।।
tā gāvo vṛṣṭipātena pīḍyantāṃ vacanān mama ।। sāhāyyaṃ vaḥ kariṣyāmi vāyvambūtsargayojitam ।। vātavarṣaṃ mahābhīmam abhāvāya gavāṃ dvija ।। ekaṃ dhārāmahāsārapūraṇenābhavan mune ।।
nādāpūritadikcakrair dhārāsāram apātyata ।। adhaś cordhvaṃ ca tiryak ca jagad āpyam ivābhavat ।। dhūtāḥ prāṇāñ jahuḥ sannatrikasakthiśirodharāḥ ।। gāvo vivatsāś ca kṛtā vāripūreṇa cāparāḥ ।।
trāhi trāhīty alpaśabdāḥ kṛṣṇam ūcur ivārtakāḥ ।। atīvārtaṃ harir dṛṣṭvā maitreyācintayat tadā ।। tad etad akhilaṃ goṣṭhaṃ trātavyam adhunā mayā ।। dhārayiṣyāmi goṣṭhasya pṛthucchatram ivopari ।।
utpāṭyaikakareṇaiva dhārayām āsa līlayā ।। viśadhvam atra sahitāḥ kṛtaṃ varṣanivāraṇam ।। praviśyatāṃ na bhetavyaṃ giripātasya nirbhayaiḥ ।। śakaṭāropitair bhāṇḍair gopyaś cāsārapīḍitāḥ ।।
vrajaukovāsibhir harṣavismitākṣair nirīkṣitaḥ ।। saṃstūyamānacaritaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ śailam adhārayat ।। indreṇa coditā vipra gopānāṃ nāśakāriṇaḥ ।। mithyāpratijño balabhid vārayām āsa tān ghanān ।।
niṣkramya gokulaṃ hṛṣṭaṃ svasthānaṃ punar āgamat ।। svasthāne vismitamukhair dṛṣṭas tais tu vrajaukasaiḥ ।। rocayām āsa kṛṣṇasya darśanaṃ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। govardhanagirau kṛṣṇaṃ dadarśa tridaśeśvaraḥ ।।
kṛtsnasya jagato gopaṃ vṛtaṃ gopakumārakaiḥ ।। kṛtacchāyaṃ harer mūrdhni pakṣābhyāṃ pakṣipuṃgavam ।। śakraḥ sasmitam āhedaṃ prītivistāritekṣaṇaḥ ।। tvatsamīpaṃ mahābhāga naitac cintyaṃ tvayānyathā ।।
avatīrṇo akhilādhāra tvam eva parameśvaraḥ ।। samādiṣṭā mahāmeghās taiś caitat kadanaṃ kṛtam ।। tenāhaṃ toṣito vīra karmaṇātyadbhutena te ।। tvayāyam adripravaraḥ kareṇaikena yad dhṛtaḥ ।।
tvayā trātābhir atyarthaṃ yuṣmatsatkārakāraṇāt ।। upendratve gavām indro govindas tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। abhiṣekaṃ tayā cakre pavitrajalapūrṇayā ।। prasnavodbhūtadugdhārdrāṃ sadyaś cakrur vasuṃdharām ।।
prītyā sapraśrayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ punar āha śacīpatiḥ ।। yad bravīmi mahābhāga bhārāvataraṇecchayā ।। avatīrṇo arjuno nāma sa rakṣyo bhavatā sadā ।। sa rakṣaṇīyo bhavatā yathātmā madhusūdana ।।
tam ahaṃ pālayiṣyāmi yāvat sthāsyāmi bhūtale ।। na tāvad arjunaṃ kaścid devendra yudhi jeṣyati ।। keśī kuvalayāpīḍo narakādyās tathāpare ।। tatra viddhi sahasrākṣa bhārāvataraṇaṃ kṛtam ।।
nārjunasya ripuḥ kaścin mamāgre prabhaviṣyati ।। nivṛtte bhārate yuddhe kuntyai dāsyāmy avikṣatān ।। āruhyairāvataṃ nāgaṃ punar eva divaṃ yayau ।। ājagāmātha gopīnāṃ dṛṣṭipūtena vartmanā ।।
ūcuḥ prītyā dhṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tena govardhanācalam ।। gāvaś ca bhavatā trātā giridhāraṇakarmaṇā ।। divyaṃ ca karma bhavataḥ kim etat tāta kathyatām ।। dhṛto govardhanaś cāyaṃ śaṅkitāni manāṃsi naḥ ।।
yathā tvadvīryam ālokya na tvāṃ manyāmahe naram ।। karma cedam aśakyaṃ yat samastais tridaśair api ।। cintyamānam ameyātmañ śaṅkāṃ kṛṣṇa prayacchati ।। kiṃ vāsmākaṃ vicāreṇa bāndhavo asi namo astu te ।।
prāyeṇa tvaṃ mahābāho harir vā rudra eva vā ।। brahmā sendro yamo vāpi varuṇo vā kuberakaḥ ।। anyo vā sarvadevānāṃ nātha x ta bhuvo bhavaḥ ।। namo astu te devadeva yad asmākaṃ hitaṃ tathā ।।
ity evam uktas tair gopaiḥ kṛṣṇo apy āha mahāmune ।। ślāghyo vāhaṃ tataḥ kiṃ vo vicāreṇa prayojanam ।। tadātmabandhusadṛśī buddhir vaḥ kriyatāṃ mayi ।। ahaṃ vo bāndhavo jāto naitac cintyam ato anyathā ।।
yayur gopā mahābhāga tasmin praṇayakopini ।। tathā kumudinīṃ phullām āmoditadigantarām ।। vilokya saha gopībhir manaś cakre ratiṃ prati ।। jagau kalapadaṃ śaurir nānātantrīkṛtavratam ।।
ājagmus tvaritā gopyo yatrāste madhusūdanaḥ ।। dattāvadhānā kācic ca tam eva manasāsmarat ।। yayau ca kācit premāndhā tatpārśvam avilajjitā ।। tanmayatvena govindaṃ dadhyau mīlitalocanā ।।
tadaprāptimahāduḥkhavilīnāśeṣapātakā ।। nirucchvāsatayā muktiṃ gatānyā gopakanyakā ।। mānayām āsa govindo rāsārambharasotsukaḥ ।। anyadeśaṃ gate kṛṣṇe cerur vṛndāvanāntaram ।।
kṛṣṇe nibaddhahṛdayā idam ūcuḥ parasparam ।। anyā bravīti kṛṣṇasya mama gītir niśamyatām ।। nihatā pūtanā tadvac śakaṭaṃ parivartitam ।। sakhyaḥ paśyata kṛṣṇasya mama vikramam adbhutam ।।
bāhum āsphoṭya kṛṣṇasya līlāsarvasvam ādade ।। alaṃ vṛṣṭibhayenātra dhṛto govardhano mayā ।। anyā bravīti ca sakhī paśya tvaṃ mām akalmaṣam ।। nānāprakārayā kṛṣṇaṃ śobhitaṃ vanamālayā ।।
gopī bravīti caivānyā kṛṣṇalīlānukāriṇī ।। gopyo vyagrāḥ samaṃ cerū ramyaṃ vṛndāvanaṃ vanam ।। prapannānāṃ tatas tāsāṃ kṛṣṇamārgānusārataḥ ।। prāvartata samullāpaḥ kṛṣṇasyānveṣaṇaṃ prati ।।
pulakāñcitasarvāṅgī vikāsinayanotpalā ।। padāny etāni kṛṣṇasya līlālaṃkṛtagāminaḥ ।। padāni tasyāś caitāni ghanāny alpatanūni ca ।। yenāgrākrāntimātrāṇi padāny atra mahātmanaḥ ।।
anyajanmani sarvātmā viṣṇur abhyarcito yayā ।। nandagopasuto yāto mārgeṇānena paśyata ।। yā gantavye drutaṃ yāti nimnapādāgrasaṃsthitiḥ ।। anāyattapadanyāsā lakṣyate padapaddhatiḥ ।।
nairāśyān mandagāminyā nivṛttaṃ lakṣyate padam ।। tena kṛṣṇena yenaiṣā tvaritā padapaddhatiḥ ।। nivartadhvaṃ śaśāṅkasya naitad dīdhitigocare ।। yamunātīram āgamya jagus taccaritaṃ tadā ।।
gopyas trailokyagoptāraṃ kṛṣṇam akliṣṭaceṣṭitam ।। kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti prāha nānyad udīrayat ।। kācin mīlitalolākṣī tadbhāgavatamānasā ।। sarvātmānaṃ tam abhajad govindaṃ viṣṇum avyayam ।।
vilokya netrabhṛṅgābhyāṃ papau tanmukhapaṅkajam ।। tasyaiva rūpaṃ dhyāyantī yogārūḍheva cābabhau ।। ninye anunayam anyāś ca karasparśena mādhavaḥ ।। rarāma rāsagoṣṭhībhir udāracarito hariḥ ।।
gopījanena naivābhūd ekasthānasthirātmanā ।। cakāra tatkarasparśanimīlitadṛśaṃ hariḥ ।। anuyātaśaratkāvyageyagītir anukramāt ।। jagau gopījanas tv ekaṃ kṛṣṇanāma punaḥ punaḥ ।।
dadau bāhulatāṃ skandhe gopī madhunighātinaḥ ।। gopī gītastutivyājanipuṇā madhusūdanam ।। pulakodgamasasyāya svedāmbughanatāṃ gatau ।। sādhu kṛṣṇeti kṛṣṇeti tāvat tā dviguṇaṃ jaguḥ ।।
pratilomānulomena bhejur gopāṅganā harim ।। yathābdakoṭipratimaḥ kṣaṇas tena vinābhavat ।। kṛṣṇaṃ gopāṅganā rātrau ramayanti ratipriyāḥ ।। reme tābhir ameyātmā kṣapāsu kṣapitāhitaḥ ।।
ātmasvarūparūpo asau vyāpya vāyur iva sthitaḥ ।। vāyuś cātmā tathaivāsau vyāpya sarvam avasthitaḥ ।। trāsayan samado goṣṭham ariṣṭaḥ samupāgataḥ ।। khurāgrapātair atyarthaṃ dārayan vasudhātalam ।।
saṃrambhāviddhalāṅgūlaḥ kaṭhinaskandhabandhanaḥ ।। viṇmūtraliptapṛṣṭhāṅgo gavām udvegakārakaḥ ।। pātayan sa gavāṃ garbhān daityo vṛṣabharūpadhṛk ।। sūdayaṃs tāpasān ugro vanāny aṭati yaḥ sadā ।।
gopā gopastriyaś caiva kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti cukruśuḥ ।। tacchabdaśravaṇāc cāsau dāmodaramukhaṃ yayau ।। abhyadhāvata duṣṭātmā kṛṣṇaṃ vṛṣabhadānavaḥ ।। na cacāla tataḥ sthānād avajñāsmitalīlayā ।।
jaghāna jānunā kukṣau viṣāṇagrahaṇācalam ।। apīḍayad ariṣṭasya kaṇṭhaṃ klinnam ivāmbaram ।। mamāra sahasā daityo mukhāc choṇitam udvaman ।। jambhe hate sahasrākṣaṃ purā devagaṇā yathā ।।
pralambe nidhanaṃ nīte dhṛte govardhanācale ।। hatāyāṃ pūtanāyāṃ ca śakaṭe parivartite ।। yaśodādevakīgarbhaparivartādy aśeṣataḥ ।। vasudevaṃ prati tadā kopaṃ cakre sudurmatiḥ ।।
jagarha yādavāṃś caiva kāryaṃ caitad acintayat ।। tāvad eva mayā vadhyāv asādhyau rūḍhayauvanau ।। etābhyāṃ mallayuddhena ghātayiṣyāmi durmadau ।। tathā tathā yatiṣyāmi yāsyete saṃkṣayaṃ yathā ।।
tayor ānayanārthāya preṣayiṣyāmi gokulam ।। tatraivāsāv atibalas tāv ubhau ghātayiṣyati ।। ghātayiṣyati vā gopau vasudevasutāv ubhau ।। hantuṃ kṛtamatir vīram akrūraṃ vākyam abravīt ।।
itaḥ syandanam āruhya gamyatāṃ nandagokulam ।। nāśāya kila saṃbhūtau mama duṣṭau pravardhataḥ ।। āneyau bhavatā gatvā mallayuddhāya tāv ubhau ।। tābhyāṃ sahānayor yuddhaṃ sarvaloko atra paśyatu ।।
sa vā haniṣyate pāpau vasudevātmajau śiśū ।। haniṣye pitaraṃ cemam ugrasenaṃ ca durmatim ।। vittaṃ cāpahariṣyāmi duṣṭānāṃ madvadhaiṣiṇām ।। eteṣāṃ ca vadhāyāhaṃ yatiṣye anukramāt tataḥ ।।
praśāsiṣye tvayā tasmān matprītyā vīra gamyatām ।। gopāḥ samānayanty āśu tvayā vācyās tathā tathā ।। prītimān abhavat kṛṣṇaṃ śvo drakṣyāmīti satvaraḥ ।। niścakrāma tadā puryā mathurāyā madhupriyaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇasya nidhanākāṅkṣī vṛndāvanam upāgamat ।। plutavikrāntacandrārkamārgo gopān upādravat ।। gopyaś ca bhayasaṃvignā govindaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। satoyajaladadhvānagambhīram idam uktavān ।।
bhavadbhir gopajātīyair vīravīryaṃ vilopyate ।। daiteyabalavāhyena valgatā duṣṭavājinā ।। pātayiṣyāmi daśanān vadanād akhilāṃs tava ।। vivṛtāsyas tu so apy enaṃ daiteyāśva upādravat ।।
praveśayām āsa tadā keśino duṣṭavājinaḥ ।। śātitā daśanāḥ petuḥ sitābhrāvayavā iva ।। vināśāya yathā vyādhir āsaṃbhūter upekṣitaḥ ।। vipāṭitauṣṭho bahulaṃ saphenaṃ rudhiraṃ vaman ।। b
cukrośa balavān daityaḥ sāsradeho vicetanaḥ ।। b so akṣiṇī vivṛte cakre niḥsṛte muktabandhane ।। d svedārdragātraḥ śrāntaś ca niryatnaḥ so abhavat tataḥ ।। nipapāta dvidhābhūto vaidyutena yathā drumaḥ ।।
keśinas te dvidhābhūte śakale dve virejatuḥ ।। anāyastatanuḥ svastho hasaṃs tatraiva tasthivān ।। tuṣṭuvuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣam anurāgamanoramam ।। keśinaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā harṣanirbharamānasaḥ ।।
nihato ayaṃ tvayā keśī kleśadas tridivaukasām ।। avṛttapūrvam anyatra draṣṭuṃ svargād upāgataḥ ।। yāni tair vismitaṃ cetas toṣam etena me gatam ।। dhūtakesarajālasya hreṣato abhrāvalokinaḥ ।।
tasmāt keśavanāmnā tvaṃ loke khyāto bhaviṣyasi ।। paraśvo ahaṃ sameṣyāmi tvayā keśiniṣūdana ।। bhārāvatārakartā tvaṃ pṛthivyāḥ pṛthivīdhara ।। draṣṭavyāni mayā yuṣmatpraṇītāni janārdana ।।
tvayā sabhājitaś cāhaṃ svasti te astu vrajāmy aham ।। viveśa gokulaṃ gopīnetrapānaikabhājanam ।। kṛṣṇasaṃdarśanākāṅkṣī prayayau nandagokulam ।। yo aham aṃśāvatīrṇasya mukhaṃ drakṣyāmi cakriṇaḥ ।।
yad unnidrābjapatrākṣaṃ viṣṇor drakṣyāmy ahaṃ mukham ।। adya me saphale netre adya me saphalā giraḥ ।। yan me parasparālāpo dṛṣṭvā viṣṇuṃ bhaviṣyati ।। tat puṇḍarīkanayanaṃ viṣṇor drakṣyāmy ahaṃ mukham ।।
drakṣyāmi tat paraṃ dhāma devānāṃ bhagavanmukham ।। ijyate yo akhilādhāras taṃ drakṣyāmi jagatpatim ।। avāpa tam anantādim ahaṃ drakṣyāmi keśavam ।। yasya svarūpaṃ jānanti sprakṣyaty aṅgaṃ sa me hariḥ ।।
yo vitatyāvyayo vyāpī sa vakṣyati mayā saha ।। cakāra jagato yo ajaḥ so adya mām ālapiṣyati ।। kartuṃ manuṣyatāṃ prāptaḥ svecchādehadhṛg avyayaḥ ।। so avatīrṇo jagatyarthe mām akrūreti vakṣyati ।।
yanmāyāṃ nālam uttartuṃ jagat tasmai namo namaḥ ।। yogī māyām ameyāya tasmai vidyātmane namaḥ ।। vedāntavedibhir viṣṇuḥ procyate yo nato asmi tam ।। sadasat tena satyena mayy asau yātu saumyatām ।।
puruṣas tam ajaṃ nityaṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ harim ।। akrūro gokulaṃ prāptaḥ kiṃcit sūrye virājati ।। vatsamadhyagataṃ phullanīlotpaladalacchavim ।। pralambabāhum āyāmituṅgoraḥsthalam unnasam ।।
tuṅgaraktanakhaṃ padbhyāṃ dharaṇyāṃ supratiṣṭhitam ।। sāndranīlalatāhastam sitāmbhojāvataṃsakam ।। tasyānu balabhadraṃ ca dadarśa yadunandanaḥ ।। meghamālāparivṛtaṃ kailāsādrim ivāparam ।।
pulakāñcitasarvāṅgas tadākrūro abhavan mune ।। bhagavadvāsudevāṃśo dvidhā yo ayam avasthitaḥ ।। apy aṅgam etad bhagavatprasādād datte aṅgasaṅge phalavan mama syāt ।। yasyāṅgulisparśahatākhilāghair avāpyate siddhir anāśadoṣā ।।
cakraṃ ghnatā daityapater hṛtāni daityāṅganānāṃ nayanāñjanāni ।। tathāmaratvaṃ tridaśādhipatyaṃ manvantaraṃ pūrṇam apetaśatruḥ ।। kartāvamānopahataṃ dhig astu taj janmanaḥ sādhu bahiṣkṛto yaḥ ।। kiṃ vā jagaty atra samastapuṃsām ajñātam asyāsti hṛdi sthitasya ।।
aṃśāvatāraṃ puruṣottamasya anādimadhyāntamayasya viṣṇoḥ ।। akrūro asmīti caraṇau nanāma śirasā hareḥ ।। saṃspṛśyākṛṣya ca prītyā sugāḍhaṃ pariṣasvaje ।। tataḥ praviṣṭau saṃhṛṣṭau tam ādāyātmamandiram ।।
bhuktabhojyo yathānyāyam ācacakṣe tatas tayoḥ ।। yathā ca devakī devī dānavena durātmanā ।। yaṃ caivārthaṃ samuddiśya sa kaṃsena visarjitaḥ ।। uvācākhilam apy etaj jñātaṃ dānapate mayā ।।
vicintyaṃ nānyathaitat te viddhi kaṃsaṃ hataṃ mayā ।। gopavṛddhāś ca yāsyanti hy ādāyopāyanaṃ bahu ।। trirātrābhyantare kaṃsaṃ haniṣyāmi sahānugam ।। suṣvāpa balabhadraś ca nandagopagṛhe tataḥ ।।
akrūreṇa samaṃ gantum udyatau mathurāṃ prati ।। niśaśvāsātiduḥkhārtaḥ prāha cedaṃ parasparam ।। nāgarastrīkalālāpamadhu śrotreṇa pāsyati ।। cittam asya kathaṃ bhūyo grāmyagopīṣu yāsyati ।।
prahṛtaṃ gopayoṣitsu nirghṛṇena durātmanā ।। nāgarīṇām atīvaitat kaṭākṣekṣitam eva ca ।। bhavatīnāṃ punaḥ pārśvaṃ kayā yuktyā sameṣyati ।। krūreṇākrūrakeṇātra nirāśena pratāritaḥ ।।
yenemam akṣṇor āhlādaṃ nayaty anyatra no harim ।। ratham āruhya govindas tvaryatām asya vāraṇe ।। guravaḥ kiṃ kariṣyanti dagdhānāṃ virahāgninā ।। nodyamaṃ kurute kaścid govindavinivartane ।।
pāsyanty acyutavaktrābjaṃ yāsāṃ netrālipaṅktayaḥ ।। udvahiṣyanti paśyantaḥ svadehaṃ pulakāñcitam ।। govindāvayavair dṛṣṭair atīvādya bhaviṣyati ।। vistārikāntinayanā yā drakṣyanty anivāritam ।।
uddhṛtāny atra netrāṇi vidhātrākaruṇātmanā ।। dhanyās te pathi ye kṛṣṇaṃ yāntaṃ saumyavapur harim ।। kautukenānimeṣākṣāḥ paśyanti hy anivāritam ।। śaithilyam upayānty āśu kareṣu valayāny api ।।
evam ārtāsu yoṣitsu ghṛṇā kasya na jāyate ।। akrūra tvaṃ mahābāho vada vācātisaumyayā ।। asya gopījanasyārtiṃ kimarthaṃ kartum arhasi ।। kīdṛgvidhā kṛtāsmābhir nikṛtis te janeśvara ।।
vidhātur vā mahābāho tasya kṛṣṇasya vā hareḥ ।। balabhadro vārayituṃ necchate dhruvam apy ayam ।। evam ārtāsu yoṣitsu pralapantīṣv itas tataḥ ।। ratham āsthāya gacchantam idam ūcur varāṅganāḥ ।।
dūrībhūto harir yena so api reṇur na lakṣyate ।। tatyāja vrajabhūbhāgaṃ saha rāmeṇa keśavaḥ ।। prāptā madhyāhnasamaye rāmākrūrajanārdanāḥ ।। yāvat karomi kālindyām āhnikārhaṇam ambhasi ।।
dadhyau brahma paraṃ vipra praviśya yamunājale ।। kundāmalāṅgam unnidrapadmapatrāruṇekṣaṇam ।। saṃstūyamānaṃ gandharvair vanamālāvibhūṣitam ।। cārukuṇḍalinaṃ mattam antar jalatale sthitam ।।
caturbāhum udārāṅgaṃ cakrādyāyudhabhūṣaṇam ।। śakracāpataḍinmālāvicitram iva toyadam ।। dadarśa kṛṣṇam akliṣṭaṃ puṇḍarīkāvataṃsakam ।। vicintyamānaṃ tatrasthair nāsāgranyastalocanaiḥ ।।
so acintayad rathāc chīghraṃ katham atrāgatāv iti ।। tato niṣkramya salilād ratham abhyāgataḥ punaḥ ।। rāmakṛṣṇau yathāpūrvaṃ manuṣyavapuṣānvitau ।। saṃstūyamānau gandharvamunisiddhamahoragaiḥ ।।
tuṣṭāva sarvavijñāna, ,mayam acyutam īśvaram ।। vyāpine naikarūpaikasvarūpāya namo namaḥ ।। namo avijñeyarūpāya parāya prakṛteḥ prabho ।। ātmā ca paramātmā ca tvam ekaḥ pañcadhā sthitaḥ ।।
brahmaviṣṇuśivākhyābhiḥ kalpanābhir udīritaḥ ।। anākhyeyābhidhānaṃ tvāṃ nato asmi parameśvara ।। tad brahma paramaṃ nityam avikāri bhavān aja ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇācyutānantaviṣṇusaṃjñābhir īḍyase ।।
viśvātmaṃs tvam iti vikārabhāvahīnaḥ sarvasmin na hi bhavato asti kiṃcid anyat ।। toyeśo dhanapatir antakas tvam eko bhinnārthair jagad abhipāsi śaktibhedaiḥ ।। rūpaṃ paraṃ sad iti vācakam akṣaraṃ yaj jñānātmane sadasate praṇato asmi tasmai ।। pradyumnāya namas tubhyam aniruddhāya te namaḥ ।।
arcayām āsa sarveśaṃ puṣpadhūpair manomayaiḥ ।। brahmabhūte ciraṃ sthitvā virarāma samādhitaḥ ।। ājagāma rathaṃ bhūyo nirgamya yamunāmbhasaḥ ।। vismitākṣas tadākrūras taṃ ca kṛṣṇo abhyabhāṣata ।।
vismayotphullanayano bhavān saṃlakṣyate yataḥ ।। tad atrāpi hi paśyāmi mūrtimat purataḥ sthitam ।। tenāścaryapareṇāhaṃ bhavatā kṛṣṇa saṃgataḥ ।। bibhemi kaṃsād dhig janma parapiṇḍopajīvinām ।।
saṃprāptaś cātisāyāhne so akrūro mathurāṃ purīm ।। padbhyāṃ yātaṃ mahāvīryau rathenaiko viśāmy aham ।। yuvayor hi kṛte vṛddhaḥ sa kaṃsena nirasyate ।। praviṣṭau rāmakṛṣṇau ca rājamārgam upāgatau ।।
jagmatur līlayā vīrau mattau bālagajāv iva ।। ayācetāṃ surūpāṇi vāsāṃsi rucirānanau ।। bahūny ākṣepavākyāni prāhoccai rāmakeśavau ।। pātayām āsa kopena rajakasya śiro bhuvi ।।
kṛṣṇarāmau mudā yuktau mālākāragṛhaṃ gatau ।। etau kasya kuto vaitau maitreyācintayat tataḥ ।। sa tarkayām āsa tadā bhuvaṃ devāv upāgatau ।। bhuvaṃ viṣṭabhya hastābhyāṃ pasparśa śirasā mahīm ।।
dhanyo aham arcayiṣyāmīty āha tau mālyajīvakaḥ ।। cārūṇy etāny athaitāni pradadau sa vilobhayan ।। dadau puṣpāṇi cārūṇi gandhavanty amalāni ca ।। śrīs tvāṃ matsaṃśrayā bhadra na kadācit tyajiṣyati ।।
yāvad dināni tāvac ca na naśiṣyati saṃtatiḥ ।। mamānusmaraṇaṃ prāpya divyaṃ lokam avāpsyasi ।। yuṣmatsaṃtatijātānāṃ dīrgham āyur bhaviṣyati ।। saṃprāpsyati mahābhāga yāvat sūryo bhaviṣyati ।।
nirjagāma muniśreṣṭha mālākāreṇa pūjitaḥ ।। dadarśa kubjām āyāntīṃ navayauvanagocarām ।। bhavatyā nīyate satyaṃ vadendīvaralocane ।। prāha sā lalitaṃ kubjā taddarśanabalātkṛtā ।।
naikavakreti vikhyātām anulepanakarmaṇi ।। bhavaty aham atīvāsya prasādadhanabhājanam ।। āvayor gātrasadṛśaṃ dīyatām anulepanam ।। anulepanaṃ ca dadau gātrayogyam athobhayoḥ ।।
sendracāpau virājetāṃ sitakṛṣṇāv ivāmbudau ।। utpāṭya tolayām āsa dvyaṅgulenāgrapāṇinā ।। tataḥ sā ṛjutāṃ prāptā yoṣitām abhavad varā ।। vastre pragṛhya govindaṃ vraja gehaṃ mameti vai ।।
evam uktas tayā śaurī rāmasyālokya cānanam ।। prahasya kubjāṃ tām āha naikavakrām aninditām ।। ity uktavantīm ālokya prahasan harir abravīt ।। visasarja jahāsoccai rāmasyālokya cānanam ।।
dhanuḥśālāṃ tato yātau citramālyopaśobhitau ।। ākhyāte sahasā kṛṣṇo gṛhītvāpūrayad dhanuḥ ।। cakāra sumahāśabdaṃ mathurā yena pūritā ।। rakṣisainyaṃ nikṛtyobhau niṣkrāntau kārmukālayāt ।।
bhagnaṃ śrutvātha kaṃso api prāha cāṇūramuṣṭikau ।। mallayuddhe nihantavyau mama prāṇaharau hi tau ।। dāsyāmy abhimatān kāmān nānyathaitan mahābalau ।। hantavyau tadvadhād rājyaṃ sāmānyaṃ vo bhaviṣyati ।।
provācoccais tvayā mallasamājadvāri kuñjaraḥ ।। ghātanīyau niyuddhāya raṅgadvāram upāgatau ।। āsannamaraṇaḥ kaṃsaḥ sūryodayam udaikṣata ।। rājamañceṣu cārūḍhāḥ saha bhṛtyair mahībhṛtaḥ ।।
kṛtaḥ kaṃsena kaṃso api tuṅgamañce vyavasthitaḥ ।। anye ca vāramukhyānām anye nāgarayoṣitām ।। akrūravasudevau ca mañcaprānte vyavasthitau ।। antakāle api putrasya drakṣyāmi ruciraṃ mukham ।।
hāhākārapare loke āsphoṭayati muṣṭike ।। dṛṣṭvā kuvalayāpīḍaṃ ghoradantaṃ sudāruṇam ।। krīḍitvā suciraṃ kṛṣṇaḥ karidantapadāntare ।। dantadvayaṃ tu jagrāha karābhyāṃ kariṇas tadā ।।
jaghāna vāmapādena mastake hastinas tataḥ ।। utpāṭya vāmadantaṃ tu dakṣiṇenaiva pāṇinā ।। tāḍayām āsa yantāraṃ tasyāsīc chatadhā śiraḥ ।। dakṣiṇaṃ dantam utpāṭya balabhadro api tatkṣaṇāt ।।
saroṣas tena pārśvasthān gajapālān apothayat ।। sa papāta hatas tena balabhadreṇa līlayā ।। sahasrākṣeṇa vajreṇa tāḍitaḥ parvato yathā ।। tatas tūtplutya vegena rauhiṇeyo mahābalaḥ ।। A
īṣad dhasantau tau vīrau balabhadrajanārdanau ।। gopaveṣadharau bālau raṅgadvāram upāgatau ।। tataḥ kuvalayāpīḍo mahāmātrapracoditaḥ ।। abhyadhāvata vegena hantuṃ gopakumārakau ।।
hāhākāro mahāñ jajñe raṅgamadhye dvijottama ।। baladevo api taṃ dṛṣṭvā vacanaṃ cedam abravīt ।। hantavyo hi mahābhāga nāgo ayaṃ śatrucoditaḥ ।। ity uktaḥ so agrajenātha baladevena vai dvija ।।
siṃhanādaṃ tataś cakre mādhavaḥ paravīrahā ।। kareṇa karam ākṛṣya keśavaḥ keśisūdanaḥ ।। dantam ekaṃ samutpāṭya tāḍayām āsa kuñjaraḥ ।। utpāṭya vāmadantaṃ tu dakṣiṇenaiva pāṇinā ।।
sa papāta mahīpṛṣṭhe meruśṛṅgam ivāparam ।। īśo api sarvajagatāṃ bālalīlānusārataḥ ।। A bhrāmayām āsa taṃ śaurir airāvatasamaṃ bale ।। B madāsṛganuliptāṅgau gajadantavarāyudhau ।।
praviṣṭau sumahāraṅgaṃ balabhadrajanārdanau ।। kṛṣṇo ayaṃ balabhadro ayam iti lokasya vismayāt ।। kṣiptaṃ tu śakaṭaṃ yena bhagnau ca yamalārjunau ।। dhṛto govardhano yena saptarātraṃ mahāgiriḥ ।।
nihatā yena durvṛttā dṛśyatāṃ so ayam acyutaḥ ।। prayāti līlayā yoṣinmanonayananandanaḥ ।। gopālo yādavaṃ vaṃśaṃ magnam abhyuddhariṣyati ।। avatīrṇo mahīm aṃśo nūnaṃ bhāraharo bhuvaḥ ।।
ity evaṃ varṇite paurai rāme kṛṣṇe ca tatkṣaṇāt ।। b praviṣṭe nagaram abhyetau viśvalokāvalokitau ।। b uras tatāpa devakyāḥ snehasnutapayodharam ।। d yuveva vasudevo abhūd vihāyābhyāgatāṃ jarām ।।
nāgarastrīsamūhaś ca draṣṭuṃ na virarāma tam ।। evaṃ tā rājakanyāś ca mahiṣyaḥ purayoṣitaḥ ।। agraṇyagaṇikāś caiva kanyā nāgarikāḥ striyaḥ ।। kaṃsārihṛdayāsaktacetanās tā varastriyaḥ ।।
garhayantyo atha rājānam bhramantyas taddidṛkṣayā ।। icchantyo manasas tasya jayety ūcur jayaṃ tataḥ ।। gajayuddhakṛtāyāsasvedāmbukaṇikācitam ।। paribhūya sthitaṃ janma saphalaṃ kriyatāṃ dṛśaḥ ।।
vipakṣakṣapaṇaṃ vakṣo bhujayugmaṃ ca bhāmini ।। balabhadram imaṃ nīlaparidhānam upāgatam ।। kriyate balabhadrasya hāsyam etad vilokyatām ।। samupaiti na santy atra kiṃ vṛddhā yuktakāriṇaḥ ।।
na kiṃcid api jānāti yuktāyuktaṃ mahīpatiḥ ।। balābalam avijñātum anenātra na śakyate ।। kimarthaṃ mantriṇaś caite mantriṇo rājakarmaṇi ।। kva vajrakaṭhinābhogaśarīro ayaṃ mahāsuraḥ ।।
daiteyamallāś cāṇūrapramukhās tv atidāruṇāḥ ।। yad bālabalinor yuddhaṃ madhyasthaiḥ samupekṣyate ।। itthaṃ purastrīlokasya vadataś cālayan bhuvam ।। b niruddhaṃ prāṣṇikair yuktaṃ śrutvā tau rāmakeśavau ।। b
vavalga baddhakakṣyo antar janasya bhagavān hariḥ ।। d pade pade tadā bhūmir yan na śīrṇā tad adbhutam ।। niyuddhakuśalo daityo balabhadreṇa muṣṭikaḥ ।। kṣepaṇair muṣṭibhiś caiva kīlavajranipātanaiḥ ।।
jānubhiś cānyanirghātais tathā bāhuvighaṭṭitaiḥ ।। jānubhiś cāśmabhir ghātaiḥ śirobhir avaghaṭṭitaiḥ ।। pādoddhūtaiḥ pramṛṣṭaiś ca tayor yuddham abhūn mahat ।। balaprāṇaviniṣpādyaṃ samājotsavasaṃnidhau ।।
prāṇahānim avāpāgryāṃ tāvat tāval lavāl lavam ।। khedāc cālayatā kopān nijaśekharakesaram ।। vārayām āsa tūryāṇi kaṃsaḥ kopaparāyaṇaḥ ।। khe saṃgatāny avādyanta devatūryāṇy anekaśaḥ ।।
ity antardhānagā devās tadocur atiharṣitāḥ ।। utpāṭya bhrāmayām āsa tadvadhāya kṛtodyamaḥ ।। bhūmāv āsphoṭayām āsa gagane gatajīvitam ।। raktasrāvamahāpaṅkāṃ cakāra sa tadā bhuvam ।।
yuyudhe daityamallena cāṇūreṇa yathā hariḥ ।। pātayitvā dharāpṛṣṭhe niṣpipeṣa gatāyuṣam ।। vāmamuṣṭiprahāreṇa pātayām āsa bhūtale ।। nīte kṣayaṃ tośalake sarve mallāḥ pradudruvuḥ ।।
samānavayaso gopān balād ākṛṣya harṣitau ।। gopāv etau samājaughān niṣkrāmyetāṃ balād itaḥ ।। avṛddhārheṇa daṇḍena vasudevo api hanyatām ।। gāvo hriyantām eteṣāṃ yac cāsti vasu kiṃcana ।।
utplutyāruhya taṃ mañcaṃ kaṃsaṃ jagrāha vegataḥ ।। kaṃsaṃ sa pātayām āsa tasyopari papāta ca ।। kṛṣṇena tyājitaḥ prāṇān ugrasenātmajo nṛpaḥ ।। cakarṣa dehaṃ kaṃsasya raṅgamadhye mahābalaḥ ।।
kṛtā kaṃsasya dehena vegeneva mahāmbhasaḥ ।। sunāmā balabhadreṇa līlayaiva nipātitaḥ ।। avajñayā hataṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇena mathureśvaram ।। devakyāś ca mahābāhur baladevasahāyavān ।।
smṛtajanmoktavacanau tāv eva praṇatau sthitau ।। tathāvayoḥ prasādena kṛtoddhāraś ca keśava ।। durvṛttanidhanārthāya tena naḥ pāvitaṃ kulam ।। pravartete samastātmaṃs tvatto bhūtabhaviṣyatī ।।
tvam eva yajño yaṣṭā ca yajñānāṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। samudbhavaḥ samastasya jagatas tvaṃ janārdana ।। devakyāś cātmajaprītyā tad atyantaviḍambanā ।। kva me manuṣyakasyaiṣā jihvā putreti vakṣyati ।।
kayā yuktyā vinā māyāṃ so asmattaḥ saṃbhaviṣyati ।। sa koṣṭhotsaṅgaśayano manuṣyāj jāyate katham ।। ābrahmapādapam ayaṃ jagad etad īśa tvatto vimohayasi kiṃ parameśvarātman ।। nīto asi gokulam ito atibhayākulasya vṛddhiṃ gato asi mama nāsti mamatvam īśa ।।
tvaṃ viṣṇur īśa jagatām upakārahetoḥ prāpto asi naḥ parigataṃ vigato hi mohaḥ ।। mohāya yaducakrasya vitatāna sa vaiṣṇavīm ।। bhavantau kaṃsabhītena dṛṣṭau saṃkarṣaṇena ca ।। tat khaṇḍam āyuṣo vyarthaṃ sādhūnām upajāyate ।।
kurvatāṃ saphalaṃ janma dehināṃ tāta jāyate ।। kaṃsapratāpavīryābhyām āvayoḥ paravaśyayoḥ ।। yathāvad abhipūjyātha cakratuḥ pauramānanam ।। vilepur mātaraś cāsya duḥkhaśokapariplutāḥ ।।
tāḥ samāśvāsayām āsa svayam asrāvilekṣaṇaḥ ।। abhyaṣiñcat tathaivainaṃ nijarājye hatātmajam ।। cakāra pretakāryāṇi ye cānye tatra ghātitāḥ ।। uvācājñāpaya vibho yat kāryam aviśaṅkitaḥ ।।
mayi bhṛtye sthite devān ājñāpayatu kiṃ nṛpaiḥ ।। uvāca cainaṃ bhagavān keśavaḥ kāryamānuṣaḥ ।। dīyatām ugrasenāya sudharmā bhavatā sabhā ।। sudharmākhyā sabhā yuktam asyāṃ yadubhir āsitum ।।
dadau so api sudharmākhyāṃ sabhāṃ vāyoḥ puraṃdaraḥ ।। bubhujuḥ sarvaratnāḍhyāṃ govindabhujasaṃśrayāt ।। śiṣyācāryakramaṃ vīrau khyāpayantau yadūttamau ।। astrārthaṃ jagmatur vīrau baladevajanārdanau ।।
kṛtopanayanakramau ।। vedābhyāsakṛtaprītī ।। darśayāṃ cakratur vīrāv ācāram akhile jane ।। ahorātraiś catuḥṣaṣṭyā tad adbhutam abhūd dvija ।।
vicintya tau tadā mene prāptau candradivākarau ।। sāṅgāṃś ca caturo vedān sarvaśāstrāṇi caiva hi ।। ūcatur vriyatāṃ yā te dātavyā gurudakṣiṇā ।। ayācata mṛtaṃ putraṃ prabhāse lavaṇārṇave ।।
tatheti coktvā prayayau rāmeṇa sahitodadhim ।। uvāca na mayā putro hṛtaḥ sāṃdīpaner iti ।। rathenāgatya cārṇavam ।। dīyatāṃ sāgara kṣipraṃ putraṃ sāṃdīpaner iti ।।
tataḥ sa vyathitas tūrṇaṃ ।। jagrāha so asti salile mamaivāsurasūdana ।। kṛṣṇo jagrāha tasyāsthiprabhavaṃ śaṅkham uttamam ।। devānāṃ vavṛdhe tejo yāty adharmaś ca saṃkṣayam ।।
baladevaś ca balavāñ jitvā vaivasvataṃ yamam ।। pitre pradattavān kṛṣṇo balaś ca balināṃ varaḥ ।। prahṛṣṭapuruṣastrīkāv ubhau rāmajanārdanau ।। astiṃ prāptiṃ ca maitreya tayor bhartṛhaṇaṃ harim ।।
hantum abhyāyayau kopāj jarāsaṃdhaḥ sa yādavam ।। akṣauhiṇībhiḥ sainyasya trayoviṃśatibhir vṛtaḥ ।। yuyudhāte samaṃ tasya balinau balisainikaiḥ ।। āyudhānāṃ purāṇānām ādāne munisattama ।।
ākāśād āgatau vipra tathā kaumodakī gadā ।। manasābhimataṃ vipra saunandaṃ musalaṃ tathā ।। purīṃ viviśatur vīrāv ubhau rāmajanārdanau ।। jīvamāne gate kṛṣṇas taṃ nāmanyata nirjitam ।।
jitaś ca rāmakṛṣṇābhyām apakrānto dvijottama ।। yadubhir māgadho rājā cakre kṛṣṇapurogamaiḥ ।। apakrānto jarāsaṃdhaḥ svalpasainyair balādhikaḥ ।। tat tu saṃnidhimāhātmyaṃ viṣṇor aṃśasya cakriṇaḥ ।।
astrāṇy anekarūpāṇi yad arātiṣu muñcati ।। tasyāripakṣakṣapaṇe kiyān udyamavistaraḥ ।। kurvan balavatā saṃdhiṃ hīnair yuddhaṃ karoty asau ।। karoti daṇḍapātaṃ ca kvacid eva palāyanam ।।
līlā jagatpates tasya chandataḥ saṃpravartate ।। yadūnāṃ saṃnidhau sarve jahasur yādavās tataḥ ।। sutam icchaṃs tapas tepe yaducakrabhayāvaham ।। dadau varaṃ ca tuṣṭo asmai varṣe dvādaśame haraḥ ।।
tadyoṣitsaṃgamāc cāsya putro abhūd alisaṃnibhaḥ ।। abhiṣicya vanaṃ yāto vajrāgrakaṭhinorasam ।। papraccha nāradas tasmai kathayām āsa yādavān ।। gajāśvarathasaṃpannaiś cakāra paramodyamam ।।
yādavān prati sāmarṣo maitreya mathurāṃ purīm ।। yavanena raṇe gamyaṃ māgadhasya bhaviṣyati ।। hantā tad idam āyātaṃ yadūnāṃ vyasanaṃ dvidhā ।। striyo api yatra yudhyeyuḥ kiṃ punar vṛṣṇipuṃgavāḥ ।।
yādavābhibhavaṃ duṣṭā mā kurvaṃs tv arayo adhikāḥ ।। yayāce dvādaśa purīṃ dvārakāṃ tatra nirmame ।। prākāragṛhasaṃbādhām indrasyevāmarāvatīm ।। āsanne kālayavane mathurāṃ ca svayaṃ yayau ।।
nirjagāma sa govindo dadṛśe yavaneśvaram ।। anuyāto mahāyogicetobhiḥ prāpyate na yaḥ ।। yatra śete mahāvīryo mucukundo nareśvaraḥ ।। pādena tāḍayām āsa matvā kṛṣṇaṃ sudurmatiḥ ।।
utthāya mucukundo api dadarśa yavanaṃ nṛpaḥ ।। tatkrodhajena maitreya bhasmībhūtaś ca tatkṣaṇāt ।। nidrārtaḥ sumahat kālaṃ nidrāṃ vavre varaṃ surān ।। dehajenāgninā sadyaḥ sa tu bhasmībhaviṣyati ।।
vasudevasya tanayo yador vaṃśasamudbhavaḥ ।। mucukundo api tatrāsau vṛddhagargavaco asmarat ।। prāha jñāto bhavān viṣṇor aṃśas tvaṃ parameśvara ।। dvāparānte harer janma yador vaṃśe bhaviṣyati ।।
sa tvaṃ prāpto na saṃdeho martyānām upakārakṛt ।। vākyaṃ namati caivorvī yuṣmatpādaprapīḍitā ।। na sehur mama tejas te tvattejo na sahāmy aham ।। yaḥ saṃsmarati tasyaitat tejas tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।।
sa prasīda prapannārtihantar hara mamāśubham ।। medinī gaganaṃ vāyur āpo agnis tvaṃ tathā manaḥ ।। puṃsaḥ parataraṃ yac ca vyāpy ajanmavikalpavat ।। avṛddhināśaṃ tad brahma tvam ādyantavivarjitam ।।
siddhāś cāpsarasas tvatto manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ khagāḥ ।। sarīsṛpā mṛgāḥ sarve tvattaḥ sarve mahīruhāḥ ।। b sthūlā madhyās tathā sūkṣmāḥ sūkṣmāt sūkṣmatarāś ca ye ।। b yac ca bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyac ca kiṃcid atra carācaram ।। d
tat sarvaṃ tvaṃ jagatkartar nāsti kiṃcit tvayā vinā ।। tāpatrayābhibhūtena na prāptā nirvṛtiḥ kvacit ।। mayā nātha gṛhītāni tāni tāpāya cābhavan ।। bhāryā bhṛtyajano ye ca śabdādyā viṣayāḥ prabho ।।
pariṇāme tad eveśa tāpātmakam abhūn mama ।। mattaḥ sāhāyyakāmo abhūc śāśvatī kutra nirvṛtiḥ ।। śāśvatī prāpyate kena parameśvara nirvṛtiḥ ।। avāpya tāpān paśyanti pretarājānanaṃ narāḥ ।।
prāpnuvanti narā duḥkham asvarūpavidas tava ।। mamatvagarvagartāntar bhramāmi parameśvara ।। saṃsāraśramaparitāpataptacetā nirvāṇe pariṇatadhāmni sābhilāṣaḥ ।। prāheśaḥ sarvabhūtānām anādir bhagavān hariḥ ।।
avyāhataparaiśvaryo matprasādopabṛṃhitaḥ ।। jātismaro matprasādāt tato mokṣam avāpsyasi ।। guhāmukhād viniṣkrāntaḥ dadṛśe so alpakān narān ।। naranārāyaṇasthānaṃ prayayau gandhamādanam ।।
jagrāha mathurām etya hastyaśvasyandanojjvalam ।। parābhibhavaniḥśaṅkaṃ babhūva ca yadoḥ kulam ।। jñātidarśanasotkaṇṭhaḥ prayayau nandagokulam ।। tathaivābhyavadat premṇā bahumānapuraḥsaram ।।
hāsyaṃ cakre samaṃ kaiścid gopair gopījanais tathā ।। gopyaś ca premakupitāḥ procuḥ serṣyam athāparāḥ ।। kaccid āste sukhaṃ kṛṣṇaś calatpremalavātmakaḥ ।। saubhāgyamānam adhikaṃ karoti kṣaṇasauhṛdaḥ ।।
apy asau mātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ sakṛd apy āgamiṣyati ।। yasyāsmābhir vinā tena vināsmākaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। na tyaktas tatkṛte asmābhir akṛtajñadhvajo hi saḥ ।। saṃdeśaiḥ sāmamadhurair nāsmān smarati kutracit ।।
karoti kṛṣṇo vaktavyaṃ bhavatā rāma nānṛtam ।। apetaprītir asmāsu durdarśaḥ pratibhāti naḥ ।। ruruduḥ sasvaraṃ gopyo hariṇā hṛtacetasaḥ ।। rāmeṇāśvāsitā gopyaḥ kṛṣṇasyātimanoharaiḥ ।।
kathāś cakāra reme ca saha tair vrajabhūmiṣu ।। mānuṣachadmarūpasya śeṣasya dharaṇībhṛtaḥ ।। upabhogārtham atyarthaṃ varuṇaḥ prāha vāruṇīm ।। anantasyopabhogāya tasya gaccha mude śubhe ।।
vṛndāvanavanotpannakadambatarukoṭare ।। āghrāya madirātarṣam avāpātha purātanam ।। patantīṃ vīkṣya maitreya prayayau paramāṃ mudam ।। pragīyamāno lalitaṃ gītavādyaviśāradaiḥ ।।
āgaccha yamune snātum icchāmīty āha vihvalaḥ ।। nājagāma tataḥ kruddho halaṃ jagrāha lāṅgalī ।। pāpe nāyāsi nāyāsi gamyatām icchayānyataḥ ।। yatrāste balabhadro asau plāvayām āsa tad vanam ।।
prasīdety abravīd rāmaṃ muñca māṃ musalāyudha ।। so ahaṃ tvāṃ halapātena vineṣyāmi sahasradhā ।। bhūbhāge plāvite tasmin mumoca yamunāṃ balaḥ ।। avataṃsotpalaṃ cāru gṛhītvaikaṃ ca kuṇḍalam ।।
tato vyamuñcad yamunāṃ yācito bhagavān balaḥ ।। vijagāha jalaṃ strībhiḥ karaura bhir ivebharāṭ ।। kāmaṃ vihṛtya salilād uttīrṇāyāsitāmbare ।। bhūṣaṇāni mahārghāṇi dadau kāntiśubhāṃ srajam ।।
samudrābhe tathā vastre nīle lakṣmīr ayacchata ।। nīlāmbaradharaḥ sragvī śuśubhe kāntisaṃyutaḥ ।। māsadvayena yātaś ca punaḥ sa dvārakāṃ purīm ।। upayeme balas tasyāṃ jajñāte niśaṭholmukau ।।
vasitvā vāsasī nīle mālām āmucyakāñcanīm ।। reje svalaṃkṛtilipto māhendra iva vāraṇaḥ ।। adyāpi dṛśyate rājan yamunākṛṣṭavartmanā ।। balasyānantavīryasya vīryaṃ sūcayatīva hi ।।
evaṃ sarvā niśā yātā ekaiva ramaro vraje ।। rāmasyākṣiptacittasya mādhuryair vrajayoṣitām ।। rukmī tasyābhavat putro rukmiṇī ca varāṅganā ।। na dadau yācate caināṃ rukmī dveṣeṇa cakriṇe ।।
bhīṣmako rukmiṇā sārdhaṃ rukmiṇīm uruvikramaḥ ।। bhīṣmakasya purīṃ jagmuḥ śiśupālapriyaiṣiṇaḥ ।। prayayau kuṇḍinaṃ draṣṭuṃ vivāhaṃ cedibhūbhṛtaḥ ।। antaḥpraviṣṭā rājānaḥ śatravaḥ pūrvam āgatāḥ ।।
iti matvā tathā kṛṣṇo bahir vā samakalpayat ।। vipakṣabhāram āsajya rāmādyeṣv atha bandhuṣu ।। śiśupālajarāsaṃdhaśālvādyāś ca mahībhṛtaḥ ।। nirjitāś ca samāgamya rāmādyair yadupuṃgavaiḥ ।।
kṛtvā pratijñāṃ rukmī ca hantuṃ kṛṣṇam abhidrutaḥ ।। nirjitaḥ pātitaś corvyāṃ līlayaiva sa cakriṇā ।। hantuṃ kṛtamatiḥ kṛṣṇo rukmiṇaṃ yuddhadurmadam ।। praṇamya yācito brahma rukmiṇyā bhagavān hariḥ ।।
eka eva mama bhrātā na hantavyas tvayādhunā ।। krodhaṃ niyamya deveśa bhrātṛbhikṣā pradīyatām ।। ity ukto asau pariṣvaktaḥ kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।। rukmī bhojakaṭaṃ nāma puraṃ kṛtvāvasat tadā ।।
rākṣasena vivāhena saṃprāptāṃ madhusūdanaḥ ।। jahāra śambaro yaṃ vai yo jaghāna ca śambaram ।। śambaraś ca mahāvīryaḥ pradyumnena kathaṃ hataḥ ।। yas tenāpahṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ sa kathaṃ vijaghāna tam ।।
etad vistarataḥ śrotum icchāmi sakalaṃ guro ।। mamaiṣa hanteti mune hṛtavān kālaśambaraḥ ।। kallolajanitāvarte sughore makarālaye ।। na mamāra ca tasyāpi jaṭharānaladīpitaḥ ।।
ghātito asuravaryāya śambarāya niveditaḥ ।। kārayām āsa sūdānām ādhipatyam aninditā ।। kumāraṃ manmathataror dagdhasya prathamāṅkuram ।। ity evaṃ kautukāviṣṭāṃ tāṃ tanvīṃ prāha nāradaḥ ।।
śambareṇa hṛto viṣṇos tanayaḥ sūtikāgṛhāt ।। nararatnam idaṃ subhru visrabdhā paripālaya ।। bālyād evātirāgeṇa rūpātiśayamohitā ।। sābhilāṣā tadā sā tu babhūva gajagāminī ।।
pradyumnāyānurāgāndhā tannyastahṛdayekṣaṇā ।। antrāntare bhīṣmakasya dākṣiṇyā tasya bhūpateḥ ।। śuśrāva rukmiṇīṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kanyāṃ rūpeṇa viśrutām ।। sāpi śuśrāva kaṃsāriṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kamalalocanam ।।
abhilāṣarasodāraṃ kim apy āste manas tayoḥ ।। bhīṣmakasyātmajo rukmī bhujaśālī raṇotkaṭaḥ ।। vīro bibharti yaḥ spardhāṃ bhuvi bhārgavabhīṣmayoḥ ।। anujāṃ rukmiṇīṃ dṛptaḥ sa kṛṣṇenārthitaḥ sadā ।।
na dadau kaṃsadāso ayam iti dveṣād udāharat ।। tato jarāsandhagirā śiśupālāya bhūbhuje ।। tāṃ dattam udyayau putrīṃ bhīṣmakaḥ putrasaṃmate ।। vasudevas vasuḥ putraḥ śiśupālo atha tatpurīm ।।
kṛṣṇādibhir vṛṣṇivīrair varayātrānimantritaiḥ ।। dantavakrajarāsandhamukhyaiś ca saha rājabhiḥ ।। sa vivāhotsave prāyād bhīṣmakeṇābhipūjitaḥ ।। bhavānīpūjitavyagrāṃ tatra locanacandrikām ।।
dadarśa rukmiṇīṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇasārāyatekṣaṇām ।। dṛṣṭvā tām atha vaikuṇṭhaḥ sotkaṇṭhāṃ manmathākulaḥ ।। jahāra paśyatāṃ nṝṇāṃ sahasā bhīṣmakātmajām ।। na hatvā malinācāraṃ kṛṣṇaṃ durnayakāriṇam ।।
svapuraṃ samupeṣyāmi vīravrataparicyutaḥ ।। ity uktvā ratham āruhya vīrair anugato nṛpaḥ ।। vātoddhūtapatākāgraḥ sa yayau nādayan diśaḥ ।। dūrād āyāntam ālokya rathastho rukmiṇīsakhaḥ ।।
tasthau hariḥ parāvṛttya karṇāntākṛṣṭakārmukaḥ ।। divyāstravarṣiṇaḥ śauricchittvā sarvāyudhāny atha ।। rukmiṇaṃ tīvranārācair vivyādha hṛdaye nimiḥ ।। mūrcchite patite tasmin vidrute rājamaṇḍale ।।
rarakṣa śaurir dayayā rukmiṇāṃ rukmiṇīgirā ।। yāte dvāravatīṃ kṛṣṇe vinivṛtteṣu vṛṣṇiṣu ।। kuṇḍinākhyaṃ puraṃ rukmī praviveśa na lajjayā ।। pratijayāparityaktaḥ puraḥ saṃvidadhe puram ।।
puraṃ bhojakaṭaṃ nāma mānabhaṅgaṃ vicintayan ।। jayaśriyam ivādāya śriyaṃ mūrtyantarāgatām ।। kāmas tu vāsudevāṃśo dagdhaḥ prākchūdramanyunā ।। dehopapattaye bhūyas tam eva pratyapadyata ।।
sa eva xx vaidarbhyāṃ kṛṣṇavīryasamudbhavaḥ ।। pradyumna iti vikhyātaḥ arvato navamaḥ pituḥ ।। taṃ śambaraḥ kālarūpī hṛtvā tokam anirdiśam ।। sa viditvātmanaḥ śatruṃ prāsyodanvaty agād gṛham ।।
taṃ nirjagāra balavān mīnaḥ so apy aparaiḥ saha ।। vṛto jālena mahatā gṛhīto matsyajīvibhiḥ ।। taṃ śambarāya kaivartā upājahur upāyanam ।। sūdā mahānasaṃ nītvā vidyan svadhitinā drutam ।।
dṛṣṭvā tad udare bālaṃ māyāvatyai nyavedayan ।। nārado akathayat sarvaṃ tasyāḥ śaṅkitacetasaḥ ।। bālasya tattvam utpattiṃ matsyodaraniveśanam ।। sā ca kāmasya vai patnī ratir nāma yaśasvinī ।।
patyur nirdagdhadehasya dehotpattiṃ pratīkṣitī ।। nirūpitā śambareṇa sā sūpaudanasādhane ।। kāmadevaṃ śiśuṃ buddhvā cakre snehaṃ tadārbhake ।। nātidīrgheṇa kālena sa kārṣṇī rūḍhayauvanaḥ ।।
janayām āsa nārīṇāṃ vīkṣantīnāṃ suvibhramam ।। mātṛbhāvām apāhāya kim evaṃ vartase anyathā ।। tanayaṃ tvām ayaṃ viṣṇor hṛtavān kālaśambaraḥ ।। sā tu roditi te mātā kāntādyāpy ativatsalā ।।
krodhākulīkṛtamanā yuyudhe ca mahābalaḥ ।। saptamāyā vyatikramya māyāṃ saṃyuyuje aṣṭamīm ।। utpatya ca tayā sārdham ājagāma pitur gṛham ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇasaṃkalpā babhūvuḥ kṛṣṇayoṣitaḥ ।।
dhanyāyā khalv ayaṃ putro vartate navayauvane ।। sabhāgyā jananī vatsa tvayā kāpi vibhūṣitā ।। harer apatyaṃ suvyaktaṃ bhavān vatsa bhaviṣyati ।। antaḥpuracarāṃ devīṃ rukmiṇīṃ prāha harṣayan ।।
hṛto yenābhavad bālo bhavatyāḥ sūtikāgṛhāt ।। śambarasya na bhāryeyaṃ śrūyatām atra kāraṇam ।। śambaraṃ mohayām āsa māyārūpeṇa rūpiṇī ।। darśayām āsa daityasya tasyeyaṃ madirekṣaṇā ।।
viśaṅkā nātra kartavyā snuṣeyaṃ tava śobhanā ।। nagarī ca samastā sā sādhu sādhv ity abhāṣata ।। avāpa vismayaṃ sarvo dvāravatyāṃ janas tadā ।। suṣeṇaṃ cāruguptaṃ ca bhadracāruṃ tathā param ।।
rukmiṇy ajanayat putrān kanyāṃ cārumatīṃ tathā ।। kālindī mitravindā ca satyā nāgnajitī tathā ।। madrarājasutā cānyā suśīlā śīlamaṇḍanā ।। ṣoḍaśāsan sahasrāṇi strīṇām anyāni cakriṇaḥ ।।
pradyumnaḥ prathamas teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ rukmiṇīsutaḥ ।। svayaṃvarasthāṃ jagrāha sā ca taṃ tanayaṃ hareḥ ।। aniruddho raṇe ruddho vīryodadhir ariṃdamaḥ ।। dauhitrāya dadau rukmī tāṃ spardhann api śauriṇā ।।
tasyā vivāhe rāmādyā yādavā hariṇā saha ।। b kalyāṇārthaṃ tataḥ sarve ye cānye bhūbhṛtas tathā ।। b rukmiṇo nagaraṃ jagmur nāmnā bhojakaṭaṃ dvija ।। d kaliṅgarājapramukhā rukmiṇaṃ vākyam abruvan ।।
na jayāmo balaṃ kasmād dyūte nainaṃ mahādyute ।। sabhāyāṃ saha rāmeṇa cakre dyūtaṃ ca vai tadā ।। dvitīye api paṇe cānyat sahasraṃ rukmiṇā jitaḥ ।। balabhadro ajayat tāni rukmī dyūtavidāṃ varaḥ ।।
dantān vidarśayan mūḍho rukmī cāha madoddhataḥ ।। mudhaivākṣāvalepāndho yo avamene akṣakovidān ।। rukmiṇaṃ cāpi durvākyaṃ kopaṃ cakre halāyudhaḥ ।। glahaṃ jagrāha rukmī ca tadarthe akṣān apātayat ।।
mayeti rukmī prāhoccair alīkoktair alaṃ bala ।। evaṃ tvayā ced vijitaṃ mayā na vijitaṃ katham ।। baladevasya taṃ kopaṃ vardhayantī mahātmanaḥ ।। anuktvāpi vacaḥ kiṃcit kṛtaṃ bhavati karmaṇā ।।
jaghānāṣṭāpadenaiva rukmiṇaṃ sa mahābalaḥ ।। babhañja dantān kupito yaiḥ prakāśaṃ jahāsa saḥ ।। jaghāna ye anye tatpakṣāḥ bhūbhṛtaḥ kupito balaḥ ।। tad rājamaṇḍalaṃ sarvaṃ babhūva kupite bale ।।
novāca kiṃcin maitreya rukmiṇībalayor bhayāt ।। dvārakām ājagāmātha yaducakraṃ sa keśavaḥ ।। ājagāmātha maitreya mattairāvatapṛṣṭhagaḥ ।। kathayām āsa daityasya narakasya viceṣṭitam ।।
praśamaṃ sarvaduḥkhāni nītāni madhusūdana ।। pravṛtto yas tathā keśī te sarve nihatās tvayā ।। nāśaṃ nītās tvayā sarve ye anye jagadupadravāḥ ।। yajviyajñāṃśasaṃprāptyā tṛptiṃ yānti divaukasaḥ ।।
tac chrutvā tatpratīkāraprayatnaṃ kartum arhasi ।। karoti sarvabhūtānām upaghātam ariṃdama ।। hṛtvā hi so asuraḥ kanyā rurodha nijamandire ।। mandarasya tathā śṛṅgaṃ hṛtavān maṇiparvatam ।।
jahāra so asuro adityā vāñchaty airāvataṃ gajam ।। yad atra pratikartavyaṃ tat svayaṃ parimṛśyatām ।। gṛhītvā vāsavaṃ haste samuttasthau varāsanāt ।। cintayām āsa ca vibhur manasā pannagāśanam ।।
satyabhāmāṃ samāropya yayau prāgjyotiṣaṃ puram ।। tato jagāma maitreya paśyatāṃ dvārakaukasām ।। ācitā mauravaiḥ pāśaiḥ kṣurāntair bhūr dvijottama ।। tato muruḥ samuttasthau taṃ jaghāna ca keśavaḥ ।।
cakradhārāgninirdagdhāṃś cakāra śalabhān iva ।। prāgjyotiṣapuraṃ dhīmāṃs tvarāvān samupādravat ।। kṛṣṇasya yatra govindo jaghne daityān sahasraśaḥ ।। kṣiptvā cakraṃ dvidhā cakre cakrī daiteyacakrahā ।।
upatasthe jagannāthaṃ vākyaṃ cedam athābravīt ।। tvatsparśasaṃbhavaḥ putras tadāyaṃ mayy ajāyata ।। gṛhāṇa kuṇḍale ceme pālayāsya ca saṃtatim ।। aṃśena lokam āyātaḥ prasādasumukhaḥ prabho ।।
jagatāṃ tvaṃ jagadrūpaḥ stūyate acyuta kiṃ tava ।। sarvabhūtātmabhūtasya stūyate tava kiṃ tadā ।। yadā tadā stutir nāsti kimarthā te pravartate ।। tat kṣamyatām adoṣāya tvatsutaḥ sa nipātitaḥ ।।
ratnāni narakāvāsāj jagrāha munisattama ।। śatādhikāni dadṛśe sahasrāṇi mahāmune ।। kāmbojānāṃ tathāśvānāṃ niyutāny ekaviṃśatim ।। preṣayām āsa govindaḥ sadyo narakakiṃkaraiḥ ।।
āropayām āsa harir garuḍe patageśvare ।। adityāḥ kuṇḍale dātuṃ jagāma tridivālayam ।। sabhāryaṃ ca hṛṣīkeśaṃ līlayaiva vahan yayau ।। upatasthus tato devāḥ sārghyapātrā janārdanam ।।
sitābhraśikharākāraṃ praviśya dadṛśe aditim ।। dadau narakanāśaṃ ca śaśaṃsāsyai janārdanaḥ ।। tuṣṭāvāditir avyagrā kṛtvā tatpravaṇaṃ manaḥ ।। sanātanātman sarvātman bhūtātman bhūtabhāvana ।।
triguṇātīta nirdvandva śuddha sarvahṛdisthita ।। janmādibhir asaṃspṛṣṭa svapnādiparivarjita ।। hutāśano mano buddhir bhūtādis tvaṃ tathācyuta ।। brahmaviṣṇuśivākhyābhir ātmamūrtibhir īśvara ।।
