kūṣmāṇḍāś ca piśācāś ca gandharvā manujās tathā ।। paśavo mṛgāḥ pataṃgāś ca tathaiva ca sarīsṛpāḥ ।। b paśava uragā mīnā mṛgāś ca vanajātayaḥ ।। b kīṭāś caiva pataṅgāś ca tathaiva ca sarīsṛpāḥ ।। b
vṛkṣagulmalatāvallīsamastatṛṇajātayaḥ ।। d dehabhedā bhavān sarve ye kecit pudgalāśrayāḥ ।। anātmany ātmavijñānaṃ yayā mūḍho nirudhyate ।। asve svam iti bhāvo atra yat puṃsām upajāyate ।।
saṃsāramātur māyāyās tavaitan nātha ceṣṭitam ।। te taranty akhilām etāṃ māyām ātmavimuktaye ।। viṣṇumāyāmahāvartamohāndhatamasā vṛtāḥ ।। yad ete puruṣā māyā saiveyaṃ bhagavaṃs tava ।।
ārādhito na mokṣāya māyāvilasitaṃ hi tat ।। jāyate yad apuṇyānāṃ so aparādhaḥ svadoṣajaḥ ।। ajñānaṃ jñānasadbhāvabhūtaṃ bhūteśa nāśaya ।। gadāhastāya te viṣṇo śaṅkhahastāya te namaḥ ।।
na jānāmi paraṃ yat te prasīda parameśvara ।। mātā devi tvam asmākaṃ prasīda varadā bhava ।। ajeyaḥ puruṣavyāghra martyaloke bhaviṣyasi ।। satyabhāmā praṇamyāha prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ ।।
bhaviṣyaty anavadyāṅgī sarvakālaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। yathāvat pūjayām āsa bahumānapuraḥsaram ।। śacī ca satyabhāmāyai pārijātasya puṣpakam ।। na dadau mānuṣīṃ matvā svayaṃ puṣpair alaṃkṛtā ।।
devodyānāni hṛdyāni nandanādīni sattama ।। śaityāhlādakaraṃ tāmrabālapallavaśobhitam ।। pārijātaṃ jagannāthaḥ keśavaḥ keśisūdanaḥ ।। tutoṣa paramaprītyā tarurājam anuttamam ।।
kasmān na dvārakām eṣa nīyate kṛṣṇa pādapaḥ ।। madgehaniṣkuṭārthāya tad ayaṃ nīyatāṃ taruḥ ।। satye yathā tvam ity uktaṃ tvayā kṛṣṇāsakṛt priyam ।। tad astu pārijāto ayaṃ mama gehavibhūṣaṇam ।।
sapatnīnām ahaṃ madhye śobheyam iti kāmaye ।। tathā xxx kā bhūtvā ratim utpādayāmi te ।। rugmiṇīprabhṛtibhyas te devībhyaś cātisundarī ।। etena pārijātena bhavāmi tava karmaṇā ।।
yathāhaṃ mādhava vibho tathā mām adhikāṃ kuru ।। āropayām āsa haris tam ūcur vanarakṣiṇaḥ ।। pārijātaṃ na govinda hartum arhasi pādapam ।। utpanno devarājāya dattaḥ so api dadau punaḥ ।।
mahiṣyai sumahābhāga devyai śacyai kutūhalāt ।। utpādito ayaṃ na kṣemī gṛhītvainaṃ gamiṣyasi ।। mauḍhyāt prārthayase kṣemī gṛhītvainaṃ hi ko vrajet ।। vajrodyatakaraṃ śakram anuyāsyanti cāmarāḥ ।।
vipākakaṭu yat karma tan na śaṃsanti paṇḍitāḥ ।। kā śacī pārijātasya ko vā śakraḥ surādhipaḥ ।। samutpannaḥ surāḥ kasmād eko gṛhṇāti vāsavaḥ ।। sāmānyaḥ sarvalokasya pārijātas tathā drumaḥ ।।
tat kathyatām alaṃ kṣāntyā satyā hārayati drumam ।। satyabhāmā vadaty etad iti garvoddhatākṣaram ।। madbhartur harato vṛkṣaṃ tat kāraya nivāraṇam ।। pārijātaṃ tathāpy enaṃ mānuṣī hārayāmi te ।।
śacī cotsāhayām āsa tridaśādhipatiṃ patim ।। prayayau pārijātārtham indro yodhayituṃ dvija ।। babhūvus tridaśāḥ sajjāḥ śakre vajrakare sthite ।। śakraṃ devaparīvāraṃ yuddhāya samupasthitam ।।
mumoca ca śaravrātaṃ sahasrāyutasaṃmitam ।। mumucus tridaśāḥ sarve astraśastrāṇy anekaśaḥ ।। ciccheda līlayaiveśo jagatāṃ madhusūdanaḥ ।। cakāra khaṇḍaśaś cañcvā bālapannagadehavat ।।
pṛthivyāṃ pātayām āsa bhagavān devakīsutaḥ ।। cakāra śaurir arkaṃ ca dṛṣṭidṛṣṭaṃ hataujasam ।। cakravicchinnaśūlāgrā rudrā bhuvi nipātitāḥ ।। śārṅgeṇa preritair astā vyomni śālmalitūlavat ।।
bhakṣayaṃs tāḍayan devān dārayaṃś ca cacāra vai ।। parasparaṃ vavarṣāte dhārābhir iva toyadau ।। devaiḥ samastair yuyudhe śakreṇa ca janārdanaḥ ।। jagrāha vāsavo vajraṃ kṛṣṇaś cakraṃ sudarśanam ।।
vajracakradharau dṛṣṭvā devarājajanārdanau ।। na mumoca tathā cakraṃ śakraṃ tiṣṭheti cābravīt ।। satyabhāmābravīd vīraṃ palāyanaparāyaṇam ।। pārijātasragābhogā tvām upasthāsyate śacī ।।
apaśyato yathā pūrvaṃ praṇayābhyāgatāṃ śacīm ।। nīyatāṃ pārijāto ayaṃ devāḥ santu gatavyathāḥ ।। na dadarśa gṛhāyātām upacāreṇa māṃ śacī ।। tataḥ kṛtavatī śakra bhavatā saha vigraham ।।
rūpeṇa garvitā sā tu bhartrā strī kā na garvitā ।। prāha cainām alaṃ caṇḍi sakhi khedātivistaraiḥ ।। jitasya tena me vrīḍā jāyate viśvarūpiṇā ।। tenodbhavapralayapālanakāraṇena vrīḍā kathaṃ bhavati devi nirākṛtasya ।।
tam ajam akṛtam īśaṃ śāśvataṃ svecchayainaṃ jagadupakṛtimartyaṃ ko vijetuṃ samarthaḥ ।। prahasya bhāvagambhīram uvācendraṃ dvijottama ।। kṣantavyaṃ bhavataivaitad aparādhakṛtaṃ mama ।। gṛhīto ayaṃ mayā śakra satyāvacanakāraṇāt ।।
tavaivaitat praharaṇaṃ śakra vairividāraṇam ।। jānīmas tvāṃ bhagavato na tu sūkṣmavido vayam ।। jagataḥ śalyaniṣkarṣaṃ karoṣy asurasūdana ।। martyaloke tvayā mukte nāyaṃ saṃsthāsyate bhuvi ।।
devadeva jagannātha kṛṣṇa viṣṇo mahābhuja ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇe śārṅgāsidhara mādhava ।। prasaktaiḥ siddhagandharvaiḥ stūyamānaḥ surarṣibhiḥ ।। āgamiṣyati deveśa svayam eva triviṣṭapam ।।
harṣam utpādayām āsa dvārakāvāsināṃ dvija ।। niṣkuṭe sthāpayām āsa pārijātaṃ mahātarum ।। vāsyate yasya puṣpotthagandhenorvī triyojanam ।। dadṛśuḥ pādape tasmin kurvato mukhadarśanam ।।
striyaś ca kṛṣṇo jagrāha narakasya parigrahān ।। vibhajya pradadau kṛṣṇo bāndhavānāṃ mahāmatiḥ ।। tāḥ kanyā narakeṇāsan sarvato yāḥ samāhṛtāḥ ।। jagrāha vidhivat pāṇīn pṛthaggeheṣu dharmataḥ ।।
tāvanti cakre rūpāṇi bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ ।। mamaiva pāṇigrahaṇaṃ bhagavān kṛtavān iti ।। uvāsa vipra sarvāsāṃ viśvarūpadharo hariḥ ।। bhānuṃ bhaimarikaṃ caiva satyabhāmā vyajāyata ।।
babhūvur jāmbavatyāṃ ca sāmbādyā bāhuśālinaḥ ।। saṃgrāmajitpradhānās tu śaibyāyāś cābhavan sutāḥ ।। avāpa lakṣmaṇā putrāḥ kālindyāś ca śrutādayaḥ ।। aṣṭāyutāni putrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇāṃ śataṃ tathā ।।
pradyumnād aniruddho abhūd vajras tasmād ajāyata ।। bāṇasya tanayām ūṣām upayeme dvijottama ।। chinnaṃ sahasraṃ bāhūnāṃ yatra bāṇasya cakriṇā ।। kathaṃ kṣayaṃ ca bāṇasya bāhūnāṃ kṛtavān hariḥ ।।
mahat kautūhalaṃ jātaṃ kathāṃ śrotum imāṃ hareḥ ।। krīḍantīm upalakṣyoccaiḥ spṛhāṃ cakre tadāśrayām ।। alam atyarthatāpena bhartrā tvam api raṃsyase ।। ko vā bhartā mamety enāṃ punar apy āha pārvatī ।।
kariṣyati sa te bhartā rājaputri bhaviṣyati ।। tathaivābhibhavaṃ cakre rāgaṃ cakre ca tatra sā ।। kva gato asīti nirlajjā maitreyoktavatī sakhīm ।। tasyāḥ sakhy abhavat sā ca prāha ko ayaṃ tvayocyate ।।
tadā viśvāsam ānīya sarvam evābhyavādayat ।। devyā tathaiva tatprāptau yo abhyupāyaḥ kuruṣva tam ।। durvijñeyam idaṃ vastu prāptuṃ cāpi na śakyate ।। tathāpi kaścit kartavyaḥ upakāraḥ priye tava ।।
saptāṣṭadinaparyantaṃ kālaṃ tāvat pratīkṣyatām ।। ity uktvābhyantaragṛhaṃ gatvopāyam athākarot ।। manuṣyāṃś cābhilikhyāsyai citralekhā vyadarśayat ।। manuṣyeṣu dadau dṛṣṭiṃ teṣv apy andhakavṛṣṇiṣu ।।
pradyumnadarśane vrīḍādṛṣṭiṃ ninye anyato dvija ।। dṛṣṭvātyarthavilāsinyā lajjā kvāpi nirākṛtā ।। so ayaṃ so ayam itīty ukte tayā sā yogagāminī ।। b citralekhābravīd enām uṣāṃ bāṇasutāṃ tadā ।। b
ayaṃ kṛṣṇasya pautras te bhartā devyā prasāditaḥ ।। b aniruddha iti khyātaḥ prakhyātaḥ priyadarśanaḥ ।। b prāpnoṣi yadi bhartāram imaṃ prāptaṃ tvayākhilam ।। b duṣpraveśā purī pūrvaṃ dvārakā haripālitā ।। b
tathāpi yatnād bhartāram ānayiṣyāmi te sakhi ।। b rahasyam etad vaktavyaṃ na kasyacid api priye ।। b acirād āgamiṣyāmi sahasva virahaṃ mama ।। b yayau dvāravatīm ūṣāṃ samāśvāsya tataḥ sakhīm ।। d
deva bāhusahasreṇa nirviṇṇo ahaṃ vināhavam ।। bhaviṣyati vinā yuddhaṃ bhārāya mama kiṃ bhujaiḥ ।। piśitāśijanānandaṃ prāpsyase tvaṃ tadā raṇam ।। bhagnaṃ ca dhvajam ālokya hṛṣṭo harṣāntaraṃ yayau ।।
aniruddham athāninye citralekhā varāpsarāḥ ।। vijñāya rakṣiṇo gatvā śaśaṃsur daityabhūpateḥ ।। jaghāna parighaṃ loham ādāya paravīrahā ।। yudhyamāno yathāśakti yadā vīryeṇa nirjitaḥ ।।
tatas taṃ pannagāstreṇa babandha yadunandanam ।। yadūnām ācacakṣe taṃ baddhaṃ bāṇena nāradaḥ ।। yoṣitā pratyayaṃ jagmur yādavā nāmarair iti ।। balapradyumnasahito bāṇasya prayayau puram ।।
yayau bāṇapurābhyāśaṃ nītvā tān saṃkṣayaṃ hariḥ ।। bāṇarakṣārtham atyarthaṃ yuyudhe śārṅgadhanvanā ।। avāpa baladevo api śramam āmīlitekṣaṇaḥ ।। vaiṣṇavena jvareṇāśu kṛṣṇadehān nirākṛtaḥ ।।
taṃ vīkṣya kṣamyatām asyety āha devaḥ pitāmahaḥ ।। ātmany eva layaṃ ninye bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ ।। evam ukto bhagavatā praṇipatya jvaro abravīt ।। devadeva mahādeva praṇatārtiharācyuta ।।
vijvarās te bhaviṣyantīty uktvā cainaṃ yayau jvaraḥ ।। dānavānāṃ balaṃ viṣṇuś cūrṇayām āsa līlayā ।। yuyudhe śaṃkaraś caiva kārtikeyaś ca śauriṇā ।। cukṣubhuḥ sakalā lokāḥ yatrāstrāṃśupratāpitāḥ ।।
menire tridaśā yatra vartamāne mahāhave ।। devāś ca bhayasaṃtrastāḥ prārthayantas tato harim ।। prārthitaḥ śaṃkaraś cāpi parājayaṃ gṛhītavān ।। tataḥ praṇeśur daiteyāḥ pramathāś ca samantataḥ ।।
na śaśāka tadā yoddhuṃ kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā ।। kṛṣṇahuṃkāranirdhūtaśaktiś cāpayayau guhaḥ ।। pramathānāṃ tataḥ sainyaṃ bāṇavarṣād anīnaśat ।। nīte pramathasainye ca saṃkṣayaṃ śārṅgadhanvanā ।।
bāṇas tatrāyayau yoddhuṃ kṛṣṇakārṣṇibalaiḥ saha ।। vivyādha bāṇaiḥ prabhraśya dharmataś cāpalāyata ।। balaṃ balena dadṛśe bāṇo bāṇaiś ca cakriṇā ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇasya bāṇena yuddham āsīt samantataḥ ।।
bibheda keśavaṃ bāṇo bāṇaṃ vivyādha cakrabhṛt ।। parasparaṃ kṣatiparau paramāmarṣiṇau dvija ।। prācuryeṇa harir bāṇaṃ hantuṃ cakre tato manaḥ ।। jagrāha daityacakrārir hariś cakraṃ sudarśanam ।।
nagnā daiteyavidyābhūt koṭavī purato hareḥ ।। mumoca bāṇam uddiśya chettuṃ bāhuvanaṃ ripoḥ ।। chedaṃ cakre asurāpāstaśastraughakṣapaṇādṛtam ।। mumukṣur bāṇanāśāya vijñātas tripuradviṣā ।।
vilokya bāṇaṃ dordaṇḍacchedāsṛksrāvavarṣiṇam ।। pareśaṃ paramātmānam anādinidhanaṃ param ।। līleyaṃ sarvabhūtasya tava ceṣṭopalakṣaṇā ।। tat tvayā nānṛtaṃ kāryaṃ yan mayā vyāhṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।।
mayā dattavaro daityas tatas tvāṃ kṣamayāmy aham ।। prasannavadano bhūtvā gatāmarṣo asuraṃ prati ।। tvadvākyagauravād etan mayā cakraṃ nivartitam ।। matto avibhinnam ātmānaṃ draṣṭum arhasi śaṃkara ।।
yo ahaṃ sa tvaṃ jagac cedaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।। b matto nānyad aśeṣaṃ yat tat tvaṃ jñātum ihārhasi ।। b avidyāmohitātmānaḥ puruṣā bhinnadarśinaḥ ।। d vadanti bhedaṃ paśyanti cāvayor antaraṃ hara ।।
prasanno ahaṃ gamiṣyāmi tvaṃ gaccha vṛṣabhadhvaja ।। tadbandhaphaṇino neśur garuḍānilaśoṣitāḥ ।। ājagmur dvārakāṃ rāmakārṣṇidāmodarāḥ purīm ।। putrapautraiḥ parivṛtas tatra reme janārdanaḥ ।।
devībhiḥ satataṃ vipra bhūbhārataraṇecchayā ।। jigāya śakraṃ śarvaṃ ca sarvān devāṃś ca līlayā ।। tat kathyatāṃ mahābhāga paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me ।। narāvatāre kṛṣṇena dagdhā vārāṇasī yathā ।।
avatīrṇas tvam ity ukto janair ajñānamohitaiḥ ।। naṣṭasmṛtis tataḥ sarvaṃ viṣṇucihnam acīkarat ।। tyaktvā cakrādikaṃ cihnaṃ madīyaṃ nāma cātmanaḥ ।। ātmano jīvitārthāya tato me praṇatiṃ vraja ।।
nijacihnam ahaṃ cakraṃ samutsrakṣye tvayīti vai ।। jñātas tvadvākyasadbhāvo yat kāryaṃ tad vidhīyatām ।। samutsrakṣyāmi te cakraṃ nijacihnam asaṃśayam ।। saṃpādayiṣye śvas tubhyaṃ tad apy eṣo avilambitam ।।
yathā tvatto bhayaṃ bhūyo na me kiṃcid bhaviṣyati ।। garutmantam athāruhya tvaritaṃ tatpuraṃ yayau ।। sarvasainyaparīvāraḥ pārṣṇigrāha upāyayau ।। pauṇḍrako vāsudevo asau keśavābhimukhaṃ yayau ।।
cakrahastaṃ gadākhaḍgabāhuṃ pāṇigatāmbujam ।। vakṣaḥsthale kṛtaṃ cāsya śrīvatsaṃ dadṛśe hariḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā taṃ bhāvagambhīraṃ jahāsa garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। nistriṃśarṣṭigadāśūlaśaktikārmukaśālinā ।।
gadācakranipātaiś ca sūdayām āsa tadbalam ।। uvāca pauṇḍrakaṃ mūḍham ātmacihnopalakṣaṇam ।। samutsṛjeti cihnāni tat te saṃpādayāmy aham ।। garutmān eṣa nirdiṣṭaḥ samārohatu te dhvajam ।।
pothito gadayā bhagno garutmāṃś ca garutmatā ।। yuyudhe vāsudevena mitrasyāpacitau sthitaḥ ।। kāśipuryāṃ sa cikṣepa kurvaṃl lokasya vismayam ।। punar dvāravatīṃ prāpto reme svargagato yathā ।।
janaḥ kim etad ity āha kenety atyantavismitaḥ ।। purohitena sahitas toṣayām āsa śaṃkaram ।। varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti tadā taṃ provāca nṛpātmajam ।। samuttiṣṭhatu kṛṣṇasya tvatprasādān maheśvara ।।
mahākṛtyā samuttasthau tasyaivāgniniveśanāt ।। kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇeti kupitā kṛtyā dvāravatīṃ yayau ।। yayau śaraṇyaṃ jagatāṃ śaraṇaṃ madhusūdanam ।। utpāditā mahākṛtyety avagamyātha cakriṇā ।।
cakram utsṛṣṭam akṣeṣu krīḍāsaktena līlayā ।। kṛtyām anujagāmāśu viṣṇucakraṃ sudarśanam ।। nanāśa veginī vegāt tad apy anujagāma tām ।। viṣṇucakrapratihataprabhāvā munisattama ।।
samastaśastrāstrayutaṃ cakrasyābhimukhaṃ yayau ।। kṛtyāgarbhām aśeṣāṃ tāṃ tadā vārāṇasīṃ purīm ।। aśeṣakośakoṣṭhāṃ tāṃ durnirīkṣyāṃ surair api ।। dadāha tad dhareś cakraṃ sakalām eva tāṃ purīm ।।
tac cakraṃ prasphuraddīpti viṣṇor abhyāyayau karam ।। śrotuṃ parākramaṃ brahman tan mamākhyātum arhasi ।। tat kathyatāṃ mahābhāga yad anyat kṛtavān balaḥ ।। anantenāprameyena śeṣeṇa dharaṇībhṛtā ।।
balād ādattavān vīraḥ sāmbo jāmbavatīsutaḥ ।। bhīṣmadroṇādayaś cainaṃ babandhur yudhi nirjitam ।। maitreya cakruś cakruś ca tān nihantuṃ mahodyamam ।। mokṣyanti te madvacanād yāsyāmy eko hi kauravān ।।
bāhyopavanamadhye abhūn na viveśa ca tat puram ।। gām arghyam udakaṃ caiva rāmāya pratyavedayan ।। ājñāpayaty ugrasenaḥ sāmbam āśu vimuñcata ।। karṇaduryodhanādyāś ca cukrudhur dvijasattama ।।
arājyārhaṃ yador vaṃśam avekṣya musalāyudham ।। ājñāṃ kurukulotthānāṃ yādavaḥ kaḥ pradāsyati ।। tad alaṃ pāṇḍuraiś chatrair nṛpayogyair viḍambitaiḥ ।। vimokṣyāmo na bhavato nograsenasya śāsanāt ।।
nanāma sā kṛtā keyam ājñā svāmini bhṛtyataḥ ।। ko doṣo bhavatāṃ nītir yat prītyā nāvalokitā ।। premṇaitan naitad asmākaṃ kulād yuṣmatkulocitam ।। kṛtaikaniścayās tūrṇaṃ viviśur gajasāhvayam ।।
utthāya pārṣṇyā vasudhāṃ jaghāna sa halāyudhaḥ ।। āsphoṭayām āsa tadā diśaḥ śabdena pūrayan ।। uvāca cātitāmrākṣo bhṛkuṭīkuṭilānanaḥ ।। ugrasenasya yenājñāṃ manyante adyāpi laṅghanam ।।
ājñāṃ pratīcched dharmeṇa saha devaiḥ śacīpatiḥ ।। b mārutasya mate sthitvā tuṣṭe rājñāṃ sabhāṃ dadau ।। b samadhyāste sudharmāṃ tām ugrasenaḥ śacīpateḥ ।। d ugrasenaḥ samadhyāste sudharmāṃ na śacīpatiḥ ।।
bibharti yasya bhṛtyānāṃ so apy eṣāṃ na mahīpatiḥ ।। adya niṣkauravām urvīṃ kṛtvā yāsyāmi tatpurīm ।। duḥśāsanādīn bhūriṃ ca bhūriśravasam eva ca ।। yamajau kauravāṃś cānyān hatvā sāśvarathadvipān ।।
dvārakām ugrasenādīn gatvā drakṣyāmi bāndhavān ।। athavā kauravādhānīṃ samastaiḥ kurubhiḥ saha ।। b bhārāvataraṇe śīghraṃ devarājena coditaḥ ।। b bhāgīrathyāṃ kṣipāmy āśu nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam ।। d
prākāravapre vinyasya cakarṣa musalāyudhaḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā saṃkṣubdhahṛdayāś cukruśuḥ sarvakauravāḥ ।। upasaṃhriyatāṃ kopaḥ prasīda musalāyudha ।। avijñātaprabhāvāṇāṃ kṣamyatām aparādhinām ।।
niṣkramya svapurāt tūrṇaṃ kauravā munipuṃgava ।। kṣāntam eva mayety āha balo balavatāṃ varaḥ ।। eṣa prabhāvo rāmasya balaśauryopalakṣaṇaḥ ।। preṣayām āsur udvāhadhanabhāryāsamanvitam ।।
kṛtaṃ yad anyat tenābhūt tad api śrūyatāṃ tvayā ।। sakhābhavan mahāvīryo dvivido nāma vānaraḥ ।। narakaṃ hatavān kṛṣṇo devarājena coditaḥ ।। yajñavidhvaṃsanaṃ kurvan martyalokakṣayaṃ tathā ।।
bibheda sādhumaryādāṃ kṣayaṃ cakre ca dehinām ।। kvacic ca parvatākṣepair grāmādīn samacūrṇayat ।। punaś cārṇavamadhyasthaḥ kṣobhayām āsa sāgaram ।। plāvayaṃs tīrajān grāmān purādīn ativegavān ।।
luṭhan bhramaṇasaṃmardaiḥ saṃcūrṇayati vānaraḥ ।। niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāraṃ maitreyāsīt suduḥkhitam ।। revatī ca mahābhāgā tathaivānyā varastriyaḥ ।। reme yaduvaraśreṣṭhaḥ kubera iva mandare ।।
musalaṃ ca cakārāsya saṃmukhaṃ saviḍambanam ।। pānapūrṇāṃś ca karakāñ cikṣepāhatya vai padā ।। tathāpi tam avajñāya cakre kilakilādhvanim ।। so api śailaśilāṃ bhīmāṃ jagrāha plavagottamaḥ ।।
bibheda yādavaśreṣṭhaḥ sā papāta mahītale ।। vegenāgamya roṣeṇa talenorasy atāḍayat ।। papāta rudhirodgārī dvividaḥ kṣīṇajīvitaḥ ।। maitreya śatadhā vajrivajreṇeva hi tāḍitam ।।
praśaśaṃsus tathābhyetya sādhv etat te mahat kṛtam ।। jagan nirākṛtaṃ vīra diṣṭyā sa kṣayam āgataḥ ।। ity uktvā divam ājagmur devā hṛṣṭāḥ saguhyakāḥ ।। karmāṇy aparimeyāni śeṣasya dharaṇībhṛtaḥ ।।
cakre duṣṭakṣitīśānāṃ tathaiva jagataḥ kṛte ।। avatārayām āsa hariḥ samastākṣauhiṇīvadhāt ।। kṛtvā bhārāvataraṇaṃ bhuvo hatvākhilān nṛpān ।। b vyakto mānuṣyakaṃ bhāvaṃ devadevo janārdanaḥ ।। b
kṛtvā cānyāni kāryāṇi devānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। b duryodhanasya viprarṣe yudhiṣṭhirapurogamaiḥ ।। b pāṇḍavair bhedam utpannam upekṣeta vibhus tadā ।। b anyamodachataḥ [??] kṛṣṇas tato vairam akārayat ।। b
tatra hatvā kurūn sarvān pāṇḍaveyaiḥ parasparam ।। b jagāma nirvṛtiṃ devo jagatāṃ patir īśvaraḥ ।। b akṣohinyo hatās tatra aṣṭādaśa mahāmune ।। b śāpavyājena viprāṇām upasaṃhṛtavān kulam ।। d
sāṃśo viṣṇumayaṃ sthānaṃ praviveśa punar nijam ।। kathaṃ ca mānuṣaṃ deham utsasarja janārdanaḥ ।। viśvāmitras tathā kaṇvo nāradaś ca mahāmuniḥ ।। b durvāsādyāś ca ṛṣayas tīrthe piṇḍārake mune ।। b
piṇḍārake mahātīrthe dṛṣṭā yadukumārakaiḥ ।। d sāmbaṃ jāmbavatīputraṃ bhūṣayitvā striyaṃ yathā ।। iyaṃ strī putrakāmasya babhroḥ kiṃ janayiṣyati ।। divyajñānopapannās te vipralabdhāḥ kumārakaiḥ ।। b
munayaḥ kupitāḥ procur musalaṃ janayiṣyati ।। d sarvayādavasaṃhārakāraṇaṃ balavattaram ।। d yenākhilakulotsādo yādavānāṃ bhaviṣyati ।। f kṛtrimas trinābhitalaṃ bhītvādyaivaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
ugrasenāya musalaṃ jajñe sāmbasya codarāt ।। jajñe sa cairakāś cūrṇaḥ prakṣiptas tair mahodadhau ।। khaṇḍaṃ cūrṇayituṃ śekur naikaṃ te tomarākṛti ।। ghātitasyodarāt tasya lubdho jagrāha taṃ jarāḥ ।।
naicchat tad anyathākartuṃ vidhinā yat samāhitam ।। rahasy evam ahaṃ dūtaḥ prahito bhagavan suraiḥ ।। vijñāpayati vaḥ śakras tad idaṃ śrūyatāṃ prabho ।। bhagavān avatīrṇo atra tridaśaiḥ saṃprasāditaḥ ।।
tvayā sanāthās tridaśā bhavantu tridive sadā ।। idānīṃ gamyatāṃ svargo bhavatā yadi rocate ।। tat sthīyatāṃ yathākālam ākhyeyam anujīvibhiḥ ।। prārabdha eva hi mayā yādavānām api kṣayaḥ ।।
avatārya karomy etat saptarātreṇa satvaraḥ ।। yādavān upasaṃhṛtya yāsyāmi tridaśālayam ।। prāpta evāsmi mantavyo devendreṇa tathā suraiḥ ।। kṣites tebhyaḥ kumāro api yadūnāṃ nāpacīyate ।।
yāsyāmy amaralokasya pālanāya bravīhi tān ।। maitreya divyayā gatyā devarājāntikaṃ yayau ।। dadarśa dvārakāpuryāṃ vināśāya divāniśam ।। mahotpātāñ chamāyaiṣāṃ prabhāsaṃ yāma mā ciram ।।
ity uktavati govinde yātukāme divaṃ punaḥ ।। evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena yādavapravaras tataḥ ।। manye kulam idaṃ sarvaṃ bhagavān saṃhariṣyati ।। nāśāyāsya nimittāni kulasyācyuta lakṣaye ।।
naranārāyaṇasthāne tatpāvitamahītale ।। ahaṃ svargaṃ gamiṣyāmi upasaṃhṛtya vai kulam ।। dvārakāṃ ca mayā tyaktāṃ samudraḥ plāvayiṣyati ।। madveśma caitaṃ muktvaiva bhayān matto jalāśayaḥ ।।
tatra saṃnihitaś cāhaṃ bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। naranārāyaṇasthānaṃ keśavenānumoditaḥ ।। prabhāsaṃ prayayuḥ sārdhaṃ kṛṣṇarāmādibhir dvija ।। cakrus tatra mudā pānaṃ vāsudevānumoditāḥ ।।
ativādendhano jajñe kalahāgniḥ kṣayāvahaḥ ।। svaṃ svaṃ tu bhujyatāṃ teṣāṃ kalaho nirnimittayāḥ ।। saṃgharṣo vā dvijaśreṣṭha tan mamākhyātum arhasi ।। mṛṣṭaṃ madīyam annaṃ te na mṛṣṭam iti bhāṣatām ।।
mṛṣṭāmṛṣṭakathā jajñe saṃgharṣakalahau tadā ।। tataś cānyonyam abhyetya krodhasaṃraktalocanāḥ ।। kṣīṇaśastrāś ca jagṛhuḥ pratyāsannām athairakām ।। tayā parasparaṃ jaghnuḥ saṃprahāre sudāruṇe ।।
aniruddhādayaś cānye pṛthur vipṛthur eva ca ।। erakārūpibhir vajrais te nijaghnuḥ parasparam ।। sahāyaṃ menire prāptaṃ te nijaghnuḥ parasparam ।। vadhāya so api musalaṃ muṣṭir loham abhūt tadā ।।
jaghnuś ca sahasābhyetya tathānye vai parasparam ।। paśyato dārukasyāśu hṛto aśvair dvijasattama ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ hariṃ kṛtvā jagmur ādityavartmanā ।। ṛte kṛṣṇaṃ mahābāhuṃ dārukaṃ ca mahāmune ।।
dadṛśāte mukhāc cāsya niṣkrāmantaṃ mahoragam ।। prayayāv arṇavaṃ siddhaiḥ pūjyamānas tathoragaiḥ ।। praviveśa ca tattoyaṃ pūjitaḥ pannagottamaiḥ ।। idaṃ sarvaṃ tvam ācakṣva vasudevograsenayoḥ ।।
yoge sthitvāham apy etat parityakṣye kalevaram ।। yathemāṃ nagarīṃ sarvāṃ samudraḥ plāvayiṣyati ।। na stheyaṃ dvārakāmadhye niṣkrānte tatra pāṇḍave ।। tenaiva saha gantavyaṃ yatra yāti sa kauravaḥ ।।
pālanīyas tvayā śaktyā jano ayaṃ matparigrahaḥ ।। gṛhītvā yātu vajraś ca yadurājo bhaviṣyati ।। pradakṣiṇaṃ ca bahuśaḥ kṛtvā prāyād yathoditam ।। ānināya mahābuddhir vajraṃ cakre tathā nṛpam ।।
brahmātmani samāropya sarvabhūteṣv adhārayat ।। niṣprapañce mahābhāga saṃyojyātmānam ātmani ।। turyāvasthasalīlaṃ ca śete sma puruṣottamaḥ ।। yogayukto abhavat pādaṃ kṛtvā jānuni sattama ।।
musalāvaśeṣalohaikasāyakanyastatomaraḥ ।। tale vivyādha tenaiva tomareṇa dvijottama ।। praṇipatyāha caivainaṃ prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ ।। kṣamyatāṃ nātmapāpena dagdhaṃ māṃ dagdhum arhasi ।।
gaccha tvaṃ matprasādena lubdha svargaṃ surāspadam ।। āruhya prayayau svargaṃ lubdhakas tatprasādataḥ ।। brahmabhūte avyaye acintye vāsudevamaye amale ।। tatyāja mānuṣaṃ deham atītya trividhāṃ gatim ।।
saṃskāraṃ lambhayām āsa tathānyeṣām anukramāt ।। upaguhya harer dehaṃ viviśus tā hutāśanam ।। viveśa jvalitaṃ vahniṃ tatsaṅgāhlādaśītalam ।। devakī rohiṇī caiva viviśur jātavedasam ।।
niścakrāma janaṃ sarvaṃ gṛhītvā vajram eva ca ।। vajraṃ janaṃ ca kaunteyaḥ pālayañ chanakair yayau ।। svargaṃ jagāma maitreya pārijātaś ca pādapaḥ ।। tasminn evāvatīrṇo ayaṃ kālakāyo balī kaliḥ ।।
yadudevagṛhaṃ tv ekaṃ nāplāvayata sāgaraḥ ।। nityaṃ saṃnihitas tatra bhagavān keśavo yataḥ ।। viṣṇukrīḍānvitaṃ sthānaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāpāt pramucyate ।। cakāra vāsaṃ sarvasya janasya munisattama ।।
dṛṣṭvā striyo nīyamānā dasyūnāṃ nihateśvarāḥ ।। ābhīrā mantrayām āsuḥ sametyātyantadurmadāḥ ।। nayaty asmān atikramya dhig etad bhavatāṃ balam ।। karṇādīṃś ca na jānāti balaṃ grāmanivāsinām ।।
sarvān evāvajānāti kiṃ vo bāhubhir unnataiḥ ।। sahasraśo abhyadhāvanta taṃ janaṃ nihateśvaram ।। nivartadhvam adharmajñā yadi na stha mumūrṣavaḥ ।। strījanaṃ caiva maitreya viṣvaksenaparigraham ।।
āropayitum ārebhe na śaśāka ca vīryavān ।। na sasmāra tathāstrāṇi cintayann api pāṇḍavaḥ ।। tvagbhedaṃ te paraṃ cakrur astā gāṇḍīvadhanvanā ।। yudhyataḥ saha gopālair arjunasya bhavakṣaye ।।
yan mayā śarasaṃghātaiḥ sakalā bhūbhṛto jitāḥ ।। ābhīrair apakṛṣyanta kāmāc cānyāḥ pravavrajuḥ ।। jaghāna dasyūṃs te cāsya prahārāñ jahasur mune ।। jagmur ādāya te mlecchāḥ samastā munisattama ।।
aho bhagavatā tena mukto asmīti ruroda vai ।। sarvam ekapade naṣṭaṃ dānam aśrotriye yathā ।। yad asāmarthyayukte api nīcavarge jayapradam ।। puṇyenaiva vinā tena gataṃ sarvam asāratām ।।
vinā tena yad ābhīrair jito ahaṃ katham anyathā ।। cakāra tatra rājānaṃ vajraṃ yādavanandanam ।। tam upetya mahābhāgaṃ vinayenābhyavādayat ।। uvāca pārthaṃ vicchāyaḥ katham atyantam īdṛśaḥ ।।
dṛḍhāśābhaṅgaduḥkhīva bhraṣṭacchāyo asi sāmpratam ।। viṣṇuṃ natvā sarvakāmapradaṃ bho tenedaṃ te rūpam īdṛg vibhāti ।। agamyastrīratir vā tvaṃ tenāsi vigataprabhaḥ ।। kiṃ vā kṛpaṇavittāni hṛtāni bhavatārjuna ।।
duṣṭacakṣurhato vāpi niḥśrīkaḥ katham anyathā ।। tenātīvāsi vicchāyo nyūnair vā yudhi nirjitaḥ ।। prokto yathāvad ācaṣṭe vyāsāyātmaparābhavam ।। yā śrīś chāyā ca naḥ so asmān parityajya harir gataḥ ।।
hīnā vayaṃ mune tena jātās tṛṇamayā iva ।। sāratā yābhavan mūrtā sa gataḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। na tatyāja sa govindas tyaktvāsmān bhagavān gataḥ ।। yatprabhāvena nirdagdhāḥ sa kṛṣṇas tyaktavān bhuvam ।।
vibhāti tāta naiko ahaṃ virahe tasya cakriṇaḥ ।। vinā tenādya kṛṣṇena gopālair asmi nirjitaḥ ।। gataṃ tena vinābhīrair laguḍais tannirākṛtam ।। yatato mama nītāni dasyubhir laguḍāyudhaiḥ ।।
hṛtaṃ yaṣṭipraharaṇaiḥ paribhūya balaṃ mama ।। nīcāvamānapaṅkāṅkī nirlajjo asmi pitāmaha ।। kṛṣṇaśabdasya bhājo vai traya eva mahāmune ।। @ ahaṃ ca tvaṃ ca devaś ca yathārhaṃ kṛtavān vibhuḥ ।। @
kṛṣṇe tasmin mahābāhau mahātmani mahīpatau ।। @ mama cittaṃ yathāśaktaṃ nānyo vedeha vedmy aham ।। @ bhaktānnapānakrīḍābhir bhūmau asau devakīsutaḥ ।। @ kṛtavān yo mama prītiṃ saevākarṣati me manaḥ ।। @
kalevaram idaṃ tyakṣye pāsye vā viṣam ulbaṇam ।। @ pate vā parvatāgrāt tu jalaṃ vā praviśe mune ।। @ pravekṣyāmy agnim ujvālya vatsye prāyopaveśanam ।। @ taṃ vinā devadeveśam idaṃ me pāñcabhautikam ।। @
śarīram idam atyugraṃ kaṭhinaṃ kliṣṭakalpanam ।। @ amedhyamūtrasaṃpūrṇabhājanaṃ paricāpalam ।। @ atikaṣṭaṃ kaṣṭataraṃ jīvituṃ notsahe kṣaṇam ।। @ sarvaṃ śūnyam idaṃ viśvaṃ pratibhāti mahāmune ।। @
śaṅkhacakragadāśārṅganandakāyudhadhāriṇam ।। @ vinā taṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ devadevaṃ khagadhvajam ।। @ harivirañciharayor īśaṃ citradhvajaṃ mune ।। @ apaśyamāno jīvāmi katham atra mahāmune ।। @
tvam evetthaṃ x maharṣer āvayo prāṇasaṃsthitim ।। @ kathaṃ tena vinā jiṣṇuṃ viṣṇum atyadbhutaṃ mune ।। @ yat sarvaṃ tadīyam iti loke viśrutam adbhutam ।। @ madīyam eva jānāti satye naiva ca me śape ।। @
vinā tenaiva kṛṣṇena kṛṣṇe jiṣṇo mahadbhutam ।। @ krūre asmiñ jagati krūraḥ soḍhuṃ jīvaṃ mahāmune ।। @ na śaknomi hareḥ padbhyāṃ śape tasya mahātmanaḥ ।। @ avehi sarvabhūteṣu kālasya gatir īdṛśī ।।
kālamūlam idaṃ jñātvā bhava sthairyadhano arjuna ।। devā manuṣyāḥ paśavas taravaḥ sasarīsṛpāḥ ।। kālātmakam idaṃ sarvaṃ jñātvā śamam avāpnuhi ।। kālasvarūpī bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ kamalalocanaḥ ।।
bhārāvatārakāryārtham avatīrṇaḥ sa medinīm ।। tadartham avatīrṇo asau kālarūpī janārdanaḥ ।। vṛṣṇyandhakakulaṃ sarvaṃ tathā pārthopasaṃhṛtam ।। ato gataḥ sa bhagavān kṛtakṛtyo yathecchayā ।।
ante antāya samartho ayaṃ sāmprataṃ vai yathā kṛtam ।। bhavanti bhavakāleṣu puruṣāṇāṃ parākramāḥ ।। teṣām arjuna kālotthaḥ kiṃ nyūnābhibhavo na saḥ ।। vaikuṇṭhād āgato viṣṇus tam eva gatavān prabhuḥ ।।
tasmāt pārtha na śocas tvam aśocyo bhagavān hariḥ ।। tvattas tathaiva bhavato dasyubhyo ante tadudbhavaḥ ।। karoti sarvabhūtānāṃ nāśaṃ cānte jagatpatiḥ ।। tavodbhave sa kaunteya sahāyo abhūj janārdanaḥ ।। b
bhāvābhāve ca sa tadā sahayogaṃ janārdanaḥ ।। b bhavānte tvadvipakṣās te keśavenāvalokitāḥ ।। d ābhīrebhyaś ca bhavataḥ kaḥ śraddadhyāt parābhavam ।। tvayā yat kauravā dhvastā yad ābhīrair bhavāñ jitaḥ ।।
tad apy ahaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ kathayāmi tavārjuna ।। bahūn varṣagaṇān pārtha gṛṇan brahma sanātanam ।। babhūva tatra gacchantyo dadṛśus taṃ surastriyaḥ ।। tuṣṭuvus taṃ mahātmānaṃ praśaśaṃsuś ca pāṇḍava ।।
vinayāvanatāś cainaṃ praṇemuḥ stotratatparāḥ ।। sarvās tāḥ kauravaśreṣṭha variṣṭhaṃ taṃ dvijanmanām ।। mattas tad vriyatāṃ sarvaṃ pradāsyāmy atidurlabham ।। prasanne tvayy aparyāptaṃ kim asmākam iti dvija ।।
tad icchāmaḥ patiṃ prāptuṃ viprendra puruṣottamam ।। tam uttīrṇaṃ ca dadṛśur virūpaṃ vakram aṣṭadhā ।। tāḥ śaśāpa muniḥ kopam avāpya kurunandana ।। bhavatībhiḥ kṛtā tasmād eṣaṃ śāpaṃ dadāmi vaḥ ।।
macchāpopahatāḥ sarvā dasyuhastaṃ gamiṣyatha ।। punaḥ surendralokaṃ vai prāha bhūyo gamiṣyatha ।। bhartāraṃ prāpya tā yātā dasyuhastaṃ varāṅganāḥ ।। tenaivākhilanāthena sarvaṃ tad upasaṃhṛtam ।।
balaṃ tejas tathā vīryaṃ māhātmyaṃ copasaṃhṛtam ।। viprayogāvasānaś ca saṃyogaḥ saṃcayāt kṣayaḥ ।। teṣām evetare ceṣṭāṃ śikṣantaḥ santi tādṛśāḥ ।। parityajyākhilaṃ tantraṃ gantavyaṃ tapase vanam ।।
paraśvo bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ yathā yāsi tathā kuru ।। dṛṣṭaṃ caivānubhūtaṃ ca kathitaṃ tad viśeṣataḥ ।। rājye parīkṣitaṃ kṛtvā yayuḥ pāṇḍusutā vanam ।। jātasya yad yador vaṃśe vāsudevasya ceṣṭitam ।।
yaś caitac caritaṃ tasya kṛṣṇasya śṛṇuyāt sadā ।। sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।। vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva vistareṇa mahāmune ।। vyākhyāto bhavatā vaṃśo yādavānāṃ mahātmanām ।। @
asti kiṃcin mayā prārthyam adhyātmaśravaṇecchayā ।। @ sarvasaṃśayabhettāras tvām ṛte anye na santi bhoḥ ।। @ dvaitam eke praśaṃsanti advaitam apare janāḥ ।। @ dvayaṃ te ke praśaṃsanti mahātmāno mahāmune ।। @
adhyātmam akhilaṃ brahman vyākhyāmi bhavato mune ।। @ durbodhatvād ekamanāḥ śṛṇuṣva gadato mama ।। @ śrutvāvadhāraya mune pāraṃ tv asmān na vidyate ।। @ na bhūtāni hṛṣīkāni tathāntaḥkaraṇāny api ।। @
prāṇo vā prakṛtir vāpi paraṃ brahmeti śabdyate ।। @ na sattā lakṣaṇaṃ brahma yasmāt sadasataḥ param ।। @ utpattes tv ātmanaḥ svasya nāpy ākāśaḥ paraṃ viduḥ ।। @ na jātirūpalabdhes tu neti nety ucyate yataḥ ।। @
svayaṃ vedyaṃ hi tad brahma kumārī strīsukhaṃ yathā ।। @ acchedyaṃ tad abhedyaṃ tu satyaṃ jñānam anantakam ।। @ śuddhaṃ muktaṃ prabuddhaṃ yat sukhaduḥkhavivarjitam ।। @ yat pūrṇam acalaṃ nityaṃ tathā ṣaḍbhāvavarjitam ।। @
atīndriyam avarṇaṃ tu nityānandaṃ tathā mune ।। @ asthūlam aṇu nādīrgham ahrasvam atamas tathā ।। @ asnehaṃ ca tathācchāyaṃ ravamātrakakāyakam ।। @ prakāśaṃ vāṃśike yasya tat paraṃ brahma maharṣe ।। @
kham ivaikarasāvāptir api bhaktā jarāmarā ।। @ cakṣurādyavadhānā sā viparītā vibhāvyate ।। @ savyāpāre śarīre asmin nirvyāpāram akalmaṣam ।। @ cintayan sarvam ātmānaṃ mukta eveti vegapī ।। @
pramāṇotpannayā buddhyā yo vidyāṃ jñātum icchati ।। @ dīpenāsau dhruvaṃ paśyed guhākukṣigataṃ tamaḥ ।। @ yadā cittam asaṃsaktaṃ tadīyaṃ sarvavastuṣu ।। @ bhavatīha tadā yogī maitreya paramātmavit ।। @
svareṇa saṃdhayed yogam asvaraṃ bhāvayet param ।। @ asvareṇa tu bhāvena tv abhāvo bhāvam ādiśet ।। @ tad eva niṣphalaṃ brahma nirvikalpaṃ nirañjanam ।। @ tad brahmāham iti jñātvā brahmabhāvo bhaved dhruvam ।। @
ātiṣṭhet sādhanaṃ yatra yāti tatraiva bandhayet ।। @ evaṃ saṃbādhayed artham upāyena tu buddhimān ।। @ yatra yatra bhaved vedas tat tad astv iti cintayet ।। @ maitreya tena rūpeṇa so amṛtatvāya kalpyate ।। @
prakṛtijñeyasadṛśī dṛśyarūpaṃ svam ātmakam ।। @ yo veda paramaṃ vedaṃ mukta ity ucyate mune ।। @ vedadvāreṇa yo vedaṃ paśyaty ātmānam ātmani ।। @ tasmin vede kalābhāvān niṣphalaṃ paripaśyati ।। @
ravamātrakadehasya grāhyatvād api rodhata ।। @ tatraiva sthāpayec cittaṃ dṛṣṭvābhyāsam adaivatam ।। @ ravamātrakadeho aham avidyādeham āśritaḥ ।। @ avidyābhiprapanno ayam iti xx na muhyati ।। @
yac chrotavyaṃ ca yad dṛśyaṃ yac ca bhoktavyam ity uta ।। @ ghrātavyaṃ caiva spṛṣṭavyaṃ buddhigrāhyaṃ tathaiva ca ।। @ sarvaṃ tad brahmabuddhyā tu kurvāṇo na nibadhyate ।। @ ravamātraśarīraṃ tu brahma sarvatra dṛśyate ।। @
amedhyādibhir asaṃspṛṣṭaṃ yathā nirmalatāṃ gatam ।। @ ahaṃ tadaiva nānyo asmi tasmāt tadvac ca nirmalaḥ ।। @ maitreya nāvasīdanti parāparavido janāḥ ।। @ adhaś cordhvaṃ ca tiryak ca nānyaṃ paśyanti yoginaḥ ।। @
anyarūpe pranaṣṭe tu kṛtsne sthāvarajaṅgame ।। @ avyayaṃ ca prapaśyanti tad evānyan na kiṃcana ।। @ avidyārūpe pranaṣṭe ca suṣuptipralaye api ca ।। @ prabuddhās tu smariṣyanti tad evānyan na maharṣe ।। @
sarvavastuṣu pūrṇeṣu punaś cūrṇīkṛteṣu ca ।। @ tadantam eva paśyanti tasya tattvaṃ na dṛśyate ।। @ sarveṣu vedatantreṣu sarveṣu samayeṣu bhoḥ ।। @ idam eva prapaśyanti tatas tattvavido janāḥ ।। @
brahmarūpam idaṃ sarvam evaṃ paśyet sadā naraḥ ।। @ hatvāpi sa imāṃl lokān sarvāśī sarvavikrayī ।। @ sarvān niṣiddhān kṛtvāpi karmabhir na sa badhyate ।। @ dharmādharmavimuktātmā brahmabhūyāya kalpate ।। @
nirātmakam idaṃ proktaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ sānakam ucyate ।। @ recakaṃ pūrakaṃ kṛtvā vāyum ārohayet tataḥ ।। @ brahmanāḍī smṛtā tatra kāyamadhye vyavasthitā ।। @ jyotirāgrā cakramūlā sūkṣmā cakrāntarānugā ।। @
adṛśyarūpā sā sarvaiḥ paśyanti paramarṣayaḥ ।। @ pradyumno bhagavāñ jyotir bahirdhāma vyavasthitaḥ ।। @ māṃsād adhaḥ pauṇḍarīkād dhṛdayagranthir ucyate ।। @ tena saṃkramayed vāyuṃ purāṇakaraṇena tu ।। @
jyotiṣaḥ prāpaṇābhyāsāt sarvavāyujayo bhavet ।। @ tatraikadeśam ākṛṣya kecin nyasyanti maulike ।। @ tena labdhopalabdhās tu gacchanti jyotiṣaḥ padam ।। @ ye tu tattvaṃ prapaśyanti maulike sthāpayanty uta ।। @
punar brahmaṇi niṣṇātās te amṛtatvāya kalpate ।। @ etat tu sānakaṃ proktaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ divyam anuttamam ।। @ śreyāṃsaḥ pūrvam icchanti saṃnyāsāt sarvakarmaṇām ।। @ tyaktasarvakriyārambhāḥ paraṃ sāṃkhyaṃ pracakṣate ।। @
sāṃkhyamārgas tvayaivokto yogamārgas tvyayocyatām ।। @ atha yogaṃ pravakṣyāmi guhyād guhyataraṃ param ।। @ yaj jñātvā munayaḥ sarve padaṃ gacchanty anāmayam ।। @ sāṃkhyāt tattvāt paraṃ yogaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। @
ye yogam anutiṣṭhanti sāṃkhyam apy anutiṣṭate ।। @ tasmād yogaṃ praśaṃsanti munayo munisattama ।। @ dehinas tv ātmasaṃyogād yogam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ।। @ dehīpāpanibandhatvāt pūrvaṃ pāpakṣayaṃ caret ।। @
guṇais tu bandhitatvāc ca guṇānāṃ haraṇaṃ tataḥ ।। @ dehī dehanibandhatvāt tasyāpi haraṇaṃ caret ।। @ mukhyānāṃ caiva śūnyānāṃ balavattvān niyāmanam ।। @ evaṃ kṛtvā sma dṛśyantu saṃyojyātmānam ātmani ।। @
dharmādharmavinirmukto mukta eva bhaved dhruvam ।। @ guṇānāṃ tejaso rūpaṃ deharūpaṃ ca dehinaḥ ।। @ ālambya vinaśet paścād yogasiddhim abhīpsatā ।। @ ālambanān nirālambaṃ paśyanti paramarṣayaḥ ।। @
ālambanaṃ na cet pūrvaṃ na ca bandhavimokṣaṇam ।। @ recapūrakakumbhaiś ca pūrvaṃ pāpakṣayaṃ caret ।। @ pūrvarātralayaiḥ śāntyā dehino dṛśyatāṃ nayet ।। @ vedasārāt tu saṃyogaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। @
evaṃ yogavidhiḥ prokto yoge sarvaṃ samāpyate ।। @ evaṃ sāṃkhyaṃ ca yogaṃ ca pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। @ anayos tv apṛthagjñānān mukto bhavati nānyathā ।। @ sāṃkhyayogāv upāyau dvāv upeyas tv eka eva tu ।। @
devo nārāyaṇas tv ekaḥ paramātmety udāhṛtaḥ ।। @ ravamātrakadehas tu sarvavyāpyājarāmaraḥ ।। @ taraṅgajaṅgamasthās nu svamāyātamasāvṛtaḥ ।। @ bahvākāra ivābhāti māyayā puruṣottamaḥ ।। @
evaṃ yo veda yogīndraḥ sa vai mukto bhaven naraḥ ।। @ yat pṛṣṭavān asi mune tad uktaṃ paramārthataḥ ।। @ kim anyac chrotum icchā te hy asti maitreya pṛccha tat ।। @ jñānāmṛtam idaṃ śrutvā nāsti dhanyataro mama ।। @
manye ahaṃ bhagavān adya prasādaṃ kṛtavān iti ।। @ adyāhaṃ vītasaṃdeho bhavaṃ viprarṣabha prabho ।। @ tathāpi kiṃcit pṛcchāmi durbodhatvān mahāmune ।। @ mahāpralayasaṃjñāṃ ca kalpānte ca mahāmune ।।
kalpānte prākṛte caiva pralaye jāyate yathā ।। caturyugasahasre tu brahmaṇo dve dvijottama ।। divyair varṣasahasrais tu tad dvādaśabhir ucyate ।। ādyaṃ kṛtayugaṃ muktvā maitreyāntyaṃ tathā kalim ।।
kriyate copasaṃhāras tathānte ca kalau yuge ।। dharmaś catuṣpād bhagavan yasmin viplavam ṛcchati ।। tan nibodha samāsena vartate yan mahāmune ।। na sāma-ṛgyajurvedaviniṣpādanahaitukī ।।
na dāmpatyakramo naiva vahnidevātmakaḥ kramaḥ ।। sarvebhya eva varṇebhyo yogyaḥ kanyāvarodhane ।। yaiva saiva ca maitreya prāyaścittakriyā kalau ।। devatāś ca kalau sarvāḥ sarvaḥ sarvasya cāśramaḥ ।।
dharmo yathābhirucitair anuṣṭhānair anuṣṭhitaḥ ।। strīṇāṃ rūpamadaś caiva keśair eva bhaviṣyati ।। kalau striyo bhaviṣyanti tadā keśair alaṃkṛtāḥ ।। bhartā bhaviṣyati kalau vittavān eva yoṣitām ।।
svāmitvahetuḥ saṃbandho bhāvī nābhijanas tadā ।। arthāś cātmopabhogāntā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।। anyāyāvāptavitteṣu puruṣāś ca spṛhālavaḥ ।। paṇārdhārdhārdhamātre api kariṣyati tadā dvija ।।
kṣīrapradānasaṃbandhi bhāvi goṣu ca gauravam ।। bhaviṣyanti tadā sarvā gaganāsaktadṛṣṭayaḥ ।। ātmānaṃ ghātayiṣyanti tadāvṛṣṭyādiduḥkhitāḥ ।। prāpsyanti vyāhatasukhapramodā mānavāḥ kalau ।।
kariṣyanti kalau prāpte na ca pitryodakakriyām ।। bahuprajālpabhāgyāś ca bhaviṣyanti kalau striyaḥ ।। kurvantyo gurubhartṝṇām ājñāṃ bhetsyanty anādṛtāḥ ।। paruṣānṛtabhāṣiṇyo bhaviṣyanti kalau striyaḥ ।।
asadvṛttā bhaviṣyanti puruṣeṣu kulāṅganāḥ ।। gṛhasthāś ca na hoṣyanti na dāsyanty ucitāny api ।। bhikṣavaś cāpi mitrādisnehasaṃbandhayantraṇāḥ ।। hāriṇo janavittānāṃ saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge ।।
yaś ca yaś cābalaḥ sarvaḥ sa sa bhṛtyaḥ kalau yuge ।। śūdravṛttyā pravartsyanti kārukarmopajīvinaḥ ।। pāṣaṇḍasaṃśrayāṃ vṛttim āśrayiṣyanty asaṃskṛtāḥ ।। godhūmānnayavānnāḍhyān deśān yāsyanti duḥkhitāḥ ।।
adharmavṛddhyā lokānām alpam āyur bhaviṣyati ।। nareṣu nṛpadoṣeṇa bālamṛtyur bhaviṣyati ।। navāṣṭadaśavarṣāṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tathā kalau ।। nātijīvati vai kaścit kalau varṣāṇi viṃśatiḥ ।।
yatas tato vinaṅkṣyanti kālenālpena mānavāḥ ।। yadā yadā hi maitreya hānir dharmasya lakṣyate ।। tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā mahātmabhiḥ ।। tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।।
tadā tadā kaler vṛddhir anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।। tadānumeyaṃ prādhānyaṃ kaler maitreya paṇḍitaiḥ ।। ijyate puruṣair yajñais tadā jñeyaṃ kaler balam ।। aṭṭaśūlā janapadā śivaśūlāś catuṣpathā ।।
keśaśūlā striyaḥ sarvā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।। kaler vṛddhis tadā prājñair anumeyā dvijottama ।। nārcayiṣyanti maitreya pāṣaṇḍopahatā narāḥ ।। ity evaṃ vipra vakṣyanti pāṣaṇḍopahatā narāḥ ।।
phalaṃ tathālpasāraṃ ca vipra prāpte kalau yuge ।। śūdraprāyās tathā varṇā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।। bhaviṣyati kalau prāpte uśīraṃ cānulepanam ।। śyālādyā hāribhāryāś ca suhṛdo munisattama ।।
iti codāhariṣyanti śvaśurānugatā narāḥ ।। narāḥ pāpāny anudinaṃ kariṣyanty alpamedhasaḥ ।। yad yad duḥkhāya tat sarvaṃ kalikāle bhaviṣyati ।। tadā praviralo vipra kvacil loko bhaviṣyati ।।
karoti yaṃ kṛtayuge kriyate tapasā hi saḥ ।। tac chrūyatāṃ mahābhāga gadato mama tattvataḥ ।। munīnām apy abhūd vādaḥ kaiś cāsau kriyate sukham ।। yayus te saṃśayaṃ praṣṭuṃ maitreya munipuṃgavāḥ ।।
vedavyāsaṃ mahābhāgam ardhasnātaṃ sutaṃ mama ।। tasthus taṭe mahānadyās taruṣaṇḍam upāśritāḥ ।। teṣāṃ munīnāṃ bhūyaś ca mamajja sa nadījale ।। utthāya sādhu sādhv iti śūdra dhanyo asi cābravīt ।।
yoṣitaḥ sādhu dhanyās tās tābhyo dhanyataro asti kaḥ ।। upatasthur mahābhāgā munayas te sutaṃ mama ।। kimartham āgatā yūyam iti satyavatīsutaḥ ।। alaṃ tenāstu tāvan naḥ kathyatām aparaṃ tvayā ।।
yac cāha bhagavān sādhu dhanyāś ceti punaḥ punaḥ ।। tat kathyatāṃ tato hṛtsthaṃ pṛcchāmas tvāṃ prayojanam ।। śrūyatāṃ bho muniśreṣṭhā yad uktaṃ sādhu sādhv iti ।। dvāpare tac ca māsena ahorātreṇa tat kalau ।।
prāpnoti puruṣas tena kaliḥ sādhv iti bhāṣitam ।। yad āpnoti tad āpnoti kalau saṃkīrtya keśavam ।। svalpāyāsena dharmajñās tena tuṣṭo asmy ahaṃ kaleḥ ।। tataḥ svadharmasaṃprāptair yaṣṭavyaṃ vidhivad dhanaiḥ ।।
patanāya tathā bhāvyaṃ tais tu saṃyamibhiḥ sadā ।। bhojyapeyādikaṃ caiṣāṃ necchāprāptikaraṃ dvijāḥ ।। jayanti te nijāṃl lokān kleśena mahatā dvijāḥ ।। nijāñ jayati vai lokāñ śūdro dhanyataras tataḥ ।।
niyamo muniśārdūlās tenāsau sādhv itīritam ।। pratipādyaṃ ca pātreṣu yaṣṭavyaṃ ca yathāvidhi ।। tathāsadviniyogāya vijñeyaṃ gahanaṃ nṛṇām ।। nijāñ jayati vai lokān prājāpatyādikān kramāt ।।
kurvatī samavāpnoti tatsālokyaṃ yato dvijāḥ ।। tṛtīyaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ tena mayā sādhv iti yoṣitām ।। tat pṛcchata yathākāmaṃ ahaṃ vakṣyāmi vaḥ sphuṭam ।। anyasminn eva tat praśne yathāvat kathitaṃ tvayā ।।
vismayotphullanayanāṃs tāpasāṃs tān upāgatān ।। tato hi vaḥ prasaṅgena sādhu sādhv iti bhāṣitam ।। narair ātmaguṇāmbhobhiḥ kṣālitākhilakilbiṣaiḥ ।। tathā strībhir anāyāsāt patiśuśrūṣayaiva hi ।।
dharmasaṃsādhane kleśo dvijātīnāṃ kṛtādiṣu ।। apṛṣṭenāpi dharmajñāḥ kim anyat kriyatāṃ dvijāḥ ।। yathāgataṃ dvijā jagmur vyāsoktikṣatasaṃśayāḥ ।। atyantaduṣṭasya kaler ayam eko mahān guṇaḥ ।।
kīrtanād eva kṛṣṇasya muktabandho paraṃ vrajet ।। prākṛtām antarālāṃ ca tām apy eṣa vadāmi te ।। naimittikaḥ prākṛtikas tathaivātyantiko mataḥ ।। ātyantikaś ca mokṣākhyaḥ prākṛto dviparārdhikaḥ ।।
dviguṇīkṛtayā jñeyaḥ prākṛtaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ ।। tato aṣṭādaśame bhāge parārdham abhidhīyate ।। tadāvyakte akhilaṃ vyaktaṃ svahetau layam eti vai ।। taiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ kāṣṭhā triṃśat kāṣṭhās tathā kalā ।।
nāḍikā tu pramāṇena kalā daśa ca pañca ca ।। māgadhena pramāṇena jalaprasthas tu sa smṛtaḥ ।। ahorātraṃ muhūrtās tu triṃśan māso dinais tathā ।। tribhir varṣaśatair varṣaṃ ṣaṣṭyā caivāsuradviṣām ।।
caturyugasahasraṃ tu kathyate brahmaṇo dinam ।। tadante caiva maitreya brāhmo naimittiko layaḥ ।। śṛṇuṣva prākṛtaṃ bhūyas tava vakṣyāmy ahaṃ layam ।। anāvṛṣṭir atīvogrā jāyate śatavārṣikī ।।
kṣayaṃ yānti muniśreṣṭha pārthivāny anupīḍanāt ।। kṣayāya yatate kartum ātmasthāḥ sakalāḥ prajāḥ ।। tataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇur bhānoḥ saptasu raśmiṣu ।। b suṣupto harati kleśaś ca x viśva tathaiva ca ।। b
viśvadyaxs tathātharvā vasuḥ saṃyad vasus tathā ।। b sthitaḥ pibaty aśeṣāṇi jalāni munisattama ।। d śoṣaṃ nayati maitreya samastaṃ pṛthivītalam ।। pātāleṣu ca yat toyaṃ tat sarvaṃ nayati kṣayam ।।
ta eva raśmayaḥ sapta jāyante sapta bhāskarāḥ ।। dahanty aśeṣaṃ trailokyaṃ sapātālatalaṃ dvija ।। sādrinadyarṇavābhogaṃ niḥsneham abhijāyate ।। bhavaty eṣā ca vasudhā kūrmapṛṣṭhopamākṛtiḥ ।।
śeṣāhiśvāsasaṃbhūtaḥ pātālāni dahaty adhaḥ ।। bhūmim abhyetya sakalaṃ babhasti vasudhātalam ।। jvālāmālāmahāvartas tatraiva parivartate ।। jvālāvartaparīvāram upakṣīṇacarācaram ।।
kṛtādhikārā gacchanti maharlokaṃ mahāmune ।। gacchanti janalokaṃ te daśāvṛttyā paraiṣiṇaḥ ।। mukhaniśvāsajān meghān karoti munisattama ।। uttiṣṭhanti tadā vyomni ghorāḥ saṃvartakā ghanāḥ ।।
dhūmravarṇā ghanāḥ kecit kecit pītāḥ payodharāḥ ।। kecid vaiḍūryasaṃkāśā indranīlanibhāḥ kvacit ।। indragopanibhāḥ kecin manaḥśilanibhās tathā ।। indragopanibhāḥ kecit tataḥ śikhinibhās tathā ।।
manaḥśilābhāḥ kecid vai haritālanibhāḥ pare ।। kecit puravarākārāḥ kecit parvatasaṃnibhāḥ ।। mahārāvā mahākāyāḥ pūrayanti nabhastalam ।। varṣantas te mahāsārās tam agnim atibhairavam ।। b
śamayanti jagat sarvaṃ varṣanti munisattama ।। b hastihastanibhābhis te dhārābhir aniśaṃ tadā ।। b śamayanty akhilaṃ vipra trailokyāntaravistṛtam ।। d plāvayanto jagat sarvaṃ varṣanti munisattama ।।
bhuvarlokaṃ tathaivordhvaṃ plāvayanti divaṃ dvija ।। varṣanti te mahāmeghā varṣāṇām adhikaṃ śatam ।। evaṃ bhavati kalpānte samastaṃ munisattama ।। vāsudevasya māhātmyān nityasya paramātmanaḥ ।।
ekārṇavaṃ bhavaty etat trailokyam akhilaṃ tataḥ ।। nāśayan vāti maitreya varṣāṇām aparaṃ śatam ।। anādir ādir viśvasya pītvā vāyum aśeṣataḥ ।। brahmarūpadharaḥ śete bhagavān ādikṛd dhariḥ ।।
brahmalokagataiś caiva cintyamāno mumukṣubhiḥ ।। ātmānaṃ vāsudevākhyaṃ cintayan parameśvaraḥ ।। nimittaṃ tatra yac chete brahmarūpadharo hariḥ ।। nimīlaty etad akhilaṃ māyāśayyāśaye acyute ।।
ekārṇave kṛte loke tāvatī rātrir iṣyate ।। brahmasvarūpadhṛg viṣṇur yathā te kathitaṃ purā ।। naimittikas te kathitaḥ prākṛtaṃ śṛṇvataḥ param ।। samasteṣv eva lokeṣu pātāleṣv akhileṣu ca ।।
kṛṣṇecchākārite tasmin pravṛtte pratisaṃcare ।। āttagandhā tato bhūmiḥ pralayatvāya kalpate ।। āpas tadā pravṛddhās tu vegavatyo mahāsvanāḥ ।। salilenaivormimatā lokāṃs tāṃs tān samantataḥ ।।
vyāptam evābhavat sarvaṃ jagad etad dvijottama ।। naśyanty āpas tatas tāś ca rasatanmātrasaṃkṣayāt ।। agnyavasthe tu salile tejasā sarvato vṛte ।। sarvam āpūryate arcibhis tadā jagad idaṃ śanaiḥ ।।
jyotiṣo api paraṃ rūpaṃ vāyur atti prabhākaram ।। praṇaṣṭe rūpatanmātre hṛtarūpo vibhāvasuḥ ।। nirāloke tadā loke vāyvavasthe ca tejasi ।। ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca tiryak ca dodhavīti diśo daśa ।।
praśāmyati tato vāyuḥ khaṃ tu tiṣṭhaty anāvṛtam ।। sarvam āpūrayac caiva sumahat tat prakāśate ।। śabdamātraṃ tadākāśaṃ sarvam āvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।। abhimānātmako hy eṣa bhūtādis tāmasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
bhūtādiṃ grasate cāpi mahān vai buddhilakṣaṇaḥ ।। urvī mahāṃś ca jagataḥ prānte antar bāhyatas tathā ।। pratyāhāre tu tāḥ sarvāḥ praviśanti parasparam ।। saptadvīpasamudrāntaṃ saptalokaṃ saparvatam ।।
jyotir vāyau layaṃ yāti yāty ākāśe samīraṇaḥ ।। mahāntam ebhiḥ sahitaṃ prakṛtir grasate dvija ।। procyate prakṛtir hetuḥ pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ param ।। vyaktasvarūpam avyakte tasmin maitreya līyate ।।
so apy aṃśaḥ sarvabhūtasya maitreya paramātmanaḥ ।। sattāmātrātmake jñeye jñānātmany ātmanaḥ pare ।। sa viṣṇuḥ sarvam evedaṃ yato nāvartate yatiḥ ।। puruṣaś cāpy ubhāv etau līyete paramātmani ।।
viṣṇur nāmnā sa vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate ।। tābhyām ubhābhyāṃ puruṣaiḥ sarvamūrtiḥ sa ijyate ।। yajñeśvaro yajñapumān puruṣaiḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।। nivṛtte yogibhir mārge viṣṇur muktiphalapradaḥ ।।
yac ca vācām aviṣaye tat sarvaṃ viṣṇur avyayaḥ ।। paramātmā ca viśvātmā viśvarūpadharo hariḥ ।। puruṣaś cāpi maitreya vyāpiny avyāhatātmani ।। tad ahas tasya maitreya viṣṇor īśasya kathyate ।।
tatra sthite niśā cānyā tatpramāṇā mahāmune ।। upacāras tathāpy eṣa tasyeśasya dvijocyate ।। ātyantikam atho brahman nibodha pratisaṃcaram ।। utpannajñānavairāgyaḥ prāpnoty ātyantikaṃ layam ।।
śārīro bahubhir bhedair bhidyate śrūyatāṃ ca saḥ ।। gulmārśaḥśvāsaśvayathucchardyādibhir anekadhā ।। bhidyate dehajas tāpo mānasaṃ śrotum arhasi ।। śokāsūyāvamānerṣyāmātsaryādibhavas tathā ।।
ity evamādibhir bhedais tāpo hy ādhyātmikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sarīsṛpādyaiś ca nṛṇāṃ janyante cādhibhautikaḥ ।। tāpo dvijavaraśreṣṭha kathyate cādhidaivikaḥ ।। duḥkhaṃ sahasraśo bhedair bhidyate munisattama ।।
ulbasaṃveṣṭito bhugnapṛṣṭhagrīvāsthisaṃhatiḥ ।। atitāpibhir atyarthaṃ vardhamānātivedanaḥ ।। śakṛnmūtramahāpaṅkaśāyī sarvatrapīḍitaḥ ।। āste garbhe atiduḥkhena nijakarmanibandhanaḥ ।।
prājāpatyena vātena pīḍyamānāsthibandhanaḥ ।। kleśair niṣkrāntim āpnoti jaṭharān mātur āturaḥ ।। vijñānabhraṃśam āpnoti jātaś ca munisattama ।। pūtivraṇān nipatito dharaṇyāṃ kṛmiko yathā ।।
snānapānādikāhāram avāpnoti parecchayā ।। bhakṣyamāṇo api naivaiṣāṃ samartho vinivāraṇe ।। bālabhāve yadāpnoti ādhibhautādikāni ca ।। na jānāti kutaḥ ko ahaṃ kvāhaṃ gantā kimātmakaḥ ।।
kiṃ kāryaṃ kim akāryaṃ vā kiṃ vācyaṃ kiṃ ca nocyate ।। kiṃ kartavyam akartavyaṃ kiṃ vā kiṃ guṇadoṣavat ।। avāpyate narair duḥkhaṃ śiśnodaraparāyaṇaiḥ ।। ajñānināṃ pravartante karmalopās tato dvija ।।
tasmād ajñānināṃ duḥkham iha cāmutra cottamam ।। vicalacchīrṇadaśano valisnāyuśirāvṛtaḥ ।। nāsāvivaraniryātalomapuñjaś caladvapuḥ ।। utsannajaṭharāgnitvād alpāhāro alpaceṣṭitaḥ ।।
mandībhavacchrotranetraḥ sravallālāvilānanaḥ ।। tatkṣaṇe apy anubhūtānām asmartākhilavastūnām ।। śvāsakāsamahāyāsasamudbhūtaprajāgaraḥ ।। bhṛtyātmaputradārāṇām avamānāspadīkṛtaḥ ।।
hāsyaḥ parijanasyāpi nirviṇṇāśeṣabāndhavaḥ ।। saṃsmaran yauvane dīrghaṃ niḥśvasity atitāpitaḥ ।। maraṇe yāni duḥkhāni prāpnoti śṛṇu tāny api ।। muhur glāniḥ paravaśo muhur jñānalavānvitaḥ ।।
ete kathaṃ bhaviṣyantīty atīvamamatākulaḥ ।। śarair ivāntakasyograiś chidyamānāsthibandhanaḥ ।। saṃśuṣyamāṇatālvoṣṭhapuṭo ghuraghurāyate ।। tāpena mahatā vyāptas tṛṣā cārtas tathā kṣudhā ।।
tataś ca yātanādehaṃ kleśena pratipadyate ।। śṛṇuṣva narake yāni prāpyante puruṣair mṛtaiḥ ।। yamasya darśanaṃ cogram ugramārgavilokanam ।। pratyekaṃ narake yāś ca yātanā dvija duḥsahāḥ ।।
kuṭhāraiḥ kṛtyamānānāṃ bhūmau cāpi nikhanyatām ।। gṛdhraiḥ saṃbhakṣyamāṇānāṃ dvīpibhiś copabhujyatām ।। uccān nipātyamānānāṃ kṣipyatāṃ kṣepayantrakaiḥ ।। prāpyante nārakair vipra teṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate ।।
svarge api pātabhītasya kṣayiṣṇor nāsti nirvṛtiḥ ।। garbhe vilīyate bhūyo jāyamāno astam eti ca ।। madhyamaṃ vā vayaḥ prāpya vārddhake vā dhruvā mṛtiḥ ।। tantukāraṇapakṣmaughair āste kārpāsabījavat ।।
bhavanty anekaduḥkhāni tathaiveṣṭavipattiṣu ।। tad eva duḥkhavṛkṣasya bījatvam upagacchati ।। kriyate na tathā bhūri sukhaṃ puṃsāṃ yathāsukham ।। vimuktipādapacchāyām ṛte kutra sukhaṃ nṛṇām ।।
garbhajanmajarādyeṣu sthāneṣu prabhaviṣyataḥ ।। bheṣajaṃ bhagavatprāptir ekāntātyantikī matā ।। tatprāptihetur jñānaṃ ca karma coktaṃ mahāmune ।। śabdabrahmāgamamayaṃ paraṃ brahma vivekajam ।।
yathā sūryas tathā jñānaṃ yad viprarṣe vivekajam ।। tad etac chrūyatām atra saṃbandhe gadato mama ।। śabdabrahmaṇi niṣṇātaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati ।। parayā tv akṣaraprāptir ṛgvedādimayāparā ।।
anirdeśyam arūpaṃ ca pāṇipādādyasaṃyutam ।। vyāpy avyāptaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ taṃ vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ ।। śrutivākyoditaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।। vācako bhagavacchabdas tasyādyasyākṣayātmanaḥ ।।
jñāyate yena taj jñānaṃ param anyat trayīmayam ।। pūjāyāṃ bhagavacchabdaḥ kriyate hy aupacārikaḥ ।। maitreya bhagavacchabdaḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇe ।। netā gamayitā sraṣṭā gakārārthas tathā mune ।।
jñānavairāgyayoś caiva ṣaṇṇāṃ bhaga itīraṇā ।। sa ca bhūteṣv aśeṣeṣu vakārārthas tato avyayaḥ ।। paramabrahmabhūtasya vāsudevasya nānyagaḥ ।। śabdo ayaṃ nopacāreṇa anyatra hy upacārataḥ ।।
vetti vidyām avidyāṃ ca sa vācyo bhagavān iti ।। bhagavacchabdavācyāni vinā heyair guṇādibhiḥ ।। bhūteṣu ca sa sarvātmā vāsudevas tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। nāmavyākhyām anantasya vāsudevasya tattvataḥ ।।
dhātā vidhātā jagatāṃ vāsudevas tataḥ prabhuḥ ।। dhātā vidhātā parameśvaraś ca sa vāsudevo na yataḥ paro anyaḥ ।। atītasarvāvaraṇo akhilātmā tenāstṛtaṃ yad bhuvanāntarāle ।। icchāgṛhītābhimatorudehaḥ saṃsādhitāśeṣajagaddhito asau ।।
paraḥ parāṇāṃ sakalā na yatra kleśādayaḥ santi parāvareśe ।। sarveśvaraḥ sarvadṛk sarvavettā samastaśaktiḥ parameśvarākhyaḥ ।। saṃdṛśyate vāpy avagamyate vā taj jñānam ajñānam ato anyad uktam ।। vyarthaṃ janmaśataṃ tasya śrutvā vaktraparāṅmukhaḥ ।।
aśvamedhasamaṃ jñeyaṃ kurukṣetraśatādhikam ।। niṣphalaṃ jīvitaṃ tasya asya jñānaparāṅmukhaḥ ।। tatprāptikāraṇaṃ brahma tad etad iti paṭhyate ।। svādhyāyayogasaṃpattyā paramātmā prakāśate ।।
na māṃsacakṣuṣā draṣṭuṃ brahmabhūtaḥ sa śakyate ।। jñāte yatrākhilādhāraṃ paśyeyaṃ parameśvaram ।। janakāya purā yogaṃ tathāhaṃ kathayāmi te ।। kathaṃ tayoś ca saṃvādo yogasaṃbandhavān abhūt ।।
kṛtadhvajaś ca nāmnāsīt sadādhyātmaratir nṛpaḥ ।। putro amitadhvajasyāpi khāṇḍikyajanako abhavat ।। keśidhvajo apy atīvāsīd ātmavidyāviśāradaḥ ।। keśidhvajena khāṇḍikyaḥ svarājyād avaropitaḥ ।।
rājyān nirākṛtaḥ so atha durgāraṇyacaro abhavat ।। brahmavidyām adhiṣṭhāya tartuṃ mṛtyum avidyayā ।। dharmadhenuṃ jaghānograḥ śārdūlo vijane vane ।। prāyaścittaṃ sa papraccha kim atreti vidhīyate ।।
kaśerur api tenoktas tatheti prāha bhārgavam ।। sa gatvā tam apṛcchac ca so apy āha śṛṇu yan mune ।। vetty eka eva tvacchatruḥ khāṇḍikyo yo jitas tvayā ।। prāpta eva mayā yajño yadi māṃ sa haniṣyati ।।
tataś cāvikalo yāgo muniśreṣṭha bhaviṣyati ।। vanaṃ jagāma yatrāste khāṇḍikyaḥ sa mahāmatiḥ ।। provāca krodhatāmrākṣaḥ samāropitakārmukaḥ ।। kṛṣṇājinadhare vetsi na mayi prahariṣyati ।।
yeṣāṃ mayā tvayā cogrāḥ prahitāḥ śitasāyakāḥ ।। ātatāyy asi durbuddhe mama rājyaharo ripuḥ ।। na tvāṃ hantuṃ vicāryaitat kopaṃ bāṇaṃ vimuñca vā ।। mantrayām āsa khāṇḍikyaḥ sarvair eva mahāmatiḥ ।।
hate tu pṛthivī sarvā tava vaśyā bhaviṣyati ।। hate tu pṛthivī sarvā mama vaśyā bhaviṣyati ।। na hanmi cel lokajayo mama tv asya vasuṃdharā ।। nāhaṃ manye lokajayād adhikā syād vasuṃdharā ।।
tasmād enaṃ na haniṣye yat pṛcchati vadāmi tat ।। praṣṭavyaṃ yat tvayā sarvaṃ tat pṛcchasva vadāmy aham ।। kathayitvā sa papraccha prāyaścittaṃ hi tadgatam ।। prāyaścittam aśeṣeṇa yad vai tatra vidhīyate ।।
yāgabhūmim upāgamya cakre sarvāḥ kriyāḥ kramāt ।। kṛtakṛtyas tato bhūtvā cintayām āsa pārthivaḥ ।। tathaivārthijano apy arthair yojito abhimatair mayā ।। aniṣpannakriyaṃ cetas tathāpi mama kiṃ yathā ।।
khāṇḍikyāya na datteti mayā vai gurudakṣiṇā ।। maitreya durgagahanaṃ khāṇḍikyo yatra saṃsthitaḥ ।। tasthau hantuṃ kṛtamatis tam āha sa punar nṛpaḥ ।। guror niṣkrayadānāya mām avehi tvam āgatam ।।
so ahaṃ te dātum icchāmi vṛṇuṣva gurudakṣiṇām ।। guruniṣkṛtikāmo atra kim ayaṃ prārthyatām iti ।। kṛtibhiḥ prārthyate rājyam anāyāsitasainikaiḥ ।। svalpakālaṃ mahīrājyaṃ mādṛśaiḥ prārthyate katham ।।
paramārthaḥ kathaṃ ko atra yūyaṃ nātra vicakṣaṇāḥ ।। uvāca kim avaśyaṃ tvaṃ dadāsi gurudakṣiṇām ।। bhavān adhyātmavijñānaparamārthavicakṣaṇaḥ ।। tat kleśapraśamāyālaṃ yat karma tad udīraya ।।
rājyalābhād vinā nānyat kṣatriyāṇām atipriyam ।। rājyam etad aśeṣaṃ te yatra gṛdhnanty apaṇḍitāḥ ।। vadhaś ca dharmayuddhena svarājyaparipanthinām ।। yat prajāpālanaṃ yac ca svarājyapratipakṣaṇām ।।
bandhāyaiva bhavaty eṣā avidyāpy akramojjhitā ।। anyeṣāṃ doṣajā naiva dharmam evānurudhyate ।। na yācñā kṣatrabandhūnāṃ dharmāyaitat satāṃ matam ।। b janmopabhogakṣayadaṃ yogād anyan na vidyate ।। b
brahmavīhi mahābhāga yogaṃ yogaviduttama ।। b vijñātayogaśāstrārthāḥ tvam asyān nimisaṃtatau ।। b ato na yācitaṃ rājyam avidyāntargataṃ tava ।। d ahaṃmānamahāpānamadamattā na mādṛśāḥ ।।
khāṇḍikyajanakaṃ prītyā śrūyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama ।। rājyaṃ yāgāṃś ca vividhān bhogaiḥ puṇyakṣayaṃ tathā ।। śrūyatāṃ cāpy avidyāyāḥ svarūpaṃ kulanandana ।। avidyātarusaṃbhūtibījam etad dvidhā sthitam ।।
aham etad itīty uccaiḥ kurute kumatir matim ।। ātmany ātmamayaṃ bhāvaṃ kaḥ karoti kalevare ।। adehe hy ātmani prājño mamedam iti manyate ।। karoti paṇḍitaḥ svāmyam anātmani kalevare ।।
dehaś cānyo yadā puṃsas tadā bandhāya tatparam ।। yadi nāmāsya kāyasya yad antas tad bahir bhavet ।। daṇḍam ādāya loko ayaṃ śunaḥ kākāṃś ca vārayet ।। pārthivo ayaṃ tathā deho mṛdambholepanasthitiḥ ।।
āpyāyate yadi tataḥ puṃso garvo atra kiṃ kṛtaḥ ।। mohaśramaṃ prayāto asau vāsanāreṇuguṇṭhitaḥ ।। tadā saṃsārapānthasya yāti mohaśramaḥ śamam ।। ananyātiśayābādhaṃ paraṃ nirvāṇam ṛcchati ।।
duḥkhājñānamalā dharmāḥ prakṛtes te tu nātmanaḥ ।। śabdodrekādikān dharmāṃs tat karoti yathā mune ।। bhajate prākṛtān dharmān anyas tebhyo hi so avyayaḥ ।। kleśānāṃ ca kṣayakaraṃ yogād anyan na vidyate ।।
vijñātayogaśāstrārthas tvam asyāṃ nimisaṃtatau ।। yatra sthito na cyavate prāpya brahmalayaṃ muniḥ ।। bandhasya viṣayāsaṅgi mukter nirviṣayaṃ tathā ।। cintayen muktaye tena brahmabhūtaṃ pareśvaram ।।
vikāryam ātmanaḥ śaktyā loham ākarṣako yathā ।। tasyā brahmaṇi saṃyogo yoga ity abhidhīyate ।। yasya yogaḥ sa vai yogī mumukṣur abhidhīyate ।। eko vai bandhamokṣasya na dvitīyo asti kaścana ।।
pūrve samudre yaḥ panthā na sa gacchati paścimam ।। saṅgasya karmaṇā buddhiḥ pūrvotpattau na saṃbhavet ।। evaṃ dharmo abhyupāyena nānyadharmeṣu kāraṇam ।। viniṣpannasamādhis tu parabrahmopalabdhimān ।।
janmāntarair abhyasato muktiḥ pūrvasya jāyate ।। prāpnoti yogī yogāgnidagdhakarmacayo acirāt ।। seveta yogī niṣkāmo yogyatāṃ svamano nayan ।। kurvīta brahmaṇi tathā parasmin pravaṇaṃ manaḥ ।।
viśiṣṭaphaladāḥ kāmyā niṣkāmānāṃ vimuktidāḥ ।। yamākhyair niyamākhyaiś ca yuñjīta niyato yatiḥ ।। prāṇāyāmaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sabījo abīja eva ca ।। kurutaḥ sa dvidhānena tṛtīyaḥ saṃyamāt tayoḥ ।।
ālambanam anantasya yogino abhyasataḥ smṛtam ।। kuryāc cittānukārīṇi pratyāhāraparāyaṇaḥ ।। indriyāṇām avaśyais tair na yogī yogasādhakaḥ ।। vaśīkṛtais tataḥ kuryāt sthitaṃ cetaḥ śubhāśraye ।।
yadādhāram aśeṣaṃ tad dhanti doṣasamudbhavam ।। bhūpa mūrtam amūrtaṃ ca paraṃ cāparam eva ca ।। brahmākhyā karmasaṃjñā ca tathā caivobhayātmikā ।। ubhayātmikā tathaivānyā trividhā bhāvabhāvanā ।।
karmabhāvanayā cānye devādyāḥ sthāvarāś carāḥ ।। adhikārabodhayukteṣu vidyate bhāvabhāvanā ।। viśvam etat paraṃ cānyad bhedabhinnadṛśāṃ nṛpa ।। vacasām ātmasaṃvedyaṃ taj jñānaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam ।।
viśvasvarūpavairūpyalakṣaṇaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।। tataḥ sthūlaṃ hare rūpaṃ cintayed viśvagocaram ।। maruto vasavo rudrā bhāskarās tārakā grahāḥ ।। manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ śailāḥ samudrāḥ sarito drumāḥ ।।
pradhānādiviśeṣāntaṃ cetanācetanātmakam ।। mūrtam etad dhare rūpaṃ bhāvanātritayātmakam ।। parabrahmasvarūpasya viṣṇoḥ śaktisamanvitam ।। tattvāc ca śaktivikṣepāḥ tadājñāsaṃjñitā vibhoḥ ।।
avidyā karmasaṃjñānyā tṛtīyā śaktir iṣyate ।। saṃsāratāpān akhilān avāpnoty atisaṃtatān ।। sarvabhūteṣu bhūpāla tāratamyena lakṣyate ।। sarīsṛpeṣu tebhyo anyāpy atiśaktyā patattriṣu ।।
paśubhyo manujāś cāpi śaktyā puṃsaḥ prabhāvitāḥ ।। tebhyo api nāgagandharvayakṣādyā devatā nṛpa ।। hiraṇyagarbho api tataḥ puṃsaḥ śaktyupalakṣitaḥ ।। yatas tacchaktiyogena yuktāni nabhasā yathā ।।
amūrtaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ yat sad ity ucyate budhaiḥ ।। tad viśvarūparūpaṃ vai rūpam anyad dharer mahat ।। devatiryaṅmanuṣyādiceṣṭāvanti svalīlayā ।। ceṣṭā tasyāprameyasya vyāpiny avyāhatātmikā ।।
cintyam ātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ sarvakilbiṣanāśanam ।। tathā cittasthito viṣṇur yogināṃ sarvakilbiṣam ।। kurvīta saṃsthitiṃ sā tu vijñeyā śuddhadhāraṇā ।। tribhāvabhāvanātīto muktaye yogināṃ nṛpa ।।
aśuddhās te samastās tu devādyāḥ karmayonayaḥ ।। eṣā vai dhāraṇā proktā yac cittaṃ tatra dhāryate ।। tac chrūyatām anādhāre dhāraṇā nopapadyate ।। sukapolaṃ suvistīrṇalalāṭaphalakojjvalam ।।
kambugrīvaṃ suvistīrṇaśrīvatsāṅkitavakṣasam ।। pralambāṣṭabhujaṃ viṣṇum athavāpi caturbhujam ।। cintayed brahmabhūtaṃ taṃ pītanirmalavāsasam ।। kirīṭacārukeyūrakaṭakādivibhūṣitam ।।
śārṅgaśaṅkhagadākhaḍgacakrākṣavalayānvitam ।। b varadābhayahastaṃ ca mudrikāhastabhūṣitam ।। b cintayet tanmayo yogī samādhāyātmamānasam ।। d nāpayāti yadā cittāt siddhāṃ manyeta tāṃ tadā ।।
cintayed bhagavadrūpaṃ praśāntaṃ sākṣasūtrakam ।। kirīṭakeyūramukhair bhūṣaṇai rahitaṃ smaret ।। kuryāt tato avayavini praṇidhānaparo bhavet ।। taddhyānaṃ prathamair aṅgaiḥ ṣaḍbhir niṣpādyate nṛpa ।।
manasā dhyānaniṣpādyaṃ samādhiḥ so abhidhīyate ।। prāpaṇīyas tathaivātmā prakṣīṇāśeṣabhāvanaḥ ।। niṣpādya muktikāryaṃ vai kṛtakṛtyaṃ nivartate ।। bhavaty abhedī bhedaś ca tasyājñānakṛto bhavet ।।
ātmano brahmaṇo bhedam asantaṃ kaḥ kariṣyati ।। saṃkṣepavistarābhyāṃ tu kim anyat kriyatāṃ tava ।। tavopadeśenāśeṣo naṣṭaś cittamalo yataḥ ।। narendra gadituṃ śakyam api vijñeyavedibhiḥ ।।
paramārthas tv asaṃlāpyo gocare vacasāṃ na saḥ ।। yad vimuktiprado yogaḥ proktaḥ keśidhvajāvyayaḥ ।। ājagāma puraṃ brahmaṃs tataḥ keśidhvajo nṛpaḥ ।। vanaṃ jagāma govinde viniveśitamānasaḥ ।।
viṣṇvākhye nirmale brahmaṇy avāpa nṛpatir layam ।। bubhuje viṣayān karma cakre cānabhisaṃdhitam ।। avāpa siddhim atyantatāpakṣayaphalāṃ dvija ।। ātyantiko vimuktir yā layo brahmaṇi śāśvate ।।
vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva bhavato gaditaṃ mayā ।। viśiṣṭaṃ sarvaśāstrebhyaḥ puruṣārthopapādakam ।। yad anyad api vaktavyaṃ tat pṛcchādya vadāmi te ।। śrutaṃ caitan mayā bhaktyā nānyat praṣṭavyam asti me ।।
tvatprasādān mayā jñātā utpattisthitisaṃyamāḥ ।। vijñātā cāpi kārtsnyena trividhā bhāvabhāvanā ।। yathaitad akhilaṃ viṣṇor jagan na vyatiricyate ।। varṇadharmādayo dharmā viditā yad aśeṣataḥ ।।
prasīda viprapravara nānyat praṣṭavyam asti me ।। tat kṣamyatāṃ viśeṣo asti na satāṃ putraśiṣyayoḥ ।। śrute asmin sarvadoṣotthaḥ pāparāśiḥ praṇaśyati ।। vaṃśānucaritaṃ kṛtsnaṃ mayātra tava kīrtitam ।।
yakṣā vidyādharāḥ siddhāḥ kathyante apsarasas tathā ।। cāturvarṇyaṃ tathā puṃsāṃ viśiṣṭacaritā narāḥ ।। parvatāś ca mahāpuṇyāś caritāni ca dhīmatām ।। yeṣāṃ saṃśravaṇāt sadyaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।
sa sarvabhūtaḥ sarvātmā kathyate bhagavān hariḥ ।। avaśenāpi yan nāmni kīrtite sarvapātakaiḥ ।। b tasmād vyāsād ahaṃ śrutvā bhavatāṃ pāpanāśanam ।। b pumān vimucyate sadyaḥ siṃhatrastair mṛgair iva ।। d
mayaitat kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sahasraiḥ saptasaṃkhyayā ।। maitreyāśeṣapāpānāṃ dhātūnām iva pāvakaḥ ।। kalikalmaṣam atyugraṃ narakārtipradaṃ nṛṇām ।। b tannāśanaṃ paraṃ bhaktyā harismaraṇam eva hi ।। b
tat kiṃcin na sthitaṃ vipra mārgaṇīyaṃ yad anyataḥ ।। b prayāti vilayaṃ sadyaḥ sakṛd yatra ca saṃsmṛte ।। d pāvakair vasubhiḥ sādhyair viśvedevādibhiḥ suraiḥ ।। apsarobhis tathā tārānakṣatraiḥ sakalair grahaiḥ ।।
brāhmaṇādyair manuṣyaiś ca tathaiva paśubhir mṛgaiḥ ।। vanādrisāgarasaritpātālaiḥ sadharādibhiḥ ।। meror ivāṇur yasyaitad yanmayaṃ ca dvijottama ।। bhagavān kīrtito viṣṇur atra pāpapraṇāśanaḥ ।।
tan maṅgalyaṃ svastyayanaṃ tat pavitram anuttamam ।। sakalaṃ tad avāpnoti śrutvaitan munisattama ।। kṛtopavāsaḥ prāpnoti tad asya śravaṇān naraḥ ।। mahāpuṇyamayaṃ vipra tad asya śravaṇāt sakṛt ।।
mathurāyāṃ hariṃ dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim ।। tad āpnoti phalaṃ samyak samādhānena kīrtanāt ।। b tad asya śravaxxxm ādareṇa sukīrtivān ।। b purāṇasyāsya viprarṣe keśavārpitamānasaḥ ।। d
jyeṣṭhāmūle amale pakṣe dvādaśyām upavāsakṛt ।। aśvamedhasya yajñasya prāpnoty avikalaṃ phalam ।। etat kilocur anyeṣām pitaraḥ sapitāmahāḥ ।। arcayiṣyati govindaṃ mathurāyām upoṣitaḥ ।।
parām ṛddhim avāpsyāmas tāritāḥ svakulodbhavaiḥ ।। dhanyānāṃ kulajaḥ piṇḍān yamunāyāṃ pradāsyati ।। dattvā piṇḍaṃ pitṛbhyaś ca yamunāsalilāplutaḥ ।। śrutvādhyāyaṃ tad āpnoti purāṇasyāsya bhaktimān ।।
duḥsvapnanāśanaṃ nṝṇāṃ sarvaduṣṭanibarhaṇam ।। maṅgalaṃ maṅgalānāṃ ca putrasaṃpatpradāyakam ।। ṛbhuḥ priyavratāyāha sa ca bhāguraye abravīt ।। sārasvatāya tenoktaṃ bhṛguḥ sārasvatād api ।।
narmadā dhṛtarāṣṭrāya nāgāyāpūraṇāya ca ।। vāsukiḥ prāha vatsāya vatsaś cāśvatarāya vai ।। kambalāya ca tenoktam elāpatrāya tena vai ।। prāptavān etad akhilaṃ sa vai pramataye dadau ।।
jātūkarṇena caivoktam anyeṣāṃ puṇyaśālinām ।। mayāpi tubhyaṃ maitreya yathāvat kathitaṃ tv idam ।। tvam apy etac chinīkāya kaler ante vadiṣyasi ।। yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ pāpaiḥ sa sarvair dvija mucyate ।।
kṛtā tena bhaved etad yaḥ śṛṇoti dine dine ।। śrutvaitat sakalaṃ vipra purāṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ mahat ।। vācakaṃ pūjayet tatra vyāsakalpaṃ dvijottama ।। dadyāc ca kāñcanaṃ gāvaś cābhramantaṃ svaśaktitaḥ ।।
vācake pūjitaṃ vipra pūjitas tena keśavaḥ ।। śrutvā tv asya daśādhyāyān avāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ ।। jñānaṃ jñeyam anantam ādirahitaṃ sarvāmarāṇāṃ hitaṃ sa prāpnoti na saṃśayo asty avikalaṃ yad vājimedhe phalam ।। tac chṛṇvan puruṣaḥ pavitraparamaṃ bhaktyā paṭhan dhārayan prāpnoty asti na tat samastabhuvaneṣv ekāntasiddhir hariḥ ।।
muktiṃ cetasi yaḥ sthito amaladhiyāṃ puṃsāṃ dadāty avyayaḥ kiṃ citraṃ yad aghaṃ prayāti vilayaṃ tatrācyute kīrtite ।। yaṃ saṃprāpya na jāyate na mriyate no vardhate hīyate naivāsan na ca sad bhavaty ati tataḥ kiṃ vā hareḥ śrūyatām ।। yasmin brahmaṇi sarvaśaktinilaye mānāni no mānināṃ niṣṭhāyai prabhavanti hanti kaluṣaṃ śrotraṃ sa yāto hariḥ ।। nāpakṣayaṃ ca samupaity avikalpavastu yas taṃ nato asmi puruṣottamam īśam īḍyam ।।
jñānānvitaḥ sakalatattvavibhūtikartā tasmai nato asmi puruṣāya sadāvyayāya ।। avyākṛtāya bhavabhāvanakāraṇāya vande svarūpabhavanāya sadājarāya ।। oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya ।। namas te astu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣapūrvaja ।।
puṃsaḥ samastakaraṇair upakārakāya vyaktāya sūkṣmavimalāya sadā nato asmi ।। pradiśatu bhagavān aśeṣapuṃsāṃ harir apajanmajarādikāṃ sa siddhim ।।
